Acakki 1:1 I acakki piny Lubaŋa oketo polo ki lobo.
Acakki 1:2 Lobo onoŋo tye nono, onyobbe woko atata piny macol ocido wi kut matut, kun Cwiny pa Lubaŋa twago wi pii.
Acakki 1:3 Lubaŋa owacci, “Wek leŋo obed tye”; ci piny obedo leŋ.
Acakki 1:4 Lubaŋa oneno leŋo ni ber; Lubaŋa opoko kin leŋo ki colpiny.
Acakki 1:5 Lubaŋa olwoŋo leŋo ni Dyeceŋ, ki colpiny olwoŋo ni Dyewor. Piny oyuto dok piny oru, meno nino acel.
Acakki 1:6 Lubaŋa owacci, “Wek pete orine i kin pii, me poko kin pii ki pii wadi.”
Acakki 1:7 Ci Lubaŋa otiyo pete me poko pii ma tye piny i te pete ki pii ma tye malo i wi pete; ci otimme kit meno.
Acakki 1:8 Lubaŋa olwoŋo dan pete ni polo. Piny oyuto dok piny oru, meno nino me aryone.
Acakki 1:9 Lubaŋa owacci, “Wek pii ma tye i te polo ocokke, ogurre i kabedo acel, wek piny mutwo onen”; ci otimme kit meno.
Acakki 1:10 Lubaŋa olwoŋo piny mutwo ni Lobo, ki pii ma ocokke, ogurre kacel-li ni Nam; ci Lubaŋa oneno ni ber.
Acakki 1:11 Lubaŋa owacci, “Wek lum otwi i wi lobo, ki ginapita ma nyako nyiggi, ki yadi ma nyako nyiggi ma kodi tye i igi, macalo kit kwagi tye, i wi lobo”; ci otimme kit meno.
Acakki 1:12 Lum ocako twi i wi lobo, ki ginapita ma nyako nyiggi i kit kwagi acel acel, ki yadi ma nyako nyiggi ma kodi tye i igi, macalo kit kwagi tye. Ci Lubaŋa oneno ni ber.
Acakki 1:13 Piny oyuto dok piny oru, meno nino me adekke.
Acakki 1:14 Lubaŋa owacci, “Wek gin ma ryeny obed i kom pete me polo me poko dyeceŋ ki dyewor, ki me bedo ginanena ma nyuto kare ki nino ki mwaka,
Acakki 1:15 wek gubed gin ma ryeny i kom pete me polo ma menyo lobo”; ci otimme kit meno.
Acakki 1:16 Lubaŋa oketo gin madito aryo ma giryeny, wek ma ryeny madit-te aye olo dyeceŋ, ki ma ryeny matidine olo dyewor; dok oketo lwak lakalatwe bene.
Acakki 1:17 Lubaŋa oketogi i kom pete me polo me menyo lobo,
Acakki 1:18 me loyo dyeceŋ ki dyewor, ki me poko kin leŋo ki colpiny. Ci Lubaŋa oneno ni ber.
Acakki 1:19 Piny oyuto dok piny oru, meno nino me aŋwenne.
Acakki 1:20 Lubaŋa owacci, “Wek pii onywal gin makwo ma gicorre limuk, ki winyo bene gutuk lamalo i wi lobo i dan pete me polo.”
Acakki 1:21 Lubaŋa oketo nyaŋ madoŋo i nam, ki kwa gin makwo ducu ma gimol, ma gicorre limuk i pii, macalo kit kwagi tye, ki winyo ma gituk ki bwomgi, macalo kit kwagi tye. Ci Lubaŋa oneno ni ber.
Acakki 1:22 Lubaŋa omiyogi gum kun wacci, “Wunywal, wunya, wupoŋ pii ki nami, winyo bene gunya i wi lobo.”
Acakki 1:23 Piny oyuto dok piny oru, meno nino me abicce.
Acakki 1:24 Lubaŋa owacci, “Wek lobo onywal gin makwo i kit kwagi: lee ma paco, ki gin ma lak alaka, ki lee me tim macalo kit kwagi tye”; ci otimme kit meno.
Acakki 1:25 Lubaŋa oketo lee tim macalo kit kwagi tye, ki lee ma paco macalo kit kwagi tye, ki gin ma lak alaka piny i ŋom, macalo kit kwagi tye. Ci Lubaŋa oneno ni ber.
Acakki 1:26 Lubaŋa owacci, “Weku wacweyu dano ma gical ki wan; wek gin aye gulo rec ma i nam, ki winyo me polo, ki lee ma paco, ki wi lobo ducu, gulo bene gin ducu ma lak alaka wi lobo,”
Acakki 1:27 Lubaŋa ocweyo dano i Kit calle kikome; ocweyo laco ki dako.
Acakki 1:28 Lubaŋa omiyogi gum kun wacogi ni, “Wunywal, wunya, wupoŋ lobo, wulo bene; dok wulo wa rec ma i nam, ki winyo me polo, ki gin ducu makwo ma giwoto i wi lobo.”
Acakki 1:29 Lubaŋa owacci, “Nenu, amiyowu ginapita ducu ma nyako nyiggi ma tye i wi lobo ducu, ki yadi ducu ma nyako nyiggi ma kodi tye i igi; wubicamogi.
Acakki 1:30 Dok lee ducu me tim, ki winyo ducu me polo, ki gin ducu ma lak alaka wi lobo, ma gitye ki kwo, amiyo botgi ginapita ducu madyak me bedo camgi”; ci otimme kit meno.
Acakki 1:31 Lubaŋa oneno gin ma doŋ otiyo ducu, ci nen, tye mabeco twatwal. Piny oyuto dok piny oru, meno nino me abicelle.
Acakki 2:1 Polo ki lobo yam giketo otum kit meno, ki lwak mony ma tye iye ducu.
Acakki 2:2 I kom nino me abiro en aye Lubaŋa otyeko iye ticce ducu ma yam otiyo; en
oywe i kom nino me abiro i kom ticce ducu ma yam otiyo.
Acakki 2:3 Ci Lubaŋa omiyo gum i kom nino me abiro, olonyo obedo maleŋ, pien i kom nino
meno en aye Lubaŋa yam oywe iye i kom ticce ducu ma en obedo ka tiyo me keto lobo.
Acakki 2:4 Man aye acakki nya pa kwa gin ma i polo ki i lobo i kare ma giketogi kwede. I nino meno ma Rwot Lubaŋa otiyo iye polo ki lobo-ni,
Acakki 2:5 yat mo me tim onoŋo peya tye i wi lobo, onoŋo doo mo pud pe ma otwi wi lobo,
onoŋo Rwot Lubaŋa peya omiyo kot ocwer i lobo, dok onoŋo peya tye dano mo ma puro lobo;
Acakki 2:6 ento lupu ocako duny malo, ci obido lobo ducu.
Acakki 2:7 Ci Rwot Lubaŋa ocweyo dano ki apwa me ŋom, okuto yamo me yweyo i ume,
dano odoko gin makwo.
Acakki 2:8 Rwot Lubaŋa opito yadi i poto ma tye i Eden, tuŋ wokceŋ: en aye oketo iye dano
ma en ocweyo-ni.
Acakki 2:9 Dok Rwot Lubaŋa omiyo yadi gutwi i ŋom, kwa yadi ducu mamwonya ma neno
ber, ki mabeco me acama, dok oketo yat me kwo i dye poto bene, ki yat me ŋeyo
gin maber ki marac.
Acakki 2:10 Kulu yam onoŋo mol a ki i Eden, ma kelo pii i poto, iye opokke ki kunnu, odoko
kulu aŋwen.
Acakki 2:11 Nyiŋ kulu mukwoŋone Picon; en aye kulu ma mol rumo lobo Kavila ducu, ma a
iye jabu.
Acakki 2:12 Jabu ma tye i lobo meno beco; odok yat ma gilwoŋo bedola ki got onik tye
kunnu bene.
Acakki 2:13 Nyiŋ kulu me aryone Gikon, ma orumo lobo ducu me Kuc.
Acakki 2:14 Ki nyiŋ kulu me Taigric; mol dok tuŋ wokceŋ me Aciria. Ki kulu me aŋwenne
Euprate.
Acakki 2:15 Rwot Lubaŋa otero dano, oketo i poto Eden wek opur, dok ogwok bene,
Acakki 2:16 ci Rwot Lubaŋa ociko dano ni, “Yadi ducu ma tye i poto, camgi macalo imito;
Acakki 2:17 ento yat me ŋeyo gin maber ki marac pe icam, pien i nino ma ibicamo iye, en
aye ibito iye bene.”
Acakki 2:18 Ka doko Rwot Lubaŋa owaco ni, “Pe ber dano obed kene; abitimo lakony ma
romme.”
Acakki 2:19 Ci Rwot Lubaŋa ocweyo lee tim ducu ki winyo ducu me polo, nia ki i ŋom,
okelogi bot dano me neno kit ma ebicako ki nyiŋgi. Kit ma yam dano ocako ki
nyiŋ gin makwo acel acel ducu, en aye obedo nyiŋgi.
Acakki 2:20 Dano ocako nyiŋ lee ma paco ducu, ki winyo me polo, ki lee tim ducu; ento
lakony pa dano ma romme aye onoŋo pud pe onen.
Acakki 2:21 Rwot Lubaŋa omiyo nino madwoŋ omako waŋ dano; ka en tye ka nino, ci
okwanyo cogo lak ŋete acel, omwono waŋe woko ki riŋo.
Acakki 2:22 Ci cogo ma Rwot Lubaŋa okwanyoni ocweyo odoko dako, ka okelo bote.
Acakki 2:23 Dano owacci, “Man aye cogo mua i cogona kikome, ki riŋo bene mua i riŋona
kikome; gibilwoŋo nyiŋe ni Dako, pien gikwanyo ki i kom Laco.”
Acakki 2:24 Mumiyo laco weko wonne ki minne, moko kom dakone likaŋ, gin aryo gidoko
kom acel.
Acakki 2:25 I kare meno laco ki dakone onoŋo pud gibedo munero ma lewic pe makogi.
Acakki 3:1 Twol yam onoŋo ryek makato lee tim ducu ma Rwot Lubaŋa oketo. En owaco ki dako ni, “Lubaŋa mono owacci, ‘Pe wucam yat ducu ma tye i poto-ni’?”
Acakki 3:2 Dako otito ki twol ni, “Watwero camo nyig yadi ducu ma tye i poto-ni, 3ento Lubaŋa ociko ni, ‘Pe wubicamo nyig yat ma tye i dye poto, pe wugud kome bene, wek pe wuto.’”
Acakki 3:4 Ci twol owaco ki dako ni, “Pe wubito.”
Acakki 3:5 Pien Lubaŋa ŋeyo ni, ka wucamo, ci waŋwu biyabbe woko, ci wubidoko calo Lubaŋa, miyo wuŋeyo gin maber ki marac.”
Acakki 3:6 Ka dako oneno ni yat-te ber me acama, dok nen mwonya bene, dok yat meno ber, cwiny dano pyette i kome, pien miyo gidoko ryek, ci opwono nyige, ocamo; omiyo mogo bot cware, ci ocamo.
Acakki 3:7 Gin aryo ducu wangi oyabbe woko, gucako ŋeyo ni kara gitye munero, ka gukwoyo pot olam guruko i pyergi.
Acakki 3:8 Ka guwinyo Rwot Lubaŋa woto i poto i kare ma ceŋ okwe, ci dano ki dakone gukanne woko i nyim Rwot Lubaŋa i kin yadi ma tye i poto.
Acakki 3:9 Ci Rwot Lubaŋa olwoŋo dano kun wacce ni, “In mono it ye kwene, kaa?”
Acakki 3:10 En ogamo ni, “Awinyo ka iwoto i poto, ci lworo omaka, pien atye munero, akanne woko.”
Acakki 3:11 Dok openye aye ni, “Aŋa ma doŋ otitti ni it ye munero? Ityeko camo nyig yat ma onoŋo aciki ni pe icam-mi ce?”
Acakki 3:12 Dano ogamo ni, “Dako ma imiya ni obed kweda-ni aye omiya nyig yat meno, ci acamo.”
Acakki 3:13 Rwot Lubaŋa dok openyo dako ni, “Man kono itimo piŋo?” Dako ogamo ni, “Twol aye obwola, omiya acamo.”
Acakki 3:14 Rwot Lubaŋa owaco bot twol ni, “Pien in aye itimo man, giceno in makato lee ma paco ducu, ki makato lee tim ducu. Ibilak, iywane piny ki ii, dok ibicamo apwa i kare me kwoni ducu.
Acakki 3:15 Abiketo mone i kin in ki dako, ki i kin likwayi ki Likwaye; en bigoyo wii, in ibitoŋo opunye.”
Acakki 3:16 Ki bot dako owacce ni, “Abimeddi arem matek i kare me owacci, nyodo; ibinywalo litino ki arem, cwinyi bipyette i kom cwari dok en aye biloyi.”
Acakki 3:17 Ki bot Adam owacce ni, “Pien in aye iwinyo dog dakoni, ci icamo nyig yat ma aciki iye ni, ‘Pe icam’, giceno lobo piri: ibicamone ki aroma i kare me kwoni ducu.
Acakki 3:18 Loboni biceko okuto ki ocok, ibicamo pot dek ma i tim.
Acakki 3:19 Ibicamo kwon ki kwok ma cwer ki i tur nyimi, nio ka ibidok i ŋom, kit ma con gikwanyi ki iye; in apwa, dok bene ibidok i apwa.”
Acakki 3:20 Dano ocako nyiŋ dakone ni Kawa, pien en aye megi jo ducu makwo.
Acakki 3:21 Rwot Lubaŋa oyubo laa aruka, ka omiyo Adam ki dakone guruko.
Acakki 3:22 Rwot Lubaŋa owacci, “Nen, dano doŋ odoko rom ki ŋat acel i kinwa, doŋ ŋeyo gin maber ki gin marac. Kombeddi pe dok wawek orye ciŋe opwon nyig yat me kwo ocam doki, miyo doŋ bibedo makwo nakanaka.”
Acakki 3:23 Mumiyo Rwot Lubaŋa ocwale woko ki i poto Eden, wek odok opur gire ŋom ma yam gikwanye ki iye-ni.
Acakki 3:24 Oryemo dano woko, ci oketo lukerubi yo tuŋ wokceŋ me poto Eden, ki pala lucwan ma lyel mac, ma wirre tuŋŋi ki tuŋŋi, me gwoko yo ma cito i kom yat me kwo.
Acakki 4:1 Adam oŋeyo dakone Kawa, ci dakone ogamo ic, onywalo Kain, “Doŋ atyeko noŋo latin laco ma Rwot okonya kwede.”
Acakki 4:2 Ka dok onywalo ominne Abel. Abel obedo lakwat romi, Kain obedo lapur poto.
Acakki 4:3 Ka kare mo okato, Kain okelo cam ma oceko i potone, otyero bot Rwot.
Acakki 4:4 Abel okelo mere litino kayo romi ki dwologi. Ci Rwot ojolo Abel ki motte,
Acakki 4:5 ento pe ojolo Kain ki motte; omiyo Kain okeco, waŋe oballe.
Acakki 4:6 Rwot owaco bot Kain ni, “Ikeco piŋo? Waŋi oballe piŋo?
Acakki 4:7 Ka itimo maber pe giye? Ka pe itimo maber, ci bal buto i doggola macalo ŋuu ma cwinye pyette i komi; ento myero iloye.”
Acakki 4:8 Kain owaco bot ominne Abel ni, “Wacit i poto.” Ka gitye i poto, Kain ocako lweny kom ominne Abel, ci oneko woko.
Acakki 4:9 Ci Lubaŋa owaco bot Kain ni, “Omeru Abel tye kwene?” En ogamo ni, “Pe aŋeyo; an aye lagwok omera bo?”
Acakki 4:10 Rwot owacce ni, “Man doŋ itimo piŋo? Nen, remo pa omeru tye ka koko i nyima, winnye a ki i nom.
Acakki 4:11 Koni doŋ giceni woko ki i lobo, ma oŋamo doge me mato remo pa omeru ma iojo-ni.
Acakki 4:12 Ka ipuro poto, pe bicekki cam ki tekke ducu; ibibedo lamal-gaŋ kun imal ata i lobo.”
Acakki 4:13 Kain owaco bot Rwot ni, “Twon can ma imiya-ni obwoyo koma woko do.
Acakki 4:14 Nen, doŋ iryema woko tin ki i poto, abikanne woko ki i waŋi; abibedo lamal-gaŋ kun amal ata i lobo, jo ducu ma binoŋa, bi neka woko.”
Acakki 4:15 Rwot owacce ni, “Pe kumeno! Ka ŋatti mo bineko Kain, gibiculo kwor i kome tyen abiro kulu.” Rwot oketo lanyut mo i kom Kain, wek jo ma binoŋe pe guneke.
Acakki 4:16 Kain ocako a woko ki i nyim Rwot, ocito obedo i lobo Nod, tuŋ wokceŋ me Eden.
Acakki 4:17 Kain oŋene ki dakone, ci dakone ogamo ic, onywalo Enoka. Ocako gero gaŋ madit, ocako nyiŋ gaŋ meno macalo nyiŋ wode, ni Enoka.
Acakki 4:18 Enoka onywalo Irad, Irad onywalo Mekujael, Mekujael onywalo Metucael, Metucael onywalo Lamek.
Acakki 4:19 Lamek onyomo mon aryo; nyiŋ dako acel Ada, ki nyiŋ mukene Jilla.
Acakki 4:20 Ada onywalo Jabal; en aye nene won jo ma gibedo i kema, ki wegi lim makwo.
Acakki 4:21 Nyiŋ ominne Jubal, en aye nene won jo ma gigoyo opuk ki lukut nyamulere.
Acakki 4:22 Jilla onywalo Tubalkain; en aye nene latet kit kwa jami tic ducu me mola ki nyonyo. Lamin Tubal-kain nyiŋe Naama.
Acakki 4:23 Lamek owaco bot monne ni, “Ada ki Jilla, wuwiny; wun mon pa Lamek, wuwiny lok ma awacciwu: Atyeko neko dano ma omiya ret, aneko awobi mo ma ogoya-ni.
Acakki 4:24 Ka Kain gibiculo kwor i kome tyen abiro, Lamek gibiculo kwor i kome tyen pyerabiro wiye abiro kulu.”
Acakki 4:25 Adam dok oŋene ki dakone, ci dakone onywalo latin laco, ocako nyiŋe Ceji, pien owacci, “Lubaŋa dok omiya latin mukene muleyo ka Abel, ma yam Kain onekoni.”
Acakki 4:26 Ceji bene onywalo latin awobi, ocako nyiŋe Enoci. I kare meno en aye dano gucako lwoŋo iye nyiŋ Rwot.
Acakki 5:1 Man aye buk me tekwaro pa Adam. I kare ma Lubaŋa oketo dano, ocweyo i kitcalle kikome.
Acakki 5:2 Yam oketo laco ki dako, omiyogi gum, ocako nyiŋgi ni Dano i nino ma conoketogi iye-ni.
Acakki 5:3 Ka Adam doŋ otyeko ri mwaka miya acel ki pyeradek, en onywalo awobi ma calo en kikome, ci ocako nyiŋe Ceji.
Acakki 5:4 Mwaka pa Adam ma onoŋo doŋ otyeko nywalo Ceji romo miya aboro, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:5 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Adam ducu oromo mwaka miya aboŋwen ki pyeradek; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 5:6 Ka Ceji doŋ otyeko ri mwaka miya acel ki abic, ci onywalo Enoci.
Acakki 5:7 Ceji ori i ŋe nywalo Enoci mwaka miya aboro ki abiro, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:8 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Ceji ducu oromo mwaka miya aboŋwen ki apar wiye aryo; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 5:9 Ka Enoci doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyeraboŋwen, ci onywalo Kenan.
Acakki 5:10 Enoci ori i ŋe nywalo Kenan mwaka miya aboro ki apar wiye abic, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:11 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Enoci ducu oromo mwaka miya aboŋwen ki abic; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 5:12 Ka Kenan doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyerabiro, ci onywalo Maalalel.
Acakki 5:13 Kenan ori i ŋe nywalo Maalalel mwaka miya aboro ki pyeraŋwen, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:14 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Kenan ducu oromo mwaka miya aboŋwen ki apar; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 5:15 Ka Maalalel doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyerabicel wiye abic, ci onywalo Jared.
Acakki 5:16 Maalalel ori i ŋe nywalo Jared mwaka miya aboro ki pyeradek, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:17 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Maalalel ducu oromo mwaka miya aboro ki pyeraboŋwen wiye abic; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 5:18 Ka Jared doŋ otyeko ri mwaka miya acel ki pyerabicel wiye aryo, ci onywalo Enoka.
Acakki 5:19 Jared ori i ŋe nywalo Enoka mwaka miya aboro, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:20 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Jared ducu oromo mwaka miya aboŋwen ki pyerabicel wiye aryo; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 5:21 Ka Enoka doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyerabicel wiye abic, ci onywalo Metucela.
Acakki 5:22 Enoka obedo ka wot kacel ki Lubaŋa i ŋe nywalo Metucela mwaka miya adek, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:23 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Enoka ducu oromo mwaka miya adek ki pyerabicel wiye abic.
Acakki 5:24 Enoka obedo ka wot kacel ki Lubaŋa; ci orwenyo woko matwal, pien Lubaŋa otere woko.
Acakki 5:25 Ka Metucela doŋ otyeko ri mwaka miya acel ki pyeraboro wiye abiro, ci onywalo Lamek.
Acakki 5:26 Metucela ori i ŋe nywalo Lamek mwaka miya abiro ki pyeraboro wiye aryo, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:27 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Metucela ducu oromo mwaka miya aboŋwen ki pyerabicel wiye aboŋwen; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 5:28 Ka Lamek doŋ ori mwaka miya acel ki pyeraboro wiye aryo, ci onywalo wode,
Acakki 5:29 ma ocako nyiŋe Nua, kun wacci, “I lobo ma yam Rwot oceno-ni, latin man aye bimiyo waywe ki aroma tic me ciŋwa.”
Acakki 5:30 Lamek ori i ŋe nywalo awobe mukene ki anyira bene.
Acakki 5:31 Kit meno nino me kwo pa Lamek ducu oromo mwaka miya abiro ki pyerabiro wiye abiro; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 5:32 Nua ka otyeko mwaka me ditte, miya abic, ci onywalo Cem, Kam ki Yafeci.
Acakki 6:1 Ka dano gucako medde wi lobo, ci gunywalo anyira.
Acakki 6:2 Ka awobe pa Lubaŋa guneno anyira pa dano beco, gucako yero me anyoma ki i kingi.
Acakki 6:3 Ci Rwot owacci, "Cwinya pe doŋ bibedo i dano matwal, pien en kom mamwa, ento kare me kwone bibedo mwaka miya acel ki pyeraryo."
Acakki 6:4 Jo Nepil onoŋo gitye i lobo i kare meno, ki lacen bene, i kare ma awobe pa Lubaŋa guyabo wi anyira pa dano, gunywalo kwedgi litino. Gin aye cog jo matego mukwoŋo i lobo, ma nyiŋgi ŋene matek.
Acakki 6:5 Rwot oneno ni bal pa dano odoko dit woko i wi lobo, dok tam ducu ma cwinygi lwodo kare ducu kemo bal keken.
Acakki 6:6 Rwot oŋut pi cweyo dano i lobo, ocwero cwinye matek.
Acakki 6:7 Rwot owacci, "Abijwero dano woko ma yam aketo-ni ki wi lobo, dano ki lee ki gin ma lak alaka ki winyo me polo, pien doŋ atyeko ŋut pi cweyogi."
Acakki 6:8 Ento Nua aye onoŋo yomo cwiny Rwot.
Acakki 6:9 Man aye tekwaro pa Nua. Nua yam obedo dano ma kite atir, ma pe ki bal mo i kin yalwakke; Nua obedo ka wot kacel ki Lubaŋa.
Acakki 6:10 Nua onoŋo tye ki awobene adek, Cem, Kam ki Yafeci.
Acakki 6:11 Lobo oballe woko ki i nyim Lubaŋa, onoŋo doŋ opoŋ ki bwami.
Acakki 6:12 Ka Lubaŋa oneno lobo, oneno oballe woko, pien dano ducu gutyeko balle woko i kit bedogi i wi lobo.
Acakki 6:13 Ci Lubaŋa owaco ki Nua ni, "Agik pa dano ducu doŋ obino i nyima, pien gupoŋo lobo woko ki bwami; nen, abityekogi woko, kacel ki lobo bene.
Acakki 6:14 Pa yeya meri ki yat gofer; ci ipok kicika i yeya, ka imwon iye ki ŋeye ki odok abic
Acakki 6:15 Ibitiyone kit man: yeya borre biromo yadi miya acel ki pyerabic, ki lacce yadi pyeraryo wiye abic, borre tuŋ malo yadi apar wiye abic.
Acakki 6:16 Tuc waŋ dirica i yeya, kun iweko danne malo doŋ futi acel ki nucu; ka iket doggola i but yeya, ci ipok iye obed kabedo adek, ma pinnye, me aryone ki me adekke ma malone.
Acakki 6:17 Pien nen, abicoro pii aluka madwoŋ i wi lobo, wek otyek kom gin ducu ma tye ki kwo, i te polo, wek gin ducu ma gitye i wi lobo oto woko.
Acakki 6:18 Ento in aye abimoko gicikkena kwedi; ibidonyo i yeya, in kacel ki litinoni, ki dakoni, ki mon pa awobeni ducu.
Acakki 6:19 Kwany gin makwo ducu ma gitye ki kom ki aryo aryo ki i kit kwagi acel acel, ci ipikgi i yeya, wek gubed kwo kacel ki in; gubed co ki mon.
Acakki 6:20 Winyo macalo kit kwagi tye, lee macalo kit kwagi tye, gin ma lak alaka i ŋom macalo kit kwagi tye, gin bibino boti ki aryo aryo ki i kit kwagi acel acel wek gubed kwo.
Acakki 6:21 Dok iter kit kwa cam ducu ma gicamo, ci ikangi; wek gubed me acamagi bene."
Acakki 6:22 Nua otimo kumeno; ocobo ducu macalo Lubaŋa ocike.
Acakki 7:1 Rwot owaco bot Nua ni, "Dony i yeya, in kacel ki jo ma i odi ducu, pien atyeko neno ni in aye kiti atir i nyima ki i kin yalwak me kare man.
Acakki 7:2 Ter lee ma gicamo abiro abiro, twonne ki minne, ki lee ma gikwero aryo aryo, twonne ki minne;
Acakki 7:3 ki winyo me polo bene abiro abiro, ma co ki ma mon, wek kit kwagi obed makwo wi lobo ducu.
Acakki 7:4 Pien odoŋ nino abiro, ka doŋ abimiyo kot cwer i lobo nino pyeraŋwen dyeceŋ ki dyewor benebene, ci gin ducu makwo ma yam aketo-ni, abijwerogi woko ki i wi lobo."
Acakki 7:5 Nua ocobo kit ma Rwot ocike kwede ducu.
Acakki 7:6 Nua onoŋo doŋ tye ki mwaka me ditte miya abicel i kare ma pii aluka ocorre i wi lobo.
Acakki 7:7 Ci Nua ki dakone ki awo bene ki mongi gudonyo i yeya pi riŋo pii aluka.
Acakki 7:8 Lee ducu ma gicamo ki ma gikwero, ki winyo-gu, ki gin ma lak alaka i ŋom,
Acakki 7:9 gudonyo i yeya bot Nua aryo aryo, laco ki dako.
Acakki 7:10 I ŋe nino abiro pii aluka opoŋ, obyennye i wi lobo.
Acakki 7:11 I mwaka me miya abicel me dit pa Nua, i dwe me aryo, i nino dwe me apar wiye abirone, i nino meno aye waŋ it ducu me kut matut gumwoc woko ki pii, ki polo bene oyabbe.
Acakki 7:12 Ci kot ocorre i wi lobo nino pyeraŋwen dyeceŋ ki dyewor benebene.
Acakki 7:13 I kom nino meno kikome, Nua ki awobene Cem, Kam ki Yafeci, ki dakone en Nua, ki mon wote adek kacel kwedgi, gudonyo i yeya,
Acakki 7:14 gin ki lee tim ducu macalo kit kwagi tye, ki lee ma paco ducu macalo kit kwagi tye, ki gin ducu ma lak alaka wi lobo macalo kit kwagi tye, ki winyo ducu macalo kit kwagi tye, winyo ducu ki kitgi ducu mapatpat.
Acakki 7:15 Gin ducu ma gitye ki kwo gudonyo i yeya bot Nua ki aryo aryo.
Acakki 7:16 Gin ma gudonyo iye me kit kom ducu mapatpat, ma co ki ma mon, gudonyo iye kit ma con Lubaŋa ociko ki Nua; ci Rwot oloro wigi woko.
Acakki 7:17 Pii aluka ori wi lobo pi nino pyeraŋwen kulu; pii opoŋ, omedde ameda nio ka otiŋo yeya, otero yeya malo twatwal nia ki wi lobo.
Acakki 7:18 Pii opoŋ, omedde, ocegge woko wi lobo; yeya obedo ka kwaŋ i wi pii malo.
Acakki 7:19 Pii ocegge woko wi lobo ki tekke, nio ka oumo wi godi maboco ma tye i te polo ducu.
Acakki 7:20 Pii omedde, omwonyo wi godi woko futi pyeraryo kulu.
Acakki 7:21 Gin makwo ducu ma yam giwoto i wi lobo guto woko; winyo, lee ma paco, ki lee tim, gin ducu ma nya, ma gicorre limuk i wi lobo, kacel ki dano, ducu guto woko.
Acakki 7:22 Gin ducu ma yam gitye ki yweyo me kwo i umgi, ma i wi tura, guto woko.
Acakki 7:23 Lubaŋa ojwero gin ducu makwo ma yam gitye wi lobo, dano ki lee ki gin ma lak alaka, ki winyo me polo; ojwerogi woko nia ki i lobo. Nua keken aye odoŋ, ki jo ma yam gitye kwede i yeya-ni.
Acakki 7:24 Ci pii ocegge wi lobo nino miya acel ki pyerabic kulu.
Acakki 8:1 Lubaŋa opo kom Nua ki lee tim ducu, ki lee ma paco ducu ma yam tye kacel kwede i yeya. Lubaŋa omiyo yamo okodo wi lobo, ci pii ocako dwon.
Acakki 8:2 Waŋ it me kut matut oculle woko, ki polo bene ocegge woko, ki kot ma corre a ki i polo bene ocok woko,
Acakki 8:3 pii omedde ki dwon woko i wi lobo jwijwi. Ka nino okato miya acel ki pyerabic, pii onoŋo odwon woko.
Acakki 8:4 I dwe me abiro, i nino dwe apar wiye abirone, yeya ogem i wi got Ararat.
Acakki 8:5 Pii omedde ki dwon woko nio kwede i dwe me apar; i dwe me apar, i nino dwe acel, wi godi maboco gucako nen.
Acakki 8:6 Ka nino pyeraŋwen okato, Nua oyabo waŋ dirica ma yam otuco i yeya-ni,
Acakki 8:7 ocwalo agak woko; ci obedo ka tuk, kun wirre kwede tuŋŋi ki tuŋŋi, nio ka piny otwo woko.
Acakki 8:8 Dok ocwalo amam woko nia ki bote, wek enen ka pii doŋ otyeko dwon woko ki i lobo ada.
Acakki 8:9 Ento amam pe omedo ki noŋo ka ma opye iye ki tyene, ci odok bote cen i yeya, pien onoŋo pii pud omwonyo wi lobo woko ducu. Ci Nua oryeyo bade, omake, odwoke i yeya bote.
Acakki 8:10 Dok okuro pi nino abiro mukene, ka dok ocwalo amam woko nia ki i yeya.
Acakki 8:11 Amam dok odok bote i yeya ma onoŋo piny doŋ oyuto; nen, en otino pot yat jeituni ma opwono madyak i doge. Kit meno Nua oniaŋ ni pii doŋ otyeko dwon woko ki i wi lobo.
Acakki 8:12 Dok omedde ki kuro pi nino abiro mukene, dok ocwalo amam woko; ci doŋ pe odok bote matwal.
Acakki 8:13 I mwaka me miya abicel ki acel me dit pa Nua, i dwe mukwoŋo, i nino dwe acel, en aye pii otwo iye woko liweŋ wi lobo. Nua ocako puto wi yeya woko, ci oneno wi lobo otwo woko.
Acakki 8:14 I dwe me aryo, i nino dwe pyeraryo wiye abiro, onoŋo lobo doŋ otwo woko.
Acakki 8:15 Lubaŋa owaco bot Nua ni,
Acakki 8:16 "Doŋ ikat woko ki i yeya, in ki dakoni, ki awobeni ki mongi kacel kwedi.
Acakki 8:17 Kel woko gin makwo ducu ma gitye kwedi, wa kit kom ducu, winyo ki lee ki gin ducu ma lak alaka wi lobo, wek gucorre i wi lobo, kun ginywal, ginya i wi lobo."
Acakki 8:18 Kit meno Nua okato woko, ki awobene ki dakone, ki mon pa awobene kacel kwede.
Acakki 8:19 Ki lee ducu ki gin ducu ma lak alaka, ki winyo ducu, gin ducu ma giwoto wi lobo, gucako mol, gukato woko ki i yeya, ma oporo kit kwagi ducu.
Acakki 8:20 Nua ocano keno tyer pi Rwot, ci oyero lee ma gicamo ki i kit kwagi acel acel, ki winyo ma gicamo ki i kit kwagi acel acel, otyero gitum awaŋa i wi keno tyer.
Acakki 8:21 Ka Rwot oŋweyo gin ma ŋwece kur ma yomo cwiny. Rwot oloko i cwinye kekene ni, "An pe dok abiceno lobo pi dano, kadi bed tam ducu ma i cwinye kemo bal keken nia wa i tinone; pe doŋ abineko gin makwo ducu kit ma yam atimo.
Acakki 8:22 Ka lobo pud tye, ci kare me coc ki kac, wa koyo ki lyeto, ki oro ki cwir, dyeceŋ ki dyewor, pe bigik matwal."
Acakki 9:1 Lubaŋa omiyo gum i kom Nua ki litino awo bene kun waco ni, "Wunywal, wunya, wek wupoŋ lobo.
Acakki 9:2 Lee tim ducu bilworowu ki myelkom, wa winyo bene ducu me polo, ki gin ma lak alaka i ŋom, ki rec ducu ma i nam bene; gityeko miyogi ducu i ciŋwu.
Acakki 9:3 Gin ducu ma woto, ma kwo, gibibedo cam mewu; kit ma yam amiyowu pot dek-ki, doŋ amiyowu jami ducu.
Acakki 9:4 Ento pe wubicamo riŋo kacel ki kwone, ma en aye remone.
Acakki 9:5 Atikane abipido pi remo kwowu; abipido pire bot lee ducu, wa ki bot dano bene; ki tuŋ bot dano acel acel abipido pi kwo pa ominne.
Acakki 9:6 Ka ŋatti mo ooyo remo pa dano mo, ci dano meno gibioyo remone bene; pien Lubaŋa ocweyo dano i calle kikome.
Acakki 9:7 Wun wunywal, wunya wumedde madwoŋ i wi lobo, wunya iye."
Acakki 9:8 Lubaŋa dok owaco bot Nua ki awobene ma onoŋo gitye kacel kwede ni,
Acakki 9:9 "Nen, amoko gicikkena kwedwu ki likwayowu ma bilubowu,
Acakki 9:10 ki gin makwo ducu ma gitye kwedwu, winyo ki lee ma paco ki lee tim ducu ma gitye kacel kwedwu, gin ducu ma gukato woko ki i yeya.
Acakki 9:11 Amoko gicikkena kwedwu ni, pii aluka pe dok bineko gin makwo, dok pe bibedo aluka ma bityeko lobo."
Acakki 9:12 Lubaŋa dok owacci, "Man aye lanyut me gicikke ma aketo i kin an ki wun ki gin makwo ducu ma gitye kwedwu, ma bibedo matwal i yalwak ducu.
Acakki 9:13 Aketo danyu mera i pol, ma bibedo lanyut me gicikkena i kin an ki lobo.
Acakki 9:14 Ka amiyo pol oyuŋŋe i wi lobo, ci danyu binen i pol,
Acakki 9:15 abipo gicikke ma tye i kin an kwedwu ki gin makwo ducu ma gitye ki kom; dok pii bene pe dok bidoko aluka ma romo tyeko gin makwo ducu.
Acakki 9:16 Ka danyu tye i pol, ci abineno, ci abipo gicikkena ma bedo matwal i kin Lubaŋa ki gin makwo ducu ma gitye ki kom i wi lobo."
Acakki 9:17 Lubaŋa owaco bot Nua ni, "Man doŋ lanyut me gicikkena ma doŋ amoko i kin an ki gin makwo ducu ma tye i wi lobo."
Acakki 9:18 Awobe pa Nua ma yam gukatti woko ki i yeya-ni gin Cem, Kam ki Yafeci. Kam en aye won Kanaan.
Acakki 9:19 Litino awobe pa Nua adek-ki aye lwak ducu ma i wi lobo gua i komgi.
Acakki 9:20 Nua aye yam obedo lapur mukwoŋo. Ci opito olok i potone,
Acakki 9:21 omato koŋo vinone, ci omer woko, obuto i kemane ma pe oumo kome.
Acakki 9:22 Ci Kam, won Kanaan, ka oneno wonne pe oumo kome, otito ki omegine aryo ma gitye woko-ni.
Acakki 9:23 Ci Cem ki Yafeci gutiŋo boŋo i wi gwokgi gin aryo, ka gucako wot kun gijer ki yo ŋegi, ci guumo ki kom wongi ma onoŋo tye nono, kun wangi neno cen, ci pe guneno kom wongi ma tye nono-ni.
Acakki 9:24 Ka Nua oco ki i waŋ mero koŋo vinone, ci oŋeyo gin ma wode matidine otiyo i kome,
Acakki 9:25 ci owacci, "Gicen Kanaan; en bibedo opii i kin lwak opii pa omege."
Acakki 9:26 Dok owaco bene ni. "Gipwo Rwot Lubaŋa pa Cem; wek Kanaan obed opiine.
Acakki 9:27 Lubaŋa oyab lobo pa Yafeci obed malac, wek en obed i kema pa Cem; ka dok Kanaan obed opiine bene."
Acakki 9:28 Nua ori mwaka miya adek ki pyerabic nia i kare ma pii aluka ocorre i wi lobo
Acakki 9:29 Kare me kwo pa Nua ducu oromo mwaka miya aboŋwen ki pyerabic; ka doŋ oto.
Acakki 10:1 Man aye tekwaro pa litino awobe pa Nua, Cem, Kam ki Yafeci. Gunywalo litino awobe i ŋe kare ma pii aluka ocorre i wi lobo.
Acakki 10:2 Litino awobe pa Yafeci aye Gomer, Magog, Madai, Javan, Tubal, Mecek ki Tirac.
Acakki 10:3 Litino awobe pa Gomer aye Acikenaj, Ripat ki Togarma.
Acakki 10:4 Litino awobe pa Javan aye Elica, Tarcic, Kitim ki Dodanim.
Acakki 10:5 Jo ma i dog nam guket ki i kom jo meno. Magi aye litino awobe pa Yafeci ki lobogi, kun ŋat acel acel loko leb tugi, macalo kakagi ki rokgi tye kwede.
Acakki 10:6 Magi aye litino awobe pa Kam: Kuc, Ejipt, Put ki Kanaan.
Acakki 10:7 Litino awobe pa Kuc aye Seba, Kavila, Cabta, Raama ki Cabteka. Litino awobe pa Raama aye Ceba ki Dedan.
Acakki 10:8 Kuc onywalo mere Nimulodi; en aye dano ma okwoŋo bedo oteka i wi lobo.
Acakki 10:9 En obedo ladwar oken i nyim Rwot; mumiyo giwacci, "Calo Nimulodi ma ladwar oken i nyim Rwot-ti."
Acakki 10:10 Acakki kerre onoŋo Babel, Erek, Akkad ki Kalne; gin ducu gibedo i lobo Cinar.
Acakki 10:11 Nia i lobo meno kerre omedde, ocito oo wa i Aciria, ci ogero iye Nineve,
Acakki 10:12 ki Recen ma i kin Nineve ki Kala; meno aye gaŋ madit.
Acakki 10:13 Ejipt onywalo jo Lud, jo Anam, jo Leab, jo Naptuk,
Acakki 10:14 jo Patruc ki jo Kaptor, ma en aye kaka ma jo Piliciti gua ki i komgi.
Acakki 10:15 Kanaan onywalo Cidon latin kayone, ki Ket,
Acakki 10:16 jo Jebuc, jo Amor, jo Girgac,
Acakki 10:17 jo Kiv, jo Arki, jo Cin,
Acakki 10:18 jo Arvad, jo Jemar ki jo Kamat. Lacen kaka pa jo Kanaan gucako ket woko ata.
Acakki 10:19 Waŋ lobo pa jo Kanaan ocakke ki i Cidon odok kwede i yo tuŋ Gerar, nio kwede wa Gaja; ka odok yo tuŋ Codom ki Gomora ki Adma ki Jeboim, nio kwede wa Laca.
Acakki 10:20 Magi aye litino awobe pa Kam, macalo kakagi, ki lebgi, ki lobogi, ki rokgi tye kwede.
Acakki 10:21 Cem, omin Yafeci maditte, en aye kwaro litino pa Eber ducu, en bene onywalo litino.
Acakki 10:22 Litino awobe pa Cem aye Elam, Acur, Arpakcad, Lud ki Aram.
Acakki 10:23 Litino awobe pa Aram gin aye Uj, Kul, Geter ki Mac.
Acakki 10:24 Arpakcad onywalo Cela, Cela onywalo Eber.
Acakki 10:25 Eber onywalo litino awobe aryo; nyiŋ ŋat acel onoŋo Peleg, pien i kare mere aye gipoko iye lobo, ki nyiŋ ominne onoŋo Yokotan.
Acakki 10:26 Yokotan onywalo Almodad, Celep, Kajarmavet, Jera,
Acakki 10:27 Adoram, Ujal, Dikla
Acakki 10:28 Obal, Abimael, Ceba,
Acakki 10:29 Opir, Kavila ki Jobab; magi gin ducu litino awobe pa Yokotan.
Acakki 10:30 Lobo ma gubedo iye wane ocakke ki i Meca, odok kwede yo tuŋ Cepar nio
kwede wa lobo godi ma tuŋ wokceŋ.
Acakki 10:31 Magi aye litino awobe pa Cem, macalo kakagi, lebgi, lobogi, ki rokgi tye kwede.
Acakki 10:32 Man aye kaka pa litino awobe pa Nua, kit ma tekwarogi tye kwede, i rokgi; rok
ocako ket nia ki i komgi oromo lobo, cakke i ŋe kare ma pii aluka ocorre i wi lobo.
Acakki 11:1 Lobo ducu yam onoŋo tye ki leb acel, ki lok bene onoŋo lam.
Acakki 11:2 Ka dano gucako dak nia ki tuŋ wokceŋ, gunoŋo lobo mubedo bar i lobo Cinar, ci gubedo iye kunnu.
Acakki 11:3 Ka gucako lok kekengi ni, "Wubin, wek watimu matafali, wawaŋgi woko matek." Ci gutiyo ki matafali ma ka got, ki odok macol lamwon kingi.
Acakki 11:4 Dok guwaco ni, "Wubin, wek wageru gaŋwa, ki ot ma wiye ocudo malo ogudo polo, wek wamiyu nyiŋwa oyweki, wek pe waket woko ata i wi lobo ducu."
Acakki 11:5 Ka Rwot olor piny ka neno gaŋ ki ot ma wiye ocudo malo ma litino pa dano gugero,
Acakki 11:6 Rwot owacci, "Nen, guribbe rok acel, ki lebgi bene acel; man aye pud acakki gin ma gibitiyo, dok gin ma gibitamo pi tiyone pe doŋ biloyogi.
Acakki 11:7 Wubin waloru piny, warub legbi woko, wek ŋat acel acel pe oniaŋ leb pa wadi."
Acakki 11:8 Kit meno Rwot okeyogi woko nia ki kunnu, guromo lobo ducu, ci guweko gero gaŋ meno.
Acakki 11:9 Mumiyo nyiŋe gucako ni Babel, pien kenyo aye Rwot orubo iye leb ducu ma i lobo, dok Rwot okeyogi woko nia ki kunnu, guromo lobo ducu.
Acakki 11:10 Man aye likwayo pa Cem. Ka Cem doŋ tye ki mwaka me ditte miya acel, ci onywalo Arpakcad munoŋo doŋ pii aluka okato mwaka aryo.
Acakki 11:11 Cem ori i ŋe nywalo Arpakcad mwaka miya abic, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 11:12 Ka Arpakcad doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyeradek wiye abic, ci onywalo Cela.
Acakki 11:13 Arpakcad ori mwaka miya aŋwen ki adek ma doŋ otyeko nywalo Cela, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 11:14 Ka Cela doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyeradek, ci onywalo Eber.
Acakki 11:15 Cela ori mwaka miya aŋwen ki adek ma doŋ otyeko nywalo Eber, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 11:16 Ka Eber doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyeradek wiye aŋwen, ci onywalo Peleg.
Acakki 11:17 Eber ori mwaka miya aŋwen ki pyeradek ma doŋ otyeko nywalo Peleg, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 11:18 Ka Peleg doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyeradek, ci onywalo Reu.
Acakki 11:19 Peleg ori mwaka miya aryo ki aboŋwen ma doŋ otyeko nywalo Reu, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 11:20 Ka Reu doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyeradek wiye aryo, ci onywalo Cerug.
Acakki 11:21 Reu ori mwaka miya aryo ki abiro ma doŋ otyeko nywalo Cerug, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 11:22 Ka Cerug doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyeradek, ci onywalo Nakor.
Acakki 11:23 Cerug ori mwaka miya aryo ma doŋ otyeko nywalo Nakor, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 11:24 Ka Nakor doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyeraryo wiye aboŋwen, ci onywalo Tera.
Acakki 11:25 Nakor ori mwaka miya acel ki apar wiye aboŋwen ma doŋ otyeko nywalo Tera, dok omedde ki nywalo awobe ki anyira bene.
Acakki 11:26 Ka Tera doŋ otyeko ri mwaka pyerabiro, ci onywalo Abram, Nakor ki Karan.
Acakki 11:27 Man aye likwayo pa Tera. Tera onywalo Abram, Nakor ki Karan; Karan onywalo Lot.
Acakki 11:28 Karan okwoŋo to ki wonne Tera i lobo ma yam ginywale iye, i gaŋ me Ur pa jo Kaldaya.
Acakki 11:29 Ci Abram ki Nakor gunyomo mon; dako pa Abram nyiŋe Carai, dako pa Nakor nyiŋe Mirika, en aye nya pa Karan won Mirika ki Icika.
Acakki 11:30 Onoŋo Carai lalur, pe tye ki latin mo.
Acakki 11:31 Tera otero wode Abram, ki Lot wod pa Karan, ma lakware, ki Carai ci-wode, dako pa Abram, ci gudak woko ki i Ur, gaŋ pa jo Kaldaya, gucito kacel kun gikemo lobo Kanaan; ento ka guo i Karan, koŋ gudikke kenyo.
Acakki 11:32 Nino me kwo pa Tera oromo mwaka miya aryo ki abic; ka Tera oto i Karan.
Acakki 12:1 Rwot owaco bot Abram ni, “A woko ki i lobo tuwu, ki i kakawu, ki i paco pa woru, ci icit i lobo ma abinyutti.
Acakki 12:2 Abimiyi idoko rok madit, abimiyi gum bene, abimiyo nyiŋi bedo dit, pien ibibedo lakelgum.
Acakki 12:3 Abimiyo gum i kom jo ma leggi gum, abiceno ŋat mo ma biceni; dok piri en aye kaka ducu ma wi lobo bilimo iye gumgi.”
Acakki 12:4 Kit meno Abram ocako wot, macalo Rwot ocike; ki Lot bene owoto kacel kwede. Abram onoŋo doŋ tye ki mwaka me ditte pyerabiro wiye abic i kare ma en a kwede ki i Karan.
Acakki 12:5 Abram ocito ki dakone Carai, ki Lot latin pa ominne, ki lwak limgi ducu ma gucoko kacel, ki lwak jo ducu ma gucokke botgi ki i Karan; gutiŋo wot me cito i lobo Kanaan. Ka doŋ gutyeko o i lobo Kanaan,
Acakki 12:6 Abram obaro dye lobo obino i kabedo ma i Cekem, nio wa i te yat kworo me More. I kare meno onoŋo jo Kanaan aye gitye i lobo meno.
Acakki 12:7 Ci Rwot dok onen bot Abram kun wacce ni, “Abimiyo lobo man bot likwayi.” Ocano keno tyer kunnu pi Rwot ma onen bote-ni.
Acakki 12:8 Ka dok odak woko ki kunnu, okobo i te got ma tye yo tuŋ wokceŋ me Betel, oguro iye kemane, kun weko Betel yo tuŋ potoceŋ, ki Ai yo tuŋ wokceŋ; dok ocano keno tyer pi Rwot kunnu, ci olwoŋo iye nyiŋ Rwot.
Acakki 12:9 Abram dok okobo, omedde ki wotte yo tuŋ Negeb . Abram i lobo Ejipt
Acakki 12:10 Kec onoŋo opoto i lobo, omiyo Abram owoto piny i Ejipt, wek koŋ ebed kunnu, pien kec onoŋo doŋ lyet twatwal i lobo.
Acakki 12:11 I kare ma cok donyo i Ejipt, owaco bot dakone Carai ni, “Aŋeyo ni in i dako ma nen mwonya;
Acakki 12:12 ka Luejipt gibineni, ci gibiwacci, ‘Man dakone’; ci gibineka woko, ento gibiweki makwo.
Acakki 12:13 Wac ni, in lamera, ci gibibedo kweda maber piri, miyo abikwo piri.”
Acakki 12:14 Ka Abram otyeko donyo i Ejipt, ci Luejipt guneno dako meno mwonya matek twatwal.
Acakki 12:15 Ka ludito ma i kal pa Parao guneno, ci guboro pire bote, gutero dako wa i ot pa Parao.
Acakki 12:16 Ci omiyo Parao obedo maber ki Abram pi Carai: gikolle lim, romi, ki twoni; twoni kana, lwak opii ki aŋeca-gu, megi kana-gu, ki lwak kinaga-gu.
Acakki 12:17 Ento Rwot ocwalo cog two gemo mogo madoŋo i kom Parao ki jo ma i ode, pi Carai dako pa Abram.
Acakki 12:18 Omiyo Parao olwoŋo Abram bote, ci openye ni, “Itima kuman piŋo? Piŋo nene pe ititta atir ni en dakoni?
Acakki 12:19 Piŋo dok iwaco ni, ‘En lamera,’ omiya akwanyo, odoko dakona? Nen doŋ, dakoni ennu. Kwany icit kwede giri.”
Acakki 12:20 Parao ociko jone pire, ci gulwoke iyo, kacel ki dakone, ki lwak jami ducu ma yam tye bote.
Acakki 13:1 Kit meno Abram odwogo woko ki i Ejipt, en ki dakone, ki lwak jami ducu ma yam tye bote, kacel ki Lot, ci gutiro i Negeb.
Acakki 13:2 I kare meno onoŋo Abram odoko lalonyo dyaŋ mada, ki lim me ryal, ki jabu-gu.
Acakki 13:3 Okobo, omedde ki wotte nia ki i Negeb, odak wa Betel, ka ma yam koŋ okwono guro iye kemane, ma tye i kin Betel ki Ai,
Acakki 13:4 i kabedo ma yam okwoŋo caŋo iye keno tyer; ki kunnu aye dok Abram olwoŋo iye nyiŋ Rwot.
Acakki 13:5 Ki Lot ma yam onywako wot ki Abram, ceŋ tye ki romi ki dyaŋi-gu ki kema bene.
Acakki 13:6 Lobo onoŋo doŋ pe romo ka kwat pi gin aryo ducu; pien onoŋo gin ducu ciŋgi ki lim madwoŋ, ma pe romogi bedo kacel.
Acakki 13:7 Onoŋo mone doŋ tye i kin lukwa lim pa Abram ki lukwa lim pa Lot. I kare meno onoŋo jo Kanaan ki jo Periji aye gibedo i lobo meno.
Acakki 13:8 Abram ocako waco ki Lot ni, “Pe wawek mone obed i kin in ki an, ki i kin lukwa limmi ki lukwa limma, pien wan ot acel.
Acakki 13:9 Lobo man ducu pe ineno i nyimi ene? Ber ipokke giri woko keni ki i koma. Ka ibidok tuŋ acam, ci an abidok gira tuŋ acuc: ce ka in idok tun acuc, ci an abidok gira tuŋ acam.”
Acakki 13:10 Ci Lot ocako tiŋo waŋe malo, ka oneno nota Jordan ducu ma iye ki pii macalo poto pa Rwot, rom ki lobo Ejipt mudok yo tuŋ Joar; man yam otimme i kare ma Rwot peya ojwero Codom ki Gomora.
Acakki 13:11 Pienno Lot oyero gire pire kene lobo ducu ma yam tye i nota Jordan, ci Lot ocako dak yo tuŋ wokceŋ: kit meno gupokke woko kekengi.
Acakki 13:12 Abram obedo mere i lobo Kanaan, kun Lot kono bedo mere i kin gaŋi ma gitye i nota, ocako dak ki kemane nio wa Codom.
Acakki 13:13 Jo ma i Codom onoŋo jo maraco, balgi dwoŋ twatwal i nyim Rwot.
Acakki 13:14 Rwot oloko ki Abram ma doŋ onoŋo gutyeko pokke woko ki Lot ni, “Tiŋ waŋi malo, nen piny nia ki i kabedo ma it ye iye-ni, nen tuŋ acam ki tuŋ acuc, ki tuŋ wokceŋ ki tuŋ potoceŋ;
Acakki 13:15 pien lobo meno ducu ma ineno-ni abimiyone boti ki bot likwayi matwal.
Acakki 13:16 Abimiyo likwayi bedo pol ma rom ki apwa me ŋom; mumiyo ka ŋatti mo twero kwano wel apwa me ŋom, ci likwayi welgi bikwanne.
Acakki 13:17 Doŋ ia malo, iwot i dye lobo-ni, wek inen borre ki lacce, pien abimiyo boti.”
Acakki 13:18 Kit meno Abram okobo kemane, odak, obedo i te kworo me Mamre, ma tye i Kebron; dok ocano keno tyer pi Rwot kunnu.
Acakki 14:1 I kare pa Amrapel kabaka me Cinar, ki Ariok kabaka me Ellacar, ki Kedor-laomer kabaka me Elam, ki Tidal kabaka me Goyim,
Acakki 14:2 luker meno guribbe ka lweny i kom Bera kabaka me Codom, ki Birca kabaka me Gomora, ki Cinab kabaka me Adma, ki Cemeber kabaka me Jeboim, ki kabaka me Bela, en aye Joar.
Acakki 14:3 Mony man ducu guribbe ka lweny i nota me Ciddim, en aye nam me Kado.
Acakki 14:4 Gubedo i te loc pa Kedor-laomer pi mwaka apar wiye aryo, ento gujemo woko i mwaka me apar wiye adekke.
Acakki 14:5 I mwaka me apar wiye aŋwenne, Kedor-laomer ki luker ma yam gitye kwede gubino dok guero lweny, ci guloyo jo Repaim i Aciterot-Kamaim, ki jo Jujim i Kam, ki jo Emim i Cave-Kiriataim,
Acakki 14:6 ki jo Kori i lobo godi megi me Ceir, nio wa i El-paran i waŋ apokki lobo ma tuŋ tim;
Acakki 14:7 ka dok gudwogo cen, gucito wa i En-micipat, en aye Kadec, guloyo lobo ducu pa jo Amalek, ki jo Amor bene ma gibedo i Kajajon-tamar.
Acakki 14:8 Ka dok kabaka me Codom, kabaka me Gomora, kabaka me Adma, kabaka me Jeboim, ki kabaka me Bela, ma co, aye Joar, gucito guero lweny i nota me Ciddim,
Acakki 14:9 i kom Kedor-laomer kabaka me Elam, ki Tidal kabaka me Goyim, ki Amrapel kabaka me Cinar, ki Ariok kabaka me Ellacar, luker aŋwen guribbe ka lweny i kom luker abic.
Acakki 14:10 Nota me Ciddim onoŋo tye iye bur odok macol; ka luker me Codom ki me Gomora guriŋo woko, jo mukene gupoto i bur meno, ki jo mukene mudoŋŋe guriŋo, gularo i got.
Acakki 14:11 Ci merok guyako jami pa jo Codom ki Gomora ducu, ki camgi ducu, gumol, gucito kwede,
Acakki 14:12 guyako bene Lot latin pa omin Abram, ma onoŋo obedo i Codom, ki jamine ducu, guwoto kwede woko.
Acakki 14:13 Ci dano acel mo ma obwot oriŋo, obino otito ki Abram ma Laibru, ma onoŋo bedo i te kworo pa Mamre, ma en Laamor, omin Ecikol ki Aner; gin yam gucikke pi ribbe ki Abram.
Acakki 14:14 Ka Abram owinyo ni watgi mony oyako woko, ci oywayo monnye, ka otelo wi jo mupwonyo lweny ma ginywalogi i pacone, jo ma giromo miya adek ki apar wiye aboro, ci olubo korgi nio wa i Dan.
Acakki 14:15 En opoko i monnye i dyewor; gucako poto i komgi, en ki luticce, ci guryemogi nio wa i Koba, i tuŋ acam me Damaciko.
Acakki 14:16 Ka oyako jami ducu, odwogo kwede, kacel ki watgi Lot, jamine ducu ki mongi ki lwakgi ducu. Melkijedek olamo gum i kom Abram
Acakki 14:17 Ka doŋ odwogo ki ka ma en oloyo iye Kedor-laomer ki Luker ma gitye kwedeni, ci kabaka me Codom ocito ka ŋolo wiye i waŋa yo wa i nota me Cave, ma en aye Nota pa Kabaka.
Acakki 14:18 Melkijedek kabaka me Calem okelo iye mugati ki koŋo vino; en aye onoŋo ajwaka pa Lubaŋa Mamalo Twal.
Acakki 14:19 Olamo gum i kome kun waco ni, “Lubaŋa Mamalo Twal ma laket polo ki lobo omi gum i kom Abram;
Acakki 14:20 gipwo Lubaŋa Mamalo Twal ma omiyo lumerokki i ciŋi!” Ci Abram omiye dul acel me apar me jami ducu ma en oyako.
Acakki 14:21 Kabaka me Codom dok owaco ki Abram ni, “Miya mera dano aye ater, ento in iter giri jami ducu obed meri.”
Acakki 14:22 Ento Abram odok iye bot kabaka me Codom ni, “Doŋ atyeko kwoŋo kwoŋ woko bot Rwot Lubaŋa Mamalo Twal, ma laket polo ki lobo-ni,
Acakki 14:23 ni, pe abigamo gin mo ki boti kadi latin uci, nyo del war mo, nyo gin mo i kin jami ma meri-ni, wek pe ibed ka wacci, ‘Amiyo Abram olony.’
Acakki 14:24 Pe dok abigamo gin mo, doŋ agik ki gin ma awobe gucamo-ni, ki dul lim ma apoko ki jo ma gucito kweda-ni; wek doŋ Aner, ki Ecikol Mamre guter jamigi gigi.”
Acakki 16:1 Carai dako pa Abram pe omedo ki nywalle latin mo, dok en onoŋo tye ki aŋecane ma anyira Ejipt ma nyiŋe Agar.
Acakki 16:2 Carai owaco ki Abram ni, “Nen, macalo Rwot ogeŋa nywalo latin mo-ni, cit idony i wi aŋecana, wek gwok nyo abinoŋo iye latin mo ma en binywalo.” Ci Abram owinyo dog Carai.
Acakki 16:3 Kit meno, i kare ma Abram otyeko bedo i lobo Kanaan mwaka apar, Carai dako pa Abram otero Agar anyira Ejipt ma aŋecane, omiye bot cware Abram wek obed dakone.
Acakki 16:4 Ocako bedo ki Agar, ci Agar ogamo ic. Ka Agar oneno ni doŋ egamo ic, ocako gayo Carai ki waŋ me cac.
Acakki 16:5 Carai owaco ki Abram ni, “Kipwola mupoto i koma odok meri! Amiyo aŋecana i kori; ka en oneno ni doŋ egamo ic, ci ocako gayo an ki waŋ me cac. Myero Rwot doŋ oŋol kop mapol i kin in ki an!”
Acakki 16:6 Ento Abram ogamo dog Carai ni, “Nen, aŋecani tye Dok i tweroni giri, in itim giri kit ma imito i kome.” Omiyo Carai ocako timme aromaroma, nio ka olwi, oriŋo woko ki bote.
Acakki 16:7 Lamalaika pa Rwot onoŋe i waŋ it mo ma i dye tim; it meno tye i yo ma cito Cur.
Acakki 16:8 Obino openye ni, “Agar, aŋeca pa Carai, in mono ia ki kwene kaa, dok icito wa kwene kaa?” En ogamo ni, “An alwi ariŋo Carai, min ot ma abedo i ode.”
Acakki 16:9 Lamalaika ogamo ni, “Dok cen bot min ot meno, ci iwore.”
Acakki 16:10 Lamalaika pa Rwot dok omedo lok ni, “An abimiyo likwayi nya mapol twatwal, ma ŋatti mo pe romo kwano welgi pi polgi.”
Acakki 16:11 Dok lamalaika pa Rwot omedde ka wacce ni, “Nen, igamo ic, ibinywalo latin laco, dok ibicako nyiŋe Icmael; pien Rwot obedo ka neno aromani.
Acakki 16:12 En bibedo dano ma cal ki kana me tim, en bitugge i kom dano ducu, ki dano ducu bene bitugge i kome; en bibedo i kabedone pat kun pyem ki utmegine ducu.”
Acakki 16:13 Ci Agar ocako nyiŋ Rwot ma oloko kwede ni, “In Lubaŋa ma neno.” Onoŋo en owacci, “An atyeko neno Lubaŋa ada, aneno en ci pud atye makwo gira?”
Acakki 16:14 Mumiyo nyiŋ waŋ it meno gicako ni, Beer-lakai-roi; ma tye i kin Kadec ki Bered.
Acakki 16:15 Agar onywalo ki Abram latin laco; Abram ocako nyiŋ latinne ma Agar onywalo ni Icmael.
Acakki 16:16 Abram onoŋo tye ki mwaka me ditte pyeraboro wiye abicel i kare ma Agar onywalo Icmael.
Acakki 17:1 Ka Abram onoŋo tye ki mwaka me ditte pyeraboŋwen wiye aboŋwen ci Rwot onen bot Abram kun wacce ni, “An Lubaŋa Matwero-ducu, bed i nyima laboŋo bal mo,
Acakki 17:2 ci abiketo gicikkena i kin an ki in, dok abimiyi inya mapol twatwal.”
Acakki 17:3 Abram oryebbe piny i nyime; Lubaŋa owacce ni,
Acakki 17:4 “Nen, gicikkena amini eno, in ibibedo kwaro rok mapol.
Acakki 17:5 Nia tin nyiŋi pe dok bibedo Abram , ento nyiŋi bibedo Abraim , pien aketo in wek ibed kwaro rok mapol.
Acakki 17:6 Abimiyi inya twatwal; abimiyi idoko rok mapol, ki luker bene gibia ki i komi.
Acakki 17:7 Dok abimoko gicikkena i kin an ki in ki likwayi ma bilubi, ki i yalwakgi ducu, me bedo gicikke ma bedo matwal, wek abed Lubaŋani, ki Lubaŋa pa likwayi ma bilubi bene.
Acakki 17:8 Dok abimiyo boti ki bot likwayi ma bilubi lobo ma ibedo iye-ni macalo welo, en aye lobo ducu me Kanaan, wek obed mewu matwal; dok an aye abibedo Lubaŋagi.”
Acakki 17:9 Ka Lubaŋa dok owaco bot Abraim ni, “Ki tuŋ boti, in ibigwoko gicikkena, in ki likwayi ducu ma bilubi, ki yalwakgi ducu.
Acakki 17:10 Man aye gicikkena, ma wubi gwoko, i kin an ki in ki likwayi ma bilubi: Gibiliro litino awobe ducu ma i kinwu.
Acakki 17:11 Wubiliro del kom nyimwu me co woko, wek obed gin ma nyuto gicikkena i kin an ki wun.
Acakki 17:12 Latin laco ma romo nino aboro gibiliro del kom nyime; co ducu gibilirogi i yalwak ki yalwakgi ducu, nia i kom litino ma ginywalogi i pacowu, nio kom litino ma wuwilo awila ki limwu ki bot lurok bene, ma pe wunywalogi anywala.
Acakki 17:13 Gin ducu ma ginywalogi i pacowu, ki ma giwilogi awila ki limwu, ducu gibilirogi, wek gicikkena obed i del kom nyimwu, wek obed gicikke ma bedo matwal.
Acakki 17:14 Ka laco mo onen ma pe giliro del kom nyime me co, waŋe birwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi, pien oturo gicikkena.”
Acakki 17:15 Ka Lubaŋa dok owaco ki Abraim ni, “Lok ma dok tuŋ bot Carai, dakoni, pe dok gibilwoŋo nyiŋe ni Carai, ento nyiŋe doŋ bibedo Cara .
Acakki 17:16 Abimiye gum, dok makato ducu abimiyo en nywalli latin laco; abimiye gum, en bibedo min rok mapol, ki luker pa rok mapol gibia ki i kome.”
Acakki 17:17 Ci Abraim opoto piny aryeba ic ki nyero, kun tamo gire kekene ni, “Dano ma ditte doŋ romo mwaka miya kulu aye dok binywalo latin? Ki Cara bene ma ditte doŋ romo mwaka pyeraboŋwen ku lu dok binywalo latin?”
Acakki 17:18 Abraim ocako waco bot Lubaŋa ni, “Myero Icmael aye doŋ obed makwo i nyimi!”
Acakki 17:19 Lubaŋa owacce ni, “Pe gire, ento dakoni Cara aye binywalli latin laco, dok ibicako nyiŋe Icaka, dok abimoko gicikkena kwede wek obed gicikke ma bedo matwal bot Likwaye ducu ma bilube.
Acakki 17:20 Ki ma dok tuŋ bot Icmael bene, atyeko winyo in, ci nen, abimiye gum, abimiyo en binywal dok nya mapol twatwal; en bibedo kwaro luker apar wiye aryo, abimiye bedo rok madit.
Acakki 17:21 Ento abimoko gicikkena ki Icaka, latin ma Cara aye binywalli i kare macalo man i mwaka ma bino.”
Acakki 17:22 Ka Lubaŋa doŋ otyeko lok ki Abraim, ci oa woko ki bote, odok malo.
Acakki 17:23 Abraim otero Icmael ki lwak opii ducu ma ginywalogi i ode, nyo ma giwilogi ki lim, co ducu ma gitye i kin litino ma i ot pa Abraim, ci oliro del kom nyimgi me co woko i nino meno kikome, kit macalo Lubaŋa ocike kwede.
Acakki 17:24 Ka Abraim onoŋo tye ki mwaka me ditte pyeraboŋwen wiye aboŋwen en aye gicako Liro iye del kom nyime.
Acakki 17:25 Ki wode Icmael onoŋo doŋ tye ki mwaka me ditte apar wiye adek ka gicako Liro del kom nyime.
Acakki 17:26 I nino meno kikome en aye Abraim ki wode Icmael giliro iye del kom nyimgi,
Acakki 17:27 kacel ki jo ducu ma gitye i ode, litino ma ginywalo i ode, ki jo ma giwilogi ki lim ki bot lurok; gin bene gilirogi kacel kwede.
Acakki 18:1 Rwot dok onen bot Abraim i te kworo ma tye i Mamre, ma onoŋo obedo i dog kemane i kare ma piny Lyet.
Acakki 18:2 Otiŋo waŋe malo, ci oneno jo adek gucuŋ i nyime. Ka onenogi, oriŋo nia ki i dog kema, ocito ka ŋolo wigi, ci oryebbe piny i ŋom,
Acakki 18:3 kun wacci, “Laditta, ka gum okaya i nyimi, pe ikat an laticci akata.
Acakki 18:4 Wek koŋ gikel pii mo matitidi, wek wulwok ki tyenwu, ka doŋ wuywe i te yat-ti,
Acakki 18:5 dok acito ka omo kwon mo manok wek wubwol ki dogwu, ka doŋ wucak kato giwu, macalo doŋ wubino bota-ni.” Ci gin gugamo ni, “Citim kit ma iwaco-ni.”
Acakki 18:6 Abraim orune ocito bot Cara i kema, owacce ni, “Job moko mapwotte ma romo adita adek, inywan, ited capat matitino.”
Acakki 18:7 Abraim oriŋo i idwol, okwanyo wod twon ma riŋone pud yom mamit, omiyo bot awobine, ci oyubo oyotoyot.
Acakki 18:8 Ka okelo cak lukulu ki cak malibo, ki dek riŋo ma gitedo, oketo i nyimgi; en ocuŋ i ŋetgi ka konyogi, i te yat, kun gicamo.
Acakki 18:9 Gupenye ni, “Dakoni Cara kono tye kwene?” En ogamo ni, “En tye i kema.”
Acakki 18:10 Owacci, “Abidwogo boti i kare me cwir, ma noŋo dakoni Cara doŋ tye ki wode.” Cara onoŋo tye ki i ŋeye i dog kema, winyo lokgi.
Acakki 18:11 I kare meno onoŋo Abraim ki Cara mwaka me ditogi doŋ dwoŋ: dok Cara onoŋo doŋ pe neno dwe macalo mon wadigi.
Acakki 18:12 Mumiyo Cara onyerre kekene, kun wacci, “Ma doŋ ati, aloc woko, ki cwara bene doŋ oti, oloc woko, dok wabinoŋo yomcwiny odye?”
Acakki 18:13 Rwot owaco bot Abraim ni, “Cara onyero mono piŋo, ma wacci, ‘An mono dok abinywalo latin, ma kombeddi doŋ ati woko-ni?’
Acakki 18:14 Tye gin mo matek ma loyo Rwot? Ka kare oromo ci abidwogo dok kany, i dye cwir, anoŋo Cara doŋ tye ki wode.”
Acakki 18:15 Ento Cara okwero woko kun waco ni, “An pe anyero gira.” Ogamo doge ni, “Pe, ento me nyero aye inyero.” Abraim olego pi Codom
Acakki 18:16 Ka jo meno gucako a woko ki kunnu, ci guneno yo tuŋ Codom; ci Abraim olwokogi iyo.
Acakki 18:17 Rwot owacci, “Myero akan gin ma acito ka tiyone woko bot Abraim kulu,
Acakki 18:18 macalo Abraim obedoko rok madit ki matek, ma rok ducu ma i wi lobo gibilimo gum ki i kome?
Acakki 18:19 Pe; an doŋ atyeko yero en, wek ocik litinone ki jo ma i ode ma gibilube gumok ka lubo korayo pa Rwot ma gitiyo gin ma tye atir kun giŋolo bene kop atir; wek lacen Rwot omi ki Abraim gin ma yam otyeko cikke kwede-ni.”
Acakki 18:20 Ka doŋ Rwot owacce ni, “Pien koko i kom Codom ki Gomora doŋ okato kare, ki balgi doŋ dwoŋ twatwal,
Acakki 18:21 abicito botgi wek acinen ka ada gitye ka tiyo kit ma koko i komgi owinnye kwede bota-ni; ka pe, ci abiŋeyo.”
Acakki 18:22 Kit meno gulokke, gucako wot me kemo i Codom; ento Abraim pud ocuŋ i nyim Rwot aye.
Acakki 18:23 Lacen Abraim onyiko bote cok, owacci, “In ada ibityeko jo ma kitgi atir kacel ki jo maraco?
Acakki 18:24 Ka gwok nyo jo ma kitgi atir binoŋŋe pyerabic i gaŋ meno, ci ibityeko kabedo meno woko, pe ibijalo gaŋ meno pi jo pyerabic ma kitgi atir ma gitye iye-ni?
Acakki 18:25 Pe kumene! In pe myero inek jo ma kitgi atir kacel ki jo maraco, kun imiyo jo ma kitgi atir bene bedo rom ki jo maraco. Laŋolkop me lobo ducu pe bitimo gin ma nen, atir, bo?”
Acakki 18:26 Rwot ogamo ni, “Ka anoŋo i Codom jo ma kitgi atir pyerabic ma tye i gaŋ meno, abijalo kabedo meno ducu pigi.”
Acakki 18:27 Abraim ogamo dok ni, “Nen, an doŋ adyerre me lok kwedi, in Rwot, an mera apwa ki buru mamwa.
Acakki 18:28 Gwok nyo ka ce birem jo abic me romo jo pyerabic? Ci ibityeko gaŋ meno ducu woko pi jo abic murem-mi?” Ogamo ni, “An pe abityekone ka ce anoŋo kunnu jo pyeraŋwen wiye abic.”
Acakki 18:29 Dok onwoyo aye, owacci, “Ce ka ibinoŋo kunnu jo pyeraŋwen keken kono?” Ogamo ni, “Pi jo pyeraŋwen-ni pe abitimo iye gin mo.”
Acakki 18:30 Dok owacci, “Pe kiniga omaki, in Rwot, an abilok doki. Ka ce binoŋŋe kunnu jo pyeradek kono?” En ogamo ni, “Pe abitimo ce abinoŋo kunnu jo pyeradek.”
Acakki 18:31 En dok owacci, “Nen, an doŋ adyerre me lok kwedi, in Rwot. Gwok nyo jo pyeraryo binoŋŋe kunnu kono?” Ogamo ni, “Pi jo pyeraryo-nu pe abityeko gaŋ.”
Acakki 18:32 Dok onwoyo aye ni, “Pe kiniga omaki, in Rwot, an abilok doki tyen acel keken. Gwok ka ibinoŋo kunnu jo apar keken kono?” Ogamo ni; “Pi jo apar-ri pe abitye kone.”
Acakki 18:33 Ci doŋ Rwot ocako cito, ka doŋ otyeko lok ki Abraim; ci Abraim odok gire i kabedone.
Acakki 19:1 Lumalaika aryo gubino i Codom otyeno; gunoŋo Lot obedo piny i dog gaŋ me Codom. Ka Lot onenogi, ci oa malo, ocito ka jologi, oryebbe, okulo waŋe piny i ŋom,
Acakki 19:2 kun wacci, “Luditona, alegowu, wulokke, wudwog kany, wudony i oda an laticwu, wubed iye nino acel, wulwok iye tyenwu, ci doŋ wubia giwu odiko con, wucito i yo wotwu.” Gugamo ni, “Pe; piny biru ki wan i dye gaŋ, kany.”
Acakki 19:3 En odiyogi ki tek mada, ci gulokke, gudonyo i ode; otedogi karama, omyenogi kwon ma pe girubo iye tobi, ka gucamo.
Acakki 19:4 Ento ma pud peya gubuto piny, lwak co ma i gaŋ, jo me Codom, awobe wa ki ludito bene, guteŋŋe woko ducu, gubino, gurumo ot woko.
Acakki 19:5 Gulwoŋo Lot, gupenye ni, “Jo ma gubino boti otyeno-ni gitye kwene? Kelgi woko botwa kany, wekwaŋene kwedgi.”
Acakki 19:6 Lot okato, ocito botgi i doggola, ci oloro doggola woko cut ki i ŋeye,
Acakki 19:7 kun waco ni, “Alegowu, utmega, pe wutim tim aranyi.
Acakki 19:8 Wunen, an atye kany ki anyirana aryo ma pud peya guŋene ki co. Wek gin aye akelgi botwu, wutimgi giwu kit ma wumito; ento pe wutim gin mo i kom jo man, pien doŋ gudonyo i oda.”
Acakki 19:9 Ento guwacci, “Nyik cen!” Ka doŋ guwacci “Nye man obino kany macalo labedo, dok mito doko laŋolkop ce? Wan koni doŋ watimi marac makato gin.” Ka gucako dille matek i kom Lot, kun ginyiko pi turo kika.
Acakki 19:10 Ento lumalaika meno gurwako ciŋgi, ci guywayo Lot gukelo i ot botgi, ci guloro doggola woko.
Acakki 19:11 Gucoro waŋ dano ma gudille ka i doggola-ni, ludito ki awobe bene, wangi ocor woko, gubedo ka paŋŋe ka yenyo doggola, ci guol woko ata.
Acakki 19:12 Jo meno gucako waco ki Lot ni, “In dok it ye ki jo mukene ma watwu kany bene? Macalo cog anyirani, ki litino awobe ki anyiragi, nyo ki ŋatti mo ma tye i gaŋ kany. Wua kwedgi woko ki i kabedo man;
Acakki 19:13 pien wayubbe me tyeko gaŋ man woko. Koko ma i kom jo ma gitye iye odoko dit i nyim Rwot, Rwot ocwalowa ni doŋ wabin, watyek woko.”
Acakki 19:14 Mumiyo Lot okato ocito, olwoŋo cog anyirane, ma onoŋo nene gimito nyomo anyirane-ni, kun wacci, “Wua woko ki i kabedo man, pien Rwot obetyeko gaŋ man woko.” Ento ki bot cog anyirane nen calo lok oree.
Acakki 19:15 Ka piny doŋ oru, Lumalaika guruyo Lot, kun giwacci, “A woko, icit ki dakoni ki anyirani aryo ma gitye kanynyi, wek pe ginekgi i can ma gibemiyo i kom gaŋ man.”
Acakki 19:16 Ento en obedo ka galle, mumiyo jo meno gumako ciŋgi, gupeyogi woko, en ki dakone ki anyirane aryo; Rwot obedo ki kica i komgi, gikelogi wa i ŋe gaŋ woko.
Acakki 19:17 Ka doŋ gukelogi woko, ci gucikogi ni, “Wuriŋ wular kwowu; pe wulokke wunen ŋewu, pe wugik i yo ka mo i nota, wuriŋ wular godi, wek pe wuto.”
Acakki 19:18 Lot owaco ki gin ni, “Aa, luditona;
Acakki 19:19 nen, an doŋ gum okaya ki botwu, dok wunyuto i koma kica madwoŋ pi Laro kwona; ento pe atwero riŋo nio wa i godi, miyo gin marac dok poto i koma, ci neka woko.
Acakki 19:20 Nen, gaŋ macokke loka ca, ma aromo riŋo alaro iye, dok gaŋŋe tidi mo. Wek ariŋ alar kunnu; pe gaŋŋe nen tidi twatwal? Wek alar kwona do!”
Acakki 19:21 Owacce ni, “Nen, gum meno dok amiyi bene aye; pe doŋ abibalo gaŋ ma iloko pire-ni.
Acakki 19:22 Doŋ irune oyoto, ilar kunnu; peya atwero timo gin mo nio ka io wa kunnu.” Mumiyo nyiŋ gaŋ meno gucako ni Joar.
Acakki 19:23 Ceŋ otuc ma onoŋo Lot donyo i Joar.
Acakki 19:24 Ci Rwot ocwalo gweŋ calfa ma mac oliyo woko, ocwer piny nia ki i polo, ocorre i kom Codom ki Gomora,
Acakki 19:25 obalo gaŋ meno woko, ki notane ducu, ki lwak jo ducu ma gibedo i gaŋi meno, ki gin ducu ma gidoŋo i ŋom.
Acakki 19:26 Ento dako pa Lot mudoŋ cen aŋec-ci, olokke oneno ŋeye, ci olokke odoko wir kado cut.
Acakki 19:27 Abraim oa odiko con, ci ocito i kabedo ma yam koŋ ocuŋ iye i nyim Rwot-ti.
Acakki 19:28 Ci obolo waŋe oneno yo tuŋ Codom ki Gomora, ki tuŋ lobo ducu ma i nota-nu, ci oneno yito ma duny i lobo-nu, macalo ruk mac mukur.
Acakki 19:29 Kit meno Rwot otyeko gaŋi ducu ma i nota i nino meno, ka Lubaŋa opo pi Abraim, omiyo okwanyo Lot woko, wek can pe opot i kome, i kare ma obalo gaŋ ma yam Lot obedo iye woko. Kwaro pa jo Moab ki jo Ammon
Acakki 19:30 Lot oa woko ki i Joar, ocito obedo i godi, kacel ki anyirane aryo-nu, pien onoŋo lworo bedo i Joar; odonyo obedo i boro, kacel ki anyirane aryo-nu.
Acakki 19:31 Nyare me kayone ocako waco bot laminne matidi ni, “Wonwa doŋ oteggi, pe tye laco mo i wi lobo ma bibino botwa ka bedo kwedwa i kit pa dano ma wi lobo-ni.
Acakki 19:32 Bin, wek wami wonwa koŋo vino, omati, ci wabibuto kwede, wek wanoŋ nyodo, wonwa aye onywal kwedwa.”
Acakki 19:33 Ka gumiyo wongi omato koŋo vino i dyewor meno cut, latin kayone ocito, obuto ki wonne, ma kun pe ŋeyo ka nyare obuto kwede, ki kare ma nyare oa kwede malo.
Acakki 19:34 Orwone latin kayone dok owaco bot matidine ni, “Nen, tin dyewor doŋ atyeko buto ki wora; wek dok wamiye omat koŋo vino tin dyewor, wek in dok icit ibut kwede, wek wanoŋ nyodo, wonwa aye onywal kwedwa.”
Acakki 19:35 Dok gumiyo wongi koŋo vino omato i dyewor meno bene; nyare matidi-ni dok oa, ocito obuto kwede; en pe oŋeyo ka nyare obuto kwede, ki kare ma nyare oa kwede malo.
Acakki 19:36 Kit meno anyira pa Lot aryonu ducu gunywal ki wongi.
Acakki 19:37 Kayone onywalo latin laco, ocako nyiŋe Moab; en aye odoko kwaro jo Moab nio wa kombeddi.
Acakki 19:38 Nyare matidine bene dok onywalo latin laco, ci ocako nyiŋe Ben-ammi; en aye odoko kwaro jo Ammon wa kombeddi.
Acakki 20:1 Abraim ocako wot me cito i lobo me Negeb ma tye i kin Kadec ki Cur, obedo i Gerar, ka ma otiro iye macalo labedo.
Acakki 20:2 Abraim ocako lok i kom dakone Cara ni, “En lamera.” Ci Abimelek kabaka me Gerar ocwalo jone guomo Cara.
Acakki 20:3 Ento Lubaŋa obino bote i waŋ lek dyewor, lok kom Cara, dako pa Abraim kun wacce ni, “Nen, in i dano ma lato, pien dako ma in iomo-ni dako ma cware tye.”
Acakki 20:4 Abimelek onoŋo peya obedo kwede; ci en ogamo ni, “Rwot, in mono ibineko rok mo ma pe obalo?
Acakki 20:5 Pe en aye gire otitta kun wacca ni, ‘Dako-ni lamera?’ Dako kikome bene owaco ni, ‘En omera.’ Atimo man ma cwinya leŋ, ki ciŋa bene pe obalo gin mo.”
Acakki 20:6 Lubaŋa dok owacce i waŋ lek ni, “Iyo, aŋeyo ni itimo kumeno ma cwinyi leŋ, ci onoŋo an aye abedo ka geni, oweko pe itimo bal mo i nyima; mumiyo pe aye in igudo kome.
Acakki 20:7 Doŋ idwok dako-ni bot cware gire; pien en lanebi, en bilego piri, ci ibikwo. Ento ka ikwero dwoko dako-nu bot cware, ber iŋe ni ibito woko ada, in ki jo ma i paconi ducu.”
Acakki 20:8 Abimelek oa malo odiko con, olwoŋo luticce ducu, otito botgi lok meno ducu, ci gubedo ki lworo madwoŋ.
Acakki 20:9 Ka Abimelek olwoŋo Abraim bote, owacce ni, “Itimowa kuman piŋo? Aballi gin aŋo, mumiyo in ikelo bal madit i koma ki i kom kerra? In itimo gin ma pe myero atiya i kom dano.”
Acakki 20:10 Ka dok Abimelek owaco bot Abraim ni, “Onoŋo mono itamo niŋo, mumiyo itimo kit man?”
Acakki 20:11 Abraim ogamo ni, “Lok mumiyo atiyo, pien onoŋo atamo ni, Lubaŋa pe gilworo i kabedo man, gibineka woko pi dakona.
Acakki 20:12 Ada mere lamera kikome, nya pa wora, ento pe latin pa maa kikome, ci odoko dakona.
Acakki 20:13 I kare ma Lubaŋa okwanya okwanya woko ki i paco pa wora, ma abedo ka wirre, acako wacce ni, ‘Pi kicani myero itima kit man: i kabedo ducu ma wabio iye, ibinyuta ni, Man omera.’ ”
Acakki 20:14 Ci Abimelek okelo romi ki twoni ki lwak opii ki lwak aŋeca, omiyogi bot Abraim, ci odwoko dakone Cara bote.
Acakki 20:15 Abimelek owacce ni, “Nen, lobona tye i nyimi en; bed ka ma imito.”
Acakki 20:16 Ki tuŋ bot Cara owacci, “Nen, atyeko miyo bot cwari cekel me ryal ma romo alip acel, pi waro kop woko ki i komi i waŋ dano ducu ma ibedo kwedgi, wek ibed laboŋo bal mo i komi.”
Acakki 20:17 Ka Abraim olego Lubaŋa, ci Lubaŋa ocaŋo Abimelek ki dakone bene, ki lwak aŋecane, ci gucako nywalo litino;
Acakki 20:18 pien onoŋo Rwot ogeŋo nyodo woko i ot pa Abimelek pi lok kom Cara, dako pa Abraim.
Acakki 21:1 Rwot dok olimo Cara kit ma con owaco, ci otime kit ma yam ociko kwede.
Acakki 21:2 Cara ogamo ic, ci onywalo latin laco ki Abraim, ma kun en doŋ oti woko, i kare ma yam Lubaŋa otitte pire-ni.
Acakki 21:3 Abraim ocako nyiŋ latin ma ginywalle, ma Cara aye onywalo-ni, ni Icaka.
Acakki 21:4 Abraim oliro wode Icaka ka doŋ otyeko nino aboro me ditte, kit ma yam Lubaŋa ocike kwede.
Acakki 21:5 Abraim onoŋo doŋ mwaka me ditte romo miya acel, ka doŋ wode Icaka ginywalo.
Acakki 21:6 Cara owacci, “Lubaŋa doŋ omiya anyero; wa ŋat ma biwinyo bene binyera.”
Acakki 21:7 Ci owacci, “Aŋa ma kono ceŋ owaco ki Abraim ni waŋ mo Cara bidoto latin? Nen ka doŋ anywalle awobi ma doŋ en oti, oloc woko.” Giryemo Agar ki Icmael woko
Acakki 21:8 Latin odoŋo, ci gijuke dot woko; Abraim otedo karama madit i nino ma gijuko iye Icaka dot-ti.
Acakki 21:9 Ento ka Cara oneno wod pa Agar ma anyira Ejipt, ma yam onywal ki Abraim, ka tuko ki latinne Icaka,
Acakki 21:10 en owaco bot Abraim ni, “Ryem aŋeca man ki wode, gucit woko, pien wod pa aneca-ni pe bibedo laleyo kacel ki woda Icaka.”
Acakki 21:11 Lok meno cwiny Abraim ocwer iye matek, en pi wode.
Acakki 21:12 Ento Lubaŋa owaco ki Abraim ni, “Pe cwinyi ocwer pi latin ki pi aŋecani; gin ducu ma Cara owacci, tim kit ma en otitti, pien litino pa Icaka aye gibilwoŋogi ni likwayu.
Acakki 21:13 Dok abimiyo wod pa aŋeca bene doko rok, pien en latinni.”
Acakki 21:14 Abraim opuk odiko con, okwanyo kwon ki opiro pii, omiyo Agar, olwoke otere i yo, ci oŋabo jami ki latinne i wi gwoke, ocwale kwede woko. Dako meno ocito gire, obedo ka lak ata i tim me Beer-ceba.
Acakki 21:15 Ka pii ma i opiro otum woko, ci opyelo latinne piny i te yat buŋa mo.
Acakki 21:16 Ka oweko latinne, ocito cen ka ma borre rom ki ka ma ka gibayo atero gik iye; pien owacci, “Pe myero anen to pa latinna.” En obedo i anyim kuca, ci latin odaŋŋe ki koko.
Acakki 21:17 Lubaŋa owinyo koko pa latin, lamalaika pa Rwot ocako lwoŋo Agar ki i polo, kun wacce ni, “Man lok aŋo Agar? Pe doŋ i lwor, pien Lubaŋa doŋ otyeko winyo dwan koko pa latin ki ka ma ipyele iye-ni.
Acakki 21:18 Doŋ ia malo, itiŋ latin, ci ikwake matek, pien abimiyo en doko rok madit.”
Acakki 21:19 Ka Lubaŋa oyabo waŋe, ocako neno waŋ pii; ci ocito otwomo, opiko i opirone poŋ, ka omiyo wode omato.
Acakki 21:20 Lubaŋa obedo ki latin meno; odoŋo, obedo i tim, odoko ladwar matek ki atero.
Acakki 21:21 Obedo i tim Paran; minne onyomme nya jo Ejipt. Abraim ki Abimelek gucikke
Acakki 21:22 I kare meno Abimelek ki ladit wi monnye Pikol guwaco bot Abraim ni, “Lubaŋa tye kwedi i gin ducu ma itiyo;
Acakki 21:23 kombeddi doŋ ikwoŋ kwoŋ kweda i nyiŋ Lubaŋa ni, pe ibiumo waŋa, kadi wa litinona ki likwaya bene; macalo an bene atimi ber-ri, in bene ibitima ber, ki lobona ma koni in labedo iye-ni.”
Acakki 21:24 Abraim ogamo ni, “Abikwoŋo.”
Acakki 21:25 Abraim ocako kok bot Abimelek pi waŋ pii mo ma onoŋo luticce gucerre woko kome.
Acakki 21:26 Abimelek ogamo ni, “An pe amedo ki ŋeyo ŋatti mo mutimo lakit lok-ku; in bene pe imedo ki titta lokke. Pe amedo ki winyo lokke nio wa tin!”
Acakki 21:27 Lacen Abraim okwanyo romi ki twoni, omiyogi bot Abimelek, ci gin jo aryo guketo gicikke i kingi.
Acakki 21:28 Abraim oyero bwoŋi romi abiro, oketogi pat.
Acakki 21:29 Abimelek owaco ki Abraim ni, “Bwoŋi romi abiro ma iketo pat-ti kono piŋo?”
Acakki 21:30 Ogamo ni, “Bwoŋi romi magi abiro ma ibigamogi ki i ciŋa-ni, ibiketogi pi bedo cadenna ma nyuto ni, an aye yam akwinyo waŋ pii man.”
Acakki 21:31 Mumiyo kabedo meno gilwoŋo ni Beer-ceba, pien onoŋo gin aryo ducu gukwoŋŋe iye ki kwoŋ.
Acakki 21:32 Kit meno guketo gicikke i Beer-ceba. Ka doŋ Abimelek ki Pikol ladit lawi monnye gua, gudok i lobo pa jo Piliciti.
Acakki 21:33 Abraim opito yat anaŋa i Beer-ceba, ci olwoŋo iye nyiŋ Rwot, Lubaŋa Mabedo Nakanaka.
Acakki 21:34 Abraim ori i lobo pa jo Piliciti kare malac.
Acakki 22:1 I ŋe lok meno ducu, Lubaŋa otemo Abraim kun wacce ni, “Abraim!” En ogamo ni, “Ana ene.”
Acakki 22:2 Owacce ni, “Kwany wodi Icaka, iter, en wodi acel keken, ma imaro-ni, wot kwede i lobo Moria, wek icit ityere kunnu, obed gitum awaŋa i kom got mo ma abititti ki kunnu.”
Acakki 22:3 Kit meno Abraim opuk odiko con, otweyo kom me bedo i wi kanane, okwanyo awobene aryo, ocito kwedgi, kacel ki wode Icaka; otoŋo yen me waŋo gitum, oa, okemo i kabedo ma Rwot otitte-ni.
Acakki 22:4 I ninome adekke, Abraim otiŋo waŋe, ci oneno kabedo meno ka maborbor.
Acakki 22:5 Ka Abraim owaco bot awobe aryo ma tiyo bote-ni ni, “Wun wubed koŋ kany kacel ki kana; an ki latin-ni wabicito anyim loka ca ka woro Lubaŋa, ka dok wabidwogo botwu.”
Acakki 22:6 Abraim otiŋo yen me lawaŋ gitum, ocibo i wi wode Icaka; en omako mac ki pala i ciŋe, ka gucako wot kacel.
Acakki 22:7 Icaka owaco bot wonne Abraim ni, “Wora!” En ogamo ni, “Aŋa ene, woda.” Ci owacce ni, “Nen ba, watye ki mac ki yen, ento romo me gitum tye kwene?”
Acakki 22:8 Abraim ogamo, owacce ni, “Lubaŋa aye bimiyo romo me gitumme, latinna.” Kit meno, gumedde gigi kacel ki wotgi.
Acakki 22:9 Ka guo i kabedo ma Lubaŋa yam otitte, ci Abraim ocano keno tyer, ka ocano yen i wiye, otweyo wode Icaka, ci opyelo i wi keno, obuto i wi yen.
Acakki 22:10 Abraim otiŋo ciŋe, okwanyo pala me neko wode.
Acakki 22:11 Lamalaika pa Rwot olwoŋe ki i polo, kun wacce ni, “Abraim! Abraim!” En ogamo ni, “An atye ene.”
Acakki 22:12 Owacce ni, “Pe iket ciŋi i kom latin-nu, pe itim gin mo i kome bene; doŋ tin atyeko niaŋ atir ni ilworo Lubaŋa, pien pe itwona wodi, wodi acel keken, nen imiya.”
Acakki 22:13 Abraim otiŋo waŋe malo, ci oneno nyok romo tye i ŋeye ma tuŋe omoko i agaba; Abraim ocito okelo nyok romo-nu, ci otyero me bedo gitum awaŋa ma ka wode.
Acakki 22:14 Abraim ocako nyiŋ kabedo meno ni, Rwot aye bimiyo; macalo giwaco nio wa onyo ni, “Gibimiyo wa i wi got pa Rwot.”
Acakki 22:15 Dok lamalaika pa Rwot olwoŋo Abraim nia ki i polo tyen me aryone kun waco ni,
Acakki 22:16 “Rwot owacci, Doŋ akwoŋŋe ki nyiŋa kekena ni, pi tim man, ma pe itwona wodi, ma kun en wodi acel keken-ni,
Acakki 22:17 abimiyi gum ada; abimiyo likwayi ginya mapol macalo lwak lakalatwe me polo, ma rom ki kweyo ma i dog nam Dok likwayi aye gibiloyo gaŋ pa merokgi;
Acakki 22:18 rok ducu ma i lobo gibilimo gumgi ki i kom likwayi, pien ityeko woro doga.”
Acakki 22:19 Lacen Abraim odok cen bot awobene, ka gua kunnu, gudok kacel kwedgi wa i Beer-ceba; Abraim obedo i Beer-ceba. Likwayo pa Nakor
Acakki 22:20 I ŋe lok meno ducu, gitero lok bot Abraim ni, “Nen, Mirika otyeko nywalo litino ki omeru Nakor:
Acakki 22:21 latin kayone Uj, ki Buj ominne, Kemuel won Aram,
Acakki 22:22 Keced, Kajo, Pildac, Jidlap, ki Becweri.”
Acakki 22:23 Becweri onywalo Labeka. Mirika onywalo Litino aboro ki Nakor omin Abraim.
Acakki 22:24 Dakone ma aŋeca, ma nyiŋe Reuma, onywalo bene Teba, Gakam, Takac ki Maaka.
Acakki 23:1 Cara ori mwaka miya acel ki pyeraryo wiye abiro; meno aye wel mwaka me kwo pa Cara.
Acakki 23:2 Cara oto i Kiriat-arba, ma en aye Kebron, ma i lobo Kanaan; Abraim odonyo i ot okumo, okoko Cara ki pig waŋe.
Acakki 23:3 Lacen Abraim oa woko ki i nyim lato, ocito owaco bot jo Kit ni,
Acakki 23:4 “An a welo, ma doŋ atyeko bedo i kinwu; wumiya dul lobo mo i kinwu ma bibedo kabedo me yiko dano, wek ayik iye dakona-ni, oa woko ki i waŋa.”
Acakki 23:5 Jo Kit gugamo dog Abraim ni,
Acakki 23:6 “Winy, laditwa; in laker madit i kinwa kany. Yik kom latoni i lyel maber ma iyero i kin lwak lyel mewa-ni: pe tye ŋatti mo ma i kinwa ma bitwonni lyelle, nyo ma bigeŋi ni pe iyik latoni iye.”
Acakki 23:7 Abraim oa malo, ci oryebbe i nyim jo Kit, ma wegi lobo-nu,
Acakki 23:8 kun wacogi ni, “Ka onoŋo wumito ayik latona wek oa woko ki i waŋa, wuwiny lokka, wulegga Epron ma wod pa Jokar,
Acakki 23:9 wek oye mina boro ma i Makpela, ma mere-ni, ma tye i wi agikki potone. Wek oŋolla welle kikome ma romo wilone, omi bota i nyimwu, obed mera me kabedo me yik.”
Acakki 23:10 I kare meno onoŋo Epron bene tye, obedo i kin jo Kit, ci Epron Lakit ogamo dog Abraim, ma jo Kit ducu giwinyo, kacel ki lwak ducu ma gibedo i gaŋ meno,
Acakki 23:11 kun waco ni, “Pe kumeno ladit, winy lokka; amini poto, dok amiyi wa ki boro ma tye iye-ni ki i nyim lutuwa ducu; yik iye kom latoni”
Acakki 23:12 Abraim dok oryebbe i nyim wegi lobo-nu,
Acakki 23:13 ka owaco ki Epron, ma wegi lobo ducu giwinyo ni, “Ento ka imito, ci winy lokka. Abimiyi wel lawil poto, in ibigamo lim ki i ciŋa, wek ayik iye kom latona.”
Acakki 23:14 Epron owaco bot Abraim ni,
Acakki 23:15 “Laditta, winy lokka ya; wel dul poto-nu romo cekel me ryal miya aŋwen, meno kono gin aŋo ki tuŋ boti ki an bene? Yik iye kom latoni.”
Acakki 23:16 Abraim owinyo dog Epron; ci opimo ki Epron wel ryal ma owaco i nyim jo Kit, ma romo cekel me ryal miya aŋwen kulu, kun pimo ki kidi mijan ma lucat-wil gipimo kwedeni.
Acakki 23:17 Kit meno poto pa Epron ma i Makpela-ni, ma yam tye tuŋe wokceg me Mamre, poto kacel ki boro ma yam tye i poto-nu, ki yadi ducu ma tye i pota-nu, ma gurumo dyere ducu, gimiyogi, gimokogi ducu
Acakki 23:18 me bedo pa Abraim, ki i nyim jo Kit ducu, kacel ki i nyim lwak ducu ma gibedo i gaŋ meno.
Acakki 23:19 Ka lok meno otum, Abraim oyiko dakone Cara i boro ma tye i poto Makpela yo tuŋ wokceŋ me Mamre, ma en aye Kebron, ma i lobo Kanaan.
Acakki 23:20 Lukit gumoko ni poto-nu, kacel ki boro ma tye iye, gubed pa Abraim me kabedo me yik.
Acakki 24:1 I kare ma Abraim doŋ oti, ma mwaka me ditte doŋ dwoŋ, dok onoŋo Lubaŋa doŋ otyeko miyo gum ki Abraim i gin ducu,
Acakki 24:2 ci Abraim owaco ki laticce ma tye i ode, ma onoŋo loyo jamine ducu, ma oteggi i kingi, ni, “Rwak ciŋi odony ki piny i te ema,
Acakki 24:3 wek ami ikwoŋ ki nyiŋ Rwot, Lubaŋa me polo ki lobo, ni, pe ibinyomo nyako mo bot woda ma i kin anyira Kanaan, ma abedo i kingi-ni,
Acakki 24:4 ento ibicito i lobo tuwa, i kakawa; en aye ibinyomo iye dako bot woda Icaka.”
Acakki 24:5 Laticce ogamo ni, “Gwok nyo dako aye pe biye bino kweda wa i lobo man; myero an aye adok ki wodi i lobo tuwu ma yam ibino, ia ki iye-ni?”
Acakki 24:6 Abraim owacce ni, “Nen maber ni, pe icito ki woda idwoko cen kunnu.
Acakki 24:7 Rwot Lubaŋa me polo ma yam okwanyo an ki i paco pa wora-ni, ki i lobo ma ginywala iye-ni, ma yam oloko kweda kun kwoŋŋa kwoŋ ni, ‘Abimiyo lobo man bot likwayi,’ en bicwalo lamalaikane i nyimi, ci ibinyomo dako bot woda nia ki kunnu.
Acakki 24:8 Ento ka dako aye pe oye bino kwedi, ci kwoŋŋa-ni pe bimaki; ento woda aye pe myero idok kwede cen kunnu.”
Acakki 24:9 Kit meno laticce orwako ciŋe, odonyo ki piny ki i te em laditte Abraim, ocako kwoŋo kwoŋ i kom lok meno.
Acakki 24:10 Laticce okwanyo kinaga pa rwode ma romo apar, ka ocako wot, kun otero bene jami mabeco mapatpat; ci oa me wot i Mecopotamia, i gaŋ pa Nakor.
Acakki 24:11 En omiyo kinaga orumo coŋgi piny i ŋe gaŋ ma cok ki waŋ pii i kin otyeno abwora, i kare ma mon gicito iye ka twomo pii.
Acakki 24:12 Ci olego ni, “Ai Rwot, Lubaŋa pa laditta Abraim, mi lok ducu owotta maber tin. Alegi inyut mar meri ma pe lokke i kom rwoda Abraim.
Acakki 24:13 Nen, acuŋ i ŋet waŋ pii en, ki anyira ma i gaŋ guebino bene ka twomo pii.
Acakki 24:14 Nyako mo ma abilege pii amata, ni, ‘Koŋ icib aguluni piny, wek imiya pii amati,’ ci nyako ma biwaco gire kene ni, ‘Koŋ imati, ka doŋ abimiyo kinagani bene gimato’, wek en aye obed nyako ma iyero pi laticci Icaka. Kit meno bimiyo aŋeyo ni; in doŋ inyuto ki laditta mar meri ma pe lokke-ni.”
Acakki 24:15 Ma pud peya otyeko lokke, ci nen, Labeka, nya pa Becweri, wod pa Mirika, dako pa Nakor, ma omin Abraim, otuc i waŋ pii ki agulu piine ma obolo i wi gwoke.
Acakki 24:16 Nyakone onoŋo neno mwonya twatwal, nyako ma ŋattt mo peya omako ciŋe. Ci nyako meno olor, odonyo i waŋ pii, otwomo pii opoŋo agulu piine, ka odwogo, okatti kwede woko.
Acakki 24:17 Latic meno oriŋo, oŋolle i kome, ci owacce ni, “Alegi ba, koŋ imiya pii ma i aguluni amati.”
Acakki 24:18 Nyako ogamo ni, “Koŋ imat, laditta”; en otugi tiŋo agulu piine i ciŋe, omiye omato.
Acakki 24:19 Ka otyeko, ci owaco gire kene ni. “Abitwomo pii, amiyo ki kinagani bene, nio ka gumato pii oromogi.”
Acakki 24:20 Oyotoyot oonyo pii i weer, ci oriŋo odok ka twomo pii i waŋ it, otwomo pii nio ka oromo kinaga ducu.
Acakki 24:21 Laco meno ociko waŋe i kome laliŋ, wek eniaŋ ka Rwot otyeko miyo luguma okaye i yo wotte-ni, nyo pe.
Acakki 24:22 Ka kinaga gutyeko mato pii, laco meno okwanyo atego um me jabu ma pekke romo nucu cekel, ki atego jabu aryo me ŋut ciŋ ma pekgi rom ki cekel apar me jabu, omiyo ki nyako meno
Acakki 24:23 kun penye ni, “In mono i nya pa ŋa? Kabuto mo twero noŋŋe piwa i gaŋ pa woru?”
Acakki 24:24 En ogamo ni, “An anya pa Becweri ma wod pa Mirika, ma onywalo ki Nakor.”
Acakki 24:25 Dok otitte ni, “Watye bene ki reŋ kal ki cam ma romo, wa kabuto bene noŋŋe.”
Acakki 24:26 Laco meno okula wiye piny, ci oworo Rwot,
Acakki 24:27 kun waco ni, “Gipwo Rwot, Lubaŋa pa laditta Abraim, ma pe oweko mar mere ma pe lokke, ki adane, i kom laditta. An bene, Rwot doŋ otyeko telo wiya, okela wa i ot ma i kaka pa laditta kikome.”
Acakki 24:28 Ci anyaka oriŋo otito lok mutimme ducu bot jo ma tye i ot pa minne.
Acakki 24:29 Labeka onoŋo tye ki ominne ma nyiŋe Laban. Ci Laban oriŋo ocito bot laco meno, wa i waŋ it.
Acakki 24:30 Ka oneno atego um, ki atego i ŋut ciŋ laminne, ki pi winyo lok pa laminne Labeka ni, “Laco-ni oloko bota kit man,” ci owoto bot laco-nu, nen, onoŋo ocuŋ cok ki kinagane i ŋet waŋ it.
Acakki 24:31 Owacce ni, “Bin wa i ot, pien Rwot otyeko miyi gum; piŋo dok icuŋ ki i ŋe gaŋ woko? Pien doŋ atyeko yubo ot ki kabuto pa kinaga bene.”
Acakki 24:32 Laco-ni obino, odonyo i ot; ka Laban ocako gonyo del woko ki i kom kinaga, omiyo reŋ kal ki cam bot kinaga, okelo pii lalwok tyene ki tyen jo ma owoto kwede.
Acakki 24:33 Ka gikelo cam gicibo i nyime wek ocam; ento en owacci, “An peya abicam, nio ka atito kit kwena ma giora kwede.” Ci ogamo ni, “Tit do.”
Acakki 24:34 Ci en otito ni, “An latic pa Abraim.
Acakki 24:35 Rwot otyeko miyo gum madit omako laditta, doŋ odoko dano madit, omiyo en olimo lim makwo, dyegi ki dyaŋi, ryal ki jabu, lwak opii ki lwak aŋeca, kinaga mapol, ki lwak kana.
Acakki 24:36 I kare ma laditta doŋ oteggi, ci Cara dako pa laditta ocako nywalo latin laco, en aye gimiye oleyo lim ducu ma en tye kwede.
Acakki 24:37 Laditta omiya akwoŋo kwoŋ, kun owacca ni, ‘Pe ibinyomo nyako mo bot woda ki i kin anyira Kanaan, i lobo ma abedo iye-ni;
Acakki 24:38 ento ibicito i ot pa wora, ki i kin lutuwa, en aye icinyom iye dako bot woda.’
Acakki 24:39 Ci agamo dog laditta ni, ‘Gwok nyo dako pe biye bino kweda kono.’
Acakki 24:40 Ento en odokka iye ni, ‘Rwot ma abedo alubo cikke-ni bicwalo lamalaikane nywako kwedi yo, ci luguma bikayi iyo wotti; in ibinyomo dako bot woda nia i ot pa wora kikome.
Acakki 24:41 Ci kwoŋŋa doŋ pe bimaki, ka doŋ icito bot lutuwa; ka ce gin aye pe gumiyi nyako, ci kwoŋŋa doŋ pe bimaki.’
Acakki 24:42 “Tin ka ao i waŋ pii, ci alego ni, ‘Ai Rwot, Lubaŋa pa laditta Abraim, ka tin ibimiyo luguma kaya i wotta man ma awoto iye-ni,
Acakki 24:43 ci nen, acuŋ i ŋet waŋ pii en; nyako mo ma bibino ka twomo pii, an abiwacce ni, “Alegi ba, miya pii mo ki aguluni amati,”
Acakki 24:44 nyako ma bigamo ni, “Koŋ Imati, dok abitwomo mukene pi kinagani bene,” en aye obed dako ma Rwot oyero me bedo dako pa wod pa laditta.’
Acakki 24:45 “I kare ma pud peya atyeko loko lok ma tye i cwinya, ci nen, Labeka otuc, mubolo agulu piine i wi gwoke, ci olor odonyo i waŋ pii, ka otwomo pii. Ci alege ni ‘Miya pii amat ba!’
Acakki 24:46 En otugi tiŋo agulu piine ki i wi gwoke kun waco ni, ‘Koŋ imati, ci abimiyo kinagani bene gimato.’ Ci an amato, ka en omiyo kinagana bene gumato.
Acakki 24:47 Dok apenye ni, ‘In kono i nya pa aŋa kaa?’ En ogamo ni, ‘An anya pa Becweri ma wod pa Nakor, ma Mirika aye onywalo.’ Kit meno an acako keto agit i ume, ki atego jabu i ŋut ciŋe ryoryo.
Acakki 24:48 Ka akulo wiya piny, aworo Rwot ci apwoyo Rwot, Lubaŋa pa laditta Abraim, ma otela i yo maber, omiya anoŋo nya pa omin laditta me atera bot wode.
Acakki 24:49 Kombeddi ka wubitic ki laditta ki mar ki ada, wutitta; ka pe bene wutitta; wek alokke adok yo tuŋ ciŋ acuc nyo tuŋ acam.”
Acakki 24:50 Laban ki Becweri gugamo ni, “Lok man oa ki bot Rwot; pe watwero dokki iye marac nyo maber.
Acakki 24:51 Nen, en Labeka tye i nyimi enno; in ikwany en, wuwot kwede, wek en ocit obed ci-wod pa laditti, macalo Rwot doŋ otyeko wacone.”
Acakki 24:52 Ka latic pa Abraim owinyo lok meno, ocako ryebbe piny i ŋom i nyim Rwot.
Acakki 24:53 Latic okelo lwak atego ryal ki atego jabu, ki lwak ginaruka, otiŋo omiyogi bot Labeka; ka dok omiyo ki ominne ki bot minne jami me wel.
Acakki 24:54 En ki jo ma gitye kwede gucako camo cam ki mat, ci gubuto nino acel kunnu. Ka gua malo odiko, ci olego ni, “Doŋ wucwala adok bot laditta.”
Acakki 24:55 Laban ki minne gugamo ni, “Wek koŋ anyaka obed kwedwa kare manok, ma romo ka nino apar; lacen en doŋ bicito gire.”
Acakki 24:56 Ogamo kun waco botgi ni, “Pe wugal wiya; macalo Rwot doŋ omiyo luguma okaya i wot man, wuwek doŋ acak wot, adok bot laditta.”
Acakki 24:57 Gugamo ni, “Koŋ walwoŋ nyako, wapenye.”
Acakki 24:58 Ka gilwoŋo Labeka, gipenyo kun giwacce ni “Ibiye wot ki laco man?” En ogamo ni “Abiwot.”
Acakki 24:59 Kit meno gucako cwalo nyagi Labeka ki lapidine, kacel ki latic pa Abraim ki jone.
Acakki 24:60 Gulamo gum i kom Labeka, kun giwacce ni, “Laminwa, bed min jo alip apar; ki likwayi gulo gaŋ pa lumerokgi!”
Acakki 24:61 Lacen Labeka ki lwak aŋecane gua, gucako wot, guito wi kinaga kun gilubo kor laco meno; kit meno latic meno ocako wot ki Labeka, kun gidok i yo tugi.
Acakki 24:62 Icaka onoŋo obino oa ki Beer-lakai-roi; i kare meno onoŋo en bedo i Negeb.
Acakki 24:63 Ka Icaka ocito woko i bar ka lwodo lok otyeno; ci otiŋo waŋe malo, oneno kinaga ka bino.
Acakki 24:64 Ka Labeka otiŋo waŋe malo, oneno Icaka, ci olor woko ki i wi kinaga, opye piny.
Acakki 24:65 Owaco ki latic ni, “Meno laco mene ma loka ca, ma woto i bar kun bino ka romo kwedwa-ni?” Latic ogamo ni. “En aye laditta-ni.” Labeka okwanyo boŋo oumme kwede.
Acakki 24:66 Latic otito bot Icaka lok ducu ma otimme.
Acakki 24:67 Icaka okelo Labeka i kema, ci obedo kwede, odoko dakone, kun mare bene. Kit meno cwiny Icaka ocako kwe ki i ŋe to pa minne.
Acakki 25:1 Abraim dok onyomo dako mukene, ma nyiŋe Ketula.
Acakki 25:2 En onywalle Jimran, Yokocan, Medan, Midian, Icibak ki Cua.
Acakki 25:3 Yokocan onywalo Ceba ki Dedan; litino awobe pa Dedan gin ene: Accurim, Letucim ki Leummim.
Acakki 25:4 Litino awobe pa Midian gin aye Epa, Eper, Kanok, Abida ki Eldaa. Gin ducu likwayo pa Ketula.
Acakki 25:5 Abraim omiyo jamine ducu bot Icaka.
Acakki 25:6 Ento litino awobe pa monne ma aŋeca Abraim opoko botgi mot bene, i kare ma pud en kwo; ci ocwalogi woko cen nia ki ka ŋet wode Icaka. Gudok tuŋ wokceŋ i lobo mudok tuŋ nyaŋo. Abraim oto, giyike
Acakki 25:7 Man aye wel nino me kwo pa Abraim; oromo mwaka miya acel ki pyeraryo wiye abic.
Acakki 25:8 Abraim oomo cwinye me agikkine, ci oto woko, ma mwakane doŋ dit, dano muteggi, ma doŋ oti, ci odok bot lutugi.
Acakki 25:9 Awobene Icaka ki Icmael guyiko kome i boro lyel ma i Makpela, ma i poto pa Epron wod pa Jokar, ma Lakit, tuŋ wokceŋ me Mamre,
Acakki 25:10 i poto ma yam Abraim owilo ki bot jo Kit. Giyiko Abraim kenyo, kacel ki dakone Cara.
Acakki 25:11 Lubaŋa ocako miyo gum ki Icaka ki i ŋe to pa wonne Abraim. Icaka ocako bedo i Beer-lakai-roi.
Acakki 25:12 Man aye likwayo pa Icmael wod pa Abraim, ma Agar aŋeca pa Cara, anyira Ejipt, onywalo ki Abraim.
Acakki 25:13 Man nyiŋ litino awobe pa Icmael, kun lubo kit ma ginywalogi kwede: Nebayot, en latin kayo pa Icmael; ki Kooar, Adbeel, Mibcam,
Acakki 25:14 Micima, Duma, Maca,
Acakki 25:15 Adad, Tema, Jetur, Napic ki Kedema.
Acakki 25:16 Man, aye awobe pa Icmael, nyiŋgi ene, kun lubo gaŋgi, ki kabedogi; gin luker apar wiye aryo macalo rokgi tye.
Acakki 25:17 Icmael yam ori wi lobo mwaka miya acel ki pyeradek wiye abiro; ci oomo cwinye me agikkine, oto woko, odok bot lutugi.
Acakki 25:18 Kabedogi yam ocakke nia ki Kavila nio wa i Cur mukemo tuŋ Ejipt ma dok tuŋ Aciria; en obedo i kabedone pat kun pyem ki utmegine ducu. Nywalo Ecau ki Yakobo
Acakki 25:19 Man aye likwayo pa Icaka, wod pa Abraim: Abraim onywalo Icaka,
Acakki 25:20 Icaka onyomo dakone Labeka kun onoŋo tye ki mwaka pyeraŋwen; Labeka yam nya pa Becweri ma jo Aram, ma i lobo Paddan-aram, lamin Laban ma jo Aram.
Acakki 25:21 Icaka ocako lego Lubaŋa pi dakone, pien onoŋo lalur; ci Rwot ocwako kor legane, ka dakone Labeka ogamo ic
Acakki 25:22 I kare ma litino gubedo ka twomme ki i iye, en owacci, “Ka ce gitimme kit meno, man nyuto gin aŋo?” Ci ocito ka penyo dog Rwot.
Acakki 25:23 Ka Rwot otitte ni, “Rok aryo aye gitye i ii, jo meno aryo-nu kingi bipokke woko ki i ii; acel bibedo oteka makato lawote, latin matidi aye biloyo latin kayo.”
Acakki 25:24 Ka kare me gonnyene oromo, ci litino rudi gunen i iye.
Acakki 25:25 Onywalo latin kayo ma kome kwar, kome ducu obedo ki yer calo boŋo yer; omiyo gicako nyiŋe ni Ecau.
