Acakki 25:26 Lacen dok ginywalo ominne, kun ciŋe omako opuny tyen Ecau, omiyo gicako nyiŋe ni Yakobo. I kare ma ginywalo litino-nu onoŋo Icaka ditte doŋ romo mwaka pyerabicel. Ecau ocato dit me anywalline woko
Acakki 25:27 Awobe meno ka gudoŋo, ci Ecau obedo oken makwiri, ladwar i tim. Yakobo obedo lamwolo, kun bedo mere i kema mot.
Acakki 25:28 Icaka yam maro mere Ecau, pien onoŋo bedo ka camo ciŋe; ento Labeka dok onoŋo maro mere Yakobo.
Acakki 25:29 I kare ma Yakobo tye ka tedo dek ŋor, ci Ecau oa ki i tim, odwogo ma kec obwoye woko.
Acakki 25:30 Ecau olego Yakobo ni, “Miya dek ŋor mubok-ki acam, kec obwoya woko.” Pi lok meno omiyo gilwoŋo nyiŋe ni Edom .
Acakki 25:31 Yakobo owacce ni, “Koŋ icatta dit me anywallini.”
Acakki 25:32 Ecau ogamo ni, “An acok to woko; dit me anywalli kono konnye tye kwene?”
Acakki 25:33 Yakobo ogamo ni; “Koŋ icak ki kwoŋŋa kwoŋ.” Mumiyo en okwoŋŋe kwoŋ, ci ocato dit me anywalline woko bot Yakobo.
Acakki 25:34 Ka Yakobo omine kwon ki dek ŋor, ka ocamo, omato pii i wiye, ci oa malo, ocako wot ocito woko. Ecau ocayo dit me anywalline kit meno.
Acakki 26:1 Kec dok opoto i lobo aye, ma pat ki kec ma yam koŋ opoto i kare pa Abraim ca. Ka Icaka ocito i Gerar, bot Abimelek kabaka Piliciti.
Acakki 26:2 Ci Rwot onen bote kun wacce ni, “Pe icit i lobo Ejipt; ber ibed i lobo ma abititti.
Acakki 26:3 Koŋ ibed i lobo man, an bene abibedo kwedi, abimiyi gum; pien lobo man ducu abimiyo boti ki bot likwayi, dok abicobo kwoŋ ma yam akwoŋo bot woru Abraim.
Acakki 26:4 Abimiyo likwayi nya mapol macalo lwak lakalatwe me polo, abimiyo likwayi lobo man ducu; dok rok ducu ma wi lobo gibilimo gumgi ki i komgi;
Acakki 26:5 pien yam Abraim oworo doga, kun cobo cikka ki gin ma aciko ducu.”
Acakki 26:6 Icaka obedo i Gerar.
Acakki 26:7 Ka jo kunnu gupenye lok kom dakone, en ogamo ni, “En lamera”; pien olworo waco ni, “Dakona”, kun tamo ni, “Wek wegi lobo pe guneka woko pi Labeka”; pien onoŋo nen mwonya mada.
Acakki 26:8 Ka doŋ odikke kunnu kare malac, ci Abimelek kabaka pa jo Piliciti oneno Icaka ki i waŋ dirica ka obedo ka tuko ki dakone Labeka.
Acakki 26:9 Abimelek ocako lwoŋo Icaka owacce ni, “Nen, man dakoni; piŋo in kono nene iwacci, ‘En lamera’?” Icaka odokke iye ni, “Pien onoŋo atamo ni, ‘Wek pe guneka woko pire.’ “
Acakki 26:10 Abimelek ogamo ni, “Itimowa kuman piŋo? Ka nene dano mo obuto ki dakoni, kono ikelo bal i komwa nono.”
Acakki 26:11 Abimelek ocako juko lwakke ducu, kun waco ni, “Dano mo ka ogudo kom laco man, nyo dakone, gibineke woko.”
Acakki 26:12 Icaka ocoyo poto i lobo meno; ci okayo cam ma dodo tyen miya i mwakanu. Rwot aye omiye gum,
Acakki 26:13 dano-nu odoko lalonyo, obedo ka medde ki limo jami, nio ka odoko twon lalonyo.
Acakki 26:14 Olimo lim madwoŋ makwo, dyaŋi ki dyegi, ci gaŋŋe opoŋ ki lwak dano, omiyo nyeko omako jo Piliciti i kome.
Acakki 26:15 Onoŋo jo Piliciti gujuko waŋ it guculo woko ducu ki lobo, ma con lutic pa wonne aye yam gukwinyo i kare pa wonne Abraim.
Acakki 26:16 Abimelek ocako waco ki Icaka ni, “Doŋ koŋ ia woko ki botwa, pien itek ikatowa woko.”
Acakki 26:17 Ci Icaka oa woko ki botgi, ocito, ogony otiro i nota me Gerar, ci obedo iye.
Acakki 26:18 Icaka dok ocako golo waŋ pii ma yam gikwinyo i kare pa wonne Abraim; pien yam koŋ jo Piliciti guju kogi woko i kare ma doŋ wonne Abraim oto woko-ni; ci dok ocako lwoŋo nyiŋgi kit ma yam wonne, olwoŋogi kwede.
Acakki 26:19 Ento lutic pa Icaka gutyeko kwinyo waŋ it i nota-nu, ci gunoŋo iye waŋ it maloŋo.
Acakki 26:20 Lukwat pa jo Gerar gucako da ki lukwat pa Icaka, kun giwaco ni, “Pii man mewa.” Mumiyo en ocako nyiŋ waŋ pii meno ni. Ecek , ni pien gubedo ka da iye kwede.
Acakki 26:21 Ka doŋ okwinyo waŋ it mukene, dok gucako da pi eno bene; mumiyo olwoŋo ni Citna .
Acakki 26:22 Dok oa woko ki kunnu, okwinyo dok waŋ it mukene aye. Pe doŋ daa obedo tye pi meno; mumiyo olwoŋo nyiŋe ni Rekobot , kun waco ni, “Pien tin doŋ Rwot oyabowa kabedo malac, doŋ wabinya i lobe-ni.”
Acakki 26:23 Ka oa woko ki kunnu odak i Beer-ceba.
Acakki 26:24 Rwot dok onen bote i dyewor meno, ma wacce ni “An Lubaŋa pa woru Abraim; pe ilwor, pien atye kwedi, abimiyi gum, dok abimiyo likwayi nya mapol pi laticca Abraim.”
Acakki 26:25 Omiyo ocano keno tyer pi Rwot kunnu, ci olwoŋo iye nyiŋ Rwot; ci oguro kemane kunnu. Luticpa Icaka dok gukwinyo waŋ it kunnu. Icaka ki Abimelek gucikke
Acakki 26:26 Abimelek ocito bote, oa ki i Gerar, kacel ki Akujat lamiye tam, ki Pikol ladit lawimony mere.
Acakki 26:27 Ci Icaka owaco botgi ni, “Wunwubino bota pi lok aŋo, ma wun kono wudaga, dok yam doŋ wuryema ki i lobowu?”
Acakki 26:28 Gin gugamo ni, “Wan waneno atir ni Lubaŋa tye kwedi, mumiyo wawacci, wek kwoŋ obed i kin in ki wan, wek waket gicikke ki in,
Acakki 26:29 wek pe ibitimwa marac, macalo wan bene yam pe wagudo komi, pe bene watimo gin mo marac i komi, ento tim maberre keken, dok bene waryemi woko ia ki i kinwa ki kuc. Kombeddi in aye ŋat ma Rwot omiyo gum.”
Acakki 26:30 Ci otedogi karama, ka gucamo, gumato.
Acakki 26:31 Gua malo odiko con, ci gukwoŋo kwoŋ ŋat man ki lawote; ka doŋ Icaka olwokogi i yo tugi, gua, gupokke kwede ki kuc.
Acakki 26:32 I nino meno bene kikome en aye lutic pa Icaka gubino bote, gutitte lok kom waŋ it ma gityeko kwinyone, kun giwacce ni, “Watyeko noŋo pii.”
Acakki 26:33 Ocako nyiŋe ni Ciba, mumiyo nyiŋ gaŋ meno gilwoŋo ni Beer-ceba nio wa onyoo.
Acakki 26:34 Ka Ecau doŋ ditte romo mwaka pyeraŋwen, onyomo monne, Judit nya pa Beeri, jo Kit, ki Bacemat nya pa Elon, jo Kit bene.
Acakki 26:35 Gumiyo cwercwiny madwoŋ bot Icaka ki Labeka.
Acakki 27:1 Ka Icaka doŋ oti, ki waŋe bene doŋ ocido woko ma doŋ pe neno piny, ci olwoŋo latin kayone Ecau, owacce ni, “Latinna.” En ogamo ni, “Ana ene.”
Acakki 27:2 Ci owacce ni, “Nen, an doŋ ati woko, pe aŋeyo nino ma abito iye.
Acakki 27:3 Doŋ ikwany jami dwarri, ki jurani ki atummi, kat doŋ i tim, wek icidwarra lee,
Acakki 27:4 wek icella riŋo makur, kit ma amaro-ni, ci ikella, wek doŋ acam ciŋi, ka doŋ alammi gum ma peya ato.”
Acakki 27:5 I kare ma Icaka tye ka lok ki wode Ecau-ni, onoŋo Labeka bene winyo. Ka Ecau okato ocito ka dwaro lee i tim, wek ekel riŋo,
Acakki 27:6 Labeka owaco ki wode Yakobo ni, “Abedo ka winyo woru ka loko ki omeru ni,
Acakki 27:7 ‘Cikella riŋo, wek icella riŋo makur, wek doŋ acam ciŋi, ka doŋ alammi gum i nyim Rwot ma peya ato.’
Acakki 27:8 Mumiyo latinna, worra doga i lok ma aciki-ni.
Acakki 27:9 Wot icit i kin dyegi, icikella litino dyegi aryo ma komgi bulubulu. Wek an ayub riŋone makur ki woru, kit ma en maroni,
Acakki 27:10 wek iter ki woru ocam ciŋi, wek olammi gum ma peya oto.”
Acakki 27:11 Ento Yakobo ogamo dog minne kun wacce ni “Nen ba, omera Ecau kome ki yer, an: koma pe ki yer.
Acakki 27:12 Gwok nyo ka wora biboŋa, ci abinen macalo acito ka nyware, miyo bicena, pe bilamma gum.”
Acakki 27:13 Minne ogamo doge kun waco ni, “Wek cenni opot i koma, latinna; worra doga keken. Ber iwot, icikelgi bota.”
Acakki 27:14 En ocito, okelogi bot minne, ka minne ocelo riŋo makur, kit ma wonne maro-ni.
Acakki 27:15 Ka Labeka okwanyo ginaruka pa wode Ecau, ma en yam ruko maberre-ni, ma noŋo tye i ot bot minne, ci oruko ki Yakobo wode matidi-ni.
Acakki 27:16 Ocako boyo laa litino dyegi-nu ki bade ducu, ki ŋute bene ka ma yer pe iye;
Acakki 27:17 ka otiŋo riŋo me ocelo makur-ri, ki kwon ma omyeno, omiyo i ciŋ wode Yakobo.
Acakki 27:18 En odonyo kwede bot wonne, owacce ni, “Aba”; en oye ni, “An atye en do; in aŋa ce, latinna?”
Acakki 27:19 Yakobo ogamo dog wonne ni, “An Ecau, latin kayoni. Atyeko timo kit ma nakanen ititta-ni; doŋ i cukke, ia malo wek icam ciŋa, ka doŋ ilamma gum.”
Acakki 27:20 Icaka owaco ki wode ni, “In onoŋo riŋo oyotoyot ma rom man niŋniŋ, latinna?” En ogamo ni, “Pien Rwot Lubaŋani omiyo gum okaya oyot.”
Acakki 27:21 Dok Icaka owaco bot Yakobo ni, “Koŋ inyik cok bota kany, wek aboŋ komi, latinna, wek aŋe ka in latinna Ecau kikome ada nyo pe.”
Acakki 27:22 Ka Yakobo ocako nyiko cok bot wonne Icaka; oboŋo kome, ci owacci, “Dwani dwan Yakobo, ento badi en aye bad Ecau.”
Acakki 27:23 Ci doŋ pe omedo ki ŋene, pien onoŋo bade ki yer macalo bad ominne Ecau. Ka ocako lamme gum kun waco ni,
Acakki 27:24 “In ada latinna Ecau kikome?” En odok iye ni, “An kikoma.”
Acakki 27:25 Ka dok owacce ni, “Kel cam bota cok, wek doŋ acam ciŋ latinna, ka doŋ alammi gum.” Ci oketo cam i nyime, ka ocamo; dok okelle koŋo vino, omato bene.
Acakki 27:26 Ka dok wonne Icaka owacce ni, “Bin cok, wek inot lema, latinna.”
Acakki 27:27 Ci onyiko cok bote, ka onoto leme; ka ocako ŋweyo ŋwec ginarukane, ka olamme gum, kun wacce ni, “Nen, ŋwec kom woda kur macalo poto ma Rwot omiyo gum kome!
Acakki 27:28 Lubaŋa omiyi toyo ma luk a ki i polo, ki lobo ma ceko cam mapek.
Acakki 27:29 Lwak jo mapol obed luticci, ki rok mapol bene giryebbe piny i nyimi. In aye ibed ladit ma loyo omegi, litino pa meni ducu giryebbe piny i nyimi. Cen obed i kom dano ducu ma biceni, dok gum obed i kom jo ducu ma bilammi gum!”
Acakki 27:30 Ka doŋ Icaka otyeko lamo gum ki Yakobo okato woko manok nia ki i nyim wonne Icaka, ominne Ecau ocako dwogo nia ki ka dwarre.
Acakki 27:31 En bene ocelo riŋo makur, okelo bot wonne. Owaco ki wonne ni, “Wore, doŋ icukke, ia malo, wek icam ciŋ latinni, ka wek doŋ ilamma gum.”
Acakki 27:32 Wonne Icaka owacce ni, “In aŋa doki?” Ogamo ni, “An a wodi do, latin kayoni, Ecau do.”
Acakki 27:33 Kom Icaka ocako myel matek twatwal, kun waco ni, “Aŋa ma nakanen koŋ odwaro lee, okella-ni, ma doŋ atyeko camone woko ducu, ma onoŋo peya idwogo-ni, dok atyeko lamma gum woko do, gum doŋ bidebo gire i kome.”
Acakki 27:34 Ka Ecau owinyo lok pa wonne, ocako tokke ki cwar koko madit, magwa bene, kun waco bot wonne ni, “Lamme gum bene do, aya abana!”
Acakki 27:35 En dok owacce ni, “Omeru obino, obwola, ci doŋ otyeko buyo gummi woko.”
Acakki 27:36 Ecau owacce ni, “Pe gicako nyiŋe Yakobo atir? Nen, en doŋ oridde ka laro jamina kiryo kulu. Okwoŋo buyo dit anywillina, doki nen, in bene dok otyeko buyo gumma woko.” Dok omedde ki waco lok ni, “In nene pe igwoko gum pira ce?”
Acakki 27:37 Icaka ogamo dog Ecau ni, “Nen, doŋ atyeko keto en me bedo rwodi otum, ki omege ducu atyeko miyogi me bedo luticce; amiye wa kal ki koŋo vino ducu gubed me pito en. Gin aŋo ma dok abimiyi ba, latinna?”
Acakki 27:38 Ecau dok owaco bot wonne ni, “Onoŋo itye ki gum acel keken bo, wora? Lamma gum, lamma gom mo bene do, aya abana.” Ecau otiŋo wiye malo ka koko.
Acakki 27:39 Wonne Icaka ocako gamo lokke ni, “Nen, ibibedo bor ki lobo ma ceko cam mapek, dok ibibedo bor ki toyo ma luk a ki malo i polo.
Acakki 27:40 Ibikwo meri ki lak pala lucwanni, ibibedo latic pa omeru; ento i kare ma ibijemo i kome, ci ibituro rii okol ma oriyo i ŋutini.” Icaka ocwalo Yakobo i Karan
Acakki 27:41 Ecau ocako kwero ominne pi gum ma wonne olamo i kome-ni. Ecau opiro lok i cwinye ni, “Kare me to pa wora doŋ onyiko cok; en aye abineko iye omera Yakobo bene.”
Acakki 27:42 Ento ka gitito ki Labeka lok pa latin kayone Ecau, en ocwalo dano, olwoŋo Yakobo wode matidine, owacce ni, “Nen, omeru Ecau obedo ma cwinye yom kun oyubbe me neki.
Acakki 27:43 Mumiyo in iwor doga, latinna; a malo, ilwi, iriŋ woko bot omera Laban i Karan.
Acakki 27:44 Koŋ icibed kunnu, nio waŋ ma kiniga pa omeru opye;
Acakki 27:45 wek wiye koŋ owil i gin ma yam itimo i keme-ni; ka doŋ abicwalo dano ka omi ki kunnu. Piŋo wun aryo ducu myero wurweny woko ki i waŋa lawaŋacel?”
Acakki 27:46 Ka Labeka dok owaco bot Icaka ni, “An doŋ kwona ool woko ki kit kwo pa mon Kit. Ka dok Yakobo bene binyomo anyira Kit ma rom ki mon ma gitye i lobo-ni, ci doŋ kwona konyo aŋo?”
Acakki 28:1 Ka Icaka olwoŋo Yakobo, ci olamme gum, ka ocike ni, “In doŋ pe inyom dako mo ki i kin anyira me Kanaan.
Acakki 28:2 Ber ia, icit Paddan-aram i ot pa kwaru Becweri ma won meni; en aye inyom iye nya pa Laban ma omin meni kikome.
Acakki 28:3 Lubaŋa Matweroducu omiyi gum, omiyi inya mapol, wek ibed lwak rok mapol.
Acakki 28:4 Dok omi gum pa Abraim opot i komi, ki i kom likwayi, wek icam lobo ma ibedo iye-ni macalo welo, ma yam Lubaŋa omiyo ki Abraim!”
Acakki 28:5 Kit meno Icaka ocwalo Yakobo, ocito i Paddan-aram bot Laban, wod pa Becweri me Aram, ma omin Labeka ma min Yakobo ki Ecau. Ecau dok onyomo dako mukene
Acakki 28:6 Ecau oneno ni Icaka doŋ otyeko lamo gum i kom Yakobo, ka dok ocwale wa i Paddan-aram wek onyom dako ki kunnu, dok i kare ma olamme gum ocike ni, “In pe inyom nyako mo ki i kin Lukanaan,”
Acakki 28:7 dok Yakobo bene oworo dog wonne ki minne, ci ocito i Paddan-aram.
Acakki 28:8 Ka Ecau oneno ni kit pa anyira Kanaan pe yomo cwiny wonne Icaka,
Acakki 28:9 ci ocito bot jo Icmael, onyomo iye dako, omedo i kom mere ma con ca. Onyomo Makalat ma nya pa Icmael wod pa Abraim, ma lamiŋ Nebayot. Lek obino i wi Yakobo i Betel
Acakki 28:10 Yakobo oa ki, Beer-ceba, ci odok tuŋ Karan.
Acakki 28:11 Ka oo i kabedo mo, obuto kenyo i dyewor meno, pien onoŋo ceŋ doŋ opoto woko. Ka otiŋo got acel mo ki i kin wadi, opyelo piny, oteno ki wiye, ci onino woko i kabedo meno.
Acakki 28:12 Lek obino i wiye, oneno rwom ma gijeŋo tere ocuŋ piny i ŋom, kun wiye gijeŋo oo wa i polo; ka oneno lumalaika pa Lubaŋa kun gilor piny, ka dok giito gidok malo.
Acakki 28:13 Oneno Rwot ocuŋ tuŋ ka wiye malo, kun waco ni, “An a Rwot, Lubaŋa pa kwaru Abraim, ki Lubaŋa pa Icaka; abimiyi lobo ma ibuto iye-ni, abimiyo boti ki bot likwayi;
Acakki 28:14 dok likwayi gibibedo ma rom ki apwa me lobo, dok wubimedde wuromo yo tuŋ potoceŋ ki tuŋ wokceŋ, ki yo tuŋ acam ki tuŋ acuc bene; dok i kom in ki i kom likwayi en aye kaka ducu ma wi lobo bilimo iye gumgi.
Acakki 28:15 Nen, an atye kwedi, abigwoki ka ma ibiwoto iye ducu, dok abidwoki cen wa i lobo man; pe abiweki ata nio waŋ ma acobo gin ma atyeko i okone boti-ni.”
Acakki 28:16 Ka Yakobo oco woko ki i waŋ nino, ci owacci, “Rwot tye i kabedo-ni ada; onoŋo an kara pe aŋeyo.”
Acakki 28:17 Ci lworo ocako make, kun wacci, “Kabedo man kara lik kuman! Man ot pa Lubaŋa kikome, man aye dog gaŋ me polo.”
Acakki 28:18 Yakobo oa malo odiko con, otino got ma oteno ki wiye-ni, ci ocibo wek obed wir, ka oonyo moo i wiye.
Acakki 28:19 Ocako nyiŋ kabedo meno ni Betel ; ento nia wa con onoŋo nyiŋ kabedo meno gilwoŋo ni Luj.
Acakki 28:20 Yakobo ocako kwoŋo kwoŋ kun waco ni, “Ka Lubaŋa bibedo kweda, kun gwoka i yo man ma awoto iye-ni, ka dok bimiya kwon me acama, ki boŋŋi me aruka,
Acakki 28:21 ka ce abidwogo wa i ot pa wora ki kuc, ci Rwot doŋ bibedo Lubaŋana,
Acakki 28:22 ki got man bene, ma acibo me bedo wir, bidoko ot pa Lubaŋa: ki gin ducu ma ibimina, an bene abimini dul acel me aparre.”
Acakki 29:1 Yakobo dok omedde ki wotte, ka oo i lobo pa jo ma tuŋ wokceŋ.
Acakki 29:2 Ka obedo ka neno piny, ci oneno waŋ pii i dye bar, lwak romi gubuto piny dul adek ma gicok i ŋet waŋ pii; pien romi gimato pii i waŋ it meno. Got ma giumo ki doge bene dwoŋ:
Acakki 29:3 ka romi ducu doŋ gugurre, gucokke kunnu, ka lukwat gitorre, giloro got woko cen ki i dog waŋ pii, ka gimiyo romi gimato, ka dok giloro got, gidwoko cen, giumo ki dog waŋ pii kakare.
Acakki 29:4 Yakobo openyogi ni, “Utmega, wun wua ki kwene?” Gugamo ni, “Wan waa ki i Karan.”
Acakki 29:5 Owaco botgi ni, “Wun mono wuŋeyo Laban wod pa Nakor?” Gugamo ni, “Waŋeyo en.”
Acakki 29:6 Owaco botgi ni, “En tye maber kono?” Gugamo ni, “En tye maber gire. Nen, nyare Lakeri ka bino ki romigi ca!”
Acakki 29:7 En ogamo ni, “Nen, tipo peya olokke do, man peya kare me guro lim kacel; ber wumi pii ki romi, ci dok wuciti, wukwagi aye.”
Acakki 29:8 Ento gin gutitte ni, “Wan pe watwero miyogi, waŋ ma lim ducu gucokke, gugurre kacel, ka doŋ gicwalo got woko cen ki i dog waŋ pii, ka doŋ wamiyoromi pii.”
Acakki 29:9 Ka onoŋo en tye ka lok kwedgi, ci Lakeri ocoro ki romi pa wonne, ma onoŋo kwayogi.
Acakki 29:10 Ka Yakobo oneno Lakeri nya pa Laban, nya pa omin minne, ki romi pa nerone Laban, Yakobo okato ci ocwalo got woko cen ki i dog waŋ pii, ka ocako mi yo romi pa nerone Laban gumato pii.
Acakki 29:11 Ci Yakobo onoto lem Lakeri, kun kok matek.
Acakki 29:12 Yakobo otito ki Lakeri ni, en e wat pa wonne kikome, en e wod pa Labeka; ci en oriŋo, ocito otito ki wonne.
Acakki 29:13 Ka Laban owinyo lok kom Yakobo wod pa laminne, ci oriŋo ocito ka ŋolo wiye; okwako kore, onoto leme bene, ka ocako tere wa i ode. Yakobo oyeko lok magi ducu kikore bot Laban,
Acakki 29:14 ka Laban owacce ni, “In ada i cogona dok i riŋo koma bene!” Ci obedo kwede dwe acel.
Acakki 29:15 Laban ocako waco bot Yakobo ni, “Pien in i watta, doŋ ibitina tic nono bo? Ber ititta, imito aculli gin aŋo?”
Acakki 29:16 Onoŋo Laban tye ki anyirane aryo; nyiŋ nyare maditte Lea, ki nyiŋ matidine Lakeri.
Acakki 29:17 Lea onoŋo wane kiŋiŋic, ento Lakeri nen mwonya muliŋŋe.
Acakki 29:18 Yakobo onoŋo maro Lakeri: ci owacci, “Abitini tic mwaka abiro pi Lakeri, nyari matidi-ni.”
Acakki 29:19 Laban ogamo ni, “Onoŋo bedo ber ka amiyo en boti, kato ma kono amiyo bot dano mukene; bed bota.”
Acakki 29:20 Yakobo otiyo pi Lakeri mwaka abiro; kare meno obedo macalo nino manok mo ki bot Yakobo, pien onoŋo iye omaro Lakeri mada.
Acakki 29:21 Yakobo openyo Laban ni, “Doŋ imiya dakona wek abed kwede, pien kare doŋ oromo.”
Acakki 29:22 Laban otedo karama ci olwoŋo iye dano ducu ma gitye i kabedo meno.
Acakki 29:23 Ci okelo nyare Lea bot Yakobo otyeno, ocako bedo kwede.
Acakki 29:24 Laban omiyo aŋecane Jilpa bot nyare Lea wek okonye.
Acakki 29:25 Ka odiko ma piny oru, Yakobo oneno kara gimiye Lea. Yakobo owaco ki Laban ni, “Itima kuman piŋo? Onoŋo pe abedo ka tic boti pi Lakeri? Ibwola kuman piŋo?”
Acakki 29:26 Laban ogamo ni, “Pe gitimo kuman i lobo tuwa kany, pe gimiyo nyako matidi aye kwoŋo ger ki maditte.
Acakki 29:27 Koŋ ityek cabit pi man acel-li, ci dok wabimiyi giri mukene bene, ka ibitina tic mwaka abiro mukene.”
Acakki 29:28 Yakobo otimo kit meno; ocobo cabit pa Lea, ka Laban omiye nyare Lakeri me bedo dakone.
Acakki 29:29 Laban dok omiyo aŋecane Bila bot nyare Lakeri wek okonye.
Acakki 29:30 Yakobo ocako bedo ki Lakeri bene; cwinye omaro Lakeri makato Lea, dok omedde otiyo tic bot Laban mwaka mukene abiro. Litino ma ginywalo ki Yakobo
Acakki 29:31 Ka Rwot oneno ni gidag Lea, ci oyabo iye; ento Lakeri ocuŋ ma pe nywal.
Acakki 29:32 Lea ogamo ic, onywalo latin laco, ci ocako nyiŋe Reuben, kun waco ni, “Pien Rwot oneno aromana; koni olo doŋ cwara bimara.”
Acakki 29:33 Dok ogamo ic, ci onywalo latin laco, owacci, “Pien Rwot owinyo ni gidaga, omiyo dok omiya latin man bene”; ci ocako nyiŋe ni Cimeon.
Acakki 29:34 Lacen dok ogamo ic, onywalo latin laco, owacci, “Cwara doŋ bidwogo i koma, pien doŋ anywalle awobe adek kulu”; mumiyo gicako nyiŋ latin-nu Levi.
Acakki 29:35 Dok ogamo ic, onywalo latin laco, owacci, “Man aye kare ma abipako iye Rwot”; mumiyo ocako nyiŋ latin Juda; ci koŋ ocuŋ woko.
Acakki 30:1 Ka Lakeri oneno ni pe enywalo latin mo ki Yakobo, ci nyeko omake kom laminne. Ka owaco bot Yakobo ni, “Miya litino; ka pe, ci adene woko.”
Acakki 30:2 Kiniga omako Yakobo i kom Lakeri, kun wacce ni, “Iketa adoko Lubaŋa bo, ma en ogeŋi nywalli?”
Acakki 30:3 Lakeri ogamo ni, “Aŋecana Bila en do, doŋ ibed kwede, wek onywal latin mo ma kakara, wek an bene anoŋ litino mogo ki tuŋ bote.”
Acakki 30:4 Ci omiyo aŋecane obedo dakone, Yakobo ocako bedo kwede.
Acakki 30:5 Bila ogamo ic, onywalo latin laco ki Yakobo.
Acakki 30:6 Lakeri owaco ni, “Lubaŋa otyeko ŋolla kop, owinyo ki dwana bene, ci omiya gira latin laco”; omiyo ocako nyiŋe Dan.
Acakki 30:7 Bila aŋeca pa Lakeri dok ogamo ic, onywalo latin laco ki Yakobo me aryone.
Acakki 30:8 Lakeri dok owacci, “Ka me lweny doŋ alwenyo matek wan ki lamera, ci aloye”; mumiyo ocako nyiŋ latin Naputali.
Acakki 30:9 Ka Lea bene oneno ni doŋ ecuŋ woko, ma pe enywalo litino, ci otiŋo aŋecane Jilpa, omiyo ki Yakobo wek obed dakone.
Acakki 30:10 Aŋeca pa Lea bene onywalo latin laco ki Yakobo.
Acakki 30:11 Lea owacci, “Gum maber!” Mumiyo ocako nyiŋe Gad.
Acakki 30:12 Jilpa aŋeca pa Lea dok onywalo latin laco ki Yakobo me aryone.
Acakki 30:13 Lea owacci, “An koma gum! Pien mon gibilwoŋa ni lagumkom”; mumiyo en ocako nyiŋ latin ni Acer.
Acakki 30:14 I kare me kayo ŋano, Reuben ocito i poto, ci onoŋo iye yat nyodo, ci okelogi wa bot minne Lea. Ka Lakeri olego Lea ni, “Alegi, imiya yat nyodo pa wodi mogo do.”
Acakki 30:15 Ento en ogamo ni, “In imayo cwara woko ki bota, itamo ni lokke tidi ce? Man dok imito ni ikwany yat nyodo pa woda woko bene?” Lakeri ogamo ni, “En tin obut kwedi dyewor ma ka yat nyodo pa wodi.”
Acakki 30:16 Ka Yakobo odwogo nia ki i tim otyeno, Lea okato ocito ka ŋolo wiye iyo, owacce ni, “Myero tin idony i oda; pien atyeko wilo in ki yat nyodo pa woda.” Ci ocito obuto ki Lea i dyewor meno.
Acakki 30:17 Lubaŋa owinyo lega pa Lea, ci ogamo ic, onywalo latin laco me abicce ki Yakobo.
Acakki 30:18 Lea owacci, “Lubaŋa doŋ oculo waŋ miyo aŋecana bot cwara”; mumiyo ocako nyiŋe Icakar.
Acakki 30:19 Lea dok ogamo, oyac, onywalo latin me abicelle ki Yakobo.
Acakki 30:20 Lea dok owacci, “Lubaŋa doŋ omiya mot me lim keny mabeco; cwara doŋ biketta deyo, pien doŋ atyeko nywalle litino co abicel kulu”; mumiyo ocako nyiŋe Jabulon.
Acakki 30:21 Lacen dok onywalo nyare, ci ocako nyiŋe Dina.
Acakki 30:22 Lubaŋa doŋ ocako po i kom Lakeri, dok owinyo legane bene, ka oyabo iye.
Acakki 30:23 Ci ogamo, onywalo latin laco, kun wacci, “Lubaŋa otyeko kwanyo lewic woko ki i koma”;
Acakki 30:24 ci ocako nyiŋe Yucepu, kun wacci, “Myero Rwot dok omedda latin laco mo acel!” Lok ma Yakobo oyubo ki Laban kom mucarane
Acakki 30:25 Ka Lakeri otyeko nywalo Yucepu, ci Yakobo owaco bot Laban ni, “Doŋ icwala wek adok paco i lobo tuwa.
Acakki 30:26 Miya monna ki litinona ma yam atiyo pigi boti-ni, wek doŋ aciti; in bene iŋeyo gin ma atiyo boti do.”
Acakki 30:27 Laban ogamo ni, “Ka iye, ci koŋ alokki gin mo; pien atyeto ci aniaŋ ni Rwot omiya gum pi in.
Acakki 30:28 Ber ititta gin ma imito amini me mucarani, ci abimini.”
Acakki 30:29 Yakobo owacce ni, “In kikomi iŋeyo kit ma atiyo ki ticci, ki kit ma agwoko kwede limmi.
Acakki 30:30 Pien yam ma peya abino onoŋo limmi nok mo, nen doŋ gumedde madwoŋ mukato; Rwot obedo ka mini gum ka ma adok iye ducu. Ento an abinoŋo lim ma tuŋ bota awene?”
Acakki 30:31 En ogamo ni, “Gin aŋo ma abimini?” Yakobo ogamo ni, “In pe ibimiya gin mo wacel. Ka ibiye, tima gin macalo man, an abimedde ka kwayo limmi, ki gwokogi bene.
Acakki 30:32 Wek tin acit awot i kin limmi ducu, wek ayer ki i kingi romi ma gubedo aciri aciri ki ma abacabac, ki litino romi macol ducu, kacel ki dyegi ma gubedo abacabac ki ma aciri aciri; meno gin aye gibibedo mucarana.
Acakki 30:33 Kit meno leŋ cwinya binen lacen, ka ibibino ka ŋiyo kom mucarana. Ka ibinoŋ o dyegi ma komgi pe aciri aciri ki abacabac, ki litino romi ma pe gicol gitye i kin mega, meno gibikwano ni ma gikwalo.”
Acakki 30:34 Ci Laban ogamo ni, “Ber, wek obed kit ma iwaco-ni.”
Acakki 30:35 Ento i nino meno Laban okoyo nyogi dyegi ma gubedo kitana kitana, ki ma abacabac, ki megi dyegi ma gubedo aciri aciri ki abacabac, ma kitartar ducu, ki litino romi ducu macol, oketo i cin awobene.
Acakki 30:36 Opoko kingi woko ki Yakobo ma borre romo wot me nino adek kulu; Yakobo odoŋ ka kwayo lim pa Laban mudoŋŋe.
Acakki 30:37 Yakobo ocako jako jaŋ pobo madyak ki yaa ki ogali, ci oŋweko pokgi, wek kom kedi onen ŋwalaŋwala.
Acakki 30:38 Oketo kedi ma oŋweko komgi, opyelogi i nyim romi i weer pii, ka ma gionyo iye pii, ka ma lim cito iye ka mato pii, pien nyogine giyito megine ka gibino ka mato pii.
Acakki 30:39 Ka giyitogi i nyim kedi, omiyo ginywalo litino ma akolakol, ki ma aciri aciri ki ma abacabac.
Acakki 30:40 Yakobo dok opoko litino romi pat, oloko waŋ lim ka neno gin ma akolakol ki lwak lim pa Laban macolle ducu, ka opoko dul limme pat kun pe dok ribogi ki pa Laban.
Acakki 30:41 I kare ma nyogi yito megine matego, ci Yakobo pyelo kedi i weer pii i nyim romi, wek oyitte i nyim kedi,
Acakki 30:42 ento ka megine magorogoro aye giyitogi, en pe pyelo kedi i nyimgi; pienno lim magoro ducu pa Laban, mategone ducu pa Yakobo.
Acakki 30:43 Kit meno laco meno odoko lalonyo madwoŋ, ma tye ki lwak lim, ki lwak aŋeca ki lwak opiine, ki lwak kinaga ki kana.
Acakki 31:1 Yakobo obedo ka winyo kun awo be pa Laban giwaco ni, “Yakobo doŋ otero lim pa wonwa woko ducu, olimo lonyo nia ki i kom lim pa wonwa.”
Acakki 31:2 Yakobo oneno ni waŋ Laban oballe woko i kome, pe dok nene maber kit macon.
Acakki 31:3 Rwot owaco bot Yakobo ni, “Doŋ idok i lobo pa kwarowu bot lutuwu, an abibedo kwedi.”
Acakki 31:4 Yakobo olwoŋo Lakeri ki Lea i bar olet ka ma limme tye iye,
Acakki 31:5 ci owaco botgi ni, “An aneno waŋ wonwu ocido woko i koma, pe doŋ nena maber kit macon. Ento Lubaŋa pa wora yam tye kweda.
Acakki 31:6 Wun wuŋeyo ni atyeko tic bot wonwu ki tekka ducu;
Acakki 31:7 ci en obedo ka bwola, kun loko mucarana atata tyen apar kulu, ento Lubaŋa pe oye en otimo gin mo marac i koma.
Acakki 31:8 Ka owaco ni, ‘Lim ma abacabac bibedo meri me mucarani,’ ci lim ducu ginywal mubedo abacabac keken. Ka dok oloko doge ni, ‘Lim ma gibedo akolakol gin aye bibedo meri me mucarani,’ ci lim ducu dok ginywal akolakol.
Acakki 31:9 Meno aye kit ma Lubaŋa okwanyo kwede lim pa wonwu ci omiyogi bota.
Acakki 31:10 “I kare ma megine giyitogi, atiŋo waŋa malo ki i waŋ lek, ci aneno nyogi ma gitigo megine komgi obedo akolakol ki abacabac ki opukopuk.
Acakki 31:11 Lamalaika pa Lubaŋa owacca i waŋ lek ni,. ‘Yakobo’, an agamo ni, ‘An a ene!’
Acakki 31:12 Ci owacca ni, ‘Tiŋ waŋi malo wek inen, nyogi ducu ma gitigo megine-ni gubedo akolakol ki abacabac ki opukopuk; pien atyeko neno kit ma Laban timi kwede.
Acakki 31:13 An Lubaŋa me Betel, ka ma yam iwiro iye wir ki moo, ka ikwoŋo iye kwoŋ bota-ni. Doŋ ia malo, icit woko cen ki i lobe-ni, idok i lobo ma ginywali iye ca.’ “
Acakki 31:14 Lakeri ki Lea gugamo ni, “Tye dok dul lim mo nyo ginaleya mo ma dok odoŋ piwa i ot pa wonwa?
Acakki 31:15 Pe doŋ en nenowa macalo lurok ata? Doŋ otyeko catowa woko, tye ka camo bene lim ma gimiyo piwa woko.
Acakki 31:16 Lim ducu ma doŋ Lubaŋa otyeko kwanyo ki bot wonwa doŋ mewa ki pa litinowa; doŋ gin ducu ma Lubaŋa owacci aye itim.”
Acakki 31:17 Yakobo oa, oketo awobene ki monne i wi kinaga,
Acakki 31:18 oleko limme ducu, ma yam olimo i Paddan-aram; ci ocako wot me dok i lobo Kanaan bot Icaka.
Acakki 31:19 Laban onoŋo ocito ka ŋolo yer kom romine, ci Lakeri okwalo cal lubaŋa ki i ot pa, wonne.
Acakki 31:20 Yakobo obwolo Laban La-aram, pe otitte pi wotte.
Acakki 31:21 Olwi ki lwak lim ducu ma yam tye kwede, ka ocako wot, oŋolo kulu Euprate, ci okemo lobo godi me Gilead. Laban olubo kor Yakobo
Acakki 31:22 Ka nino okato adek kulu, ci gitito bot Laban ni, “Yakobo doŋ otyeko lwi, ocito woko.”
Acakki 31:23 En ogwarre ki lutugi, gutwarre, gulubo kore; ka guwoto nino abiro, ci gudiŋo kore cokcok i kin godi me Gilead.
Acakki 31:24 Ento Lubaŋa obino bot Laban La-aram i waŋ lek, kun wacce ni, “Gwokke, pe icilok lok mo maber nyo marac bot Yakobo.”
Acakki 31:25 Laban omako Yakobo iyo. Onoŋo doŋ otyeko gony woko i lobo godi, ci Laban ki lutugi gugony i lobo godi meno me Gilead.
Acakki 31:26 Laban ocako lok ki Yakobo ni, “Itimo kuman piŋo, ma ibwola kit man, doŋ itiŋo anyirana, ilwi kwedgi, macalo iyakogi ayaka ki pala lucwan-ni?
Acakki 31:27 Piŋo ilwi woko alwiya i muŋ ali, kun iumo waŋa ma pe ititta gin mo, ma kono nene aciki ki yomcwiny ki wer ki ajaa ki opuk?
Acakki 31:28 Piŋo pe iweko aciko litinona kun anoto lem anyirana? Man itimo gin me caro a tika.
Acakki 31:29 Onoŋo atwero timi marac; ento Lubaŋa pa woru oloko kweda tin i dyewor, ocika ni ‘Gwokke pe icilok lok mo maber nyo marac bot Yakobo.’
Acakki 31:30 Man doŋ ia icako wot woko, pien pi ot pa woru odoko mitti mada; ento dok ikwalo ki cal lubaŋana me ŋo kono?”
Acakki 31:31 Yakobo ogamo dog Laban ni, “Onoŋo abedo ki lworo, abedo ka tamo ni gwok nyo ibimayo anyirani woko ki bota.
Acakki 31:32 Ka ibinoŋo cal lubaŋani bot ŋatti mo kany, ŋat meno pe bikwo. Cim koni jamini ma inoŋo tye bota kany i nyim utmegiwa ci ikwany idok giri kwede.” Onoŋo Yakobo pe oŋeyo ni Lakeri aye ma okwalogi.
Acakki 31:33 Kit meno Laban ocako donyo i kemapa Yakobo, ki i kema pa Lea, ki i kema pa mon aŋeca aryo-nu ducu, ci pe omedo ki noŋogi; ka okato woko ki i kema pa Lea, dok odonyo i kema pa Lakeri.
Acakki 31:34 I kare meno onoŋo Lakeri otiŋo lubaŋa-nu, ci orwakogi i kom me bedo i wi kinaga; ci obedo i wigi. Laban oŋiyo jami ma i kema ducu, pe omedo ki noŋogi.
Acakki 31:35 Lakeri owaco bot wonne ni, “Laditta, pe kiniga omaki i koma ka ineno ni pe atwero a malo i nyimi, pien atye ki kit pa wan mon.” Kit meno Laban oyenyo cal lubaŋane kwe, pe omedo ki noŋogi.
Acakki 31:36 Kiniga omako Yakobo, ocako da ki Laban, kun waco bot Laban ni, “Balla doŋ tye kwene kaa? Atimo bal aŋo, mumiyo ilubo kora twatwal-li?
Acakki 31:37 Kadi bed iyenyo i kin jamina ducu, kit gin aŋo ma inoŋo i kom jami ducu ma oa i odi? Kel iket kany i nyim utmegini ki utmegina, wek guŋol kop i kin wan aryo-ni.
Acakki 31:38 An abedo kwedi mwaka pyeraryo; pe i megi romini ki megi dyegini mo opoto, pe bene acamo nyok romoni mo.
Acakki 31:39 Lim ma ŋuu aye omwodo pe akelo riŋone boti, an aye aculo gira; lim ma gikwalo i dyeceŋ ki i dyewor ipenyo bota.
Acakki 31:40 Yam abedo kit meno, kun ceŋ waŋa dyeceŋ, koyo neka dyewor, pe aketo nino mo i waŋa.
Acakki 31:41 I lwak mwaka pyeraryo ma abedo kwedi i odi-ni, atiyo boti mwaka apar wiye aŋwen pi anyirani aryo-ni, ki mwaka abicel pi limmi, ibedo ka loko mucarana tyen apar kulu.
Acakki 31:42 Ka ce Lubaŋa pa wora, Lubaŋa pa Abraim ma Icaka bene lworo, pe obedo tuŋ bota, kono tin icwala adok tuwa ki ciŋa noŋo adada. Lubaŋa oneno twon aromana, ki tic ma atiyo ki ciŋa ci tin dyewor bene ojuki.” Yakobo ki Laban gucikke
Acakki 31:43 Laban ogamo kun dok iye bot Yakobo ni, “Anyira man gin anyirana, ki litino bene gin litinona, lim bene gin limma, ki gin ma ineno-ni gin ducu limma. Ento abitimo gin aŋo tin i kom anyirana-ni, nyo i kom litinogi ma gunywalo?
Acakki 31:44 Doŋ ibin wek waket gicikke i kin in ki an, me bedo caden i kin in ki an.”
Acakki 31:45 Ci Yakobo otino got ocibo wek obed wir.
Acakki 31:46 Ka Yakobo owaco bot utmegine ni, “Wucok got”, ci gucoko got, guguro kacel, ka gucamo cam i ŋet odur got meno.
Acakki 31:47 Laban ocako nyiŋ kabedo meno ni Jegarcaduta; ento Yakobo ocako nyiŋe ni Galeed.
Acakki 31:48 Laban owacci, “Odur man en aye caden i kin in ki an tin.” Mumiyo ocako nyiŋe Galeed.
Acakki 31:49 Ocako nyiŋ wir meno ni Mijpa, pien owacci, “Rwot ogwok kin an ki in, ka kinwa doŋ bipokke woko.
Acakki 31:50 Ka ibiketo giŋi marac i kom anyirana, nyo ka dok ibinyomo mon mukene, idodogi i kom anyirana, kadi ŋatti mo pe tye kwedwa, ber ipo ni Lubaŋa en aye caden i kin in ki an.”
Acakki 31:51 Ci Laban dok owaco bot Yakobo ni, “Nen odur man, ki wir ma atyeko cibo i kin in ki an.
Acakki 31:52 Odur man aye caden, ki wir bene en caden, an pe abikato ka ŋet odur man pi cito boti, in bene pe ibikato ka ŋet odur man ki wir man pi cito bota, ni pi tim marac.
Acakki 31:53 Lubaŋa pa Abraim, Lubaŋa pa Nakor, Lubaŋa pa wongi, obed laŋolkop i kinwa.” Kit meno Yakobo okwoŋo kwoŋ ki nyiŋ Lubaŋa ma wonne Icaka lworo.
Acakki 31:54 Yakobo otyero gitum i wi got, kun olwoŋo iye utmegine ducu ka camo cam kwede, ci gucamo gubuto kunnu i wi got.
Acakki 31:55 Ka piny oru odiko con, Laban oa, onoto lem likwaye ki lem anyirane, olamo gum i komgi, ci opokke kwedgi odok i gaŋŋe.
Acakki 32:1 Yakobo omedde ki wotte ci lumalaika pa Rwot guromo kwede.
Acakki 32:2 Ka Yakobo onenogi, owacci, “Man mony pa Lubaŋa!” Mumiyo olwoŋo nyiŋ kabedo-nu ni Makanaim .
Acakki 32:3 Yakobo ocwalo lukwena bot ominne Ecau ma tye i lobo Ceir, i lobo pa jo Edom.
Acakki 32:4 Opwonyogi ni, “Wubiwaco bot laditta Ecau kit man: Laticci Yakobo owacci, ‘Doŋ atyeko bedo bot Laban abedo nio wa i kare-ni.
Acakki 32:5 Atye ki twoni ki lwak kana, ki lwak lim, ki lwak opii ki lwak aŋeca; acwalo kwena boti laditta wek anoŋ pwoc mo ki tuŋ boti.’ ”
Acakki 32:6 Ka lukwena gudwogo bot Yakobo, guwacce ni, “Wao bot omeru Ecau, en obebino ka jolo wii i yo, kacel ki jo miya aŋwen.”
Acakki 32:7 Lworo omako Yakobo matek kome bene oryaŋŋe woko; ci opoko kin jo ma onoŋo gitye kwede, ki dyegi ki dyaŋi, ki kinaga, dul aryo,
Acakki 32:8 kun tamo ni “Ka Ecau obino olwenyo i kom dul man acel-li otyeko woko, ci dul acel mudoŋ ca bibwot.”
Acakki 32:9 Yakobo olego ni, “Ai Lubaŋa pa kwara Abraim, Lubaŋa pa wora Icaka, ai Rwot in ma yam iwacca ni, ‘Doŋ idok tuwu bot kakawu, an abitimi maber,’
Acakki 32:10 an pe amyero kadi matidi mo ki mar meri ducu ma pe lokke, ki ada meri ducu ma inyuto i kom an laticci; pien con aŋolo kulu Jordan ma kun atye ki odoona keken, ci kombeddi doŋ apokke dul aryo kulu.
Acakki 32:11 Alegi ni ilara ki i ciŋ omera, lara ki i ciŋ Ecau; pien alwore, gwok nyo obebino ka nekowa ducu mon ki litinogi.
Acakki 32:12 Ento yam onoŋo iwaco ni, ‘Abitimi ber, abimiyo likwayi bedo macalo kweyo ma i dog nam, ma pe kwanne pi dwoŋŋe.’ ”
Acakki 32:13 En obuto kenyo i nino meno, okwanyo dul lim mogo ma yam tye kwede ocwalo bot ominne Ecau,
Acakki 32:14 megi dyegi miya aryo ki nyogi dyegi pyeraryo, megi romi miya aryo ki nyogi romi pyeraryo,
Acakki 32:15 megi kinaga ma ginyeto cakgi pyeradek ki litinogi, megi dyaŋi pyeraŋwen ki twoni apar, megi kana pyeraryo ki twoni kana apar.
Acakki 32:16 Otiŋo man ducu, omiyo i ciŋ luticce, kun gilekogi dul ki dul patpat. Ociko luticce ni, “Wun wukat i nyima, wek kinwu obed mabocoboco ka wutye ka lekogi.”
Acakki 32:17 Ociko latel yo ni, “Ka omera Ecau oromo kwedi, ce openyi ni, ‘Wun jo pa aŋa? Wucito kwene? Lim man ma i nyimwu-ni pa aŋa?’
Acakki 32:18 Ibiwacce ni, ‘Lim pa laticci Yakobo; gin aye mot ma ocwalo bot laditte Ecau; en bene pud odoŋ ceŋ i ŋewa.’ “
Acakki 32:19 Omedde ki pwonyo dano me aryo ki me adekke, ki gin ducu ma gileko lim, ocikogi ni, “Wubiloko lok ma romrom bot Ecau ka wuromo kwede,
Acakki 32:20 ka wubiwacce ni, ‘Dok bene laticci Yakobo aye odoŋ cen i ŋewa.’ ” Onoŋo otamo ni, “Wek akwe cwinye ki mot ma ocito anyim-mi, ci lacen olo abineno waŋe twal, dok en bene gwok doŋ bijola.”
Acakki 32:21 Kit meno mot okwoŋo nyime, kun en kikome obuto i gony i dyewor meno. Yakobo olwenyo i Peniel
Acakki 32:22 I dyewor meno en oa malo, ci okwanyo monne aryo, aŋecane aryo, kacel ki litinone apar wiye acel, owoto oŋolo kwedgi kulu Jabok i waŋ wat apara.
Acakki 32:23 Okwanyogi, omiyo guŋolo kulu, kacel ki lim ma en tye kwede ducu.
Acakki 32:24 Yakobo ka odoŋ kene, laco mo obino, ocako rette kwede nio wa kwarpiny.
Acakki 32:25 Ka laco meno oneno ni pe doŋ etwero loyo Yakobo, ci otwomo awaŋ-macce; ci em Yakobo otuk owil woko lacuŋo ma en rette kwede.
Acakki 32:26 Owacce ni, “Weka doŋ aciti, pien piny doŋ mito ru woko.” Ento Yakobo ogamo ni, “Pe abiweki, nio waŋ ma koŋ ilamma gum.”
Acakki 32:27 En ogamo ni, “Nyiŋi kono aŋa?” En owacci, “Yakobo.”
Acakki 32:28 Ci dok owacce ni, “Nia tin nyiŋi doŋ pe gibilwoŋo ni Yakobo, ento ni Icrael , pien ibedo ka lweny ki Lubaŋa, dok ki dano bene, ci imedo ki loyo.”
Acakki 32:29 Yakobo dok openye ni, “Alegi ni itucca nyiŋi do.” En owacce ni, “Ipenyo nyiŋa kono piŋo?” Omiye gum ka kenyo.
Acakki 32:30 Ci Yakobo ocako nyiŋ kabedo meno ni, Peniel, kun wacci, “Pien atyeko neno Lubaŋa waŋ ki waŋ, ento pud akwo gira aye.”
Acakki 32:31 Ceŋ otucce i Peniel kun doŋ woto ma komo akoma pi eme ma otuk owil wokoni.
Acakki 32:32 Omiyo wa i kare man Luicrael gikwero riŋo puc me bam ma tye i awaŋ-mac, pien Lubaŋa otwomo me Yakobo i ler awaŋ-mac.
Acakki 33:1 Ka Yakobo otiŋo waŋe malo, ci oneno ka Ecau bino, kacel ki jone miya aŋwen. Ocako poko litino i kin Lea ki Lakeri ki bot aŋecane aryo-ni.
Acakki 33:2 Ocwalo aŋeca ki litinogi anyim, ka dok Lea ki litinone, ka doŋ Lakeri ki Yucepu gucoko korgi ducu.
Acakki 33:3 En kikome obolle, ocito anyim, kun woto ryebbe piny tyen abiro nio ka oo kwede cok bot ominne.
Acakki 33:4 Ento Ecau otokke ki ŋwec, oriŋo ka mote, ci opoto okwako kore, ka omako ŋute, onoto leme, ci gucako koko.
Acakki 33:5 Ka dok Ecau otiŋo waŋe malo, ci oneno lwak mon ki litinogi, owacci, “Maca kono jo mene ma gibino-ni?” Yakobo ogamo ni, “Meno aye gin litino ma Lubaŋa omiyo ki laticci pi kicane.”
Acakki 33:6 Ka aŋeca gunyiko cok, kacel ki litinogi, ci guryebbe piny;
Acakki 33:7 Lea bene kit meno kacel ki litinone ka gunyiko cok ci guryebbe piny; me agikkine Yucepu ki Lakeri gunyiko cok, gin bene guryebbe piny.
Acakki 33:8 Ecau owacci, “Lwak man ma arwatte kwedgi ducu, te lokke aŋo?” Yakobo ogamo ni, “Wek anen maber-ber i nyim laditta.”
Acakki 33:9 Ento Ecau owacci, “An atye ki ma roma, omera; wek lim man ducu gubed meri.”
Acakki 33:10 Yakobo ogamo ni, “Aa, pe. Alegi ni, ka ineno an ayomo cwinyi, ci ber igam mot ma amiyi ki ciŋa-ni; pien ada, ka aneno waŋi, rom ki ma aneno waŋ Lubaŋa, pi kit cwiny maber ma ijola kwede-ni.
Acakki 33:11 Alegi igam mot ma amiyo gikelo boti-ni, pien Lubaŋa doŋ onyuto kicane i koma, dok bene atye ki mera ma roma.” Obedo ka ride ki lok meno, nio ka oye, ogamo motte.
Acakki 33:12 Lacen Ecau owacci, “Wek doŋ wanywaku yo kacel, kun atelo nyimi.”
Acakki 33:13 Ento Yakobo ogamo ni, “Laditta, iŋeyo ni litino pud peya guteggi, dok atye ka gwoko romi ki dyaŋi ma pud gidoto litinogi; ka wamiyogi wot malac, bibwoyogi woko, kadi bed pi nino acel, lim ducu gibito woko.
Acakki 33:14 Wek in laditta iwot, icit anyim i nyim laticci, kun an alubo kori motmot, muporo wot pa lim mutella yo, ki wot pa litino, nio ka abio boti i Ceir.”
Acakki 33:15 Ecau ogamo ni, “Wek awek boti jo mogo ma abino kwedgi-ni.” Ento en owacci, “Gimitte piŋo? Laditta, tima ber, wek doŋ obed kit meno.”
Acakki 33:16 Kumeno Ecau ocako wot i nino meno me dok i Ceir.
Acakki 33:17 Yakobo owoto odok mere tuŋ Cukot, ogero ode pire kene dok oguro dwol dyaŋine. Mumiyo nyiŋ kabedo meno gilwoŋo ni Cukot .
Acakki 33:18 Lacen Yakobo oo ki kuc i gaŋ me Cekem, ma tye i lobo Kanaan, kun oa ki i Paddan-aram; oguro kemane i nyim gaŋ.
Acakki 33:19 Dul-latin lobo ma oguro iye kema-ni, owilo ki bot litino pa Kamor, ma won Cekem, ki wellim ma romo miya acel.
Acakki 33:20 Ocano keno tyer kunnu, ci olwoŋo ni El-Eloe-Icrael .
Acakki 34:1 Dina nya pa Lea, ma onywalo ki Yakobo, ocito ka limo mon ma i lobo meno.
Acakki 34:2 Cekem wod pa Kamor ma Lakiv, laker me lobo meno, ka onene, ci omake tektek obuto kwede, omiye lewic.
Acakki 34:3 Cwinye omaro Dina nya pa Yakobo; omaro nyako, kun loko kwede mot mupye.
Acakki 34:4 Cekem oloko ki wonne Kamor ni, “Nyomma nyako man, obed dakona.”
Acakki 34:5 Yakobo owinyo ni otyeko ronyo nyare Dina; ento onoŋo awobene gitye ki limme i olet. Yakobo odiyo cwinye, oliŋ gire mot, nio ka gudwogo.
Acakki 34:6 Kamor won Cekem ocito bot Yakobo ka penyo keny.
Acakki 34:7 Ka awobe pa Yakobo guwinyo lok meno, gua ki i olet, gudwogo, ci gukeco, kiniga omakogi, pien otimo gin ma pe myero i Icrael, pi buta ki nya pa Yakobo, pien kit tim macalo meno pe myero otimme.
Acakki 34:8 Kamor oloko kwedgi kun waco ni, “Tipo kom woda doŋ omaro nyawu; alegowu, wuwek en onyom nyawu, obed dakone.
Acakki 34:9 Wek nyomme obed i kinwa kwedwu; wumi anyirawu botwa, wun bene wunyom anyirawa, wuter.
Acakki 34:10 Wun wubibedo kwedwa, wubibedo i lobo-ni macalo wumito; wubed iye wucat iye wilwu, wek wulim iye lim.”
Acakki 34:11 Cekem bene owaco kit meno bot won nyako ki omegine, ni, “Ber wujol kennya, abikelo botwu lim ducu ma wuŋolla.
Acakki 34:12 Wuŋolla wel lim kit ma wumito ducu ki me ayal, abikolo lim kit ma wubiwacca; ento wumiya anyom nyako-ni obed dakona.”
Acakki 34:13 Awobe pa Yakobo gugamo dog Cekem ki wonne Kamor kun gibwologi abwola, pien oronyo lamingi Dina.
Acakki 34:14 Guwaco botgi ni, “Pe watwero tiyo iye gin mo, ento miyo laminwa bot dano ma pe giliro, meno bikelo lewic i komwa.
Acakki 34:15 Tye yo acel keken; ka otimme, ci miyo waye, en ene: ka wudoko macalo wan, ka dano acel acel ma laco i kinwu olirre.
Acakki 34:16 Miyo wan doŋ wabimiyowu anyirawa, ki wan bene doŋ wabinyomo anyirawu; ci doŋ wabibedo i kinwu macalo wat acel.
Acakki 34:17 Ento ka pe wuwinyo lokwa, ka wukwero Lirre, ci wakwanyo nyawa, waa, wacito giwa.”
Acakki 34:18 Lokgi oyomo cwiny Kamor ki wode Cekem.
Acakki 34:19 Latin awobi orune ka timo woko cut, pien onoŋo cwinye yom i kom nya pa Yakobo. Onoŋo yam giwore makato jo ducu ma i ot pa wonne.
Acakki 34:20 Kit meno Kamor ki wode Cekem gucito i dog gaŋgi, ci guwaco bot jo me gaŋgi ni,
Acakki 34:21 “Jo man gimer kwedwa; waweku gin gubed i lobo, gucat wilgi iye; nen, lobo-ni tye malac ma romogi; wuwek wanyom anyiragi, wek wami gin bene gunyom anyirawa.
Acakki 34:22 Tye lok acel ma bimiyo giye bedo i kinwa, en aye bedo wat acel, ka laco acel acel i kinwa bilirre, kit macalo gin gilirre.
Acakki 34:23 Pe limgi, ki lonyogi ki lwak lee ma tye i ciŋgi ducu gibidoko limwa? Ber waye lokgi wek gubed kwedwa.”
Acakki 34:24 Ci jo ducu ma guwok ki i dog gaŋ guwinyo lok pa Kamor ki wode Cekem; co ducu ki acel acel gulirre, lwak ducu ma guwok ki i dog gaŋ meno.
Acakki 34:25 Ka nino okato adek, ma doŋ bur okwok, ci awobe pa Yakobo aryo, Cimeon ki Levi, omegi Dina, gukwanyo pala lucwan, gucito, guturo ki donyo i gaŋ ma pe wegine giŋeyo, ci guneko co woko ducu.
Acakki 34:26 Ka guneko Kamor ki wode Cekem ki pala lucwan, ci gukwanyo Dina woko ki i ot pa Cekem, gucito kwede.
Acakki 34:27 Awobe pa Yakobo gucorre i gaŋ pa luto, guyako iye jamigi pi ronyo lamingi.
Acakki 34:28 Guyako dyegigi ki dyaŋigi, ki lwak kana, ki jami ducu ma tye i gaŋ ki ma tye i potti bene.
Acakki 34:29 Guyako lwak lonyogi ducu, ki litinogi ducu ki mon megi, ki jami ma i odigi ducu, gutero matwal.
Acakki 34:30 Ci Yakobo owaco bot Cimeon ki Levi ni, “Wun wukelo ayela i koma, wumiyo nyiŋa odoko ŋwe lituny i kin wegi lobo-ni, Lukanaan ki Luperiji. An lwakka nok mo, ka ce gucokke kacel me lweny kweda, gibityeka woko liweŋ, an kacel ki oda ducu.”
Acakki 34:31 Ento gugamo ni, “Myero doŋ gubed ki laminwa macalo lakwele bo?”
Acakki 35:1 Lubaŋa owaco bot Yakobo ni, “A woko icit i Betel, wek ibed kunnu; dok ican keno tyer kunnu ka ma yam an anen iye boti i kare ma iriŋo ilwi woko ki bot omeru Ecau.”
Acakki 35:2 Omiyo Yakobo owaco bot jo ma i ode ki jo ducu ma gibedo bote ni, “Wubol lwak cal lubaŋa pa lurok ma wutye kwedgi i kinwu-ni, wulonnye kenwu, wulok ginarukawu;
Acakki 35:3 ka doŋ waayu, wacitu woko wa i Betel, wek acit acan keno tyer pi Lubaŋa ma yam ogamo doga i nino ma yam can odiŋani, ma obedo kweda i kabedo ducu ma awoto iye.”
Acakki 35:4 Gumiyo ki Yakobo cal ducu, ki agit ma noŋo tye i itgi bene; ci cal lubaŋa pa lurok ma gitye kwede Yakobo oyikogi piny i te yat kworo ma yam tye cok ki Cekem.
Acakki 35:5 Ka gitye ka wot, lworo ma oa ki bot Lubaŋa opoto i kom wegi gaŋi ma tye cok kwedgi, omiyo pe gulubo kor awobe pa Yakobo.
Acakki 35:6 Yakobo otiro i Luj ma en aye Betel, ma tye i lobo Kanaan, en kacel ki lwak dano ducu ma yam gitye kwede.
Acakki 35:7 Ocano keno tyer kunnu, olwoŋo nyiŋ kabedo meno ni El-betel pien onoŋo Lubaŋa yam onen iye bote i kare ma olwi oriŋo woko ki bot ominne.
Acakki 35:8 Debola lapidi pa Labeka oto woko, ci giyike i te yat kworo ma i ŋet Betel; mumiyo nyiŋ kabedo meno gilwoŋo ni Alon-bakut .
Acakki 35:9 Lubaŋa dok onyutte bot Yakobo i kare ma en oa ki i Paddan-aram, ci omiye gum.
Acakki 35:10 Lubaŋa owacce ni, “Nyiŋi Yakobo; pe dok gibilwoŋo nyiŋi ni Yakobo, ento nyiŋi doŋ bibedo Icrael.” Omiyo nyiŋe odoko Icrael.
Acakki 35:11 Lubaŋa dok owacce ni, “An Lubaŋa Matwero-ducu; nywal, inya; rok ki lwak rok mapol bia i komi, ki luker bene gibia ki i komi.
Acakki 35:12 Lobo ma yam amiyo ki Abraim ki Icaka abimiyo boti, ka dok abimiyo lobo bot likwayi ma gibilubi.”
Acakki 35:13 Lubaŋa ocako a ki i kabedo ka ma yam oloko iye kwede-ni odok malo.
Acakki 35:14 Ci Yakobo ocibo wii i kabedo ka ma oloko iye kwede-ni, ocibo iye wir got; oonyo gityer amata i keme, ka oliyo moo i kome.
Acakki 35:15 Yakobo ocako nyiŋ kabedo ma Lubaŋa oloko iye kwede-ni ni Betel.
Acakki 35:16 Gumedde ki wot nia ki i Betel: i kare ma pud Eprat kiborbor, mwoc Ogoyo Lakeri, ci nyodone obedo tek.
Acakki 35:17 Ka doŋ nyodone obedo tek, dako lacolo owacce ni, “Pe ilwor; tin doki ibinywalo latin laco mukene.”
Acakki 35:18 I kare ma en to ma cwinye cok ka tum, ocako nyiŋ latinne ni. Benoni; ento wonne ocako nyiŋe ni Benjamin.
Acakki 35:19 Lakeri oto woko kit meno, ci giyike i yo ma cito Eprat, ma en aye Beterekem.
Acakki 35:20 Yakobo ocibo wir got i wi lyel pa Lakeri; meno wir lyel pa Lakeri ma pud tye ocuŋ kunnu nio wa i kare man.
Acakki 35:21 Icrael omedde ki wotte, ogony i ŋe lubele me Eder ma wiye ocudo malo.
Acakki 35:22 I kare ma Icrael tye i lobo meno, ci wode Reuben otimo caro, obuto ki ci-wonne Bila ma aŋeca; ci wonne owinyo pire bene. Yakobo yam tye ki awobene apar wiye aryo.
Acakki 35:23 Litino awobe pa Lea gin aye Reuben, latin kayo pa Yakobo, Cimeon, Levi, Juda, Icakar ki Jabulon.
Acakki 35:24 Litino awobe pa Lakeri gin aye Yucepu ki Benjamin.
Acakki 35:25 Litino awobe pa Bila, aŋeca: pa Lakeri, gin aye Dan ki Naputali.
Acakki 35:26 Litino awobe pa Jilpa, aŋeca pa Lea, gin aye Gad ki Acer. Meno gin aye litino awobe pa Yakobo ma ginywalogi i Paddan-aram.
Acakki 35:27 Yakobo obino bot wonne Icaka i Mamre, i Kiriat-arba, en aye Kebron ka ma yam Abraim ki Icaka gubedo iye.
Acakki 35:28 Icaka yam ori wi lobo mwaka miya acel ki pyeraboro.
Acakki 35:29 Icaka oomo cwinye me agikkine, oto woko ci odok oto, lutugi, dano muteggi, ma doŋ oti; ci awobene Ecau ki Yakobo guyiko kome.
Acakki 36:1 Man-aye likwayo pa Ecau, en Edom.
Acakki 36:2 Ecau onyomo anyira Kanaan: Ada nya pa Elon Lakit, Okolibama nya pa Ana, wod pa Jibeon Lakiv,
Acakki 36:3 ki Bacemat nya pa Icmael, lamin Nebayot.
Acakki 36:4 Ada onywalo ki Ecau Erifaji; Bacemat onywalo Reuel;
Acakki 36:5 ki Okolibama onywalo Jeuc, Jalam ki Kora; meno aye litino awobe ma ginywalo ki Ecau i lobo Kanaan.
Acakki 36:6 Ecau otero monne ki litino awobene ki anyirane, ki lwak jo ducu ma en tye kwede, ki limme, lee mere ducu ki lonyone ducu ma olimogi ki i lobo Kanaan, odak kwedgi i lobo mukene kun opokke ki ominne Yakobo.
Acakki 36:7 Onoŋo gin ducu gitye ki lim madwoŋ, ma pe doŋ romogi bedo kacel: pien lobo ma onoŋo gibedo iye pe romo me kwayo limgi,
Acakki 36:8 Omiyo Ecau odak obedo i lobo godi me Ceir; Ecau en aye Edom.
Acakki 36:9 Likwayo pa Ecau won jo Edom ma i lobo godi me Ceir gin ene.
Acakki 36:10 Man aye nyiŋ litino awobe pa Ecau: Erifaji wod pa Ada ma, dako pa Ecau, ki Reuel wod pa Bacemat dako pa Ecau.
Acakki 36:11 Litino awobe pa Erifaji gin Teman Omar Jepo, Gatam ki Kenaj.
Acakki 36:12 Timna yam en dako pa Erifaji, wod pa Ecau, ma aŋeca; onywalo Amalek ki Erifaji. Man gin aye litino awobe pa Ada, dako pa Ecau.
Acakki 36:13 Man gin aye litino awobe pa Reuel: Nakat, Jera Cama ki Mija. Man aye litino awobe pa Bacemat dako pa Ecau.
Acakki 36:14 Man aye litino awobe pa Okolibama nya pa Ana wod pa Jibeon, dako pa Ecau; onywalo ki Ecau awobe magi: Jeuc, Jalam ki Kora.
Acakki 36:15 Magi aye litino awobe pa Ecau ma rwodi. Litino awobe pa Erifaji latin ka yo pa Ecau gin ene: rwot Teman rwot Omar, rwot Jepo, rwot Kenaj:
Acakki 36:16 rwot Kora, rwot Gatam rwot Amalek; magi aye rwodi pa Erifaji ma i lobo Edom; gin aye awobe pa Ada.
Acakki 36:17 Magi aye litino awobe pa Reuel wod pa Ecau: rwot Nakat, rwot Jera rwot Cama ki rwot Mija; meno aye rwodi pa Reuel ma i lobo Edom; gin aye litino awobe pa Bacemat, dako pa Ecau.
Acakki 36:18 Magi aye litino awobe pa Okilibama dako pa Ecau: rwot Jeuc rwot Jalam ki rwot Kora: meno gin aye rwodi ma Okolibama nya pa Ana, dako pa Ecau, onywalo.
Acakki 36:19 Gin aye litino awobe pa Ecau, en aye Edom; meno aye gin rwodigi.
Acakki 36:20 Magi aye awobe pa Ceir Lakori, ma gin wegi lobo-nu: Lotan, Cobal, Jibeon, Ana,
Acakki 36:21 Dicon, Ejer ki Dican; magi aye rwodi pa jo Kori, litino awobe pa Ceir ma i lobo Edom.
Acakki 36:22 Litino awobe pa Lotan gin aye Kori ki Eman; ki lamin Lotan en Timna.
Acakki 36:23 Magi aye litino awobe pa Cobal: Alvan, Manakat, Ebal, Cepo ki Onam.
Acakki 36:24 Magi aye litino awobe pa Jibeon: Aiya, ki Ana; en aye Ana ma yam onoŋo waŋ pii amuro ma tye i tim, i kare ma en tye ka kwayo lwak kana pa wonne Jibeon.
Acakki 36:25 Magi aye Litino pa Ana: Dicon ki Okolibama, nya pa Ana.
Acakki 36:26 Magi aye litino awobe pa Dicon: Kemdan, Eciban, Itran ki Keran.
Acakki 36:27 Magi aye litino awobe pa Ejer: Bilan, Jaavan ki Akan.
Acakki 36:28 Magi aye litino awobe pa Dican: Uj ki Aran.
Acakki 36:29 Magi aye rwodi pa jo Kori: rwot Lotan, rwot Cobal, rwot Jibeon, rwot Ana,
Acakki 36:30 rwot Dicon, rwot Ejer ki rwot Dican; meno aye rwodi pa jo Koti, kit ma calo kakagi tye kwede i lobo Ceir.
Acakki 36:31 Magi aye luker ma guloyo lobo Edom, ma onoŋo pud peya kabaka mo oloyo jo Icrael.
Acakki 36:32 Bela wod pa Beor onoŋo loyo Edom, nyiŋ gaŋ kalle gilwoŋo ni Dinkaba.
Acakki 36:33 Ka Bela oto, ci Jobab wod pa Jera me Bojra oleyo ka tyene.
Acakki 36:34 Ka Jobab oto, ci Kucam mua ki i lobo pa jo Teman oleyo ka tyene.
Acakki 36:35 Ka Kucam oto, ci Adad wod pa Bedad oleyo ka tyene. En con olwenyo, oloyo jo Midian ma gitye i lobo Moab; nyiŋ gaŋ kalle gilwoŋo Avit.
Acakki 36:36 Ka Adad oto ci Camla me Macireka oleyo ka tyene.
Acakki 36:37 Ka Camla oto, ci Caul me Rekobot ma tye i dog kulu Euprate oleyo ka tyene.
Acakki 36:38 Ka Caul oto, ci Baal-kanan wod pa Akbor oleyo ka tyene.
Acakki 36:39 Ka Baal-kanan wod pa Akbor oto, ci Kadar oleyo ka tyene; nyiŋ gaŋ kalle gilwoŋo Pau. Nyiŋ dakone Meketabel, nya pa Matred, nya pa Mejakab.
Acakki 36:40 Magi aye nyiŋ rwodi ma tuŋ bot Ecau, macalo doggolagi tye kwede, ki kabedogi, ma lubo nyiŋgi: rwot Timna, rwot Alva, rwot Jetet,
Acakki 36:41 rwot Okolibama rwot. Ela rwot Pinon,
Acakki 36:42 rwot Kenaj, rwot Teman, rwot Mibjar,
Acakki 36:43 rwot Magdiel ki rwot Iram; magi aye rwodi pa jo Edom, en aye Ecau, ma kwaro pa jo Edom, kit ma yam gibedo kwede i kabedogi, i lobo ma odoko megi.
Acakki 37:1 Yakobo obedo i lobo ma yam koŋ wonne obedo iye-ni, lobo me Kanaan.
Acakki 37:2 Man aye lok me tekwaro pa Yakobo. Ka Yucepu doŋ ditte oromo mwaka apar wiye abiro, onoŋo doŋ kwayo lim kacel ki omege; en obedo ki litino awobe pa Bila ki Jilpa, mon pa wonne; Yucepu okelo lok maraco i komgi bot wongi.
Acakki 37:3 Yakobo onoŋo maro Yucepu makato litinone ducu pien onoŋo en latin ma ginywalo ka wi tiyone; okwone kanyi mabor ma bade boco.
Acakki 37:4 Ento ka omegine guneno ni wongi maro en makato gin ducu, cwinygi ocako kwere woko, pe gitwero lok kwede maber.
Acakki 37:5 Ka Yucepu oleko lek, ci otito bot omegine, ci gumedde ameda ki kwere.
Acakki 37:6 En otito botgi ni, “Koŋ wuwiny kit lek ma aleko-ni:
Acakki 37:7 nen ba, i kare ma wabedo ka tweyo larita i poto, ci nen, laritana oa malo ocuŋ atir; ci laritawu gugurre, gurume dyere, ka giryebbe piny bot laritana.”
Acakki 37:8 Omegine gugamo ni, “In ada ibiloyowa? In aye doŋ ibiloyo wiwa?” Gumedde ki kwere doŋ marac pi lekke ki pi lokke.
Acakki 37:9 Dok oleko lek mukene, dok otito ki omegine aye, kun wacci, “Nenu ba, dok aleko lek mukene aye. Nen, ceŋ ki dwe ki lakalatwe apar wiye acel gubedo ka ryebbe piny i nyima.”
Acakki 37:10 Ka otito bot wonne ki bot omegine, wonne ocoke, ojuke matek, kun wacce ni, “Meno kit lek aŋo ma ileko kumene-ni? An ki meni ki omegini wabibino, ci wapoto waryebbe piny i nyimi ada?”
Acakki 37:11 Nyeko omako omegine i kome ento wonne okano lok meno i cwinye. Gicato Yucepu i Ejipt
Acakki 37:12 Ka omegine gucito ka kwayo lim pa wongi ma cok ki Cekem,
Acakki 37:13 ci Icrael owaco bot Yucepu ni, “Omegini pe gitye ka kwat i ŋet Cekem? Bin wek aori icit botgi.” En ogamo doge ni, “An a ene”.
Acakki 37:14 Ci owacce ni, “Koŋ, icinen ka omegini gitye maber, kacel ki lim bene, ka idwokka lok doki.” Ka ocwale nia ki i nota me Kebron, ci ocito wa i Cekem.
Acakki 37:15 Laco mo onoŋe ka woto juŋŋe atata i olet; laco meno openye ni, “In ibeyenyo aŋo?”
Acakki 37:16 En ogamo ni, “Abeyenyo omegina. Alegi ititta ka ma gitye iye ka kwayo limgi.”
Acakki 37:17 Laco meno owacce ni, “Doŋ gutyeko a woko, pien awinyo ka giwaco ni, ‘Wacitu wa i Dotan’” Yucepu ocako lubo kor omegine, ka onoŋogi i Dotan.
Acakki 37:18 Ka gunene ki ka mabor, ma onoŋo peya oo botgi cok, ci guyubo lok i kome me neke,
Acakki 37:19 kun giloko kekengi ni, “Lalek eno bino-nu.
Acakki 37:20 Wubin tin wa neke woko, wek wabole i bur mo kany; ci wabitito ni, ‘ŋuu mo aye omake, omwode woko’, wek wanen kit ma lekke-nu bicobbe kwede.”
Acakki 37:21 Reuben owinyo yub meno, ci olare ki i ciŋgi, kun wacci, “Pe wan aye waneke.”
Acakki 37:22 Reuben owacogi dok ni, “Pe giony remone mo; wubole woko i bur man ma tye i tim kany, ento pe wuket ciŋwu i kome.” Onoŋo en oyubbe me kwanye woko ki i ciŋgi pi dwoke bot wonne.
Acakki 37:23 Ka Yucepu oo bot omegine, ci gupoto i kome, gulunyo boŋo kanyine woko, kanyi mabor ma bade boco ma onoŋo oruko-ni;
Acakki 37:24 ci gumake, gutere gubole woko i bur. Bur meno onoŋo pii pe iye.
Acakki 37:25 Lacen gubedo piny ka cam; ka gutiŋo wangi, ci guneno lwak jo Icmael ma gua i Gilead, ki lwak kinaga ma gutiŋo yec odok, moo yat too ki murra, ma giwoto gicito kwede i Ejipt.
Acakki 37:26 Juda dok owaco ki omegine ni, “Konyo aŋo ka waneko ominwa dok wamuŋo tone woko?
Acakki 37:27 Wubin wek wacatu en bot jo Icmael, pe wan aye waneke ki ciŋwa, pien en ominwa, remowa kikome.” Ci omegine guworo doge.
Acakki 37:28 Jo Midian ma lucatwil gubino kenyo; ci guywayo Yucepu woko ki i bur, gucate woko bot jo Icmael, kun giwile ki cekel me ryal pyeraryo; ci gutero Yucepu wa i Ejipt.
Acakki 37:29 Ka Reuben odwogo i dog bur, ci oneno Yucepu doŋ pe i bur, ci cwinye ocwer ocako yeco boŋone woko.
Acakki 37:30 Ka odok cen bot omegine, owacogi ni “Awobi-ni doŋ pe do; man abidok kwene ba?”
Acakki 37:31 Ka gukwanyo kanyi pa Yucepu, ci guneko dyel, ka guluto kanyi i remo;
Acakki 37:32 ka gukelo kanyi mabor ma bade boco bot wongi, kun giwaco ni, “Wan wanoŋo man; koŋ iŋi, ka nyo kanyi pa wodi onyo pe.”
Acakki 37:33 Ka oŋiyo, ci owacci, “Man kanyi pa woda do; ŋuu doŋ omwode woko do; adada Yucepu doŋ ŋuu okido woko matitino do.”
Acakki 37:34 Yakobo bene cwinye ocwer, ocako yeco boŋone, ci otweyo boŋo cola i pyere, obedo ka koko wode pi kare malac.
Acakki 37:35 Awobene ducu ki anyirane gua malo gucito ka kweyo cwinye; okwero ni pe gikwe cwinye, kun wacci, “Aa pe, abilubo kor latinna i lyel ki koko.” Wonne obedo ka koke kit meno.
Acakki 37:36 Ci jo Midian gucato Yucepu woko i Ejipt bot Potipar, ladit tic pa Parao, ma loyo askari Lukur-piny.
Acakki 38:1 I kare meno Juda oa woko ki bot omegine, ocito odak bot laco mo ma i Adulam, ma nyiŋe Kira.
Acakki 38:2 Juda oneno nya pa Lakanaan mo ma nyiŋe Cua; ci onyomo, ka obedo kwede.
Acakki 38:3 Ci ogamo ic, onywalo latin laco, wonne ocako nyiŋe Er.
Acakki 38:4 Dako dok ogamo, onywalo latin laco, ocako nyiŋe Onan.
Acakki 38:5 Dok ogamo ic aye, onywalo latin laco, ocako nyiŋe Cela, Latin meno en onywalo i Kejib.
Acakki 38:6 Juda onyomo nyako ma nyiŋe Tamar ki wode Er ma latin kayone.
Acakki 38:7 Ento Er latin kayo pa Juda yam onoŋo dano marac i nyim Rwot, ci Rwot oneke woko.
Acakki 38:8 Ci Juda owaco bot Onan ni, “Dony i wi ci-omeru, ci ibed kwede macalo won ot, wek inywal kwede wi omeru.”
Acakki 38:9 Ento Onan oŋeyo ni litino pe bibedo mere; pi meno ka odonyo i wi ci-ominne, ci onyeto kodine piny, wek pe enywal kwede wi ominne.
Acakki 38:10 Gin ma otimo pe oyomo cwiny Rwot, ci oneke woko bene.
Acakki 38:11 Juda dok owaco bot ci-wode Tamar ni, “Koŋ doŋ ibed macalo daa-to i ot pa woru, nio waŋ ma woda Cela bidoŋo”, pien onoŋo lworo ni gwok bito woko, macalo omegine. Kit meno Tamar odok obedo i ot pa wonne.
Acakki 38:12 Ka kare okato, ci dako pa Juda ma nya pa Cua-ni oto woko. Ka cwiny Juda doŋ opye, ci ocito i Timna bor luŋol yer romine, onywako yo ki lareme Kira ma Laadulam.
Acakki 38:13 Ka gitito bot Tamar ni, “Kwaru okato obecito i Timna ka ŋolo yer rom ine”,
Acakki 38:14 ci olunyo boŋo cola me dalako woko, ka oumme ki kitambara, odwalo ki kome woko ducu, ka ocito obedo kwede i dogcel me Enaim, ma okemo yo me Timna; pien onoŋo oneno ni kadi bed Cela doŋ oteggi, ento peya gimiye ni olake.
Acakki 38:15 Ka Juda onene, ci otamo ni gwok dako lakwele mo, pien onoŋo en oumo waŋe woko ducu.
Acakki 38:16 Ka ocito bote ka ma obedo iye i ŋet yo, owacce ni, “Bin wek abed kwedi,” kun pe ŋeyo ni ci-wode. En ogamo ni, “Ibimiya gin aŋo kono, ka wek ibin ibed kweda?”
Acakki 38:17 En odok iye ni, “Abikwanyo latin dyel ki i kin dyegina, acwalli.” Dako-nu ogamo ni, “Ibijeŋo gin aŋo bota, ka doŋ ibicwalla?”
Acakki 38:18 Ogamo ni, “In imito ajeŋŋi gin aŋo?” En odok iye ni, “Agit meri, ki tolli, ki odooni ma tye i ciŋi-ni.” Ci otiŋo omiyogi ducu bote, ka odonyo obedo kwede, ci dako-nu oyac kwede.
Acakki 38:19 Dako oa okato ocito gire woko, olunyo boŋo kitambara ma oumme kwede-ni, ka doŋ oruko boŋo cola me dalako.
Acakki 38:20 Ka Juda ocwalo La-adulam ma lareme pi terre latin dyel, wek odwokke jami ma yam ojeŋo bot dako-nu, pe omedo ki noŋo kome.
Acakki 38:21 Obedo ka penyo jo ma i kabedo-nu ni, “Dako mo ma lakwele-ni tye kwene, ma onoŋo yam bedo i ŋet yo Enaim?” Guwacce ni, “Lakwele mo pe obedo kany.”
Acakki 38:22 Ka odok cen bot Juda, ci owacce ni, “Pe amedo ki noŋo dako-nu; ki jo ma i kabedo meno bene guwacci, ‘Lakwele mo pe yam obedo kunnu.’ “
Acakki 38:23 Juda ogamo ni, “Wek doŋ oter jami-nu obed mere, giwek nyerowa; nen, acwalo latin dyel man, ci noŋo kome aye oloyi.”
Acakki 38:24 Ka dwe adek okato, ci gitito ki Juda ni, “Ci-wodi Tamar obedo ka timme kwele kwele, ci doŋ oyac woko ki tim kwelene-ni.” Juda owacci, “Wukele woko, wek giwaŋe woko.”
Acakki 38:25 Ka gitye ka kele woko, ci en ocwalo lok bot kwarone, ni “Won jami man en aye ayac kwede.” Dok onwoyo aye ni, “Alegi ni iŋigi. Agit, ki tol ki odoo-nu jami pa aŋa kaa?”
Acakki 38:26 Juda oŋiyogi, ci otuco kun waco ni, “Dako man kite atir makata woko, pien pe amedo ki miyo en bot woda Cela.” Pe bene omedo ki bedo kwede.
Acakki 38:27 Ka kare me gonnyene oromo, ci onen ni litino rudi tye i iye.
Acakki 38:28 Ka mwoc doŋ ogoye, latin ocwalo ciŋe woko, ci lacolo otweyo uci makwar i ciŋe, kun wacci, “Man aye okwoŋo katti woko.”
Acakki 38:29 Ka doŋ oŋunyo ciŋe, odwoko cen, nen, ominne aye dok okatti woko, ci dako-nu owacci, “In doŋ ituro ki baro dye ic, ikatti woko niŋniŋ?” Mumiyo gicako nyiŋe Perej .
Acakki 38:30 Ka lacen ominne dok ginywalo kun uci makwar tye i ciŋe; ci gicako nyiŋe jera.
Acakki 39:1 Gitero Yucepu woko i Ejipt, ci Potipar ladit tic pa Parao, ma loyo askari lukurpiny, ma Laejipt, owilo en woko ki bot jo Icmael ma gutere kunnu-ni.
Acakki 39:2 Rwot yam tye ki Yucepu, ci odoko lakomegum; ocako bedo gire i ot pa laditte ma Laejipt;
Acakki 39:3 ci laditte bene oneno ni Rwot tye kwede, pien Rwot omiyo gin ducu ma en tiyo bedo maber.
Acakki 39:4 Cwiny Potipar obedo, yom i kom Yucepu, ci odoko laticce. Ocako kete obedo ladit ma loyo ode ki jamine ducu.
Acakki 39:5 Nia i kare meno ma okete obedo ladit ma loyo ode, ki lalo jamine ducu, Rwot ocako miyo gum obedo i ot pa Laejipt meno pi Yucepu; gum pa Rwot opoto i kom jami ma yam tyekwede ducu, ma i ot ki ma i poto-gu.
Acakki 39:6 Ci Potipar omiyo jami ducu i te loc pa Yucepu; pi bedo kwede omiyo doŋ pe paro gin mo, kono pi cam keken ma en camo-ni. Onoŋo Yucepu nen mabulobulo, dok mwonya matek.
Acakki 39:7 Lacen dako pa laditte cwinye ocako pyette i kom Yucepu, ci owacce ni, “Wabut kwedi.”
Acakki 39:8 Ento en okwero woko, ci owaco bot ci-laditte ni, “Nen ba, pi bedona kany omiyo laditta pe doŋ paro pi gin mo ma tye i ot-ti, dok otyeko keto gin ducu ma etye kwede i ciŋa.
Acakki 39:9 En pe doŋ tye ki dit makato an i ot man, pe tye gin mo ma dok okano ma peya omiyo i ciŋa, kono in keken, pien in i dakone. An dok acorre ka tiyo bal madit marac kuman niŋniŋ, kun atimo wa bal i kom Lubaŋa kulu?”
Acakki 39:10 Kadi bed dako meno obedo ka bito Yucepu jwijwi, pe omedo ki winyo lokke, pe oye buto kwede, kadi bedo kwede.
Acakki 39:11 Ento ka nino mo acel owec, ma, onoŋo laco mo pe i ot, ka Yucepu odonyo i ot ka tiyo ticce,
Acakki 39:12 ci dako-nu omake ki boŋone, kun wacci, “But kweda.” Ento Yucepu omwomme oweko boŋone i ciŋe, okato gire woko ki i ot.
Acakki 39:13 Ka dako-nu oneno en oweko boŋone i ciŋe, omwomme gire oka-to woko ki i ot,
Acakki 39:14 ci olwoŋo co ma gibedo i ode, ci otittigi ni, “Nenu, ladit-ti okelo Laibru-ni kany me nywarowa; obino bota i ot ni ebut kweda kulu, ci atokke adaŋŋe ki koko matek.
Acakki 39:15 Ka oneno ni atiŋo dwana malo kun agorre matek ki koko, ci otenyo ginarukane bota, ci omwomme oka-to woko ki i ot.”
Acakki 39:16 Ci opyelo boŋone ka ŋete nio ka won ot odwogo paco.
Acakki 39:17 Otitte kit lok acel-lu, kun waco ni, “Opii Laibru-ni ma ikelo i kinwa obino bota i ot ka nywara;
Acakki 39:18 ento ka atiŋo dwana oyotoyot kun adaŋŋe, ci oweko ginarukane bota, omwomme gire woko ki i ot.”
Acakki 39:19 Ka Potipar owinyo lok ma dakone olokke, ni, “Man en aye kit ma opiini otima kwede”, ci kiniga omake matek mada.
Acakki 39:20 Ocako mako Yucepu, oketo i mabuc, i kabedo ma gitweyo iye lumabuc pa kabaka, ci obedo i mabuc kunnu.
Acakki 39:21 Ento Rwot onoŋo tye ki Yucepu, ci onyutte mar mere ma pe lokke, ci omiyo en oyomo cwiny lagwok ot mabuc.
Acakki 39:22 Lagwok mabuc omiyo twer ki Yucepu me gwoko lumabuc ducu ma gitye i mabuc; gin ducu ma gitiyo kunnu, en aye loyo.
Acakki 39:23 Lagwok ot mabuc pe doŋ tamo pi gin mo ma oketo i ciŋ Yucepu, pien onoŋo Rwot tye kwede; gin ducu ma en tiyo, Rwot omiyo iye gum.
Acakki 40:1 Ka kare okato, latyer koŋo vino pa kabaka me Ejipt ki lated mugatine gubalo i nyime.
Acakki 40:2 Kiniga omako Parao i kom ludito ticce aryo-nu, ladit latyer koŋo vino ki ladit me tedo mugati,
Acakki 40:3 ci oketogi i ot pa ladit ma loyo askari lukur-piny po gwokogi, i ot mabuc ma Yucepu bene gitweye iye-ni.
Acakki 40:4 Ladit ma loyo askari lukur-piny oketogi i ciŋ Yucepu, en okurogi; ka gitweyogi i ot kol kare mo.
Acakki 40:5 Ci guleko lek i nino acel, latyer koŋo vino ki lated mugati pa kabaka me Ejipt, ma gitweyogi i ot mabuc; ŋat acel acel oleko gire lekke, kun lek acel acel tye ki tyen lokke.
Acakki 40:6 Ka Yucepu obino botgi odiko, ci onenogi kun gitye ki cwercwiny.
Acakki 40:7 Ci openyo ludito tic aryo pa Parao ma gitye kwede i ot kol i ot pa laditte, ni, “Tin waŋwu oballe woko piŋo?”
Acakki 40:8 Gugamo ni, “Tin waleko lek, ci pe tye dano mo ma gonyowa te lekke.” Yucepu owacogi ni, “Pe Lubaŋa gire aye lagony tere? Koŋ wutitta lekke mono.”
Acakki 40:9 Ci latyer koŋo vino ocako tito lekke bot Yucepu, kun wacce ni, “I waŋ lekka onoŋo olok tye i nyima,
Acakki 40:10 olok onoŋo tye ki jaŋe adek; ka pud oluro me keto: ture, ci onyak, olugo ocek woko.
Acakki 40:11 Ka amako kikopo pa Parao i ciŋa, ci aŋolo nyige, abiyo i kikopo, ka amiyo kikopo i ciŋ Parao.”
Acakki 40:12 Yucepu ogamo, owacce ni, “Man aye te lekke: jaŋe adek-ki, meno nino adek;
Acakki 40:13 i nino me adekke Parao bitiŋi ci dwoki i dog ticci, ci dok ibimiyo kikopo pa Parao i ciŋe kit macon ca, kit macalo con i kare ma in latyer koŋo vinone.
Acakki 40:14 Ento ber ipo pira ka doŋ idok i dog ticci; alegi ni in bene itima ber do, itit pira bot Parao, wek gigonya woko ki i ot man.
Acakki 40:15 Pien yam gikwala akwala ki i lobo pa jo Ibru; man bene dok giketa kany i ot kol noŋo ma pe abalo gin mo.”
Acakki 40:16 Ka ladit me tedo mugati oneno ni gigonyo te lek maber, en owaco ki Yucepu ni, “An bene onoŋo aleko lekka: onoŋo adodo aduku adek i wiya.
Acakki 40:17 I aduku mamalone ca onoŋo tye iye lwak kit gin ma gitedo ducu pi Parao, ento winyo obedo ka camogi woko ki i aduku ma tye i wiya-ni.”
Acakki 40:18 Yucepu ogamo ni, “Man aye te lekke: aduku adek en aye nino adek;
Acakki 40:19 i nino me adekke Parao bitiŋi malo, ci biŋabi i kom yat, ka winyo gibicamo riŋo komi woko.”
Acakki 40:20 Ka nino adek oromo, en aye nino ma ginywalo iye Parao, ci otedo karama ki luticce ducu, ci Parao okelo ladit latyer kono yino kacel ki ladit lated mugati i nyim luticce.
Acakki 40:21 Odwoko ladit latyer koŋo vino i dog ticce me tyero koŋo vino, ci otiŋo kikopo pa Parao omiyo i ciŋe;
Acakki 40:22 ento oŋabo: ladit lated mugati malo i kom yat kit ma nene Yucepu ogonyo kwede te lekgi.
Acakki 40:23 Ento ladit latyer koŋo vino pe omedo ki po pi Yucepu, wiye owil woko i kome matwal.
Acakki 41:1 Ka mwaka okato aryo kulu, Parao oleko lek ni onoŋo ecuŋ i ŋet kulu Nail,
Acakki 41:2 ci nen, dyaŋi abiro ma komgi pilpil ma gucwe, gubedo ka camo lum tiro.
Acakki 41:3 Dyaŋi mukene abiro dok gukatti woko ki i kulu Nail ma komgi omok, gujony woko liŋok, ma gulubo korgi, ka gucuŋ ka ŋet dyaŋi meno, ma gitye i ŋet kulu Nail.
Acakki 41:4 Dyaŋi ma komgi omok, ma gujony woko liŋok-ki gucamo dyaŋi ma komgi pilpil mucwe-ni woko. Ci Parao oco woko ki i waŋ nino.
Acakki 41:5 Ka dok onino, ci dok oleko lek mukene me aryone, oneno wit kal abiro ma ocek oluŋŋe, mabeco, ma gujany i kom tyen kai acel.
Acakki 41:6 Dok i ŋegi oneno wit kal abiro ma gulot gujany ma walgi atati, ma gubwarre woko pi yamo malyet mua ki tuŋ wokceŋ.
Acakki 41:7 Ci wite abiro ma waŋgi atati-ni gumwonyo wit kal ma ocek oluŋŋe, ma waŋgi ŋaraŋara-ni woko. Ka Parao dok oco woko ki i waŋ nino, onoŋo ni dok eleko lek aye.
Acakki 41:8 Cwinye obedo ka cwer odiko con; ci ocwalo kwena olwoŋo lutyet ki luryeko ma i Ejipt ducu. Parao otitogi lekke, ento ŋat mo pe onen ma otwero gonyo ki Parao te lekke.
Acakki 41:9 Ladit latyer koŋo vino owaco ki Parao ni, “Apo rocca tin.
Acakki 41:10 I kare ma Parao okeco i kom luticce, ci otweya i ot kol kacel ki ladit lated mugati i ot pa ladit ma loyo askari lukur-piny,
Acakki 41:11 wan ducu waleko lek i dyewor acel-lu, en ki an, waleko lek ma tyen lokgi patpat.
Acakki 41:12 Latin Ibru mo onoŋo tye kwedwa, ma obedo latic pa ladit ma loyo askari lukurpiny. Ka yam watitte, ci ogonyowa te lekwa, kun gonyo te lek pa ŋat acel acel kit ma lekke tye kwede.
Acakki 41:13 Kit ma en ogonyo te Lekwa, ci otimme kumeno; an gidwoka i dog ticca, ento lated mugati giŋabo malo i kom yat.”
Acakki 41:14 Ci Parao ocwalo kwena gilwoŋo Yucepu, gikelo woko aruya ki i ot kol; olyelo wiye, ka oloko boŋone, ci ocito odonyo bot Parao.
Acakki 41:15 Parao owaco bot Yucepu ni, “An onoŋo aleko lek, ento ŋatti mo pe onoŋŋe ma twero gonnya te lekke; abedo ka winyo ka giloko i komi ni ka iwinyo lek mo, ci itwero gonyo tere.”
Acakki 41:16 Yucepu ogamo dog Parao ni, “Meno pe a ki i iya; Lubaŋa aye bidok iye ki Parao lok me kuc.”
Acakki 41:17 Ci Parao owaco bot Yucepu ni, “Nen, iwaŋ lekka onoŋo acuŋ i ŋet kulu Nail;
Acakki 41:18 ci dyaŋi abiro mucwe ma komgi pilpil gukatti woko ki i kulu Nail, gubedo ka camo lum tiro.
Acakki 41:19 Ka dok dyaŋi mukene abiro bene gukatti woko gulubo korgi ima gigoro, komgi omok ma gujony woko liŋok, kit ma yam peya aneno i lobo me Ejipt ducu.
Acakki 41:20 Ci dyaŋi ma komgi omok ma gujony woko liŋok-ki gucamo dyaŋi abiro mucweni woko;
Acakki 41:21 ento kadi bed gucamogi woko, pe nene ni gucamogi, pien onoŋo pud gujony woko liŋok ma rom aroma ki kit ma nene gitye kwede. Ci aco woko ki iwaŋ nino.
Acakki 41:22 Dok aneno ki i waŋ Lekka wit kal abiro ma gujany i kom tyen kal acel, ma wangi ŋaraŋara mabeco;
Acakki 41:23 ka dok wite abiro muner ma wangi atati, ma gubwarre woko pi yamo malyet mua i tuŋ wokceŋ, gulot gudoŋo i ŋegi;
Acakki 41:24 ci wite ma waŋgi atati-ni gumwonyo wite abiro mabeco-ni. Ci atito bot lutyet, ento pe tye ŋatti mo ma twero gonnya tere.”
Acakki 41:25 Yucepu ogamo dog Parao owaco ni, “Lek pa Parao en lek acel; Lubaŋa doŋ onyuto ki Parao gin ma en bitiyo.
Acakki 41:26 Dyaŋi abiro mabeco-ni nyuto mwaka abiro, ki wit kal abiro mabeco bene nyuto mwaka abiro; lek aryo-nu te lokgi acel.
Acakki 41:27 Dyaŋi ma komgi otuk, ma gujony woko liŋok-ki ma dok gukatti woko gulubo korgi-ni, ki wit kal abiro mubwarre woko pi yamo malyet mua i tuŋ wokceŋ ca, meno nyuto mwaka abiro me kec.
Acakki 41:28 Tye kit macalo doŋ atito ki Parao, Lubaŋa onyuto ki Parao gin ma en bitiyo.
Acakki 41:29 Mwaka abiro bibedo ma cam bicek madwoŋ twatwal i lobo ducu me Ejipt,
Acakki 41:30 ento i ŋegi dok bibino mwaka abiro me kec, ma wi dano biwil woko i lwak camgi ma guceko i lobo Ejipt. Kec bineko lobo woko libok;
Acakki 41:31 ki lonyo cam madwoŋ-ŋi pe biŋene ni yam tye i lobo pi lok pa kec ma bilubone, pien kec meno bibedo gwa matek.
Acakki 41:32 Lek pa Parao mudodde aryo-ni nyuto ni lok man Lubaŋa aye omoko, dok bimiyo timme i kare ma cok-ki.
Acakki 41:33 “Mumiyo i kare man myero Parao oyer dano ma nen kwiri, maryek, ci oket en olo lobo Ejipt ducu.
Acakki 41:34 Dok ber Parao omedde ka keto ludito ma guloyo lobo, wek gubed ka jogo dul acel me abic me cam ma ocek i lobo Ejipt i kin mwaka abiro ma piny ocek-ki.
Acakki 41:35 Gin gubed ka guro cam ma ocek i mwaka mabeco ma cam bicek iye-ni, wek gigwok kal i te twero pa Parao, gikan me agwoka i gaŋi ducu.
Acakki 41:36 Cam meno obed dero kec me agwoka ma gigwoko i lobo Ejipt pi kec ma bipoto mwaka abiro, wek kec pe onek lobo.” Yucepu odoko lalo lobo Ejipt
Acakki 41:37 Tam man Parao oneno ni ber, kacel ki luticce ducu.
Acakki 41:38 Parao owaco ki luticce ni, “Watwero noŋo dano mukene macalo man, ma Cwiny pa Lubaŋa tye kwede bene?”
Acakki 41:39 Ci Parao owaco bot Yucepu ni, “Macalo Lubaŋa doŋ otyeko nyutti man ducu-ni, pi meno pe doŋ tye dano mo ma nen kwiri, maryek macalo in.
Acakki 41:40 In aye doŋ ibiloyo oda, ki lwakka ducu gibitiyo kun gilubo gin ma iciko; kono nyo lok ma dok i kom komker keken, en aye bimiyo abedo dit makati.”
Acakki 41:41 Parao dok owaco bot Yucepu ni, “Nen, doŋ atyeko keti me loyo lobo Ejipt ducu.”
Acakki 41:42 Ci Parao okwanyo agitte ma olunyo ki i ciŋe, orwako i ciŋ Yucepu, dok oruke ki ginaruka me boŋo camanini maber, ka dok obolo nyor jabu i ŋute;
Acakki 41:43 ka omiyo en oriŋo ki gadigadine me aryone, kun dano gidaŋŋe i nyime ni, “Rumu coŋwu!” Ci oketo en me loyo lobo Ejipt ducu kit meno.
Acakki 41:44 Parao dok omedde lok ki Yucepu kun wacce ni, “An Parao; ka in pe iye, ci pe bibedo ŋatti mo ma bitiŋo ciŋe kadi tyene i lobo ducu me Ejipt.”
Acakki 41:45 Ci Parao ocako nyiŋ Yucepu ni Japenat-panea; ci omiye Acenaci nya pa Potipera ajwaka me On me bedo dakone. Ci Yucepu ocako wot orumo lobo Ejipt ducu.
Acakki 41:46 Yucepu onoŋo doŋ mwaka me ditte romo pyeradek i kare ma donyo i tic pa Parao kabaka me Ejipt. Yucepu okato woko ki i nyim Parao, ci owoto orumo lobo Ejipt ducu.
Acakki 41:47 Cam ocek i lobo madwoŋ twatwal otyeko mwaka abiro,
Acakki 41:48 ci ocoko cam ducu ma ocek i mwaka abiro-ni i kare ma lobo Ejipt oceko cam madwoŋ, ci okano cam i dero kec i gaŋi ducu; i gaŋ acel acel en okano cam mua i potti murumo kenyo.
Acakki 41:49 Yucepu okano lwak cam madwoŋ i dero kec; cam obedo dwoŋ ma rom ki kweyo ma i dog nam, nio ka oweko pimone pien pe twero pimme.
Acakki 41:50 Ma mwaka kec peya oromo, onoŋo Yucepu doŋ tye ki litino awobe aryo, ma Acenaci nya pa Potipera ajwaka me On onywalo kwede.
Acakki 41:51 Yucepu ocako nyiŋ latin kayone ni Manace, kun wacci, “Pien Lubaŋa doŋ omiyo wiya owil woko ki i kom aromana ducu ki i kom jo ducu me ot pa wora.”
Acakki 41:52 Nyiŋ latin me aryone ocako ni Epraim, ni, “Pien Lubaŋa omiya anywal i lobo ma abedo iye ki aroma.”
Acakki 41:53 Ka mwaka abiro ma cam obedo ka cek iye madwoŋ twatwal i lobo Ejipt doŋ ogik,
Acakki 41:54 ci mwaka abiro me kec ocakke, kit ma yam Yucepu owaconi. Kec opoto i lobo ducu; ento i lobo Ejipt ducu onoŋo cam tye.
Acakki 41:55 Ka cam doŋ otum woko i lobo Ejipt ducu pi kec mupoto, dano gucako koko pi cam bot Parao; ci Parao owaco bot jo Ejipt ducu ni, “Wucit bot Yucepu wutim gin ma owacciwu.”
Acakki 41:56 Ka kec opoto oromo lobo Ejipt ducu, ci Yucepu ocako yabo dog dero kec ducu, ocato cam bot jo Ejipt, pien onoŋo kec doŋ lyet twatwal i lobo Ejipt.
Acakki 41:57 Lobo ducu gucako mol i Ejipt bot Yucepu ka wilo kal, pien onoŋo kec doŋ lyet twatwal i wi lobo ducu.
Acakki 42:1 Ka Yakobo owinyo ni kal tye i Ejipt, owaco bot awobene ni, “Piŋo wubedo ka nenne anena?”
Acakki 42:2 Ka owaco botgi ni, “Nen, an awinyo ni kal tye i Ejipt; wucit wuwilliwa kai kunnu, wek wabedu kwo, pe wato ki kec.”
Acakki 42:3 Mumiyo omegi Yucepu apar gucito i Ejipt ka wilo kal.
Acakki 42:4 Ento Yakobo pe ocwalo Benjamin, omin Yucepu, kacel ki omegine ca, pien obedo ka lworo ni gwok dok gibitime rac bene.
Acakki 42:5 Kit meno awobe pa Icrael gucito ka wil i kin jo mukene ma gicito kunnu, pien onoŋo kec oromo lobo Kanaan ducu.
Acakki 42:6 I kare meno onoŋo Yucepu odoko laloyo maber i lobo Ejipt; en obedo ka cato kal bot lwak me lobo meno. Ci omegi Yucepu bene gubino, gupoto piny aryeba cwiny i nyime, kun gukulo wangi i ŋom.
Acakki 42:7 Ka Yucepu oneno omegine, ci oŋeyogi cut, ento obedo gwa i komgi, macalo gin Lurok ata, kun gerre agera ni, “Wun wua ki kwene?” Gugamo ni, “Waa ki i lobo Kanaan, wabino ka wilo cam.”
Acakki 42:8 Kit-meno Yucepu oŋeyo omegine, ento gin pe gumedo ki ŋeye.
Acakki 42:9 Yucepu ocako po lek ma yam oleko i komgi-ni; dok owaccigi ni, “Wun lurot piny do, wun wubino ka neno lobo-ni ka kabedo mo tye noŋo.”
Acakki 42:10 Gugamo ni, “Pe kumeno Laditwa, wan luticci wabino giwa ka wilo cam.
Acakki 42:11 Wan ducu awobe pa ŋat acel, wan jo ma iwa leŋ, wan pe lurot piny.”
Acakki 42:12 Owaccigi ni, “Pe ya, wun wubino mewu ka neno kabedo mo ma tye nono.”
Acakki 42:13 Gugamo dok ni, “Wan ducu wan omego apar wiye aryo, ma awobe pa laco acel ma tye i lobo Kanaan; ci ominwa matidine odoŋ bot wonwa, ki acel aye doŋ pe.”
Acakki 42:14 Yucepu owaco ki gin ni, “Doŋ kara tye kit ma awacowu, ni wun lurot piny.
Acakki 42:15 Pi lok meno, wun doŋ gibinenowu maber kit man: macalo Parao tye makwo-ni, wun pe doŋ wubia woko i kabedo-ni, ka ominwu matidi-ni pe obino kany.
Acakki 42:16 Wucwal ŋat acel i kinwu, wek en ocikel ominwu, kun noŋo wun pud wudoŋ kany i mabuc, wek lokwu koŋ ginen maber, ka wun wutye ki ada i iwu. Ka pe, macalo Parao tye makwo-ni, wun lurot piny i ada.”
Acakki 42:17 Ci oketogi ducu i mabuc pi nino adek.
Acakki 42:18 Ka nino adek oromo, ci Yucepu owaco botgi ni, “Wutim kit man ci wubikwo, pien alworo Lubaŋa:
Acakki 42:19 ka wun jo ma iwu leŋ, wuwek ŋat acel aye gitwe odoŋ i mabuc, wek jo mukene gucit paco guter kal ki jo ma paco pi larogi ki kec,
Acakki 42:20 ka wucikel ominwu matidi-ni bota; miyo binen ni lokwu doŋ tye ada, ci pe wubito.” Ci gutimo kit meno.
Acakki 42:21 Gucako lok gigi kekengi ni, “I adane, wan woroco i kom ominwa, pien waneno cwercwinye, ka yam bako doge botwa, ci pe wamedo ki winyone; mumiyo tin can man opoto i komwa bene.”
Acakki 42:22 Reuben owacogi ni, “Yam pe atittiwu ni pe wutim bal mo i kom latin ca? Ento wun pe wumedo ki winyo, en aye mumiyo gipido pi remone i komwa-ni.”
Acakki 42:23 Pe gumedo ki niaŋ ni Yucepu winyo lokgi-ni, pien onoŋo Iadum aye tye i kingi.
Acakki 42:24 Ka oa woko ki botgi ci ocako koko; ka odok botgi obedo ka lok kwedgi. Omako
Acakki 42:25 Yucepu ociko ni doŋ gipik kal opoŋ kicaa megi, ka dok gidwok lim pa dano acel acel gipik i kicaane, dok gumi botgi peke me wotgi. Man ducu gitimo botgi.
Acakki 42:26 Ka gutweyo kal i ŋe kanagi, ci gucako wot.
Acakki 42:27 Ka ŋat acel oyabo dog kicaane i kabedo ma gibuto iye-ni, wek emi cam ki kanane, ci oneno lim giketo i dog kicaane.
Acakki 42:28 Ocako waco ki omegine ni, “Limma gidwoko kakare. Nen, tye i kicaana ene.” Ka guwinyo, ci cwinygi opoto nirim, gubedo ka cabbe kekengi ki myelkom kun giwaco ni, “Lubaŋa timowa kuman piŋo?”
Acakki 42:29 Ka gudwogo bot wongi Yakobo i lobo Kanaan, gutitte gin ducu ma otimme i komgi, kun giwaco ni,
Acakki 42:30 “Dano ma ladit me lobo-nu obedo ka lok ki gero i komwa, olokowa wadoko lurot piny.
Acakki 42:31 Ento wan watitte ni, ‘Wan jo ma iwa leŋ, wan pe lurot piny.
Acakki 42:32 Wan omego apar wiye aryo ma wonwa acel. Ominwa acel aye doŋ pe, ki acel matidine tye odoŋ bot wonwa i lobo Kanaan.’
Acakki 42:33 Ci dano meno, ladit me lobo-nu, owaco botwa ni, ‘Man aye miyo abiniaŋ ni wun jo ma iwu leŋ: wuwek ominwu acel odoŋ bota, wuter kal me laro kec i pacowu, wek wuciti.
Acakki 42:34 Wucikel ominwu matidini bota, ci doŋ abiŋeyo ni wun pe lurot piny, ento wun jo ma iwu leŋ, ci doŋ abimiyo ominwu i ciŋwu, dok wubicato wil i lobo-ni.’ ”
Acakki 42:35 Ka gitye ka onyo kal ma i kicaa megi, ci dano acel acel onoŋo lim ma nene oboyo tye i kicaane. Ka gin ki wongi guneno lim ma giboyo, ci lworo omakogi matek.
Acakki 42:36 Wongi Yakobo owaco ni, “Wutyeko litinona woko do. Yucepu doŋ pe, Cimeon bene doŋ pe, dok wumito tero Benjamin; man ducu canne poto i wiya.”
Acakki 42:37 Reuben ocako waco bot wonne ni, “Ibineko litino awobena aryo-ni ducu ka ineno pe adwoko en paco boti. Miya acit kwede, ci abikelo en paco boti.”
Acakki 42:38 Ento en ogamo, okwero woko ni, “Woda pe bicito kwedwu kunnu, pien ominne doŋ oto mere woko, en kene aye odoŋ. Ka gin marac dok otimme i kome i wotwuni, ci wubitero lwar wiya i lyel ki cwercwiny.”
Acakki 43:2 dok kal ma gikelo ki i Ejipt doŋ gucamo otum woko, wongi owaco botgi ni, “Wudok kunnu, wuciwil ki wan cam mo manok.”
Acakki 43:3 Juda ogamo doge ni, “Dano ca ocikowa matek kun waco ni, ‘Pe wubineno waŋa ka ominwu pe i kinwu.’
Acakki 43:4 Ka icwalo ominwa owoto kwedwa, ci wabicito kunnu ka willi cam;
Acakki 43:5 ento ka pe icwalo en, pe wabicito kunnu, pien dano ca owacowa ni, ‘Pe wubineno waŋa ka ominwu pe i kinwu.’ “
Acakki 43:6 Icrael owacci, “Piŋo wutima marac kuman? Piŋo dok wutito ki dano ca ni wutye ki ominwu mukene?”
Acakki 43:7 Gudok iye ni, “Dano ca openyowa ki lwak peny mapol i komwa ki i kom kakawa, kun waco ni, ‘Wonwu pud tye makwo? Ominwu mukene tye?’ Wan wadok iye i kom gin ma openyo; wan onoŋo watwero ŋeyo niŋniŋ ni en biwacci, ‘Wukel ominwu kany’?”
Acakki 43:8 Juda owaco bot wonne Icrael ni, “Mi latin i ciŋa, cwale wawot kwede, ci wabia wacito, wek wabed kwo, pe wato, wan kacel ki in ki litinowa bene.
Acakki 43:9 An abicuŋ pire; ibipenya pire. Ka ce pe abikelo en boti i kare ma adwogo, akete i nyimi, ci wek an aye abed won alii matwal;
Acakki 43:10 pien ka nene pe wagalle, kono man doŋ wawirre kunnu kiryo.”
Acakki 43:11 Ci wongi Icrael dokowaco botgi ni, “Ka doŋ myero obed kumeno ba, doŋ wutim kit man: wuter nyig yadi mogo ma wuyero me lobo-ni i kicaawu, wuter mot ki dano-nu, moo makur manok ki moo kic, odok yat ki murra, nyig otitimo ki yaa.
Acakki 43:12 Dok wuter lim ma romo culo wil tyen aryo; wutiŋ lim ma nene gidwoko giketo i dog kicaawuni; gwok nyo yam wigi owil awila.
Acakki 43:13 Wuter ki ominwu, wek wua, wucit dok bot dano-nu;
Acakki 43:14 ber Lubaŋa Matwero-ducu aye omi kica omak dano-nu i komwu, wek ocwal ominwu mukene ca ki Benjamin. Ka gityeko litinona woko, doŋ gityeka arumo do!”
Acakki 43:15 Ci gutero mot, ki wel lim ma dodo tyen aryo, kacel ki Benjamin; gua gucito i Ejipt, gucuŋ i nyim Yucepu.
Acakki 43:16 Ka Yucepu oneno ni Benjamin tye i kingi, ci owaco bot lakan jamine me ot ni, “Kel jo-nu i ot, ka inek riŋo iyubi, pien gin koni gibicam kweda dyeceŋ.”
Acakki 43:17 Dano meno otiyo kit ma Yucepu ocike, okelo jo-nu i ot pa Yucepu.
Acakki 43:18 Lworo omako omegine ka giterogi i ot pa Yucepu, guwaco ni, “Man pi lok me lim, ma nene gidwoko giketo i dog kicaawa i kare mukwoŋo ca. Mumiyo gikelowa i ot-ti, wek enoŋ lok i komwa, emakwa, wek wadok opiine, ka dok ema lwak kanawa woko.”
Acakki 43:19 Pi meno gucito bot lakan jami me ot pa Yucepu, guloko kwede ki i doggola,
Acakki 43:20 guwacce ni, “Laditta, wan wabino kany ka wilo cam i kare mukwoŋo ca;
Acakki 43:21 ka wao i kabedo ma wabuto iye-ni, wagonyo dog kicaawa, ci wanoŋo lim tye i dog kicaa pa ŋat acel acel ma i kinwa, limwa ducu onoŋo tye ki berre; en watyeko dwogo kwedeni,
Acakki 43:22 ka dok wabino ki lim me wilo cam. Pe waŋeyo ŋat ma oketolimwa i kicaawa.”
Acakki 43:23 En ogamo ni, “Wuywe ma cwinywu opye mot, pe lworo omakwu. Lubaŋa ma Lubaŋa pa wonwu en aye gwok nyo okano ki wun lim i kicaawu; an mera agamo limwu.” Ci ocito okelo Cimeon botgi.
Acakki 43:24 Dano meno oterogi i ot pa Yucepu, omiyogi pii me lwoko tyengi, ka dok omiyo cam ki kanagi.
Acakki 43:25 Guyubo motgi me atyera bot Yucepu ka bidwogo i dyeceŋ, pien guwinyo ni gibicam kunnu.
Acakki 43:26 Ka Yucepu odwogo paco, gutero motgi bote i ot, guryebbe piny i nyime.
Acakki 43:27 Openyogi ka gitye maber, kun waco ni, “Wonwu tye maber, ladit mo muti ma nene wuloko pire-ni pud tye makwo?”
Acakki 43:28 Gugamo ni, “Laticci ma wonwa tye maber, pud tye makwo.” Gukulo wigi piny, guryebbe i nyime.
Acakki 43:29 Ka otiŋo waŋe malo ci oneno ominne Benjamin, latin pa minne, owacci, “Man aye ominwu matidi-ni bo, ma nene wutitta pire-ni? Lubaŋa omini gum, latinna!”
Acakki 43:30 Yucepu okato woko oyot, pien onoŋo cwinye pukke pi ominne, ocito oyenyo ka ma myero ekok iye. Ci odonyo ka koko i kicikane.
Acakki 43:31 Ka olwoko waŋe, ci okatti woko kun diyo cwinye, owacci, “Doŋ gitok cam.”
