Lulevi 18:23 Pe ibibuto ki lee mo ma ipyedde kwede kekeni, kadi dako mo pe opyedde i kom lee mo me buta kwede; meno tim kipyeda.
Lulevi 18:24 “Pe wupyedde kekenwu i kom gin ducu, pien rok ducu ma atye ka ryemogi woko ki i nyimwu-ni gubedo ka pyedde kekengi i komgi;
Lulevi 18:25 mumiyo lobo opyedde woko, omiyo aketo can i kome pi balle, ci lobo oŋoko jo ma gibedo iye woko.
Lulevi 18:26 Ento wun myero wumak cikka ki lok ducu ma aŋolo, kun pe wutimo gin mo i kom kipyeda magi ducu, kadi anywalli me lobo, kadi larok mo ma bedo i kinwu.
Lulevi 18:27 Pien tim kipyeda meno ducu wegi lobo-ni gubedo ka timone, jo ma yam gukwoŋo nyimwu, mumiyo lobo gipyedo woko.
Lulevi 18:28 Pe wutim tim kipyeda, wek lobo pe oŋokwu woko ka wutimo tim kipyeda i kome, macalo con oŋoko kwede rok ma okwoŋo nyimwu-ni.
Lulevi 18:29 Pien jo ducu ma gutimo gin mo i kom kipyeda magi, jo ma gitimo-ni waŋgi birwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi.
Lulevi 18:30 Wumak gin ma aciko, ni, pe wunyebbe i kit me timo kipyeda macalo yam ginyebbe ka timone i nyimwu, pe wubed ka pyedde kekenwu ki kit tim macalo meno; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.”
Lulevi 19:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 19:2 “Wac bot lwak jo Icrael ducu ni, Myero wubed jo maleŋ, pien an Rwot Lubaŋawu aleŋ,
Lulevi 19:3 ŋat acel acel ma i kinwu owor minne ki wonne, doki wugwok cabitta ducu; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 19:4 Pe wulokke wudok bot cal lubaŋa-gu, pe wutim lubaŋawu me nyonyo aliya piwu kenwu; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 19:5 “Ka wutyero gitum mewu me gityer Lakwecwiny bot Rwot, wubityero i kit ma miyo Lubaŋa ye gamowu.
Lulevi 19:6 Myero wucam i nino ma wutumo iye, nyo orwone; ma odoŋ nio wa i nino me adekke gibiwaŋo awaŋa ki mac.
Lulevi 19:7 Ka ce dok pud gicamo i nino me adekke, ci bedo gin me kwer; pe doŋ gibiye gamone,
Lulevi 19:8 ŋat ma ocamo-ni bal bidok i wiye, pien opyedo gin maleŋ pa Rwot; dano meno waŋe birwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi.
Lulevi 19:9 “Ka wukayo cam ma ocek i lobowu, pe wuka woko ducu nio wa i ŋet potowu, pe dok wubed ka beko obote ma odoŋ i kare me kac.
Lulevi 19:10 Pe wupwon nyig olokwu wugwer ducu, pe bene wucok nyige ma opoto piny i poto olokwu; wubiwekogi pi konyo lucan ki lubedo; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 19:11 “Pe wukwal kwo, pe wunyebbe ka bwolo dano, pe wulok lok goba i kinwu kekenwu.
Lulevi 19:12 Pe wukwoŋ kwoŋ i nyina ki goba, ma miyo wupyedo nyiŋ Lubaŋawu; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 19:13 “Pe ibur lawoti, pe ima jamine. Pe igalle ki mucara pa lapakaca mo dyewor kulu nio wa odiko.
Lulevi 19:14 Pe iyet ladiŋit, pe iket gin mo i yo ma twomo tyen latowaŋ, ento lwor Lubaŋani; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 19:15 “Pe wuŋol kop aleŋa; pe idwor kor lacan, pe idwor dano madit, ento ŋol kop atir i kom lawoti.
Lulevi 19:16 Pe ibed ka wirre i kin lutuwu ka kwoto nyiŋgi, pe ikel lok mo ma kelo to i kom lawoti; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 19:17 “Pe ikwer omeru ki i cwinyi, ento juk lawoti ajuka, wek balle pe odok i wii.
Lulevi 19:18 Pe icul kwor, pe ibed ki akeca i kom lutuwu; ento mar lawoti macalo imarre keni; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 19:19 “Wumak cikka. Pe iye limmi onywal ki kit lee mukene; pe ico kit kodi aryo mapatpat i poto acel; pe iruk boŋo ma gicweyo ki kit uci aryo mapatpat.
Lulevi 19:20 “Ka laco mo obuto ki dako ma aŋeca ma ŋat mukene mito nyomo, ma peya gikoko gigonyo woko ki i opii, gibilaro koppe. Pe gibinekogi, pien dako onoŋo pe lone kene.
Lulevi 19:21 Laco bikelo gitum me aliine bot Rwot i doggola kema me rwatte, nyok romo me gitum me tiŋo alii.
Lulevi 19:22 Ajwaka bitimo gin lakwany bal ki i kome i nyim Rwot ki nyok romo me gitum me tiŋo alii, pi bal ma en otimo-ni, ci Lubaŋa biweko balle.
Lulevi 19:23 “Ka doŋ wuo i lobo-nu, ce wupito iye kwa yadi ducu me acama, myero wuŋe ni gijuko ni nyige peya gicamo; gibijukowu camone pi mwaka adek.
Lulevi 19:24 I mwaka me aŋwenne nyige ducu bibedo maleŋ, gibityero me lapak Rwot.
Lulevi 19:25 Ento i mwaka me abicce wutwero camo nyige, wek yadiwu gunyak ki wun nyiggi madwoŋ; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 19:26 “Pe wucam riŋo mo ma tye ki remo i kome. Pe wutyet tyet, pe wubed luyer war.
Lulevi 19:27 Pe wuko yer te wiwu, pe wulyel teŋ yer tikwu.
Lulevi 19:28 Pe wutoŋ komwu pi kwero cola, pe wuked kedo mo i komwu; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 19:29 “Pe imi nyari odok lapyeda pi timo kwele, weko lobo balle woko ki tim kwele, bimiyo lobo poŋ ki tim kipyeda.
Lulevi 19:30 Wugwok cabitta, wuwor kabedona maleŋ; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 19:31 “Pe wulokke wudok bot lukor tipo ki megi jogi, pe wucit ka yenyogi, miyo wupyedde kekenwu pi gin; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 19:32 “A malo i nyim dano ma wiye obuk lwar, wor dano ma doŋ guti, dok ilwor Lubaŋani: an a Rwot.
Lulevi 19:33 “Ka labedo mo obedo: kwedi i lobowu, pe wutime marac.
Lulevi 19:34 Labedo ma obedo kwedwu bibedo macalo latin anywalli i kinwu, ibimare macalo imarre keni; pien wun bene yam wubedo lubedo i lobo Ejipt; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 19:35 “Pe wutim rac i ŋolo kop, nyo i pimo bor me gin mo, nye pekke, nyo ditte.
Lulevi 19:36 Wubed ki mijan ma pi mo kakare, kidi lapim pek muromo kakare, aduku lapim bel muromo kakare ki agulu lapim moo muromo kakare; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu ma con akwanyowu woko ki i lobo Ejipt.
Lulevi 19:37 Wugwok cikka ki gin ma aciko ducu, wucobi; an a Rwot.”
Lulevi 20:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 20:2 “Wac bot Icrael ni, Dano mo ma i kin jo Icrael, nyo labedo ma bedo i kin jo Icrael, ma omiyo latinne mo bot jok Molek gibineko woko; lwak gibicele woko ki got.
Lulevi 20:3 An kikoma abiketo waŋa i kom dano meno, abimiyo waŋe rwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi, pien omiyo latinne bot jok Molek, kun obalo kwede kabedona maleŋ, dok opyedo nyina maleŋ.
Lulevi 20:4 Ka lwak pe guyabo wangi i kom dano meno kun en miyo latinne mo bot Molek, ce pe gumedo ki neko en,
Lulevi 20:5 ci abiketo waŋa i kom dano meno ki i kom doggolane abimiyo waŋe rwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi, en kacel ki jo ducu ma gilube pi woro jok Molek ki tim kwele kwele.
Lulevi 20:6 “Ka dano mo olokke odok bot lukor tipo ki megi jogi kun lubogi pi tim kwele kwele, abiketo waŋa i kom dano meno, abimiyo waŋe rwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi.
Lulevi 20:7 Wulonnye kekenwu wubed maleŋ, pien an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 20:8 Wugwok cikka wucobgi, pien an a Rwot ma alonyowu wudoko maleŋ.
Lulevi 20:9 Dano mo ma oceno wonne nyo minne gibineko woko; en otyeko ceno wonne nyo minne, remone dok i wiye.
Lulevi 20:10 “Ka dano mo otimo abor ki dako pa lawote, laco ki dako ma gutimo abor-ri gibinekogi woko.
Lulevi 20:11 Dano ma obuto ki ci-wonne, noŋo oketo lewic i kom wonne; gibineko gin aryo ducu, remogi dok i wigi.
Lulevi 20:12 Ka dano mo obuto ki ci-wode, gibineko gin aryo ducu, pien gutimo k ir, remogi dok i wigi.
Lulevi 20:13 Ka dano mo obuto ki laco macalo dako, gin aryo ducu gutimo gwok, gibinekogi woko, remogi dok i wigi.
Lulevi 20:14 Ka dano mo onyomo dako ci ododo ki bedoki minne bene, meno kipyeda; gibiwaŋogi woko ki mac, en ki gin mon aryo ducu, wek kipyeda pe obed i kinwu.
Lulevi 20:15 Ka dano mo obuto ki lee, gibineko woko, dok wubineko lee meno bene.
Lulevi 20:16 Ka dako mo onyiko cok ki lee ce obedo kwede, wubineko dako-nu ki lee meno; gibinekogi woko, remogi dok i wigi.
Lulevi 20:17 “Ka dano mo otero laminne, kun nya pa wonne nyo nya pa minne, ce en oneno nyime, ki nyako bene oneno kome, meno lok me lewic atika, wangi birwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi. En obedo ki laminne, bal bidok i wiye.
Lulevi 20:18 Ka dano mo obuto ki dako ma tye ki kwer, ci obedo kwede, noŋo en pe oworo remo pa dako ma cwer, dako bene lewic pe omako pi remone ma cwer-ri; gin aryo ducu wangi birwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi.
Lulevi 20:19 Pe ibed ki lamiŋ meni nyo lamiŋ woru, pien meno noŋo ibedo ki watti; balgi bidok i wigi.
Lulevi 20:20 Ka dano mo obuto ki ci-omin wonne, obedo kwede, meno no no oketo lewic i kom omin wonne; balgi bidok i wigi, gibito laboŋo latin mo.
Lulevi 20:21 Ka dano mo obedo ki ci-ominne, meno otimo kir; noŋo okelo lewic i kom ominne; gibito laboŋo latin mo.
Lulevi 20:22 “Pi meno wumak cikka ducu, ki gin ma aŋolo ducu, wucobgi, wek lobo ma atye ka terowu iye-ni pe oŋokwu woko.
Lulevi 20:23 Wun pe wulub kit pa lurok ma atye ka ryemogi woko i nyimwu-ni; pien gin gutimo gin magi ducu, mumiyo iya okwerogi woko.
Lulevi 20:24 Ento atyeko waco botwu ni, ‘Wubileyo lobogi, abimiyo botwu me bedo mewu, lobo ma mol cak ki moo kic.’ An a Rwot Lubaŋawu ma apokowu woko ki i kom rok mukene.
Lulevi 20:25 Mumiyo myero wupok kin lee ma gilony ki lee makeni, ki i kin winyo makeni ki winyo ma gilony. Pe wuballe wudok gin me kwer pi lee, nyo pi winyo, nyo pi gin mo ma corre i wi lobo, ma an doŋ atyeko pokone woko pat, ni obed keni botwu.
Lulevi 20:26 Wubed jo maleŋ pira, pien an Rwot aleŋ, doŋ atyeko pokowu woko ki i kom rok mukene ducu, wek wubed jona.
Lulevi 20:27 “Laco nyo dako mo ma lakor tipo nyo ma min jok gibineko woko; gibicelo woko ki got, remogi bidok i wigi.”
Lulevi 21:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni, “Lok ki ajwagi, awobe pa Aron, iwac botgi ni, ŋatti mo i kingi pe oballe odok keni pi gudo kom dano muto ma i kin lutugi,
Lulevi 21:2 kono nyo watgi keken ma cok kwede, macalo minne, wonne, wode, nyare, ominne,
Lulevi 21:3 nyo laminne ma peya oŋeyo co, En pud cok kwede, pien peya tye ki cware; en twero balle pire doko keni.
Lulevi 21:4 Kadi bed en won gaŋ i kin lutugi, myero pe oballe odok keni, miyo bedo kipyeda.
Lulevi 21:5 Ajwagi pe gulyel wigi, pe gulyel teŋ yer t ikgi, pe guton komgi.
Lulevi 21:6 Gubed jo maleŋ pi Lubaŋagi, pe gupyed nyiŋ Lubaŋagi, pien gin aye gityero gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot, en cam pa Lubaŋagi; pienno myero gubed jo maleŋ.
Lulevi 21:7 Pe gunyom dako ma lakwele, nyo ma doŋ tye ki meye, Gin pe gunyom dako ma cware oryemo pien ajwaka en dano maleŋ bot Lubaŋane.
Lulevi 21:8 Wubigwoke obed maleŋ pi ticce, pien en tyero cam pa Lubaŋawu; en bibedo maleŋ botwu, pien an a Rwot ma alonyowu wubed maleŋ, an bene aleŋ.
Lulevi 21:9 Ka nya pa ajwaka mo odoko lapyeda pi timo kwele, noŋo opyedo wonne; gibiwane woko ki mac.
Lulevi 21:10 “Ajwaka madit i kin omege, ma en aye gionyo moo wir i wiye, ma onoŋo gikwere wek oruk boŋŋi aruka me ticce, myero pe ogony yer wiye oket ata lijayi, pe oyec ginarukane;
Lulevi 21:11 pe odony i ot ka ma kom dano muto tye iye, pe oballe odok keni, kadi bed pi wonne nyo minne.
Lulevi 21:12 Pe okat woko nia ki i kabedo maleŋ, wek pe opyed kabedo maleŋ pa Lubaŋane, pien moo wir ma yam gikwere kwede bot Lubaŋane tye i kome; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 21:13 En myero onyom nyako ma peya oŋeyo co.
Lulevi 21:14 Pe onyom daa-to, nyo dako ma cware oryemo, nyo dako ma doŋ tye ki meye, nyo dako ma lakwele; en onyom anyira tugi ma peya oŋeyo co,
Lulevi 21:15 wek pe opyedde i kom litinone i kin lutugi; pien an a Rwot ma alonye obed maleŋ.”
Lulevi 21:16 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni
Lulevi 21:17 “Wac bot Aron ni, i kare pa likwayo wu ducu, lakwaru mo ma kome ki mwonyo pe onyik cok ka tyero cam pa Lubaŋane.
Lulevi 21:18 Pien dano ma ko me ki mwonyo pe binyiko cok bota, macalo dano ma latowaŋ, nyo laŋolo, nyo ŋat ma waŋe ki poyo, nyo ma tyene nyo bade tuŋcel laŋabu,
Lulevi 21:19 nyo ŋat ma tyene otur, nyo ma bade otur,
Lulevi 21:20 nyo dano ma kore oruŋŋe, nyo dano muran, nyo ma waŋe ocor, nyo ma twoyo gwenyo nyo nyac, nyo ma gidino mane.
Lulevi 21:21 Dano mo i kin likwayo pa ajwaka Aron ma kome ki mwonyo pe onyik cok ka tyero gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot; tekke kome ki mwonyo, pe binyiko cok ka tyero cam pa Lubaŋane.
Lulevi 21:22 En twero camo cam pa Lubaŋane, jami maleŋ makato, ki jami maleŋŋe;
Lulevi 21:23 ento pe binyiko cok ki boŋo kicika, pe bibino cok ki keno tyer, pien kome ki mwonyo, wek pe opyed kabedona ducu maleŋ-ŋi, pien an a Rwot ma alonyogi gubed maleŋ.”
Lulevi 21:24 Moses oloko kit meno bot Aron ki awo bene ki bot jo Icrael ducu.
Lulevi 22:1 Rwot dok owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 22:2 “Tit ki Aron ki awobene ni gugwokke i kom gin maleŋ pa jo Icrael ma gudyero bota, wek pe gupyed nyina maleŋ-ŋi; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 22:3 Wac botgi ni, ‘I kare pa likwayowu ducu, ka ŋatti mo ma i kin likwayowu onyiko cok ki gin maleŋ ma jo Icrael gudyero bot Rwot-ti ma kun kome ki keni, dano meno waŋe birwenyo woko ki i nyima; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 22:4 Dano mo i kin likwayo pa Aron ma ladobo, nyo ma kome cwer tut, pe ocam gin maleŋ nio ka ko me olony. Ŋatti mo ma ogudo kom gin ma odoko keni pi gudo kom dano muto, nyo dano ma kodi me co mere omol i kome,
Lulevi 22:5 nyo dano ma ogudo gin ma lak alaka ma twero miyo en doko keni, nyo ma ogudo dano ma kenine twero kobo i kome, nyo kwa gin mo ma twero miyo en doko keni;
Lulevi 22:6 dano ma ogudo gin macalo meno bibedo keni nio wa otyeno, dok pe bicamo gin maleŋ ka peya olwoko kome ki pii.
Lulevi 22:7 Ka ceŋ doŋ opoto, ci bibedo ma olony, lacen en twero camo gin maleŋ, pien en aye camme.
Lulevi 22:8 En pe ocam geŋ lee ma oto kene, nyo lee ma ŋuu omwodo, wek pe oballe kwede odok keni; an a Rwot.’
Lulevi 22:9 Gumak gin ma aciko, wek bal pe odok i wigi, ma miyo gibito ka gipyedde i kom gin ma aciko; an a Rwot ma alonyogi gubed maleŋ.
Lulevi 22:10 “Dano ata pe ocam gin maleŋ. Dano ma labedo bot ajwaka, nyo lapakaca, pe ocam gin mo maleŋ.
Lulevi 22:11 Ento ka ajwaka owilo opii ki lim, ma odoko calo gipinnye, en twero camo, ki opii ma ginywalogi i ode bene gitwero camo camme.
Lulevi 22:12 Ka dano mo mukene onyomo nya pa ajwaka, nyare-nu aye pe doŋ bicamo gin maleŋ ma gityero.
Lulevi 22:13 Ento ka nya pa ajwaka odoko daa-to, nyo cware oryemo, kun pe tye ki latin mo, ci odwogo i ot pa wonne macalo yam obedo iye ma pud tidi, twero camo cam pa wonne; ento dano ata pe ocam.
Lulevi 22:14 Ka dano mo ocamo gin mo maleŋ ma pe ocamo akaka, en bimedo acel me abic i kom welle, ci culo waŋ gin meno maleŋ bot ajwaka.
Lulevi 22:15 Ajwagi pe gupyed jami maleŋ pa jo Icrael ma gityero bot Rwot,
Lulevi 22:16 wek bal ki alii pe odok i wigi pi camo jamigi maleŋ; pien an a Rwot ma alonyogi gubed maleŋ.”
Lulevi 22:17 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni
Lulevi 22:18 “Wac bot Aron ki awo bene ki bot jo Icrael ducu ni, Ka ŋat mo ma i ot pa Icrael, nyo labedo mo ma i Icrael, miyo gityer mere, kadi obed me cobo kwoŋ, nyo gityer ma iye opwoyo ma otyero bot Rwot me gitum awaŋa,
Lulevi 22:19 ka wubikelo wod twon, nyo nyok romo, nyo nyok dyel ma kome pe ki mwonyo, Lubaŋa biye gamone.
Lulevi 22:20 Ento pe wutyer gin mo ma kome ki mwonyo, pien pe gibiye gamone piwu.
Lulevi 22:21 Ka dano mo okelo gityer lakwecwiny bot Rwot, pi cobo kwoŋ nyo pi gityer ma iye opwoyo, ma okwanyo ki i kin dyaŋi nyo i kin romi nyo dyegi, gibigamo ma komgi becone; komgi pe obed ki mwonyo mo.
Lulevi 22:22 Lee ma wane oto, nyo ma tyene otur, nyo ma oŋol, nyo ma kome cwer tut, nyo ma aŋoli omako, nyo kit two macalo meno, pe wutyer bot Rwot, pe wumigi me bedo gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot i wi keno tyer.
Lulevi 22:23 Wutwero kelo twon nyo nyok romo ma kome obedo alwaya nyo ma aduno obed gityer ma iwu opwoyo, ento pe gibigamone pi cobo kwoŋ.
Lulevi 22:24 Pe wutyer bot Rwot lee mo ma gidino mane, nyo ginyoto woko, nyo gikayo, nyo gikwanyo woko, pe wutum lee ma kit meno i lobowu.
Lulevi 22:25 Dok pe wutyer lee mo macalo meno ma wuwilo ki bot larok obed cam pa Lubaŋawu, Pe gibigamogi piwu, pien komgi ki mwonyo pi bal ma tye i komgi-ni.”
Lulevi 22:26 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 22:27 “Ka ginywalo wod twon nyo romo nyo dyel, koŋ obed bot minne pi nino abiro; nia i nino me aborone gibiye gamone me bedo gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot.
Lulevi 22:28 Kadi bed minne min dyaŋ nyo min romo, pe gibir omo neko minne ki latinne i nino acel.
Lulevi 22:29 Ka ce wutumo gityer me pwoc bot Rwot wutum i kit ma miyo giye gamowu.
Lulevi 22:30 Gicam i nino meno kikome; pe wuwek mo odoŋ nio wa odiko; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 22:31 “Kit meno wugwok cikka ducu, wucobgi; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 22:32 Pe wupyed nyiŋa maleŋ, ento jo Icrael myero guŋe ni an aleŋ; an a Rwot ma alonyowu wubed maleŋ,
Lulevi 22:33 ma ceŋ akwanyowu woko ki i lobo Ejipt wek abed Lubaŋawu; an a Rwot.”
Lulevi 23:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 23:2 “Wac bot jo Icrael ni, Nino madito ma Rwot ocikogi, ma wubituco pigi ni gubed gurre maleŋ, nino madito ma an aciko, gin ene.
Lulevi 23:3 Wubitiyo tic nino abicel, ento i nino me abirone en ceŋ cabit me yweyo mot, en aye gurre maleŋ, Pe wuti iye tic mo; en aye ceŋ cabit pa Rwot ka ma wubibedo iye ducu. Kato (Paska) ki nino madito me Mugati ma Tobi Pe Iye (Wel 28.16-25)
Lulevi 23:4 “Magi aye nino madito ma Rwot ociko, gin gurre maleŋ ma wubituco pigi i kare ma Rwot ociko pigi.
Lulevi 23:5 I dwe mukwono i nino dwe apar wiye aŋwen otyeno, en aye Kato (Paska) pa Rwot.
Lulevi 23:6 I kom nino dwe apar wiye abic me dwe acel-lu en nino madit pa Rwot me Mugati ma Tobi Pe tye; wubicamo mugati ma tobi pe iye pi nino abiro.
Lulevi 23:7 I kom nino mukwoŋone wubibedo iye ki gurre maleŋ; pe wuti iye tic mo matek.
Lulevi 23:8 Ento wubityero gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot pi nino abiro; i nino me abirone wubibedo ki gurre maleŋ, pe wuti iye tic mo matek.” Larita bel me akwata
Lulevi 23:9 Rwot dok owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 23:10 “Wac bot jo Icrael ni, Ka doŋ wuo i lobo ma abimiyowu, ka wukayo iye kac, ci wubikelo wic larita cam me wi mwaka bot ajwaka.
Lulevi 23:11 En bikwato wic larita cam i nyim Rwot, wek oye gamowu; ajwaka bikwato i nino ma lubo cabit.
Lulevi 23:12 I nino ma wubikwato iye wic larita-ni, en aye wubityero iye latin nyok romo ma ditte romo mwaka acel, ma kome pe ki mwonyo, obed gitum awaŋa bot Rwot.
Lulevi 23:13 Gityer me moko kwon ma wutyero kacel kwede bibedo moko kwon mapwotte ma romo agwata aryo, ma girubo ki moo, ma gibityero kun giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot obed gin ma ŋwece kur me yomo cwiny. Gityer amatane bibedo vino ma romo cupa aryo kt nucu.
Lulevi 23:14 Pe wucam mugati, pe wumwod nyig bel ma gicelo nyo manumo, nio wa i nino meno kikome, waŋ ma wukelo gityer pa Lubaŋawu; meno bibedo cik matwal wa i kare pa likwayowu ducu, ikabedo ducu ma wubibedo iye. Pwoyo kac (Wel 28.26-31)
Lulevi 23:15 “Ka doki wubikwano cabit abiro kulu kun wucako ki nino ma lubo cabit, en aye nino ma wutyero iye wic larita cam me gityer akwata.
Lulevi 23:16 Wukwan nino pyerabic nio i nino ma lubo cabit me abirone, ka doŋ wucak kelo gityer me moko kwon kai manyen bot Rwot.
Lulevi 23:17 Wubikelo ki i kabedowu mugati aryo me akwata ma gitedo ki moko ma romo agwata aryo; gibitedogi ki moko mapwotte ma onoŋo girubo iye tobi, gubed wi mwaka ma gityero bot Rwot.
Lulevi 23:18 Dok wubikelo litino romi abiro kacel ki mugati meno ma ditogi mwaka acel acel, ma komgi pe ki mwonyo, ki wod twon acel ki nyogi romi aryo. Gibibedo gitum awaŋa bot Rwot, kacel ki gityer me moko kwon ki gityer amata mutikogi; gin gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac, gin ma ŋwece kur me yomo cwiny Rwot.
Lulevi 23:19 Dok wubityero nyok dyel acel obed gitum me bal, ki litino nyogi romi aryo ma ditogi mwaka acel acel gubed gityer Lakwecwiny.
Lulevi 23:20 Ajwaka bikwatogi kacel ki mugati me wi mwaka gubed gityer akwata i nyim Rwot, kacel ki litino nyogi romi aryo-nu; gibibedo maleŋ bot Rwot, pi ajwaka.
Lulevi 23:21 I nino meno kikome wubibedo ki gurre maleŋ ma wutito pire ka maleŋ; pe wuti iye tic mo matek. Meno bibedo cik matwal wa i kare pa likwayowu ducu, i kabedo ducu ma wubibedo iye.
Lulevi 23:22 “Ka wukayo cam ma ocek i lobowu, pe wuka woko ducu nio wa i ŋet potowu, pe dok wubed ka beko obote ma odoŋ i kare me kac. Wubiwekogi pi konyo lucan ki lubedo; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.”
Lulevi 23:23 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni
Lulevi 23:24 “Wac bot jo Icrael ni, I dwe me abiro, i nino dwe acel, wubikwero iye nino me yweyo mot, nino me po ma gituco pire ki koko gwara, nino me gurre maleŋ.
Lulevi 23:25 Pe wuti iye tic mo matek, dok wubityero iye gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot.”
Lulevi 23:26 Rwot dok owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 23:27 “I nino dwe apar me dwe man me abiro-ni en aye bedo nino me Kwanyo Bal. Bibedo botwu nino me gurre maleŋ; wubikumo ki toncwiny, dok wubityero gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot.
Lulevi 23:28 Pe wuti tic mo i nino meno, pien en aye nino me kwanyo bal, pi timo gin lakwany bal ki i komwu i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 23:29 Ŋat ma pe okumo ki toncwiny i nino meno wane birwenyo woko ki i kin lutugi.
Lulevi 23:30 Ŋat ma otiyo tic mo i nino meno abineko woko wek pe obed i kin lutugi.
Lulevi 23:31 Pe wuti iye tic mo; meno bibedo cik matwal wa i kare pa likwayowu ducu, i kabedo ducu ma wubibedo iye.
Lulevi 23:32 En aye bibedo botwu cabit me yweyo mot, ci wubikumo iye ki toncwiny, i nino dwe aboŋwen cakke otyeno nio wa orwone otyeno en aye wubiywe mot.”
Lulevi 23:33 Rwot dok owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 23:34 “Wac bot jo Icrael ni, I nino dwe apar wiye abic me dwe man me abiro-ni en aye bibedo acakki me nino madito pa Rwot, kare me Bolo, ci tyeko nino abiro.
Lulevi 23:35 I kom nino mukwoŋo wubibedo iye ki gurre maleŋ; pe wuti iye tic mo matek.
Lulevi 23:36 Wubityero gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot pi nino abiro. I nino me aborone wubibedo iye ki gurre maleŋ, ma wubityero iye gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot; meno cokke madit me woro Lubaŋa, pe wuti iye tic mo matek.
Lulevi 23:37 “Magi aye nino madito ma Rwot ociko, ma wubitito ki lwak ni gin aye kare me gurre maleŋ, pi tyero bot Rwot gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac, gitum awaŋa, gityer me moko kwon, gitum mukene, ki gityer amata, kun acel acel bedo ki ninone ma otike,
Lulevi 23:38 kun wumedogi i kom ceŋ cabit pa Rwot me kare ducu, ki i kom mot mewu, i kom gityer mewu ducu me cobo kwoŋ, ki i kom gityerwu ducu ma iwu opwoyo ma wumiyo bot Rwot.
Lulevi 23:39 “I kom nino dwe apar wiye abic me dwe me abiro, ka doŋ wucoko cam ma ocek i lobo, wubikwero nino madito pa Rwot pi nino abiro; nino mukwoŋo bibedo nino me yweyo mot, ki nino me aborone bene bibedo nino me yweyo mot.
Lulevi 23:40 I nino mukwoŋo wubicoko iye nyig yat mabecone, ki jaŋ otit, ki jaŋ yat muluk, ki yat oget ma i ŋet kulu; ci wubibedo ki yomcwiny i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu pi nino abiro.
Lulevi 23:41 Wubikwero nino madito man pa Rwot pi nino abiro mwaka ki mwaka; meno bibedo cik matwal wa i kare pa likwayowu ducu; wubikwerone i dwe me abiro.
Lulevi 23:42 Wubibedo i bolo pi nino abiro; litino anywalli ducu ma i Icrael bibedo i bolo,
Lulevi 23:43 wek likwayowu guŋe ni, yam amiyo jo Icrael gubedo i bolo i kare ma akwanyogi woko ki i lobo Ejipt; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.”
Lulevi 23:44 Kit meno Moses otito bot jo Icrael pi nino madito ducu ma Rwot ociko pigi.
Lulevi 24:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 24:2 “Cik jo Icrael gukel boti moo me nyig jeituni ma giodo aoda, giliyo maber, me mac tara, wek giket mac laput obed ka lyel nino ducu ma pe to.
Lulevi 24:3 Aron myero ocaŋ mac olyel jwijwi i nyim Rwot nia otyeno nio odiko, ki woko i ŋe boŋo kicika ma umo canduk lok me caden, i kema me rwatte; meno bibedo cik matwal wa i kare pa likwayowu ducu.
Lulevi 24:4 En bicano laput kakare i wi okar-mac me jabu ma giliyo maber i nyim Rwot jwijwi. Mugati me aketa i nyim Rwot
Lulevi 24:5 “Dok ibikwanyo moko mapwotte, ibitedo kwede capat apar wiye aryo, kun i capat acel acel bedo iye agwata moko aryo.
Lulevi 24:6 Ibicanogi latyeŋ aryo kun iryeyogi abicel abicel i wi meja me jabu ma giliyo maber-ri.
Lulevi 24:7 I kom tyen acel acel ibiketo iye odok luban ma giliyo maten, wek obed gin me po i kom mug ati-nu, gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot.
Lulevi 24:8 I ceŋ cabit ducu Aron biryeyogi jwijwi i nyim Rwot kun gamo ki bot jo Icrael; en gicikke ma bedo matwal.
Lulevi 24:9 Bibedo pi Aron ki awobene: gibicamo i kabedo mo maleŋ, pien en gin maleŋ makato ma gimiye ki i kin gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot ma myero gimi bote dikdik.” Yeto nyiŋ Lubaŋa ki cik ma mako culo waŋ bal
Lulevi 24:10 Ceŋ mo wod pa nya jo Icrael mo ma wonne onoŋo Laejipt, okato woko i kin jo Icrael, ci ocako lwenyo ki dano mo ma Laicrael i gony.
Lulevi 24:11 Wod pa nya jo Icrael meno ocako yeto nyiŋ Lubaŋa kun ceno bene, ci gitere bot Moses. Nyiŋ minne Celomit, nya pa Dibri, ma i kaka pa Dan.
Lulevi 24:12 Ci gikete i ot kol, nio ka Rwot binyuto botgi gin ma en mito.
Lulevi 24:13 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 24:14 “Kel ŋat ma oceno cen woko i ŋe gony, jo ducu ma guwinyo lokke guket ciŋgi i wiye, ci wek lwak ducu gucele woko ki got.
Lulevi 24:15 Ka dok iwac ki jo Icrael ni, ŋat ma oceno Lubaŋane, balle bidok i wiye.
Lulevi 24:16 Ŋat ma oyeto nyiŋ Rwot gibineko woko; lwak ducu gibicele woko ki got; labedo kacel ki anywalli me lobo, ka oyeto Nyiŋ meno gibineke woko.
Lulevi 24:17 Ŋat ma oneko dano gibineke bene.
Lulevi 24:18 Ŋat ma oneko lee biculo acula; kwo giculo ki kwo.
Lulevi 24:19 Ka ŋat mo oketo ŋolo i kom lawote, en bene gibitime kit meno;
Lulevi 24:20 turo cogo giculo ki turo cogo, waŋ giculo ki waŋ, lak giculo ki lak; kit macalo oketo ŋolo i kom dano mo-ni, en bene gibiketo ŋolo i kome.
Lulevi 24:21 Ŋat ma oneko lee biculo acula; ŋat ma oneko dano gibineke woko.
Lulevi 24:22 Cik bibedo acel pi labedo ki pi anywalli me lobo; pien an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.”
Lulevi 24:23 Moses ocako lok ki jo Icrael, ci gutero dano ma oceno cen woko i ŋe gony, gucele woko ki got. Kit meno jo Icrael gutiyo kit ma Rwot ociko ki Moses.
Lulevi 25:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses i wi got Cinai ni,
Lulevi 25:2 “Wac bot jo Icrael ni, Ka doŋ wuo i lobo ma abimiyowu-ni, lobo bigwoko cabit pa Rwot.
Lulevi 25:3 Wubicoyo pottiwu mwaka abicel, wubiŋolo kin jaŋ olokwu mwaka abicel, wubicoko nyige;
Lulevi 25:4 ento mwaka me abirone en aye bibedo cabit me yweyo mot pi lobo, en cabit pa Rwot; pe wubicoyo pottiwu, pe wubiŋolo kin jaŋ olokwu.
Lulevi 25:5 Gin ma otwi kene i okaŋ pe wubikayo, pe wubicoko nyig olokwu ma pe wuŋolo kin jaŋe; bibedo mwaka me yweyo mot pi lobo.
Lulevi 25:6 Cabit man me lobo bimiyowu cam, in ki opiini ki aŋecani ki lapakacani ki labedo ma bedo boti.
Lulevi 25:7 Pi lim mewu makwo bene, ki pi lee ducu ma gitye i lobowu, gin ma cek iye ducu bedo me acamagi.
Lulevi 25:8 “Dok ibikwano cabit abiro me mwaka bene, mwaka abiro tyen abiro; kare meno me cabit abiro me mwaka bibedo mwaka pyeraŋwen wiye aboŋwen.
Lulevi 25:9 I mwaka meno ibimiyo gwara kok maloŋo i kom nino dwe apar me dwe me abiro; i nino me kwanyo bal en aye wubimiyo gwara kok romo lobowu ducu.
Lulevi 25:10 Wubikwero mwaka me pyerabic obed maleŋ, kun wutito i lobowu ducu ni kuc tye pi jo ducu ma bedo iye, En aye bibedo kare me jubili mewu, ma noŋo ŋat acel acel i kinwu dok gire i dul lobone, dok ŋat acel acel i kinwu bidok i doggolagi.
Lulevi 25:11 Mwaka me pyerabicce aye bibedo jubili mewu; pe wubicoyo iye kodi, pe wubikayo gin ma otwi kene, pe wubicoko nyig olok ma pe wuŋolo kin jaŋe.
Lulevi 25:12 Pien obedo jubili, bibedo maleŋ botwu; wubicamo gin ma oa ki i poto.
Lulevi 25:13 “I mwaka man me jubili-ni ŋat acel acel i kinwu bidok i dul lobone.
Lulevi 25:14 Ka icato lobo mo bot lawoti, nyo iwilo lobo mo ki bote, pe wubed ka bune kekenwu.
Lulevi 25:15 Ka iwilo ki bot lawoti, welle biporo wel mwaka mulubo jubili; en bicato boti kun poro wel mwaka ma ibinoŋo iye cam.
Lulevi 25:16 Ka mwaka pud odoŋ mapol, ibimedo wel ma iculo, ka mwaka doŋ odoŋ manok, ci ibidwoko welle piny, pien gin ma en tye ka cato boti en aye mwaka me cam ma bia iye.
Lulevi 25:17 Pe wubune kekenwu, ento wulwor Lubaŋawu; pien an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 25:18 “Pi meno wubilubo cikka, wubigwoko gin ma aŋolo, wubicobone, wek wubed ma lobo okwe mot.
Lulevi 25:19 Pien lobo biceko cam, wubicamo, wubiyeŋ kwede, ci wubibedo ma piny okwe mot.
Lulevi 25:20 Ka ce wuwacci, ‘Wabicamo mono gin aŋo i mwaka me abiro-nu, ka ce pe wacoyo kodi, dok pe wacoko camwa ma a iye?’
Lulevi 25:21 An abiciko gumma poto i komwu i mwaka me abicelle, wek onyak nyige ma romo pi mwaka adek kulu.
Lulevi 25:22 Ka wucoyo potowu i mwaka me aborone, noŋo pud wutye ka camo cam macon ca; nio wa i mwaka me aboŋwen i kare ma cam doŋ ocek, gikayo, noŋo pud wucamo en macon ca.
Lulevi 25:23 Lobo pe gibicato me atera woko matwal, pien lobona gira; pien wun wuwelo, dok wun lubedona.
Lulevi 25:24 I lobo ducu ma bibedo mewu wubiye ni giwar lobo.
Lulevi 25:25 “Ka ce omeru odoko lacan, ce ocato lobone mo ci watgi macok aye bibino ka waro lobo meno ma ominne ocato woko-ni.
Lulevi 25:26 Ka dano meno pe tye ki watgi mo ma twero warone, ce en kikome odoko lalonyo, ka onoŋo gin ma romo warone,
Lulevi 25:27 wek en okwan wel mwaka nia i kare ma ocato, ocul bot dano ma owilo-nu wel ma pud odon, ci potone bidok i ciŋe.
Lulevi 25:28 Ento ka pe tye ki lim ma romo dwokone i ciŋe, ci poto ma ocato-nu bidoŋ i cin lawilone nio ka mwaka me jubili oromo; gibidwoko potone i kare me jubili, bidok i ciŋe.
Lulevi 25:29 “Ka dano mo ocato ode ma tye i gaŋ madit ma gicelo ki cel, en twero warone ma peya mwaka acel oromo; bibedo ki twer me warone kadi pi mwaka kulu.
Lulevi 25:30 Ka pe giwaro ma peya mwaka acel oromo, ci ot meno ma tye i gaŋ madit ma gicelo-ni gibimoko ni doŋ bedo pa ŋat muwilo-ni matwal, wa i kare pa likwayone ducu; pe gibidwoko i kare me jubili.
Lulevi 25:31 Ento odi ma i caro ata ma pe gicelo ki cel ma orumogi gibikwanogi kacel ki potti ma i caro; gitwero warogi, dok gibidwokogi ceŋ i kare me jubili.
Lulevi 25:32 “I gaŋi pa Lulevi odi ma i gaŋi ma gimiyogi me bedo megi-ni Lulevi gitwero warogi i kare ducu.
Lulevi 25:33 Ka ce ŋat mo i kin Lulevi pe owaro, ci ot ma gicato i gaŋ mo ma omiyogi obed megi bidok bot rwode i kare me jubili, pien odi ma i gaŋ pa Lulevi meno jami megi ma gimiyogi i kin jo Icrael.
Lulevi 25:34 Ento olet ma orumo gaŋi megi pe gicato; meno lobogi matwal.
Lulevi 25:35 “Ka ce omeru ma bedo ka ŋeti odoko lacan ma pe twero konnye kekene, in ibikonye; en bibedo boti macalo weloni nyo labedo.
Lulevi 25:36 Pe igam lim mo me magoba ki bote nyo pe imed wiye, ento lwor Lubaŋani, wek omeru obed kwo ki ka ŋeti.
Lulevi 25:37 Pe ibimiyo en mako banya boti wek inoŋ iye magoba, pe imiye cam wek odwok boti kun omedo wiye.
Lulevi 25:38 An a Rwot Lubaŋawu ma yam akwanyowu ki i lobo Ejipt wek amiwu lobo Kanaan, abed Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 25:39 “Ka omeru ma bedo ka ŋeti odoko lacan, ci ocatte boti kekene, pe ibimiyo en tiyo boti macalo opii;
Lulevi 25:40 en bibedo boti macalo lapakaca nyo labedo. En bitic boti nio wa i mwaka me jubili;
Lulevi 25:41 ka lacen en bia woko ki boti, en kacel ki litinone bene. Bidok cen i doggolane, bidok i lobo pa kwarogi.
Lulevi 25:42 Pien gin luticca ma yam akwanyogi woko ki i lobo Ejipt; pe gibicatogi me bedo opii.
Lulevi 25:43 Pe ibiloyo en ki loc magwa, ento ibilworo Lubaŋani.
Lulevi 25:44 “Lok i kom opiini ki aŋecani ma ibibedo kwedgi; itwero wilo opii ki aŋeca ki bot lurok ma orumo ka ŋetwuni.
Lulevi 25:45 Wutwero wilo ki i kin lubedo ma bedo botwu, dok ki i kin doggolagi ma bedo botwu, ma ginywalogi i lobowu; gibidoko limwu.
Lulevi 25:46 Wutwero miyogi bot litino awobewu ma bilubowu, gubed ginaleyagi matwal. Wutwero miyogi gibedo opiiwu, ento omegiwu ma jo Icrael pe wubiloyogi kit meno kun ŋat man loyo wadi ki loc magwa.
Lulevi 25:47 “Ka welo mo nyo labedo mo ma tye boti odoko lalonyo, kun omeru ma tye ka ŋete odoko lacan, ci ocatte kekene bot welo nyo labedo ma tye boti-ni, nyo ocatte bot wat ma i doggola pa welo meno,
Lulevi 25:48 ka doŋ otyeko catte, ci gitwero koko; ŋat mo ma i kin omege twero koke woko.
Lulevi 25:49 Nyo omin wonne nyo latin pa omin wonne twero koke, nyo watgi mo ma i doggolagi twero koke; nyo ka en odoko lalonyo, ci kokke gire kene.
Lulevi 25:50 En bikwano wel kacel ki ŋat ma con owile-nu, kun cako i mwaka ma yam owile iye nio wa i jubili, Wel me gonye bibedo ma poro wel mwaka; kare ma en obedo kwede bot rwode gibikwano macalo kare pa lapakaca.
Lulevi 25:51 Ka ce mwaka pud odoŋ mapol, en biculo lim me koke ma oporo ki wel mwaka, kun kwanyo ki i kom wel lim ma yam giwile kwede.
Lulevi 25:52 Ka pud odoŋ mwaka manok mo i mwaka me jubili, en bikwano wel ki dano ma owile-nu; ci biculo lim me koke ma oporo wel mwaka me ticce ma pud odon.
Lulevi 25:53 En bibedo bot rwode macalo lapakaca ma giculo mwaka ki mwaka; pe gibiloye ki loc magwa kun in ineno.
Lulevi 25:54 Ka ce pe gikoke i kit yo meno, ci gibigonye i mwaka me jubili, en kacel ki litinone bene.
Lulevi 25:55 Pien jo Icrael gin aye lutic ma tuŋ ciŋa; gin aye luticca ma yam akwanyogi woko ki i lobo Ejipt; an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 26:1 “Pe wutim piwu kenwu cal lubaŋa mo, pe wucib cal apaya nyo wir jok mo, pe wucib got mo ma gigoro cal i kome ocuŋ i lobowu pi ryebbe i nyime, pien an a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Lulevi 26:2 Wubigwoko cabitta dok wubiworo ot mera maleŋ; an a Rwot.
Lulevi 26:3 “Ka wubilubo cikka kun wugwoko gin ma aciko ducu, wucobo kakare,
Lulevi 26:4 an abimiyowu kot ma cwer i karene, lobo biceko cam, yadi ma i poto binyako nyiggi.
Lulevi 26:5 Kare me dino kalwu bidikke olo wa i kare me pwono otok, pwono olok bene bidikke nio wa i kare me coyo kodi. Wubicamo cam ma romowu, doŋ, ci wubibedo i lobowu ma piny okwe mot.
Lulevi 26:6 Abimiyo kuc bedoi lobo, wubibuto piny, dano ma miyowu lworo bibedo pe. Abikwanyo ŋuu woko ki i lobo, pala lucwan pe biwok ki i lobowu.
Lulevi 26:7 Wubiryemo lumerok mewu, gibito i nyimwu ki palawu.
Lulevi 26:8 Jo abic ki i komwu gibiryemo jo miya kulu, jo miya ki i komwu biryemo jo alip apar; lumerokwu gibito i nyimwu ki palawu.
Lulevi 26:9 Abiparo piwu, abimiyo wunywal, wunya, dok abimoko gicikkena kwedwu.
Lulevi 26:10 Wubicamo cam macon i derowu pi kare malac, wubionyo maconne woko wek kabedo odoŋ pi manyenne.
Lulevi 26:11 Abiyubo kabedona i kinwu, tipo koma pe bikwerowu.
Lulevi 26:12 Abibedo ka wot i kinwu, abibedo Lubaŋawu, wun bene wubibedo jona.
Lulevi 26:13 An a Rwot Lubaŋawu ma yam akwanyowu ki i lobo Ejipt wek pe wubed opiigi; aturo rii okol ma giriyo i ŋutwu, amiyowu wutirre, wuwot atir. Can ma bino pi balo cik (Nwo 28.15-68)
Lulevi 26:14 “Ento ka pe wubiwinya, ka pe wubilubo cik magi ma aketo ducu,
Lulevi 26:15 ka ce wucayo cikka, ka iwu okworo gin ma aŋolo, ma miyo pe wubicobo gin ma aciko ducu, ento wuturo gicikkena,
Lulevi 26:16 ci abitimowu kit man: abimiyo lworo poto i komwu atura, ki aona opiyo, ki aburu ma coro waŋwu kun balo komwu woko. Dok wubicoyo kodiwu noŋo, pien lumerok gibicamo.
Lulevi 26:17 Abiketo waŋa i komwu, merok bigoyowu ki i nyimgi; jo ma gidagwu aye gibiloyowu; dok wubiriŋo ata ma kun ŋat mo pe ma ryemo korwu.
Lulevi 26:18 Ka pe wuwinyo lokka kadi bed atimo kumeno, ci abimedde ki keto can i komwu tyen abiro pi balwu.
Lulevi 26:19 Abituro tek me wakkewu woko, abimiyo polo bedo tek macalo nyonyo, ki lobowu bene bedo tek macalo mola.
Lulevi 26:20 Wubityeko tek komwu nono pien lobowu pe biceko cam, ki yadi bene pe gibinyako nyiggi.
Lulevi 26:21 “Ka wun wukemo an marac, ma pe wuwinyo lokka, ci abimedde ki kelo two mapek i komwu, ma romo lwak balwu tyen abiro.
Lulevi 26:22 Dok abicwalo ŋuu me tim i kinwu, ma bimako litinowu, ma bityeko lim makwo ma i ciŋwu, ci bijwikowu wudoko jo manok, wa yowu birido woko.
Lulevi 26:23 “Ka pe wujukke, wudwogo bota pi kit can meno, kun pud wukemo an marac aye,
Lulevi 26:24 an bene abikemowu marac, ci an ki koma abipwodowu tyen abiro pi balwu.
Lulevi 26:25 Abikelo pala lucwan i komwu me lacul kwor me balo gicikkena, Ka wugurre i gaŋwu, abicwalo two gemo magwa i kinwu, ci gibimiyowu i ciŋ lumerokwu.
Lulevi 26:26 Ka abikwanyo cam ma wukwo kwede woko, ci mon apar gibitedo mugatiwu i keno acel, dok gibipokowu mugati kun gipimowu apima; ka wubicamo; pe biyeŋowu.
Lulevi 26:27 “Ka pe wuwinyo lokka kadi bed atimo kumene, ento pud wukemo an marac,
Lulevi 26:28 ci an bene abikemowu malyet, kun an kikoma aketo can i komwu tyen abiro pi balwu.
Lulevi 26:29 Wubicamo riŋo kom litino awobewu ki riŋo kom anyirawu.
Lulevi 26:30 Abituro waŋ jogiwu ma i wi godi, abitoŋo keno tyerwu me odok eceta, kun abolo komwu ma oto i kom kom muto me cal lubaŋawu, ci tipo koma bikwerowu woko.
Lulevi 26:31 Abijwero gaŋwu woko ducu, abimiyo kabedowu ducu maleŋ doŋ noŋo, pe dok abiŋweyo ginwu ma ŋwece kur me yomo cwiny.
Lulevi 26:32 Abineko lobowu woko, wek lumerokwu ma bibedo iye gubed ki ur pire.
Lulevi 26:33 Abikeyowu i kin lurok, ci abiwoto pala lucwan ki i akura me lubo korwu, miyo lobowu bidoŋ noŋo cut, ki gaŋiwu bene gibidoŋ obur.
Lulevi 26:34 “I kare meno lobo bikwero cabitte pi kare ducu ma noŋo pud giweko ata-ni, kun wun pud wutye i lobo pa lumerokwu. I kare meno lobo biywe, kun noŋo tye ka kwero karene me yweyo mot macalo i ceŋ cabit.
Lulevi 26:35 Pi kare ma pud giweko ata-ni koŋ biywe, ki yweyo ma naka yam en pe onoŋo i cabitwu i kare ma onoŋo wun wubedo iye.
Lulevi 26:36 Jo ma i kinwu ma bidoŋ abicwalo lworo i cwinygi i lobo pa lumerokgi, miyo gibiriŋo dwan pot oboke keken ma yamo yeŋo. Gibiriŋo macalo ŋat ma riŋo pala lucwan, ci gibipoto piny kun ŋat mo pe ma ryemo korgi.
Lulevi 26:37 Gibiyokke kekengi ŋat man i kom lawote, macalo giriŋo lak pala lucwan, kadi bed ŋat mo pe ma ryemo korgi: pe wubibedo ki twero me cun i nyim lumerokwu.
Lulevi 26:38 Wubitum woko ki i kin lurok, lobo pa lumerokwu bicamo komwu woko ducu.
Lulevi 26:39 Jo ma i kinwu ma bidoŋ, komgi bilwal woko i lobo pa lumerokwu pi bal megi; dok pi bal pa kwarogi bene komgi bilwal woko macalo gin.
Lulevi 26:40 “Ento ka gibituco balgi ki bal pa kwarogi pi tim roro ma gutimo i koma, dok pi kemo an marac,
Lulevi 26:41 ma omiyo an bene akemogi marac kun aterogi i lobo pa lumerokgi; ka gibedo jo ma gulirre i cwinygi, pe i komgi keken, ci gidoko mwol ma giculo ka waŋ balgi,
Lulevi 26:42 ka doŋ abipo pi gicikkena ma acikke ki Yakobo, abipo pi gicikkena ki Icaka ki gicikkena ki Abraim, dok abipo pi lobogi.
Lulevi 26:43 Ento lobo bidoŋ ma gin jona pe iye, bigwoko cabitte ducu ma kun noŋo pud giweko woko ata ma dano pe iye. Ci gibiculo ka waŋ balgi, pien gubedo ka cayo gin ma aciko, dok tipo komgi okwero cikka.
Lulevi 26:44 Ento kadi bed kumeno, ka pud noŋo gitye i lobo pa lumerokgi, pe abicayogi, tipo koma pe bikwerogi ma romo miyo atyekogi woko liweŋ kun aturo gicikkena kwedgi, pien an a Rwot Lubaŋagi.
Lulevi 26:45 Pi gin weko abipo pi gicikkena ma acikke ki kwarogi ma yam akwanyogi woko ki i lobo Ejipt ma rok ducu gineno, wek abed Lubaŋagi; an a Rwot.”
Lulevi 26:46 Magi aye cik ki gin ma Rwot oŋolo, ki cik ma en oketo i kin en ki jo Icrael i wi got Cinai ki i dog Moses.
Lulevi 27:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Lulevi 27:2 “Wac bot jo Icrael ni, Ka dano mo okwoŋo kwoŋ ma pire tek ma otiko kom dano bot Rwot, ma myero in iŋol welle,
Lulevi 27:3 ci wel ma iŋolo pi laco ma mwaka me ditte romo pyeraryo o-wa i pyerabicel bibedo cekel me ryal pyerabic, ma giporo ki cekel me kabedo maleŋ.
Lulevi 27:4 Ka ce dano meno ma kwon otiko obedo dako, ci ibiŋolo wel me cekel pyeradek.
Lulevi 27:5 Ka mwaka me ditte romo abic o wa i pyeraryo, ibiŋolo pi laco cekel pyeraryo, pi dako cekel apar.
Lulevi 27:6 Ka ce ditte romo dwe acel o wa i mwaka abic, ibiŋolo cekel me ryal abic pi laco, cekel me ryal adek pi nyako.
Lulevi 27:7 Ka mwaka me ditte romo pyerabicel nyo makato, ibiŋolo cekel apar wiye abic pi laco, pi dako apar.
Lulevi 27:8 Ka ce dano mo lacan twatwal, ma pe twero miyo wel ma iŋolle, ci en bitero dano ma gikwoŋo pire-ni i nyim ajwaka ci ajwaka aye biŋolle wel, kun lubo gin ma dano ma okwoŋo kwoŋ-ŋu twero noŋone.
Lulevi 27:9 “Ka ce kwoŋ otiko lee mo ma gityero me bedo gityer bot Rwot, lee ducu ma kit meno ma dano miyo bot Rwot bedo maleŋ.
Lulevi 27:10 En pe bilokone woko ki gin mukene, nyo gwenyo loko ki wadi mo, maberre ki maracce, nyo maracce ki maberre; nyo ka en oloko lee mo ki lee wadi, ci gin aryo ducu ma gilokogi-ni gibibedo maleŋ.
Lulevi 27:11 Ka ce obedo lee mo ma keni, ma pe gityero me bedo gityer bot Rwot, ci dano meno bitero lee-nu i nyim ajwaka.
Lulevi 27:12 Ajwaka biŋolo welle, kadi lee-nu ber kadi rac; macalo in ajwaka iŋolo welle, ci bicuŋ kit meno.
Lulevi 27:13 Ento ka en mito kokone woko, en bimedo acel me abic i kom welle.
Lulevi 27:14 “Ka dano mo onyero ode obed maleŋ bot Rwot, ci ajwaka biŋolo welle, ka ber ka rac; ka ajwaka oŋolo welle, ci bicuŋ kit meno.
Lulevi 27:15 Ka ce ŋat ma odyero ode-ni mito warone woko, en bimedo acel me abic i kom welle ci bidok bote.
Lulevi 27:16 “Ka dano mo odyero but lobone bot Rwot ki i kom lobo ma oleyo ki bot kwarone, ci ibiŋolo welle kun poro kodi ma gitwero coyo iye; ka romo coyo iye kodi cayiri guniya adek, Gibiŋolo iye cekel me ryal pyerabic.
Lulevi 27:17 Ka en odyero potone i mwaka me jubili, ci bicuŋ i wel kikome ma iŋolo.
Lulevi 27:18 Ento ka odyero potone lacen i ŋe jubili, ajwaka biŋolo wel-lim ma myero gicul iye kun poro wel mwaka ma pud odoŋ nio i mwaka me jubili, ci wel ma yam iŋolo-ni gibidwoko piny.
Lulevi 27:19 Ka ce dano ma odyero peto-ni mito warone woko, en bimedo acel me abic i kom welle, ci bidoŋ i ciŋe.
Lulevi 27:20 Ento ka en pe mito waro po to-nu, nyo ka otyeko cato poto woko bot dano mukene, pe doŋ gibiwarone matwal.
Lulevi 27:21 Poto meno ka gigonyo i jubili bibedo maleŋ pi Rwot, macalo poto ma gikwero matwal; ci ajwaka aye doŋ bibedo rwode.
Lulevi 27:22 “Ka odyero bot Rwot poto mo ma owilo awila, ma pe dul lobo ma oleyo ki bot kwarone,
Lulevi 27:23 ajwaka biŋolo wene nio i mwaka me jubili, ci dano-nu bimiyo wel ma giŋolo i nino meno wek obed maleŋ pi Rwot.
Lulevi 27:24 Ci i mwaka me jubili poto bidok i ciŋ ŋat ma yam giwilo ki bote-ni, en ŋat ma poto-nu obedo mere kun oleyo ki bot kwarone.
Lulevi 27:25 Wel ducu ma giŋolo bilubo cekel me kabedo maleŋ, kun cekel acel romo gera pyeraryo.
Lulevi 27:26 “Ento litino kayo pa lee dano pe twero dyero, pien litino kayo ducu gibedo pa Rwot; kadi bed twon nyo romo, meno pa Rwot gire.
Lulevi 27:27 Ka lee ma keni, en biwilone ki boti i wel ma iŋolo, kun medo acel me abic i wiye; nyo ka pe gikoko, gibicatone acata i wel ma iŋolo.
Lulevi 27:28 “Ento gin ducu ma onoŋo gidyero i ciŋ Rwot matwal, ma dano mo odyero i ciŋ Rwot matwal ki i kin gin ma tye bote, kadi dano nyo lee nyo poto ma oleyo ki bot kwarone, pe gibicato kadi ki warone; gin ducu ma gidyero iciŋ Rwot matwal bedo gin maleŋ makato pi Rwot.
Lulevi 27:29 Dano mo-ni ma gidyero iciŋ Rwot matwal, ma myero ginek woko ki i kin dano, pe gitwero kokone; gibineke woko aneka.
Lulevi 27:30 “Acel me apar ducu mua i lobo, kadi bed kodi ma ocek i poto nyo nyig yat ma onyak, meno jami pa Rwot gire, gin maleŋ pa Rwot.
Lulevi 27:31 Ka dano mo mito koko gin mo i kom gin me aparre, en bimedo dul acel me abic i wiye.
Lulevi 27:32 Dul acel me apar pa dyaŋi ki romi nyo dyegi ducu, lee me aparre ducu i kin lim ducu ma kato i te odoo pa lakwat, meno bibedo maleŋ pi Rwot.
Lulevi 27:33 Rwode pe bipenyo ka ber nyo rac, dok pe bi koko kun gwenyo ki wadi mo; ka giloko, ci gin aryo ducuma gilokogi-ni gibibedo maleŋ; pe gibikokogi akoka.”
Lulevi 27:34 Magi aye cik ma yam Rwot ociko ki Moses pi jo Icrael ki i wi got Cinai.
Wel 1:1 Rwot oloko ki Moses i tim Cinai; i kema me rwatte, i kom nino dwe mukwoŋo me dwe me aryo, i mwaka me aryone nia i kare ma doŋ gua woko ki i lobo Ejipt. Owacci,
Wel 1:2 “Kwan wel lwak jo Icrael ducu, kun ilubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi kit ma Wel nyiŋgi tye kwede, kun ikwano co ducu ki acel acel,
Wel 1:3 cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo Icrael ducu ma romo cito ka lweny; wubikwanogi wun ki Aron ki bucagi.
Wel 1:4 Dok wubibedo ki dano acel ma oa ki i kaka acel acel, ma ŋat acel acel bibedo ladit wi kaka ki i ot pa kwarogi.
Wel 1:5 Man gin aye nyiŋ jo ma gibicuŋ ka konyowu: Jo pa Reuben, Elijur wod pa Cedeur;
Wel 1:6 jo pa Cimeon, Celumiel wod pa Juricadai;
Wel 1:7 jo pa Juda, Nakucon wod pa Aminadab;
Wel 1:8 jo pa Icakar, Netanel wod pa Juar;
Wel 1:9 jo pa Jabulon, Eliab wod pa Kelon;
Wel 1:10 i awobe pa Yucepu, jo pa Epraim, Elicama wod pa Amikud, jo pa Manace, Gamaliel wod pa Pedajur;
Wel 1:11 jo pa Benjamin, Abidan wod pa Gideoni;
Wel 1:12 jo pa Dan, Akiejer wod pa Amicadai;
Wel 1:13 jo pa Acer, Pagiel wod pa Okoran;
Wel 1:14 jo pa Gad, Eliacap wod pa Deuel;
Wel 1:15 jo pa Naputali, Akira wod pa Enan.”
Wel 1:16 Man gin aye dano ma giyero ki i lwak, ma gin aye lutel wi kaka pa kwarogi, gin ludito ma i kaka pa jo Icrael.
Wel 1:17 Moses ki Aron gukwanyo jo meno ma doŋ gikwano nyiŋgi-ni,
Wel 1:18 ci i kom nino mukwoŋo me dwe me aryo gucoko lwak ducu kacel. Gin gunyuto watgi kun gilubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, kit ma wel nyiŋgi tye kwede, cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeraryo dok kwede malo, ki acel acel,
Wel 1:19 macalo Rwot ociko ki Moses. En okwanogi i tim Cinai kit meno, Welgi ene:
Wel 1:20 Jo pa Reuben, latin kayo pa Icrael. Ka gikwano wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:21 wel jo ma i kaka pa Reuben oromo alip pyeraŋwen wiye abicel, ki miya abic.
Wel 1:22 Jo pa Cimeon. Ka gikwano wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:23 wel jo ma i kaka pa Cimeon oromo alip pyerabic wiye aboŋwen, ki miya adek.
Wel 1:24 Jo pa Gad. Ka gikwano wel likwayo ne kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaki me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:25 wel jo ma i kaka pa Gad oromo alip pyeraŋwen wiye abic, ki miya abicel ki pyerabic.
Wel 1:26 Jo pa Juda. Ka gikwano wel likwayo ne kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:27 wel jo ma i kaka pa Juda oromo alip pyerabiro wiye aŋwen, ki miya abicel.
Wel 1:28 Jo pa Icakar. Ka gikwano wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny.
Wel 1:29 Wel jo ma i kaka pa Icakar oromo alip pyerabic wiye aŋwen, ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 1:30 Jo pa Jabulon. Ka gikwano wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:31 wel jo ma i kaka pa Jabulon oromo alip pyerabic wiye abiro, ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 1:32 Jo pa Yucepu, jo pa Epraim. Ka gikwano wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:33 wel jo ma i kaka pa Epraim oromo alip pyeraŋwen, ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 1:34 Jo pa Manace. Ka gikwano wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:35 wel jo ma i kaka pa Manace oromo alip pyeradek wiye aryo, ki miya aryo.
Wel 1:36 Jo pa Benjamin. Ka gikwano wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki I kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:37 wel jo ma i kaka pa Benjamin oromo alip pyeradek wiye abic, ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 1:38 Jo pa Dan. Ka gikwano wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:39 wel jo ma i kaka pa Dan oromo alip pyerabicel wiye aryo, ki miya abiro.
Wel 1:40 Jo pa Acer. Ka gikwano Wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:41 wel jo ma i kaka pa Acer oromo alip pyeraŋwen wiye acel, ki miya abic.
Wel 1:42 Jo pa Naputali. Ka gikwano Wel likwayone kun gicoyo nyiŋgi ki acel acel ma lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma mwaka me ditogi romo pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo ducu ma giromo cito ka lweny.
Wel 1:43 Wel jo ma i kaka pa Naputali oromo alip pyerabic wiye adek, ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 1:44 Meno gin aye jo ma gikwano welgi, ma yam Moses ki Aron gukwano, kun lutel wi Icrael gukonyogi, jo apar wiye aryo, ma ŋat acel acel ocuŋ pi ot pa kwarogi.
Wel 1:45 Kit meno wel jo Icrael ducu ma gikwano kun gilubo odi pa kwarogi, nia ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeraryo dok kwede malo, jo Icrael ducu ma romo cito ka lweny,
Wel 1:46 welgi ducu onoŋo oromo alip miya abicel ki adek, ki miya abic ki pyerabic noŋo. Giketo jo pa Levi ka loyo kema pa Lubaŋa
Wel 1:47 Ento jo pa Levi pe gikwano welgi kacel kwedgi kun gilubo kaka pa kwarogi,
Wel 1:48 pien onoŋo Rwot owaco ki Moses ni,
Wel 1:49 “Wel kaka pa Levi aye pe ikwan, pe ibikwano welgi i kin jo Icrael;
Wel 1:50 ento ket jo pa Levi gubed ludito ma loyo tic i kema lok me caden, gulo jamine ducu, wa gin ducu ma tye iye. Gin aye bitiŋo kema ki jami ma tye iye ducu, gibitic iye, dok gibiguro kema me butogi rumo kema pa Lubaŋa.
Wel 1:51 Ka kema bicako wot, ci gin Lulevi aye gibiputo woko; dok ka gibiguro kema, Lulevi aye gibigurone. Ka ce dano mo ata onyiko cok ki kema, gibineko woko.
Wel 1:52 Jo Icrael gibiguro kemagi ki dog buca monygi, dano acel acel ki dog gonygi, ki dano acel acel i te benderane.
Wel 1:53 Ento jo pa Levi gibiguro kemagi rumo kema lok me caden, wek akemo pe opot i kom lwak jo Icrael; jo pa Levi gibigwoko kema lok me caden.”
Wel 1:54 Jo Icrael gutimo kit meno gutiyo gin ducu kit ma onoŋo Rwot ociko ki Moses.
Wel 2:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ki Aron ni,
Wel 2:2 “Jo Icrael gibiguro kemagi ŋat acel acel i te benderane, kun gitye ki lanyut me odi pa kwarogi; gibiguro kemagi kun doggi tiko kema me rwatte tuŋŋi ki tuŋŋi ducu.
Wel 2:3 Jo ma biguro kemagi yo tuŋ wokceŋ, ka ma ceŋ tuc ki iye-ni, gibibedo jo ma i te bendera pa Juda, kun gilubo buca monygi; latel wi jo pa Juda aye Nakucon ma wod pa Aminadab,
Wel 2:4 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyerabiro wiye aŋwen, ki miya abicel.
Wel 2:5 Jo ma biguro kemagi ma cok kwede gibibedo kaka pa Icakar; latel wi jo pa Icakar aye Natanel ma wod pa Jura,
Wel 2:6 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyerabic wiye aŋwen ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 2:7 Ka dok kaka pa Jabulon; latel wi jo pa Jabulon aye Eliab ma wod pa Kelon,
Wel 2:8 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyerabic wiye abiro, ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 2:9 Wel jo ducu ma i gony pa Juda, i bucagi, oromo alip miya acel ki pyeraboro wiye aŋwen, ki miya aŋwen. Ka wot ocakke, gin aye gibitelo yo.
Wel 2:10 “Ki yo tuŋ acuc en aye bendera me gony pa jo pa Reuben bicuŋ iye, kun gilubo buca monygi; latel wi jo pa Reuben aye Elijur ma wod pa Cedeur,
Wel 2:11 ma gikwano Wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyeraŋwen wiye abicel, ki miya abic.
Wel 2:12 Jo ma biguro kemagi ma cok kwede gibibedo kaka pa Cimeon; latel wi jo pa Cimeon aye Celumiel ma wod pa Juricadai,
Wel 2:13 ma gikwano Wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyerabic wiye aboŋwen ki miya adek.
Wel 2:14 Ka dok kaka pa Gad; latel wi jo pa Gad aye Eliacap wod pa Reuel,
Wel 2:15 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyeraŋwen wiye abic, ki miya abicel ki pyerabic.
Wel 2:16 Wel jo ducu ma i gony pa Reuben, i bucagi, oromo alip miya acel ki pyerabic wiye acel, ki miya aŋwen ki pyerabic. Ka wot cakke, gin aye gibimol me aryone.
Wel 2:17 “Lacen kema me rwatte bicako wot, kacel ki gony pa jo Levi, i dye gony ducu. Kit ma giguro ki kemagi gibicako wotgi kikore kit meno, kun dul acel acel tye ki kabedone, kun gilubbe aluba bendera ki bendera.
Wel 2:18 “Ki yo tuŋ potoceŋ bendera pa jo Epraim bicuŋ iye, kun gilubo buca monygi; latel wi jo pa Epraim aye Elicama ma wod pa Amikud,
Wel 2:19 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyeraŋwen, ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 2:20 Jo ma biguro kemagi ma cok kwede gibibedo kaka pa Manace; latel wi jo pa Manace aye Gamaliel ma wod pa Pedajur,
Wel 2:21 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyeradek wiye aryo, ki miya aryo.
Wel 2:22 Ka dok kaka pa Benjamin; latel wi jo pa Benjamin aye Abidan ma wod pa Gideoni,
Wel 2:23 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyeradek wiye abic, ki miya aŋwen.
Wel 2:24 Wel jo ducu ma i gony pa Epraim, i bucagi, oromo alip miya acel ki aboro, ki miya acel. Gin gibimol me adekke.
Wel 2:25 “Ki yo tuŋ acam bendera pa jo pa Dan bicuŋ iye, kun gilubo buca monygi; latel wi jo pa Dan aye Akiejer ma wod pa Amicadai,
Wel 2:26 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyerabicel wiye aryo, ki miya abiro.
Wel 2:27 Jo ma biguro kemagi ma cok kwede gibibedo kaka pa Acer; latel wi jo pa Acer en aye Pagiel ma wod pa Okoran,
Wel 2:28 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyeraŋwen wiye acel, ki miya abic.
Wel 2:29 Ka dok kaka pa Naputali; latel wi jo pa Naputali aye Akira ma wod pa Enan,
Wel 2:30 ma gikwano wel dano ma i buca monnye oromo alip pyerabic wiye adek, ki miya abicel.
Wel 2:31 Wel jo ducu ma i gony pa Dan oromo alip miya acel ki pyerabic wiye abiro, ki miya abicel. Gin gibimol me agikkine, kun gilubbe aluba bendera ki bendera.”
Wel 2:32 Meno aye jo Icrael kit ma gikwanogi kwede, kun lubo dog odi pa kwarogi; jo ducu ma i gonygi ducu ma gikwanogi i buca monygi onoŋo guromo alip miya abicel ki adek, ki miya abic ki pyerabic noŋo.
Wel 2:33 Ento jo pa Levi pe gikwano i kom jo Icrael, macalo Rwot onoŋo ociko ki Moses.
Wel 2:34 Jo Icrael yam gutiyo kit meno. Kit ma Rwot con ociko ki Moses ducu, guguro kemagi kit meno i te benderagi, gucako wot bene gumol kit meno, ŋat acel acel ki doggolane, macalo dog odi pa kwarogi tye kwede.
Wel 3:1 Magi aye likwayo pa Aron ki Moses i kare ma Rwot obedo ka lok ki Moses i wi got me Cinai.
Wel 3:2 Magi aye nyiŋ awobe pa Aron: Nadab latin kayone ki Abiu, Eleajar ki Itamar;
Wel 3:3 meno aye nyiŋ awobe pa Aron, gin aye ajwagi ma giwirogi ki moo, ma Moses yam okwerogi pi tiyo tic me bedo ajwagi.
Wel 3:4 Ento Nadab ki Abiu guto i nyim Rwot i kare ma gutyero mac mapat i nyim Rwot i tim Cinai, kit mac ma yam pe ocikogi kwede; gin pe gubedo ki litino. Mumiyo Eleajar ki Itamar gutiyo tic pa ajwagi i kare ma wongi pud kwo.
Wel 3:5 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Wel 3:6 “Kel kaka pa Levi cok, ci iketgi i nyim ajwaka wek guti bote.
Wel 3:7 Gibicobo tic mapatpat pire ki pi lwak ducu i nyim kema me rwatte, dok gibitiyo tic pi jo Icrael kun gitiyo ticgi i kema.
Wel 3:8 Gin aye gibigwoko jami ducu ma i kema me rwatte, dok gibitiyo tic pi jo Icrael kun gitiyo ticgi i kema.
Wel 3:9 Ibimiyo Lulevi bot Aron ki awobene; gityeko miyogi bote matwal kun gikwanyogi woko ki i kin jo Icrael.
Wel 3:10 Ci ibiketo Aron ki awo bene, gibitiyo ticgi me bedo ajwagi; ento ka ŋat mo mukene onyiko cok, gibineke woko.”
Wel 3:11 Rwot dok owaco bot Moses ni,
Wel 3:12 “Nen, doŋ atyeko kwanyo jo pa Levi ki i kin jo Icrael ma ka litino kayo ducu mukwono yabo ic i kin jo Icrael. Jo pa Levi aye gibibedo jona,
Wel 3:13 pien litino kayo ducu mera. I nino ma yam aneko iye litino kayo ducu ma i lobo Ejipt ca, en aye akwero iye litino kayo ducu ma i Icrael gubed mera, pa dano ki pa lee; gibibedo mera; an a Rwot.”
Wel 3:14 Rwot owaco bot Moses ki i tim Cinai ni,
Wel 3:15 “Kwan wel likwayo pa Levi, kun ilubo dog odi pa kwarogi, ki doggolagi; ibikwano co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo dwe acel dok kwede malo.”
Wel 3:16 Kit meno Moses okwano welgi kit ma Rwot owaco-ni, macalo yam ocike-ni.
Wel 3:17 Magi aye awobe pa Levi ma giyeko nyiŋgi: Gercon, Kokat ki Merari.
Wel 3:18 Magi aye nyiŋ awobe pa Gercon kun lubo doggolagi: Libni ki Cimei.
Wel 3:19 Awobe pa Kokat kun lubo doggolagi gin aye Amram, Ijar, Kebron ki Ujiel.
Wel 3:20 Awobe pa Merari kun lubo doggolagi gin aye Makali ki Muci. Meno aye doggola pa Lulevi, kun lubo dog odi pa kwarogi.
Wel 3:21 Jo pa Gercon aye doggola pa jo pa Libni ki doggola pa jo pa Cimei; meno aye doggola pa jo pa Gercon.
Wel 3:22 Welgi ka gikwano wel co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo dwe acel dok kwede malo oromo alip abiro, ki miya abic.
Wel 3:23 Doggola pa jo pa Gercon yam giguro kemagi i ŋe kema yo tuŋ potoceŋ,
Wel 3:24 kun Eliacap wod pa Lael obedo ladit ki i ot pa kwaro pa jo Gercon.
Wel 3:25 Tic pa likwayo pa Gercon i kema me rwatte obedo me gwoko kema; en aye kema kikome ki laum wiye, boŋo cuka laum doggola me doggola kema me rwatte,
Wel 3:26 boŋo cuka me aŋaba me larum dyekal, boŋo cuka laum doggola me dyekal ma orumo kema ki keno tyer, ki lwak tol lacikgi; dog tic ducu ma mitte pi jami magi.
Wel 3:27 Jo pa Kokat aye doggola pa jo pa Amram, ki doggola pa jo pa Ijar, ki doggola pa jo pa Kebron, ki doggola pa jo pa Ujiel; meno aye doggola pa jo pa Kokat.
Wel 3:28 Welgi ka gikwano Wel co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo dwe acel dok kwede malo oromo alip aboro, ki miya abicel ma gitiyo ticgi i kabedo maleŋ.
Wel 3:29 Doggola pa jo pa Kokat yam giguro kemagi i ŋet kema yo tuŋ acuc,
Wel 3:30 kun Elijapan wod pa Ujiel obedo ladit ki i ot pa kwaro me doggola pa jo. Kokat.
Wel 3:31 Ticgi obedo me gwoko canduk, meja, okarmac, keno tyer, jami me kabedo maleŋ ma ajwagi gitiyo kwedgi ducu, ki boŋo kicika; dog tic ducu ma mitte pi jami magi.
Wel 3:32 Ladit ma loyo ludito ducu pa Lulevi obedo Eleajar wod pa ajwaka Aron. En onoŋo loyo jo ma gitiyo ticgi i kabedo maleŋ.
Wel 3:33 Jo pa Merari aye doggola pa jo pa Makali ki doggola pa jo pa Muci; meno aye doggola pa jo pa Merari.
Wel 3:34 Welgi ka gikwano Wel co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo dwe acel dok kwede malo oromo alip abicel, ki miya aryo.
Wel 3:35 Ladit ki i ot pa kwarogi ma i doggola pa jo Merari obedo Juriel wod pa Abikail. Gin yam giguro kemagi i ŋet kema yo tun acam.
Wel 3:36 Tic ma gimiyo bot likwayo pa Merari obedo me gwoko lwak guti me kema, lwak riine, lwak wirre lwak tedi tere ki gin ma okemo ticce ducu; dog tic ducu ma mitte pi jami magi ducu.
Wel 3:37 Ka dok lwak wir ducu ma gurumo dyekal, ki tedi tergi ki lwak teke lagurgi, ki lwak tolle.
Wel 3:38 Jo ma yam giguro kemagi i nyim kema yo tuŋ wokceŋ, i nyim kema me rwatte ka ma cen tuc iye-ni, gin aye Moses ki Aron ki awobene. Gin onoŋo gityeko ketogi i dog tic ma i kabedo maleŋ, pi tiyo tic ducu ma mitte pi jo Icrael; ka ŋat mo mukene onyiko cok, myero ginek woko.
Wel 3:39 Wel jo Levi ducu ma yam gikwano, ma Moses ki Aron gukwano welgi pi lubo cik pa Rwot, kun lubo doggolagi, co ducu cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo dwe acel dok kwede malo, oromo alip pyeraryo wiye aryo. Koko litino kayo
Wel 3:40 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni, “Kwan wel litino kayo ducu ma co ki i kin jo Icrael, cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo dwe acel dok kwede malo; kwan welgi kun ilubo nyiŋgi.
Wel 3:41 An a Rwot; ibikwanyo jo pa Levi gubed mera ma ka litino kayo ducu ma i kin jo Icrael; dok iter lim makwo pa jo Levi ma ka litino kayo ducu ma i kin lim makwo pa jo Icrael.”
Wel 3:42 Kit meno Moses okwano Wel litino kayo ma i kin jo Icrael ducu, macalo Rwot ocike.
Wel 3:43 Litino kayo ducu ma co, macalo wel nyiŋgi tye, cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo dwe acel dok kwede malo, ka gikwano welgi onoŋo guromo alip pyeraryo wiye aryo, ki miya aryo ki pyerabiro wiye adek.
Wel 3:44 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni
Wel 3:45 “Kwany jo pa Levi gubed ma ka litino kayo ducu ma i kin jo Icrael, dok iter lim makwo pa jo Levi ma ka limgi; jo pa Levi gibibedo jona; an a Rwot.
Wel 3:46 Pi koko litino kayo miya aryo ki pyerabiro wiye adek ma i kin jo Icrael ma gudoŋ ma wel pa jo pa Levi orem woko pigi-ni,
Wel 3:47 ibigamo cekel abic abic pi dano acel acel; ibigamo kun ilubo cekel me kabedo maleŋ, ma cekel acel romo gera pyeraryo-ni.
Wel 3:48 Lim meno ma gikoko kwede wel jo ma gudoŋ-ŋi ibimiyo bot Aron ki awo bene.”
Wel 3:49 Mumiyo Moses ogamo lim me kok ki bot jo mudoŋ, ma wel pa jo Levi orem me kokogi;
Wel 3:50 ci ogamo lim ryal ki bot litino kayo pa jo Icrael ma romo cekel alip acel, ki miya adek pi pyerabicel wiye abic, kun lubo cekel me kabedo maleŋ.
Wel 3:51 Moses omiyo lim meno me kok bot Aron ki awobene, kit ma Rwot owaco-ni, macalo Rwot yam ociko ki Moses.
Wel 4:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ki Aron ni,
Wel 4:2 “Kwan wellikwayo pa Kokat ma i kin likwayo pa Levi, kun ilubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi,
Wel 4:3 cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeradek o wa i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyerabic, jo ducu ma giromo donyo i dog tic pi tiyo tic ma i kema me rwatte.
Wel 4:4 Man aye tic ma likwayo pa Kokat gibitiyo i kema me rwatte: gibitic i kom jami maleŋ makato.
Wel 4:5 Ka gony doŋ bicako wot, Aron ki awobene bidonyo i kema ka kwanyo boŋo kicika, ci giumo kwede canduk lok me caden.
Wel 4:6 Ka dok gibiumo wiye ki laa dyel, lacen gibiyaro boŋo ma bulu i kom meno, ka doŋ gibirwako talle iye.
Wel 4:7 Gibipeto boŋo ma bulu i kom meja me mugati me aketa i nyim Rwot, ka doŋ gibiketo caani i wiye, ki atabo me odok eceta, ki weer, ki cupa me onyo gityer amata; mugati ma gicano i nyim Rwot jwijwi bene obed i wiye.
Wel 4:8 Lacen gibiyaro boŋo makwar i wiye, ci meno gibiumo ki laa dyel laumme, ka doŋ gibirwako talle iye.
Wel 4:9 Ka dok gibikwanyo boŋo ma bulu, ci giumo ki okarmac, kacel ki laputte, ki magacce, ki caanine ki atabo moone ducu ma gitiyo kwede ticce;
Wel 4:10 ci gibiboyo en ki jami ticce ducu ki laa dyel laumme, ka doŋ gibipyelo i wi tal latiŋŋe.
Wel 4:11 Gibiyaro boŋo ma bulu i kom keno tyer me jabu, ka dok gibiumo kome ki gin ma gikwoyo ki laa dyel, ka doŋ gibirwako talle iye.
Wel 4:12 Gibikwanyo jami tic ducu ma gitiyo kwedgi i kabedo maleŋ, gibiboyogi ducu ki boŋo ma bulu, ka doŋ gibiumogi ki gin ma gikwoyo ki laa dyel, ci gibipyelo i wi tal latingi.
Wel 4:13 Gibijobo buru mac ma i keno me tyer woko, gibiyaro boŋo ma lamar lamar i wiye;
Wel 4:14 ka dok gibiketo iye jami tic ducu me keno tyer, ma gitiyo kwede tic i kome, weer lawaŋ mac, gin lacob riŋo, akwaya latokke ki becen, jami tic ducu me keno tyer; ka dok gibiyaro i kome laa dyel laumme, lacen gibirwako talle.
Wel 4:15 Ka Aron ki awobene doŋ gutyeko umo kabedo maleŋ ki jami ma i kabedo maleŋ ducu i kare ma giputo gony, lacen likwayo pa Kokat doŋ gibibino ka tiŋogi, ento
Wel 4:16 “Eleajar wod pa Aron aye biloyo moo tara, ki odok eceta ma ŋwece kur, ki gityer me moko kwon me nino ducu, ki moo wir, kun dok loyo kom kema ducu ki lwak jami ducu ma bedo iye, en aye kabedo maleŋ kikome ki jami ticce.”
Wel 4:17 Rwot owaco bot Moses ki Aron ni,
Wel 4:18 “Pe iwek doggola ducu me kaka pa jo pa Kokat guto gutum woko ki i kin jo pa Levi,
Wel 4:19 ento ber itimgi kit man wek gubed makwo, ma pe guto i kare ma gibino cok ki jami maleŋ makato-ni: Aron ki awobene aye bidonyo ka nyutogi tic pa ŋat acel acel ki yec ma gibitiŋo,
Wel 4:20 ento gin pe bidonyo iye ka neno kom jami maleŋ kadi matidi mo, wek pe guto.”
Wel 4:21 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Wel 4:22 “Kwan wellikwayo pa Gercon bene, kun ilubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi;
Wel 4:23 ibikwano welgi cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeradek o wa i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyerabic, jo ducu ma giromo donyo i dog tic pi tiyo tic i kom kema me rwatte.
Wel 4:24 Man en aye dog tic ma doggola pa Gercon ducu gibitiyo, me tiyo tic ki me tino yec:
Wel 4:25 gibitiŋo boŋo cuka me kema, ki kema me rwatte ki laum wiye, ki laa dyel ma giumo kwede wiye malo,
Wel 4:26 ki boŋo cuka me aŋaba me rumo dyekal, ki boŋo laum doggaŋ me dyekal ma orumo kema ki keno tyer, ki lwak tol lacikgi, ki jami tic ducu ma gitiyo kwedgi iye; gibitiyo tic ducu ma mitte i kom jami magi.
Wel 4:27 Tic pa likwayo pa Gercon ducu gibitiyo kit ma Aron ki awo bene gicikogi i kom jami ducu ma gibitinone, ki i kom gin ducu ma gibitiyone; dok in aye ibipoko yecgi ducu botgi me agwoka.
Wel 4:28 Man en aye tic pa doggola ducu pa likwayo pa Gercon ki i kema me rwatte; dog ticgi bibedo i te loc pa Itamar wod pa ajwaka Aron.
Wel 4:29 “Likwayo pa Merari ibikwano welgi kun ilubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi;
Wel 4:30 ibikwano welgi cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeradek o wa i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyerabic, jo ducu ma giromo donyo i dog tic pi tiyo tic i kema me rwatte.
Wel 4:31 Magi aye gin ma gimiyo botgi me atiŋa, ma en aye ticgi ducu ki i kema me rwatte: lwak guti me kema, ki riine, ki lwak wirre ki lwak tedi tere,
Wel 4:32 ki wir ducu ma orumo dyekal, ki tedi tergi ducu, ki lwak teke lagurgi ki tol lacikgi, ki lwak jami ticgi ducu ki gin ma okemo tic ducu. Ibipoko botgijami ma gimito ni gutiŋ kun inyuto ki nyiŋgi.
Wel 4:33 Man aye tic pa doggola ducu pa likwayo pa Merari, en aye dog ticgi ducu ki i kema me rwatte; bibedo i te loc pa Itamar wod pa ajwaka Aron.”
Wel 4:34 Moses ki Aron ki lutel wi lwak gukwano wel likwayo pa Kokat, kun lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi,
Wel 4:35 cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeradek o wa i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyerabic, jo ducu ma giromo donyo i dog tic, pi tiyo tic i kema me rwatte;
Wel 4:36 welgi ma gikwano kun lubo doggolagi oromo alip aryo, ki miya abiro ki pyerabic.
Wel 4:37 Meno aye wel doggola ducu pa jo pa Kokat, jo ducu ma gutiyo tic i kema me rwatte, ma Moses ki Aron gukwano welgi, macalo Rwot ociko ki i dog Moses.
Wel 4:38 Man wel likwayo pa Gercon ma gikwano welgi kun lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi,
Wel 4:39 cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeradek o wa i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyerabic, jo ducu ma giromo donyo i dog tic, pi tiyo tic i kema me rwatte;
Wel 4:40 welgi ma gikwano kun lubo doggolagi oromo alip aryo, ki miya abicel ki pyeradek.
Wel 4:41 Meno aye Wel doggola ducu pa likwayo pa Gercon, jo ducu ma gutiyo tic i kema me rwatte, ma Moses ki Aron gukwano welgi, macalo Rwot ociko ki i dog Moses.
Wel 4:42 Man wel likwayo pa Merari ma gikwano welgi kun lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi,
Wel 4:43 cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeradek o wa i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyerabic, jo ducu ma giromo donyo i dog tic, pi tiyo tic i kema me rwatte:
Wel 4:44 welgi ma gikwano kun lubo doggolagi oromo alip adek, ki miya aryo.
Wel 4:45 Meno aye jo me doggola pa likwayo pa Merari ma gikwanogi, ma Moses ki Aron gukwano welgi, macalo Rwot ociko ki i dog Moses.
Wel 4:46 Jo ducu ki i kin jo pa Levi ma gikwano welgi, ma Moses ki Aron ki lutel wi Icrael gukwanogi kun lubo doggolagi ki dog odi pa kwarogi
Wel 4:47 cakke ki i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyeradek o wa i kom jo ma ditogi romo mwaka pyerabic, jo ducu ma giromo donyo i dog tic pi tiyo tic mapatpat ki pi tiŋo yec i kema me rwatte
Wel 4:48 jo ma i kingi ma gikwano welgi guromo alip aboro, ki miya abic ki pyeraboro.
Wel 4:49 Macalo Rwot yam ociko kun wok ki i dog Moses ci gimiyogi ticgi kit meno, ŋat acel acel i dog ticce me tiyo tic nyo me tiŋo yec; gikwano welgi kit meno, macalo Rwot ociko ki Moses.
Wel 5:1 Rwot owaco ki Moses ni,
Wel 5:2 “Cik jo Icrael gucwal ludobo ducu gua woko ki i gony, ki dano acel acel ma kome cwer tut, ki dano acel acel ma odoko keni pi gudo kom dano muto.
Wel 5:3 Wubicwalo co wa ki mon bene, kun wucwalogi woko ki i gony, wek pe gubal gonygi ma an abedo iye-ni odok keni.”
Wel 5:4 Jo Icrael gutiyo kit meno, ci guryemogi woko i ŋe gony; macalo Rwot con owaco bot Moses, jo Icrael gutiyo kit meno. Cik ma mako culo waŋ jami
Wel 5:5 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Wel 5:6 “Wac ki jo Icrael ni, Ka ce laco mo nyo dako mo otimo bal mo ma dano timo kun giŋayo waŋ Rwot, ce otiŋo alii,
Wel 5:7 en bituco bal mere ma otimo-ni; ka dok en biculo waŋ gin marac ma otimo; bimedo iye acel me abic, ci miyo bot dano ma en otimo marac-ci.
Wel 5:8 Ento ka dano meno watte mo pe ma myero giculle waŋ gin marac-ci, ci giculo Waŋ gin marac meno bot Rwot pi ajwaka, kun gibamo i kom nyok romo me kwanyo bal ma gitimo kwede gin lakwany bal ki i kome.
Wel 5:9 Gityer ducu, nyo jami ducu maleŋ pa jo Icrael ma gikelo bot ajwaka bibedo mere.
Wel 5:10 Jami maleŋ ma dano acel acel okelo bibedo mere; gin ducu ma dano mo omiyo bot ajwaka bibedo mere.” Cik ma mako nyeko
Wel 5:11 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Wel 5:12 “Wac ki jo Icrael ni, Ka dako pa laco mo waŋe olal, ci otimo kir i kom cware,
Wel 5:13 ka laco-mo obuto kwede, ce cware pe oŋeyo, ma dako ojerre kekene kun lokke okanne woko, dok pe tye caden mo ma moko lok kom dako-nu, pien pe ginoŋe iye;
Wel 5:14 ka cwiny me nyeko omako laco, kun nyeko omake i kom dakone ma ojerre kekene-ni, nyo ka cwiny me nyeko omako laco, kun nyeko omake i kom dakone, kadi bed dako pe ojerre kekene,
Wel 5:15 ci laco bitero dakone bot ajwaka, kun tero gityer ma gimito pi dakone, agwata moko kwon acel me moko cayiri; pe bionyo moo i kome, pe biketo iye odok luban, pien meno gityer me moko kwon me nyeko, en gityer me moko kwon me lapo wic, ma bimiyo gipo pi bal meno.
Wel 5:16 “Ajwaka bikelo dako cok, ci cibo i nyim Rwot.
Wel 5:17 Ka dok ajwaka bitero pii maleŋ ki otako, ci jobo apwa ma i dye ot me kema, onyo i pii.
Wel 5:18 Ka ajwaka bicibo dako i nyim Rwot, bigonyo yer wi dako wek oket ata lijayi, ci keto gityer me moko kwon me lapo wic i cinŋ, ma en aye gityer me moko kwon me nyeko. Ajwaka bimako pii makec me ceno dano i ciŋe.
Wel 5:19 Ka ajwaka bimiyo dako-nu kwoŋo kwoŋ, kun waco ni, ‘Ka laco mo pe obuto kwedi, ka pe iŋak woko, kun ijerre kekeni ma it ye i te twero pa cwari, ci gin marac mo pe otimi pi pii man makec me ceno dano-ni.
Wel 5:20 Ento ka ce waŋi olal woko, ma pud it ye i te twero pa cwari, ka ijerre kekeni, ci laco mo ma pe cwari obuto kwedi,
Wel 5:21 ci (ajwaka bimiyo dako-nu kwoŋo kwoŋ ma kelo ceno dano kun waco ki dako- nu ni,) Rwot omi in idok ŋat ma giceno ki dano, kun dano gikwoŋo akwoŋa ki nyiŋi i kin lutuwu, i kare ma Rwot bitweyo nyodoŋi woko ci miyo ii bene deŋ woko;
Wel 5:22 wek pii man me ceno dano ocit i cin ii, omi ii odeŋ, ci otwe nyodoŋi woko.’ Dako bigamo ni, ‘Amen, Amen.’
Wel 5:23 “Lacen ajwaka bicoyo lok me ceno dano-ni i karatac, ka dok lwoko vinone woko ki pii makec-ci,
Wel 5:24 ci bimiyo dakonu mato pii makec ma giceno ki dano-ni, ci pii me ceno dano bidonyo i iye, miyo iye mwode matek.
Wel 5:25 Ka dok ajwaka bikwanyo gityer me moko kwon me nyeko woko ki i cin dako- nu, ci kwato gityer me moko kwon i nyim Rwot, tero i keno tyer.
Wel 5:26 Ka ajwaka bijobo moko me gityer poŋ ciŋ acel obed gin me po i kome, biwaŋo i wi keno tyer; ka dok lacen en bimiyo dako-nu mato pii.
Wel 5:27 Ka doŋ omiyo omato pii, ka ce onoŋo en otyeko jerre kekene kun otimo kir i kom cware, ci pii me ceno dano bidonyo i iye, miyo iye mwode matek; iye biden woko, nyodone bitwene woko, dako-ni bidoko ŋat ma giceno dano ki nyiŋe i kin lutugi.
Wel 5:28 Ento ka dako-nu pe ojerre kekene, ma bal mo pe i kome, gin marac mo pe bitimo, ci en binywalo litino.
Wel 5:29 “Man aye cik ma mako lok me nyeko, ka dako ma tye i te twero pa cware noŋo wage olal, ci ojerre kekene,
Wel 5:30 nyo ka cwiny me nyeko omako laco mo, kun nyeko omake i kom dakone; en bicibo dako i nyim Rwot, ci ajwaka bitiyo i kom dako kun lubo cik man ducu.
Wel 5:31 Laco pe bibedo ki bal mo, ento bal bidok i wi dako ka obalo.”
Wel 6:1 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Wel 6:2 “Wac bot jo Icrael ni, Ka laco mo nyo dako mo okwoŋo kwoŋ ma pire tek, kwoŋ me bedo ajula pa Lubaŋa , ci okone gire kene pi bedo dano pa Rwot,
Wel 6:3 en bikone gire kene kun pe mato koŋo vino nyo gin ma mero dano; pe bimato kono mawac ma oa i kom vino nyo i kom gin mo ma mero dano; pe bimato pig nyig olok, kadi camo nyige madyak nyo mutwone.
Wel 6:4 I kare ducu ma en okone iye gire kene, pe bicamo gin mo ma oa i kom olok, kadi nyige matino ma i iye, wa odune.
Wel 6:5 “I kare ducu ma noŋo en okwoŋo pire ni ebikone gire kene, lyedi pe bigudo wiye; bibedo dano maleŋ o wa i kare ma en okone iye pi bedo dano pa Rwot doŋ otum; biweko yer wiye lot maboco ma pe giŋolo.
Wel 6:6 “I kare ma en okone iye gire kene pi bedo dano pa Rwot, pe binyiko cok i kom dano muto.
Wel 6:7 Pe biballe doko keni kadi pi wonne nyo minne, nyo ominne, nyo laminne ka ce guto, pien gin ma nyuto konene kene pi bedo dano pa Lubaŋa pud tye i wiye.
Wel 6:8 I kare ducu me konene kene en bibedo maleŋ pi Rwot.
Wel 6:9 “Ka dano mo oto atura ka ŋete, ma miyo wiye ma okwero-ni odoko keni, en bilyelo wiye i nino me lonnyene; bilyelo i nino me abirone.
Wel 6:10 I kom nino me aborone en bitero amam aryo nyo litino akuri aryo bot ajwaka i doggola kema me rwatte.
Wel 6:11 Ajwaka bityero acel pi gitum me bal ki acel pi gitum awaŋa, kun timo gin lakwany bal ki i kom dano-nu, pien onoŋo obalo pi gudo kom dano muto. En bikwero wiye i nino meno kikome,
Wel 6:12 ci kone gire pi bedo dano pa Rwot pi karene me kone kene, dok bikelo wod romo ma ditte mwaka acel obed gitum me tiŋo alii; ento kare mukwono ca noŋo oballe noŋo, pien yer wiye ma okwero-ni odoko keni.
Wel 6:13 “Man aye cik ma mako dano ma ajula pa Lubaŋa ka karene me kone kene doŋ otum. Gibikele i doggola kema me rwatte,
Wel 6:14 ci en bityero motte bot Rwot, wod romo acel me mwaka acel, ma kome pe ki mwonyo, pi gitum awaŋa, ki bwoŋ romo acel ma ditte mwaka acel ma kome pe ki mwonyo pi gityer lakwecwiny,
Wel 6:15 kacel ki aduku me mugati ma tobi pe iye, capat me moko kwon mapwotte ma girubo ki moo, ki capat marep ma tobi pe iye ma gireyo moo i komgi, ki gityer me moko kwon ki gityer amata mutikogi.
Wel 6:16 “Ajwaka bikelogi i nyim Rwot, ci tyero gitum me balle ki gitum me tiŋo alii.
Wel 6:17 Ka dok bityero nyok romo obed gityer Lakwecwiny bot Rwot, kacel ki aduku mugati ma tobi pe iye. Ka dok ajwaka bityero gityer me moko kwon ki gityer amatane.
Wel 6:18 Dano ma ajula pa Lubaŋa bilyelo yer wiye me kone kene i doggola kema me rwatte, ci bikwanyo yer wiye me bedo ajula-ni, keto i mac ma tye i te gityer lakwecwinynyi.
Wel 6:19 Ajwaka bikwanyo bat nyok romo ka doŋ gitedo, ki capat acel ma tobi pe iye, ki i aduku, ki capat marep acel ma tobi pe iye, biketogi i dye cin ajula, ka doŋ olyelo yer wiye me kone kene.
Wel 6:20 Ajwaka bikwatogi me bedo gityer me akwata i nyim Rwot; gin aye waŋ wat maleŋ pa ajwaka, kacel ki gok ma gikwato-ni ki em ma gityero; lacen ajula doŋ twero mato koŋo vino.
Wel 6:21 “Man aye cik ma mako ajula ma okwoŋo kwoŋ. Gityerre bot Rwot bibedo ma oporo kwoŋŋe ma okwoŋo me bedo ajula pa Lubaŋa, ma en miyo kacel ki gin ma en romo noŋone: wek en oti ma oporo kwoŋ ma yam okwoŋo, kun lubo cik ma mako konene kene me bedo ajula.” Lamo gum pa ajwagi
Wel 6:22 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Wel 6:23 “Wac bot Aron ki awobene ni, Wubilamo gum i kom jo Icrael kit man: ibiwaco botgi ni,
Wel 6:24 Rwot omini gum, ogwoki;
Wel 6:25 Rwot oneni ki waŋ me kica, otimi ber
Wel 6:26 Rwot tiŋ waŋe i komi omini kuc.
Wel 6:27 Gibiketo nyiŋa i kom jo Icrael kit meno, ci an abimiyogi gum.”
Wel 7:1 Ka Moses otyeko guro kema, owiro ki moo dok okwero kacel ki jamine ducu. Ka dok owiro keno tyer ki moo bene, okwero kacel ki jami ticce ducu.
Wel 7:2 I kare meno lutel wi Icrael, ma gin ludito kaka ki i odi pa kwarogi, lutel wi kaka ma giloyo wi jo ma yam gikwano welgi-ni,
Wel 7:3 gutyero gityer megi, gukelo i nyim Rwot. Gumiyo gadigadi abicel ma gitye ki gin umo wigi, ki twoni apar wiye aryo; lutel wic aryo aryo gumiyo gadigadi acel acel, ci ŋat acel acel omiyo twon acel; gutyerogi ki i nyim kema.
Wel 7:4 Rwot dok owaco ki Moses ni,
Wel 7:5 “Gam jami-ni woko ducu ki botgi wek giti kwedgi tic ma i kema me rwatte, ci imigi bot Lulevi, macalo dog tic ma ŋat acel acel tye kwede.”
Wel 7:6 Omiyo Moses ogamo gadigadi ducu ki twoni, ci omiyogi bot Lulevi.
Wel 7:7 Gadigadi aryo ki twoni aŋwen omiyo bot likwayo pa Gercon, ma oporo dog ticgi;
Wel 7:8 ka dok gadigadi aŋwen ki twoni aboro omiyo bot likwayo pa Merari, ma oporo dog ticgi, kun gitye i te loc pa Itamar wod pa ajwaka Aron.
Wel 7:9 Ento pe omiyo gin mo bot likwayo pa Kokat, pien yam giketogi i dog tic me gwoko jami maleŋ ki me tiŋogi i wi gwokgi.
Wel 7:10 Ci lutel wic gutyero gityer me kwero keno tyer i kom nino meno ma giwiro iye ki moo-ni; lutel wic gutyero gityergi i nyim keno tyer.
Wel 7:11 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni, “Gibityero gityergi kun latel wic acel acel tyero mere i ninone, pi kwero keno me tyer.”
Wel 7:12 Ŋat ma otyero gityerre i nino mukwoŋo en aye Nakucon wod pa Aminadab, ma i kaka pa Juda.
Wel 7:13 En otyero caani me ryal acel ma pekke romo cekel miya acel ki pyeradek, ki becen me ryal acel ma pekke cekel pyerabiro, ka giporo ki cekel me kabedo maleŋ; gin aryo ducu igi opoŋ ki moko kwon mapwotte ma girubo ki moo pi gityer me moko kwon.
Wel 7:14 Ka doki atabo me jabu acel ma pekke cekel apar ma opoŋ ki odok eceta;
Wel 7:15 wod twon acel, nyok romo acel, ki wod romo acel me mwaka acel pi gitum awaŋa;
Wel 7:16 nyok dyel acel pi gitum me bal;
Wel 7:17 ka doki pi gityer lakwecwiny otyero twoni aryo, nyogi romi abic, nyogi dyegi abic, ki litino nyogi romi abic ma ditogi mwaka acel acel. Man aye gityer ma Nakucon wod pa Aminadab otyero.
Wel 7:18 I nino me aryone Netanel wod pa Juar, ma en aye latel wi jo pa Icakar otyero gityer.
Wel 7:19 Pi gityerre en otyero caani me ryal acel ma pekke romo cekel miya acel ki pyeradek, ki becen me ryal acel ma pekke cekel pyerabiro, ka giporo ki cekel me
Wel 7:20 Ka doki atabo me jabu acel ma pekke cekel apar ma opoŋ ki odok eceta;
Wel 7:21 wod twon acel, nyok romo acel, ki wod romo acel me mwaka acel pi gitum awaŋa:
Wel 7:22 nyok dyel acel pi gitum me bal;
Wel 7:23 ka doki pi gityer lakwecwiny otyero twoni aryo, nyogi romi abic, nyogi dyegi abic, ki litino nyogi romi abic ma ditogi mwaka acel acel, Man aye gityer ma Netanel wod pa Juar otyero.
Wel 7:24 I nino me adekke obedo kare pa Eliab wod pa Kelon, ma en aye latel wi jo pa Jabulon.
Wel 7:25 Pi gityerre en otyero caani me ryal acel ma pekke romo cekel miya acel ki pyeradek, ki becen me ryal acel ma pekke cekel pyerabiro, ka giporo ki cekel me kabedo maleŋ; gin aryo ducu igi opoŋ ki moko kwon mapwotte ma girubo ki moo pi gityer me moko kwon.
Wel 7:26 Ka doki atabo me jabu acel ma pekke cekel apar ma opoŋ ki o dok eceta;
Wel 7:27 wod twon acel, nyok romo acel, ki wod romo acel me mwaka acel pi gitum awaŋa;
Wel 7:28 nyok dyel acel pi gitum me bal;
Wel 7:29 ka doki pi gityer lakwecwiny otyero twoni aryo, nyogi romi abic, nyogi dyegi abic, ki litino nyogi romi abic ma ditogi mwaka acel acel. Man aye gityer ma Eliab wod pa Kelon otyero.
Wel 7:30 I nino me aŋwenne obedo kare pa Elijur wod pa Cedeur, ma en aye latel wi jo pa Reuben.
Wel 7:31 Pi gityerre en otyero caani me ryal acel ma pekke romo cekel miya acel ki pyeradek, ki becen me ryal acel ma pekke cekel pyerabiro, ka giporo ki cekel me kabedo maleŋ; gin aryo ducu igi opoŋ ki mo ko kwon mapwotte ma girubo ki moo pi gityer me moko kwon.
Wel 7:32 Ka doki atabo me jabu acel ma pekke cekel apar ma opoŋ ki odok eceta;
Wel 7:33 wod twon acel, nyok romo acel, ki wod romo acel me mwaka acel pi gitum awaŋa;
Wel 7:34 nyok dyel acel pi gitum me bal;
Wel 7:35 ka doki pi gityer lakwecwiny otyero twoni aryo, nyogi romi abic, nyogi dyegi abic, ki litino nyogi romi abic ma ditogi mwaka acel acel, Man aye gityer ma Elijur wod pa Cedeur otyero.
Wel 7:36 I nino me abicce obedo kare pa Celumiel wod pa Juricadai, ma en aye latel wi jo pa Cimeon.
Wel 7:37 Pi gityerre en otyero caani me ryal acel ma pekke romo cekel miya acel ki pyeradek, ki becen me ryal acel ma pekke cekel pyerabiro, ka giporo ki cekel me kabedo maleŋ; gin aryo ducu igi opoŋ ki moko kwon mapwotte ma girubo ki moo pi gityer me moko kwon.
Wel 7:38 Ka doki atabo me jabu acel ma pekke cekel apar ma opoŋ ki odok eceta;
Wel 7:39 wod twon acel, nyok romo acel, ki wod romo acel me mwaka acel pi gitum awaŋa;
Wel 7:40 nyok dyel acel pi gitum me bal;
Wel 7:41 ka doki pi gityer lakwecwiny otyero twoni aryo, nyogi romi abic, nyogi dyegi abic, ki litino nyogi romi abic ma ditogi mwaka acel acel, Man aye gityer ma Celumiel wod pa Juricadai otyero.
Wel 7:42 I nino me abicelle obedo kare pa Eliacap wod pa Deuel, ma en aye latel wi jo pa Gad.
Wel 7:43 Pi gityerre en otyero caani me ryal acel ma pekke romo cekel miya acel ki pyeradek, ki becen me ryal acel ma pekke cekel pyerabiro, ka giporo ki cekel me kabedo maleŋ; gin aryo ducu igi opoŋ ki moko kwon mapwotte ma girubo ki moo pi gityer me moko kwon.
Wel 7:44 Ka doki atabo me jabu acel ma pekke cekel apar ma opoŋ ki odok eceta;
Wel 7:45 wod twon acel, nyok romo acel, ki wod romo acel me mwaka acel pi gitum awaŋa:
Wel 7:46 nyok dyel acel pi gitum me bal;
Wel 7:47 ka doki pi gityer lakwecwiny otyero twoni aryo, nyogi romi abic, nyogi dyegi abic, ki litino nyogi romi abic ma ditogi mwaka acel acel, Man aye gityer ma Eliacap wod pa Deuel otyero.
Wel 7:48 I nino me abirone obedo kare pa Elicama wod pa Amikud, ma en aye latel wi jo pa Epraim.
Wel 7:49 Pi gityerre en otyero caani me ryal acel ma pekke romo cekel miya acel ki pyeradek, ki becen me ryal acel ma pekke cekel pyerabiro, ka giporo ki cekel me kabedo maleŋ; gin aryo ducu igi opoŋ ki moko kwon mapwotte ma girubo ki moo pi gityer me moko kwon,
Wel 7:50 ka doki atabo me jabu acel ma pekke cekel apar ma opoŋ ki odok eceta;
Wel 7:51 wod twon acel, nyok romo acel, ki wod romo acel me mwaka acel pi gitum awaŋa;
Wel 7:52 nyok dyel acel pi gitum me bal;
