Nwoyo Cik 8:14 Pe wiwu owil woko i kom Rwot Lubaŋawu, ma yam okwanyowu woko ki i lobo Ejipt, ki i ot me opii ca,
Nwoyo Cik 8:15 ma yam otelo wiwu wuwok kwede i tim malac ki malik bene, ma tye iye lwak twol ma kwirgi kec, ki oton, ki lobo ma orwo pii mako iye dano, ma pii pe iye-ni, ci en okelowu pii mua ki i pata got.
Nwoyo Cik 8:16 En bene opitowu i tim ki manna ma yam kwarowu pe giŋeyo, wek elokwu wudok mwol, kun temo ki cwinywu, wek otimwu ber lacen.
Nwoyo Cik 8:17 Wugwokke wuwek Lwodo lok ki i cwinywu ni, ‘Tek koma ki twero me bada gira aye omiyo alimo lonyo man.’
Nwoyo Cik 8:18 Wun wubipo i kom Rwot Lubaŋawu, pien en aye ma miyowu tek me limo lonyo; wek en omok gicikkene ma yam okwoŋo pire bot kwarowu, macalo pud tye wa kombeddi.
Nwoyo Cik 8:19 Ka ce wiwu owil woko i kom Rwot Lubaŋawu, ci wucako lubo kor lwak lubaŋa mukene, ki tiyo botgi ki ryebbe piny i nyimgi, atitowu atyer tin ni, wubito wutum woko liweŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 8:20 Wubito wutum woko macalo lurok ma Rwot tye ka miyogi to gitum woko ki i nyimwu-ni, pien pe wumedo ki woro dog Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 9:1 “Wuwiny, wun jo Icrael; wubikato loka Jordan tin, wek wucit ka camo lobo pa rok madito ki matego makatowu, ki gaŋi bene madito, ma gigoyo iye cel matek ma o wa i polo,
Nwoyo Cik 9:2 rok madit ma giboco, likwayo pa jo Anak, ma wuŋeyogi, ma yam doŋ wuwinyo nyiŋgi kun giwaco ni, ‘Aŋa ma twero cuŋ i nyim likwayo pa Anak?’
Nwoyo Cik 9:3 Pi meno myero wuŋe lok man tin ni, Ŋat ma tye ka wot i nyimwu macalo mac ma waŋo piny en aye Rwot Lubaŋawu; en aye bityekogi, en aye bitayogi woko ki i
Nwoyo Cik 9:4 “Ka doŋ Rwot Lubaŋawu otyeko ryemogi woko ki i nyimwu, pe wulwod lok ki i cwinywu ni, ‘Pi an ma abedo ma kita atir en aye omiyo Rwot okela ka camo lobo- ni’; kun kono pi bal maraco ma rok meno ducu gitimo aye omiyo Rwot biryemogi woko ki i nyimwu.
Nwoyo Cik 9:5 Pe wubicito ka camo lobogi pi kitwu ma atir, nyo pi leŋ iwu, ento pi bal maraco ma rok meno ducu gitimo en aye omiyo Rwot Lubaŋawu biryemogi woko ki i nyimwu, dok wek ecob lok ma yam okwoŋo bot kwarowu Abraim ki Icaka ki Yakobo. Jemo pa jo Icrael i Koreb (Nia 31.18–32.35)
Nwoyo Cik 9:6 “Myero doŋ wuŋe ni, pe pi kitwu ma atir en aye omiyo Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu lobo man maber-ri wek wucam; pien wun jo ma ŋutwu tek.
Nwoyo Cik 9:7 Ber wupo, dok bene wiwu pe owil kit ma yam Rwot Lubaŋawu obedo ki akemo i tim. Nia wa i nino ma yam wua iye ki i lobo Ejipt, o kwede wa i kare ma wuo i kabedo-ni, wubedo lujemo i kom Rwot.
Nwoyo Cik 9:8 Kadi wa i Koreb wumiyo Rwot obedo ki akemo, ci yam Rwot kiniga omake i komwu twatwal, omiyo onoŋo cok ka tyekowu woko.
Nwoyo Cik 9:9 I kare ma yam aito malo i wi got ka gamo kidi aryo ma apada-ni, kidi me gicikke ma yam Rwot oketo kwed wu, ci abedo i wi got, ari nino pyeraŋwen dyeceŋ ki dyewor kun pe acamo dok pe amato pii bene.
Nwoyo Cik 9:10 Ci Rwot omiya kidi aryo ma apada ma Lubaŋa onoŋo ocoyo ki ciŋe, kun ocoyo i komgi lwak lok ducu ma yam Rwot obedo ka loko i wi got ki i dye mac, i nino ma yam lwak ocokke iye ca.
Nwoyo Cik 9:11 Ka nino pyeraŋwen ki dyewor pyeraŋwen doŋ okato, Rwot omiya kidi meno aryo ma apada, gin kidi me gicikke.
Nwoyo Cik 9:12 Ka dok Rwot owacca ni, ‘A malo, icit ilor piny ki kany oyot, pien joni ma yam ikelogi ki i Ejipt gutyeko balle woko, Gulokke, gubarre woko oyot nia ki i yo ma yam acikogi kwede, gutimo gigi cal jabu ma giliyo aliya.’
Nwoyo Cik 9:13 “Rwot dok omedde ki lok kun wacca ni, ‘Atyeko neno jo man, ci nen, gin jo ma ŋutgi tek.
Nwoyo Cik 9:14 Weka gira, weka doŋ atyekgi woko liweŋ; abijwayo nyiŋgi woko ki i te polo, ci abimiyo in idoko rok matek twatwal ki madit makatogi.’
Nwoyo Cik 9:15 Ci alokke, alor piny ki i wi got, kun got tye ka waŋ ki mac. Onoŋo amako kidi apada aryo me gicikke ki ciŋa aryo ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 9:16 Ka aneno, ci nen, wutyeko timo bal i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu, Onoŋo wutimo giwu cal wod twon ma giliyo aliya, kun wulokke, wubarre woko oyot ki i yo ma yam Rwot ocikowu kwede-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 9:17 Ci ame ko kidi aryo ma apada ca, abologi woko piny ki i ciŋa aryo ducu, atyerogi woko ki i waŋwu.
Nwoyo Cik 9:18 Lacen abuto aryeba cwiny i nyim Rwot nino pyeraŋwen dyeceŋ ki dyewor kit ma con ca; pe acamo, pe amato pii bene, pi lwak bal ducu ma wubedo ka timone, kun wutimo gin ma nen marac i waŋ Rwot ma omiyo kiniga omake.
Nwoyo Cik 9:19 Pien onoŋo lworo omaka pi kiniga pa Rwot ki akecane malyet i komwu ma onoŋo cok ka tyekowu woko. Ento Rwot owinya wa i kare meno bene.
Nwoyo Cik 9:20 Kiniga yam omako Rwot i kom Aron bene matek, omiyo onoŋo doŋ cok ka neke wo ko; ento i kare ca alego pi Aron bene.
Nwoyo Cik 9:21 Dok akwanyo balwu, en aye wod twon ma wutimo-ni, ci awaŋo woko ki mac, aodo, arego woko mapwot, nio ka odoko apwa; ci aonyo apwane i kulu ma mol piny a ki i wi got.
Nwoyo Cik 9:22 “Dok bene yam i Tabera, ki i Maca ki i Kibrot-atava wubedo ka mi yo Rwot bedo ki akemo.
Nwoyo Cik 9:23 Ka yam Rwot ocwalowu nia ki i Kadec-barnea kun waco ni, ‘Wucit, wucam lobo ma doŋ amiyowu-ni’, ci wujemo woko i kom cik pa Rwot Lubaŋawu; yam pe wugene, pe wuworo doge.
Nwoyo Cik 9:24 Wun wubedo lujemo i kom Rwot nia wa i nino ma yam acako ŋeyowu iye-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 9:25 “Kit meno abuto aryeba cwiny i nyim Rwot nino pyeraŋwen dyeceŋ ki dyewor, pien onoŋo Rwot owaco ni emito tyekowu woko.
Nwoyo Cik 9:26 Ci yam alego bot Rwot ni, ‘Ai Rwot Lubaŋa, pe ityek lwakki woko, ma gin aye gipinnyi ma yam ikokogi pi ditti, ma ikwanyogi woko ki i Ejipt pi twero me badi.
Nwoyo Cik 9:27 Ber ipo i kom luticci Abraim, Icaka ki Yakobo. Pe ibed ka paro pi tek ŋut pa rok man, nyo pi timgi maraco, nyo pi balgi,
Nwoyo Cik 9:28 wek jo me lobo ma yam ikwanyowa ki iye-ni pe gubed ka waco ni,. Pien onoŋo terogi i lobo ma yam ocikke pire botgi doŋ oloyo Rwot woko, dok pien onoŋo yam kara dag wangi, en aye omiyo okwanyogi woko, wek enekgi woko i dye tim.
Nwoyo Cik 9:29 Pien gin aye lwakki, gin gipinnyi, ma doŋ ikelogi woko ki tekki madwoŋ ki pi ciŋi ma iryeyo.’
Nwoyo Cik 10:1 “I kare meno Rwot owacca ni, ‘Muk kidi ma apada aryo, ipagi macalo mukwoŋo ca; ci ibin bota i wi got malo, dok ipa canduk me bao.
Nwoyo Cik 10:2 Abicoyo i kom kidi ma apada-nu lok ma yam tye i kom kidi ma apada mukwoŋo ma yam ityero woko ca, ci ibiketogi i canduk.’
Nwoyo Cik 10:3 Kit meno atimo canduk ki bao yat lalwii, ci amuko kidi ma apada aryo, apayo ma rom ki macon ca, aito malo i wi got kun amako kidi ma apada aryo-nu i ciŋa.
Nwoyo Cik 10:4 Rwot ocoyo i kom kidi-nu macalo yam okwoŋo coyo, gin cik apar ma yam oloko ki wun i wi got ki i dye mac i nino ma yam wucokke iye ca; ci Rwot omiyogi bota.
Nwoyo Cik 10:5 Lacen alokke, alor piny ki i wi got, ci aketo kidi ma apada aryo-nu i canduk ma yam apayo-ni; gin pud gitye ene, kit ma yam Rwot ocika kwede.
Nwoyo Cik 10:6 (Jo Icrael gua ki i Beerot Benejaakan, guo Mocera. Aron oto ki kunnu, giyike bene kunnu; ci wode Eleajar oleyo ka tyene i tic me bedo ajwaka pa Lubaŋa.
Nwoyo Cik 10:7 Gua ki kunnu, guwoto guo i Gudugoda, ki nia ki i Gudugoda guo Jotibata, en aye lobo ma tye iye lwak nota ora ma igi ki pii.
Nwoyo Cik 10:8 I kare meno en aye Rwot ocako poko kaka pa Lulevi pat, gubed lutiŋ canduk me gicikke pa Rwot, gucuŋ i nyim Rwot kun gitiyo bote, dok gulam gum i nyiŋe, nio wa i nino man.
Nwoyo Cik 10:9 En gin mumiyo jo pa Levi pe gitye ki dul lobo mo nyo ginaleya mo i kin omegigi; Rwot aye ginaleyagi, kit macalo Rwot Lubaŋawu yam owaco botgi.)
Nwoyo Cik 10:10 “Yam abedo i wi got macalo i kare mukwoŋo ca, abedo nino pyeraŋwen dyeceŋ ki dyewor; ci Rwot dok owinya i kare meno bene, omiyo Rwot pe dok mito tyekowa woko.
Nwoyo Cik 10:11 Lacen Rwot owacca ni, ‘A malo, imed wotti kun itelo wi lwak, wek gudony, gucam lobo ma yam akwoŋo pire bot kwarogi ni abimiyogi.’ Gin ma Lubaŋa mito ki botwa
Nwoyo Cik 10:12 “Doŋ kombeddi, wun jo Icrael, gin ma Rwot Lubaŋawu mito ki botwu en ene keken ni, wulwor Rwot Lubaŋawu ki cwinywu ducu ki tipowu ducu,
Nwoyo Cik 10:13 dok wugwok gin ducu ma en ociko ki cik mapatpat ma acikowu kwede tin wek wubed doŋ maber.
Nwoyo Cik 10:14 Nen, Rwot Lubaŋawu aye rwot me polo, ki polo ma malo makato ducu, ki lobo ki jami ma tye ducu liweŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 10:15 Ento kadi bed kumeno, Rwot oketo cwinye i kom kwarowu, omarogi, oyero likwayogi ma gulubogi, ma gin aye wun, ki i kin rok ducu macalo wa i kare man.
Nwoyo Cik 10:16 Pienno, wubed jo ma gulirre wa i cwinygi, pe wubed jo ma ŋutgi tek.
Nwoyo Cik 10:17 Pien Rwot Lubaŋawu aye Lubaŋa pa lubaŋa ducu ki Rwot pa rwodi. En Lubaŋa madit, ma tye ki tek, ma ryaŋo kom dano; pe dworo kor dano mo, pe giwilo ki lim.
Nwoyo Cik 10:18 En ŋolo kop pa litino kic atir, ki pa mon to, dok maro lubedo bene, miyogi cam ki boŋŋi.
Nwoyo Cik 10:19 Wun bene myero wumar lubedo, pien yam wubedo lubedo i lobo Ejipt.
Nwoyo Cik 10:20 Wulwor Rwot Lubaŋawu; wuti bote kun wumoko i kome matek, dok wukwoŋ kwoŋwu ki nyiŋe keken.
Nwoyo Cik 10:21 En aye ma myero wupake; en Lubaŋawu ma yam otimo botwu tim man ducu madito ki ma ryaŋo kom dano, ma waŋwu doŋ oneno-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 10:22 Kwarowu yam gucito i Ejipt kun gin jo pyerabiro keken; ci tin Rwot Lubaŋawu doŋ omiyo wunya mapol macalo lwak lakalatwe me polo.
Nwoyo Cik 11:1 “Mar Rwot Lubaŋani, lub cikke i kare ducu, cik mapatpat ma oketo ki oŋon me cikke ki lok ma en oŋolo ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 11:2 Tin doŋ wutam, (pien pe atye ka lok ki litinowu ma yam pe giŋeyo dok ma pe guneno), wutam kit ma Rwot Lubaŋawu opwonyowu kwede pi tiro kitwu, wutam pi ditte ki bade matek ki ciŋe ma oryeyo-ni,
Nwoyo Cik 11:3 ki lwak lanyut ki ticce ma otiyo i Ejipt i kom Parao kabaka me Ejipt ki i kom lobone ducu;
Nwoyo Cik 11:4 ki gin ma otimo i kom mony pa jo Ejipt ki i kom aguraguragi ducu ki gadigadigi, ki kit ma yam omiyo pii me Nam Makwar omwonyogi woko i kare ma giryemo korwu-ni, ki kit ma Rwot otyekogi woko kwede nio wa i kare man.
Nwoyo Cik 11:5 Dok wutam gin ma yam otimo i komwu i tim nio ka wubino wuo i kabedo man;
Nwoyo Cik 11:6 wupo bene gin ma en otiyo i kom Datan ki Abiram ma awobe pa Eliab wod pa Reuben; ki kit ma yam lobo oŋamo kwede doge ci omwonyogi woko ki jo ma i otgi ducu ki kemagi ducu;
Nwoyo Cik 11:7 pien wutyeko neno ki waŋwu tic madito ma Rwot yam otiyo ducu. Gum ma binen i lobo ma Rwot ocikke me miyogi
Nwoyo Cik 11:8 “Wumak cikka ducu ma acikowu kwede tin-ni, wek wubed ki tek me cito i lobo ma wubicito loka ca ka camone obed mewu, wucam,
Nwoyo Cik 11:9 dok wek wuri pi kare malac i lobo ma yam Rwot okwoŋo pire bot kwarowu, ni ebimiyogi wa ki likwayogi bene, en lobo ma mol cak ki moo kic.
Nwoyo Cik 11:10 Pien lobo ma wubidonyo iye ka camone-ni pe rom ki lobo Ejipt ka ma yam wua iye-ni, ka ma yam wucoyo iye kodiwu ka dok wubaro waŋ piine ki tyenwu, macalo poto dek ma gicamo pote-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 11:11 Ento lobo ma wucito loka ca ka camone obed mewu obedo lobo godi ki nota-gu, ma mato pii kot ma cwer a ki i polo;
Nwoyo Cik 11:12 en aye lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu gwoko; waŋ Rwot Lubaŋawu bedo i kome nino ducu, nia i acakki mwaka o wa i agikki mwaka ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 11:13 “Ka wubilubo cikka ducu ma acikowu kwede tin-ni, ni wumar Rwot Lubaŋawu, wuti bote ki cwinywu ducu ki tipowu ducu,
Nwoyo Cik 11:14 ci en bimiyo kot cwer i lobowu i karene, i poto kot ki kot oro-gu, wek wucek kalwu ki koŋo vinowu ki moowu.
Nwoyo Cik 11:15 Dok en bimiyowu lum i oletwu me cam pa lim makwo, miyo wubinoŋo, cam ma yeŋowu.
Nwoyo Cik 11:16 Wugwokke wek pe gibwolwu, miyo wulokke: wubarre woko, wutiyo bot lwak lubaŋa mukene, wuworogi bene,
Nwoyo Cik 11:17 miyo kiniga mako Rwot i komwu, ci geŋo polo, juko kot pe cwer, miyo lobo pe ceko cam, ci wuto wutum woko oyotoyot ki i lobo maber ma Rwot bimiyowu-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 11:18 “Wubiketo lok magi ducu i cwinywu ki i tamwu; wubitweyogi i ŋut ciŋwu obed me lanyut, dok gubed me atweya i dye tur nyimwu.
Nwoyo Cik 11:19 Wupwony litinowu ki lok magi, wubed ka lok komgi ka wubedo i odiwu, ka wutye ka wot i yo, ka wubuto piny ki ka wua malo.
Nwoyo Cik 11:20 Dok wuco lok magi i yat doggola odiwu, ki i dog gaŋwu,
Nwoyo Cik 11:21 wek wun ki likwayowu wuri pi mwaka mapol i lobo ma yam Rwot okwoŋo pire bot kwarowu ni ebimiyogi pi kare ducu ma polo pud bibedo malo ka wi lobo.
Nwoyo Cik 11:22 Ka ce wubigwokke wek wulub cik man ducu ma atye ka cikowu kwede ni wulubi, kun wumaro Rwot Lubaŋawu, ma wulubo yone ducu, ma wucuŋ i kome matek,
Nwoyo Cik 11:23 ci Rwot biryemo rok mukene woko ducu ki i nyimwu, miyo wucamo lobo pa rok madito ki matego makatowu.
Nwoyo Cik 11:24 Kabedo ducu ma tyenwu binyono bibedo mewu; ci lobo ma wubiloyo bibedo nia wa i tim nio wa i Lebanon, ki nia wa i Kulu, ma en aye kulu Euprate, nio wa i nam ma yo tuŋ potoceŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 11:25 Pe tye dano mo ma bicuŋ i nyimwu; Rwot Lubaŋawu biketo lworo ki atiba piwu i kom lobo ducu ma tyenwu binyonone, kit ma yam ocikowu kwede-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 11:26 “Nen, tin aketo i nyimwu gum ki ceno dano:
Nwoyo Cik 11:27 gum bibino ka ce wulubo cik pa Rwot Lubaŋawu ma atye ka cikowu kwede tin- ni,
Nwoyo Cik 11:28 ci ceno dano bi bino ka ce pe wulubo cik pa Rwot Lubaŋawu, ento noŋo wulokke, wubarre woko nia ki i yo ma acikowu kwede tinni ci dok wulubo kor lubaŋa mukene ma yam pe wuŋeyo.
Nwoyo Cik 11:29 Ka Rwot Lubaŋawu doŋ okelowu i lobo ma wubicito iye ka camone-ni, ci wubiketo gum obed i kom got Gerijim, ki ceno dano bibedo i kom got Eba!.
Nwoyo Cik 11:30 Gin godi-nu gitye loka Jordan, ma but piny yo tuŋ potoceŋ, tuŋ ka ma ceŋ poto iye-ni, i lobo pa jo Kanaan ma gibedo i Araba, ma okemo Gilgal, ma ka ŋet yadi kworo me More;
Nwoyo Cik 11:31 Wubiŋolo Jordan, wukato loka ca ka camo lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu. Ka doŋ wucamo, ma wubedo iye,
Nwoyo Cik 11:32 ci wugwokke wek wulub cik ki oŋon me cikke ducu ma doŋ aketo i nyimwu tin- ni.
Nwoyo Cik 12:1 “Magi gin aye cik ki oŋon me cik ma wubimako matek kun wulubogi i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋa pa kwarowu bimiyowu obed mewu, pi kare ducu ma wubibedo iye i wi lobo-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 12:2 Wubibalo kabedo ducu liweŋ ka ma yam rok ducu ma ubigamo lobogi giworo iye lubaŋagi, ma gitye malo i wi godi mabocone ducu ki i wi cere ki i waŋ ayweya ma i te yadi ma potgi oluk.
Nwoyo Cik 12:3 Wumuk keno jogigi woko ducu, wuŋid wir jogi megi woko matitino, wuwaŋ yadi ma gicomo i ŋom pi woro jok ma dako ma gilwoŋo Acera, wutoŋ cal lubaŋa apaya-gi woko ducu, wunek nyiŋgi woko ki i kabedo meno.
Nwoyo Cik 12:4 Pe wubitimo kit meno i kom Rwot Lubaŋawu,
Nwoyo Cik 12:5 ento wubipenyo dog Rwot Lubaŋawu i kabedo ma en biyero ki i kin kakawu ducu pi keto iye nyiŋe wek obed pacone.
Nwoyo Cik 12:6 Kenyo aye wubicito iye, kenyo en aye wubitero iye gitum awaŋa ki gitum mewu ducu, ki dul acel me apar, ki gityer mapatpat ma wubimiyo, gityer me cobo kwoŋ, ki gityer ma iwu opwoyo, ki litino kayo pa dyaŋiwu ki pa romi ki dyegiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 12:7 Wubicamone ki kunnu i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu, ci cwinywu bibedo yom, wun ki jo ma i odiwu ducu, i kom gin ducu ma wubiketo iye ciŋwu, ma onoŋo Rwot Lubaŋawu omiyowu iye gum.
Nwoyo Cik 12:8 “Pe wubitimo kunnu kit ma watye ka timo kany i kare-ni, ma dano acel acel tye ka tiyo gin ducu ma en tamo ni tye atir;
Nwoyo Cik 12:9 pien peya wuo i kabedo me yweyowu, i lobo ma wubileyo, ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu.
Nwoyo Cik 12:10 Ento ka doŋ wukato loka Jordan, ma wubedo i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋa bimiyo me aleyawu, ka doŋ omiyo wuywe ki i lweny i kom lumerokwu ma gurumowu dyere- ni, ci doŋ wubibedo ma piny okwe mot.
Nwoyo Cik 12:11 Rwot Lubaŋawu biyero kabedo ka ma en biketo iye nyiŋe bedo iye; kenyo en aye wubikelo iye gin ducu ma acikowu-ni: gitum awaŋawu ki gitum mukene ducu, ki dul acel me apar, ki gityer mapatpat ma wubimiyo, ki gityer me cobo kwon ducu ma wukwoŋo me miyogi bot Rwot.
Nwoyo Cik 12:12 Ci cwinywu bibedo yom i nyim Rwot, wun ki awobewu ki anyirawu, opiiwu ki aŋecawu ducu, ki Lulevi ma tye i gaŋiwu, pien gin Lulevi pe gibipokogi dul lobo mo nyo kabedo mo i kinwu me aleyagi.
Nwoyo Cik 12:13 Gwokke wek pe ityer gitum awaŋani i kabedo mo ma ineno;
Nwoyo Cik 12:14 ento ibityerone ki i kabedo ma Rwot biyero ki i kakawu mo acel. Ibityero gitum awaŋani ducu kunnu, dok ibitiyo gin ducu ma aciki-ni ki kunnu.
Nwoyo Cik 12:15 “Ento wutwero neko lee me acamawu ki i gaŋiwu ducu kit ma cwinywu mito, muporo gum ma Rwot Lubaŋawu omiyowu. Dano ma kome ki keni twero camo, ki dano ma olony, macalo gicamo riŋo abur nyo til.
Nwoyo Cik 12:16 Remone keken aye pe wubicamo; wubionyo woko piny i ŋom, macalo pii.
Nwoyo Cik 12:17 Pe myero wucam dul acel me apar me kalwu, nyo me koŋo vinowu nyo me moo jeituniwu ki i gaŋiwu, kadi litino kayo pa dyaŋiwu nyo pa romi ki dyegiwu, nyo gityer me cobo kwoŋwu ma wukwoŋo, nyo gityer mewu ma cwinywu opwoyo, nyo gityer mo ma wumiyo.
Nwoyo Cik 12:18 Ento wubicamo ki i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu i kabedo ma en biyero, in ki wodi ki nyari, ki opiini, ki aŋecani, ki Lulevi ma i gaŋwu; dok cwinyi bibedo yom i nyim Rwot Lubaŋani pi gin ducu ma ibiketo iye ciŋi.
Nwoyo Cik 12:19 Gwokke pe ibwot Lulevi ata i kare ducu ma ibedo i lobowu-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 12:20 “Ka Rwot Lubaŋawu doŋ oyabo waŋ lobowu obedo malac, kit ma yam ocikke kwede botwu, ce iwacci, ‘Abicamo riŋo,’ pien onoŋo itye ki miti iye, ci itwero camo riŋo kit ma cwinyi mito.
Nwoyo Cik 12:21 Ka ce kabedo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu biyero me keto iye nyiŋe tye ka mabor ki ka ma itye-ni, ci itwero neko dyaŋŋi nyo romoni ma Rwot omiyo boti, macalo doŋ aciki; itwero camo ki i gaŋŋi kit ma cwinyi mito.
Nwoyo Cik 12:22 Itwero camone kit ma gicamo riŋo abur ki til; kadi wa dano ma kome ki keni twero camone kacel ki dano ma olony.
Nwoyo Cik 12:23 Cuŋ matek i man keken ni, pe icam remone, pien remo en aye kwo; pienno pe ibicamo kwo kacel ki riŋone.
Nwoyo Cik 12:24 Pe ibicamone, ibionyo woko i ŋom macalo pii.
Nwoyo Cik 12:25 Pe ibicamone, wek nyimi obed leŋ, in kacel ki litinoni ma bilubi, ka ce ibedo ka tiyo gin ma nen atir i waŋ Rwot.
Nwoyo Cik 12:26 Ento jamini maleŋ ducu ma myero imi, ki gityer me cobo kwoŋ, ibikwanyo icito kwede i kabedo ma Rwot biyero.
Nwoyo Cik 12:27 Ibityero gitum awaŋani ducu, riŋone ki remone, i wi keno tyer pa Rwot Lubaŋani; remo me gitummi ducu gibionyo woko i kom keno tyer pa Rwot Lubaŋani, ento riŋone ibicamo.
Nwoyo Cik 12:28 Gwokke wek ilub lok magi ducu ma aciki kwede-ni, wek nyimi obed leŋ nakanaka, in ki likwayi ma bilubi, ka ce itiyo gin ma nen maber ki ma atir i waŋ Rwot Lubaŋani. Juk i kom woro jogi
Nwoyo Cik 12:29 “Ka Rwot Lubaŋawu doŋ otyeko lurok woko ki i nyimwu ma wucito ka camo lobogi-ni, ma doŋ wucamo lobogi, wubedo iye,
Nwoyo Cik 12:30 myero wugwokke wek pe wumok i owic pi lubo kitgi, i kare ma doŋ gityekogi woko ki i nyimwu. Dok pe wubed ka penyo lok i kom lubaŋagi, kun wuwacci, ‘Rok man yam giworo lubaŋagi niŋniŋ? wek an bene aworgi kit meno.’
Nwoyo Cik 12:31 Pe ibitimo kumeno i kom Rwot Lubaŋawu, pien gibedo ka timo gin me kwer ducu ma Rwot dagi pi woro lwak lubaŋagi; giwaŋo wa awobegi ki anyiragi ki mac macalo gitum me woro lubaŋagi.
Nwoyo Cik 12:32 “Gin ducu ma acikowu kwede myero wugwokke ka lubone; pe wubimedo wiye nyo wukwanyo mogo woko.
Nwoyo Cik 13:1 “Ka ce lanebi mo onen i kinwu, nyo lalek lek mo, miyo wu lanyut nyo taŋo mo,
Nwoyo Cik 13:2 ka ce lanyut nyo taŋo ma otitti pire-ni otimme kakare, ce en owacci, ‘Wek doŋ walub kor lubaŋa mukene,’ ma yam pe iŋeyo, ‘wacak worogi,’
Nwoyo Cik 13:3 pe iwiny dog lanebi meno, lalek meno; pien noŋo Rwot Lubaŋawu tye ka temo cwinywu wek eŋe ka wumaro Rwot Lubaŋawu ki cwinywu ducu ki tipowu ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 13:4 Wulub kor Rwot Lubaŋawu kun wulworo en dok wugwoko cikke ducu; wuwor doge, wuti bote kun wucuŋ i kome matek.
Nwoyo Cik 13:5 Ento nyo lalek meno wubineko woko, pien opwonyo dano ki jemo i kom Rwot Lubaŋawu, ma yam okwanyowu woko ki i lobo Ejipt, okokowu ki i ot me opii, ci
Nwoyo Cik 13:6 “Ka ce omeru mo ma wod pa meni, nyo wodi, nyo nyari, nyo damaroni kikome, nyo laremi ma imaro ki kwoni ducu, obiti i muŋ kun wacci, ‘Wek wacit ka woro lubaŋa mogo mukene,’ ma noŋo in kikomi nyo kwarowu yam pe guŋeyo,
Nwoyo Cik 13:7 lubaŋa pa rok ma gurumowu dyere-ni, kadi ma gitye ka ma cok kwedwu nyo gitye ka mabor, nia i agikki lobo tuŋ cel cito kwede i agikkine tuŋ cel,
Nwoyo Cik 13:8 pe iye doge, pe iwiny lokke, pe kica omaki i kome, pe imuŋ lokke;
Nwoyo Cik 13:9 ento ibineke woko. Ciŋi aye bikwoŋo poto i kome me neke, lacen ciŋ lwak ducu bipoto i kome.
Nwoyo Cik 13:10 Ibicele ki got ineko woko, pien obedo ka yenyo yo me kwanyi woko ki bot Rwot Lubaŋawu ma yam okwanyowu woko ki i lobo Ejipt, ki i ot me opii.
Nwoyo Cik 13:11 Ci jo Icrael ducu gibiwinyo pire, ci gibilworo, miyo pe gibinwoyo timo bal marac macalo meno i kinwu.
Nwoyo Cik 13:12 “Gwok nyo i gaŋ mo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu me bedo iye wubiwinyo ni
Nwoyo Cik 13:13 jo mogo ma kitgi raco, ma gin jowu kikome, guywayo tam pa jo ma bedo i gaŋ meno kun giwacci, ‘Wubin wacitu ka woro lubaŋa mukene,’ ma yam pe wuŋeyo.
Nwoyo Cik 13:14 Myero wupeny lokke kun wuyenyo tere motmot; ka ce onen ni lokke otimme ada, ma gimoko ni lok me kwer macalo meno otimme i kinwu,
Nwoyo Cik 13:15 ci wubineko jo ma gibedo i gaŋ meno woko ki pala lucwan, wujwerogi woko ducu liweŋ, Jo ducu ma tye iye, ki lim makwo bene ma tye iye, myero gutum woko ki pala lucwan.
Nwoyo Cik 13:16 Wubicoko jami ma wuyako-ni ducu, wugurogi i dyekal ka maleŋ, ci wubiwaŋo gaŋ meno ki jami ducu ma tye iye woko ki mac, obed gitum ma giwaŋo ducu ki berre bot Rwot Lubaŋawu. Bibedo wi odur matwal; pe dok gibigero iye gaŋ mo.
Nwoyo Cik 13:17 Gin mo ma gidyero bot Rwot pe wubiweko doŋ i ciŋwu, wek Rwot okwany kinigane mager twatwal-li woko. Bitimowu kica kun nyuto cwiny me kica i komwu, ci miyo wunya mapol kit ma yam okwoŋo kwede bot kwarowu-ni,
Nwoyo Cik 13:18 ka ce wuworo dog Rwot Lubaŋawu, wumako cikke ducu ma acikowu kwede tin-ni dok wutiyo gin ma nen atir i waŋe.
Nwoyo Cik 14:1 “Wun aye litino pa Rwot Lubaŋawu: pe wubiŋolo komwu kenwu nyo Lyelo tur nyimwu pi kwero cola.
Nwoyo Cik 14:2 Pien wun aye jo maleŋ pa Rwot Lubaŋawu; en Rwot aye yam oyerowu ki i kin rok ducu ma tye i wi lobo wek wubed jone kikome.
Nwoyo Cik 14:3 “Pe wubicamo gin mo me kwer.
Nwoyo Cik 14:4 Magi aye gin lee ma wutwero camogi: dyaŋ, romo, dyel,
Nwoyo Cik 14:5 til, abur, ruda, dyel me tim, jubi, pura, ki romo ma i godi.
Nwoyo Cik 14:6 Lee ducu ma oboŋ tyengi akara, ma kin tyengi opokke aryo, ma nyamo omen ki i kin lee ducu wutwero camogi.
Nwoyo Cik 14:7 Ento lee ma ginyamo omen nyo ma oboŋ tyengi akara ma pe wubicamo gin ene; kinaga, apwoyo ki oduka, Gin ginyamo omen ento kin tyengi pe akara; pienno gibedo keni botwu.
Nwoyo Cik 14:8 Ki opego bene, pien kadi oboŋ tyene akara ento pe nyamo omen, en bene bedo keni botwu. Pe wucam riŋogi, pe wugud wa komgi ma oto bene.
Nwoyo Cik 14:9 “Magi aye wutwero camogi ki i kin gin ducu ma bedo i pii: gin ducu ma tye ki kiŋa ŋegi ki pok komgi wutwero camogi;
Nwoyo Cik 14:10 ento gin ma pe ki kiŋa ŋegi ki pok komgi pe wubicamogi, pien gibedo keni botwu.
Nwoyo Cik 14:11 “Wutwero camo winyo ma gilony ducu,
Nwoyo Cik 14:12 ento magi aye pe wubicamogi: ocur, acut, koga,
Nwoyo Cik 14:13 agoga, okwata ki kit kwagi ducu;
Nwoyo Cik 14:14 agak ki kit kwagi ducu;
Nwoyo Cik 14:15 udu, tebu, awewet, olwilwit ki kit kwagi ducu;
Nwoyo Cik 14:16 tula matino ki tula madoŋo, lagweno kulu,
Nwoyo Cik 14:17 kikuŋ ki ocur madito ki alwinya,
Nwoyo Cik 14:18 acebe ki ogoro ki kit kwagi ducu; ki putput ki olik.
Nwoyo Cik 14:19 “Ki kwidi ducu ma bwomgi tye gibedo keni botwu; pe wubicamogi.
Nwoyo Cik 14:20 Gin ducu ma bwomgi tye ma gilony wutwero camogi.
Nwoyo Cik 14:21 “Pe wubicamo geŋ lee mo muto kene; wutwero miyo bot labedo mo ma bedo i gaŋiwu, wek en aye ocam, nyo wutwero cato bot larok mo owil; pien wun aye rok maleŋ pa Rwot Lubaŋawu. “Pe wuted riŋo latin dyel ki cak pa minne. Cik ma mako dul acel me apar
Nwoyo Cik 14:22 “Wubimiyo dul acel me apar me jami ma wuceko i poto, ma a i poto mwaka ki mwaka.
Nwoyo Cik 14:23 Dok wubicamo dul acel me apar me kalwu ki i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu i kabedo ka ma en biyero ci keto nyiŋe bedo iye, ki dul acel me apar me koŋo vinowu ki moowu, ki litino kayo pa dyaŋiwu ki pa romi ki dyegiwu; wek wupwony lworo Rwot Lubaŋawu jwijwi.
Nwoyo Cik 14:24 Ka ce wutye ka mabor twatwal ma miyo pe wutwero kelo dul acel me apar i kare ma Rwot omiyowu iye gum-mi, pien kabedo ma Rwot oyero me keto iye nyiŋe odoko bor kwedwu,
Nwoyo Cik 14:25 ci wubicato woko wek wunoŋ cente, ci wutweyo lim meno wucito kwede i kabedo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu oyero-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 14:26 Wubitic ki lim meno pi kit gin ducu ma cwinywu mito, macalo me wilo twoni, nyo romo nyo koŋo vino nyo koŋo makecce, ki gin ducu ma cwinywu mito, ci wubicamo ki kunnu ki yomcwiny i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu, in ki jo ma i odi ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 14:27 Dok pe wubitenyo Lulevi ma gitye i gaŋwu ata, pien pe gipokogi dul lobo mo nyo gin mo me aleyagi kacel kwed wu.
Nwoyo Cik 14:28 “I agikki mwaka adek adek wubikelo iye dul acel me apar me gin ducu ma wuceko i mwaka-nu, wukano i gaŋiwu madito.
Nwoyo Cik 14:29 Ci Lulevi ma pe ki dul lobo nyo ka mo ma guleyo i kinwu, ki lubedo, ki litino kic, ki mon to ma i gaŋiwu ducu, gin ducu gibibino ka cam kwedwu giyeŋ; wek Rwot Lubaŋawu omiwu gum i kom gin ducu ma ciŋwu otiyo.
Nwoyo Cik 15:1 “I agikki mwaka abiro abiro wubiweko banya bot dano ma twal.
Nwoyo Cik 15:2 Man aye kit me weko banya: lami banya biweko banya me lim matwal ki bot dano ma yam omako banyane-ni; pe bipido banyane bot lawote matwal ma ominne, pien doŋ gityeko tito ki dano pi weko banya matwal kit ma Rwot ociko- ni.
Nwoyo Cik 15:3 Itwero pido larok ocul banyani; ento kwany cwinyi woko i kom banya ma omeru ma Laicrael omako boti.
Nwoyo Cik 15:4 Ento lacan mo pe doŋ bibedo i kinwu, pien Rwot bimiyowu gum i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu wucam me aleyawu matwal,
Nwoyo Cik 15:5 ka ce wubiworo dog Rwot Lubaŋawu kun wugwokke wek wulub cikke ducu ma acikowu kwede tin.
Nwoyo Cik 15:6 Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu gum kit ma yam ocikke kwede botwu-ni. Wubimiyo rok mapol mako banya botwu, ento wun pe wubimako banya mo; dok wubiloyo rok mapol, ento gin pe gibiloyowu.
Nwoyo Cik 15:7 “Ka tye dano mo ma lacan i kinwu, i kin omegiwu ma gitye i gaŋ mo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu, pe cwinyi obed tek, pe ijuk ciŋi woko i kom ominwu-nu ma lacan-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 15:8 Ento ikonye, imiye mako banya ma romo cobo gin ma en mito ducu, kadi bed gin aŋo.
Nwoyo Cik 15:9 Ber igwokke wek tam marac mo pe obed i cwinyi ma miyo iwacci, ‘Mwaka me abiro, ma en aye mwaka me weko banya matwal, doŋ cok,’ ci waŋi cido woko i kom omeru ma lacan-ni miyo pe doŋ imiye gin mo. Meno miyo en cako kok i komi i nyim Rwot, ci doko bal i komi.
Nwoyo Cik 15:10 Ka imiye gin mo, ber imiye ma cwinyi leŋ matwal, cwinyi pe waŋ pi gin ma imiye-ni: pien Rwot Lubaŋani bimiyi gum i kom tic ducu ma itiyo, ki i kom gin ducu ma ciŋi ogudo.
Nwoyo Cik 15:11 Lucan pe gibitum woko i lobowu, mumiyo aciki ni, ibiyabo ciŋi malac bot omeru ki jo ma piny oloyogi, ki bot lucan ma i lobowu. Tic ki opii (Nia 21.1-11)
Nwoyo Cik 15:12 “Ka ce gicato boti omeru mo, laco ma Laibru nyo dako ma Laibru, ci iwilo obed opiini nyo aŋecani, en bitiyo tic boti pi mwaka abicel. I mwaka me abirone ibiweke a woko ki boti cito gire ki kuc.
Nwoyo Cik 15:13 Ka igonye wek ociti, pe, ibiweko en cito ki ciŋe nono.
Nwoyo Cik 15:14 Ibimiye cito ki jami mapolpol, romi ki dyegi, bel ki koŋo vino, ma lubo kit ma Rwot Lubaŋani omiyi kwede gum.
Nwoyo Cik 15:15 Ibipo ni yam ibedo opii i lobo Ejipt, ka ma Rwot Lubaŋani okoki ki iye; en gin mumiyo tin aciki kumeno.
Nwoyo Cik 15:16 Ento ka en owacci, ‘An pe abia woko ki boti,’ pien en mari ki jo ma i odi ducu, pien obedo kwedwu maber,
Nwoyo Cik 15:17 ci ibikwanyo atero, ituco ki ite i doggola, ci doŋ bibedo opiini matwal. Ki aŋecani bene ibitimo kit meno.
Nwoyo Cik 15:18 Pe ibitamo ni tek twatwal me weke a woko ki boti, pien obedo ka tic boti pi mwaka abicel kulu kun ticce dodo tic pa Lapakaca kiryo pi wel manok mo. Ka itimo kit meno, Rwot Lubaŋani bimiyi gum i tic ducu ma itiyo. Kwero kom litino kayo me lim makwo
Nwoyo Cik 15:19 “Litino kayo ducu ma ginywalogi i kin dyaŋini nyo romi ki dyegini ibikwero komgi i nyim Rwot Lubaŋani, Pe ibitiyo tic mo ki litino kayo pa dyaŋini, pe ibiŋolo yer kom litino, kayo pa romini.
Nwoyo Cik 15:20 Ibicamo riŋone kacel ki jo ma i Odi, i nyim Rwot Lubaŋani mwaka ki mwaka ki i kabedo ma Rwot biyero.
Nwoyo Cik 15:21 Ento ka kome ki mwonyo, ka tyene oŋol, nyo waŋe oto, nyo tye ki kit mwonyo mo marac i kome, pe ibitumo bot Rwot Lubaŋani.
Nwoyo Cik 15:22 Wubicamo ki i gaŋwu ki kunnu; dano ma kome ki keni twero camo kacel ki dano ma olony, macalo riŋo abur ki til.
Nwoyo Cik 15:23 Remone keken aye pe wubicamo; wubionyo woko piny i ŋom macalo pii.
Nwoyo Cik 16:1 “Wugwok dwe me Abib, wukwer iye nino madit me Kato pi woro Rwot Lubaŋawu, pien i dwe me Abib yam Rwot Lubaŋawu okwanyowu iye woko ki i Ejipt dyewor.
Nwoyo Cik 16:2 Wubikwanyo gitum me Kato ki i kin romiwu nyo i kin dyaŋiwu, wutumo bot Rwot i kabedo ma en biyero, ka ma en biketo nyiŋe bedo iye.
Nwoyo Cik 16:3 Pe wubicamo mugati ma girubo iye tobi; ento wubicamo mugati ma tobi pe iye pi nino abiro pi po pi atwom ma yam wubedo kwede; pien yam wua ki i lobo Ejipt rucurucu; mumiyo ibipo pi nino ma yam wua kwede ki i lobo Ejipt pi kare me kwowu ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 16:4 Tobi mo pe myero onen botwu i lobowu ducu pi nino abiro; kadi wa riŋo mo ma ityero me gitum wi otyeno i nino mukwoŋone pe bidoŋ nio wa odiko.
Nwoyo Cik 16:5 Pe wubityero gitum me Kato ki i gaŋ mo ma i kin gaŋiwu ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu;
Nwoyo Cik 16:6 ento wubityero ki i kabedo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu biyero, ka ma en biketo nyiŋe bedo iye, Wubityero gitum me Kato kunnu wi otyeno ma ceŋ cito ka poto-ni, i ca wa ma yam wua kwede ki i Ejipt.
Nwoyo Cik 16:7 Wubitedo wucamo i kabedo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu biyero; ci odiko wubia wudok i kemawu.
Nwoyo Cik 16:8 Wubicamo mugati ma tobi pe iye pi nino abicel; i kom nino me abirone wubibedo iye ki cokke madit pi woro Rwot Lubaŋawu; pe wubitiyo iye tic mo. Nino madit me kwero wi mwaka (Nia 34.22; Levi 23.15-21)
Nwoyo Cik 16:9 “Wubikwano cabit abiro cakke ki i kare ma wukwoŋo keto iye pala kac i ŋut kal mucuŋ i poto.
Nwoyo Cik 16:10 Ka dok wubibedo ki nino madit me kwero agikki cabit abiro i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu kun wumiyo gityer ma iwu opwoyo; wubimiyo muporo gum ma Rwot Lubaŋawu omiyowu.
Nwoyo Cik 16:11 Ibibedo ki yomcwiny i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu, in ki wodi ki nyari ki opiini ki aŋecani, ki Lulevi ma gibedo i gaŋwu, ki lubedo ki litino kic ki mon-to ma tye i kinwu, ki i kabedo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu biyero, ka ma en biketo iye nyiŋe bedo iye.
Nwoyo Cik 16:12 Wubipo ni yam wubedo opii i Ejipt, ci wubigwoko cik magi ducu matek. Nino madito me Bolo (Levi 23.33-43)
Nwoyo Cik 16:13 “Wubikwero nino madito me Bolo pi nino abiro, i kare ma doŋ wukayo cam ducu wudino woko wutero paco, kacel ki pig olok ma doŋ wukayo wubiyo woko.
Nwoyo Cik 16:14 Wubibedo ki yomcwiny ka wukwero nino madito-ni, in ki wodi ki nyari, opiini ki aŋecani, kacel ki Lulevi ki lubedo, litino kic ki monto ma gibedo i gaŋiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 16:15 Wubikwero kare man pi nino abiro i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu ki i kabedo ma en biyero; pien Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu gum i cam ducu ma wuceko ki i kom tic me ciŋwu ducu, ma miyo wubibedo ki yomcwiny keken:
Nwoyo Cik 16:16 “Co ducu ma i kinwu myero gubin i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu tyen adek i mwaka acel acel ki i kabedo ma en biyero: i nino madito me Mugati ma Tobi Pe Iye, i nino madit me kwero cabit abiro, ki i nino madito me Bolo. Pe gubin i nyim Rwot ki ciŋgi noŋo;
Nwoyo Cik 16:17 dano acel acel bimiyo mot macalo en twero muporo kit gum ma Rwot Lubaŋawu omiye. Keto luŋolkop
Nwoyo Cik 16:18 “Wubiketo luŋolkop ki ludito i gaŋiwu ducu ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu, ma oporo kakawu; gin myero guŋol ki lwak kop ma atir.
Nwoyo Cik 16:19 Pe wubal te pido pa dano ma lokke tye atir; pe wuket apokapoka mo i kin dano; pe giwilwu ki limo Ka giwilo dano ki lim miyo laryeko doko lawaŋeoto ci balo te pido pa jo ma lokgi tye atir.
Nwoyo Cik 16:20 Wuŋol kop atir keken, wuŋol kop atir, wek wubed makwo, wule lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu. Woro lubaŋa mukene
Nwoyo Cik 16:21 “I kare ma wubicano keno tyer pi Rwot Lubaŋawu, pe wubipito yat mo i ŋete pi woro jok ma dako ma gilwoŋo Acera.
Nwoyo Cik 16:22 Dok pe wubicibo wir got mo cuŋ me awora; en aye gin ma Rwot Lubaŋawu okwero matek.
Nwoyo Cik 17:1 “Pe wubitumo bot Rwot Lubaŋawu twon nyo romo nyo dyel mo ma kome ki mwonyo, nyo ma tye ki kit ŋolo mo, pien meno aye bedo me kwer bot Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 17:2 “Gwok nyo gibinoŋo dano mo i gaŋ mo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu, laco nyo dako, ma otimo gin ma nen marac i waŋ Rwot Lubaŋawu pi taro gicikkene,
Nwoyo Cik 17:3 ce ocito ka woro lwak lubaŋa mukene, nyo ceŋ nyo dwe nyo gin mo ma i kin mony me polo ci oryebbe piny i nyimgi, ma en aye gin ma Rwot ociko ni pe myero gitim.
Nwoyo Cik 17:4 Ka doŋ gitito lokke botwu ci wuwinyo, wubipenyo lokke motmot, Ka ce lokke tye ada ma ŋene atir ni gin me kwer macalo meno otimme i Icrael,
Nwoyo Cik 17:5 wubikelo laco meno nyo dako meno ma otimo bal marac-ci i dog gaŋ, ci wubicelo ki got wuneko woko.
Nwoyo Cik 17:6 Dano meno gineko pi lok pa lucaden aryo nyo adek; dano mo pe gibineko pi lok pa lacaden acel keken.
Nwoyo Cik 17:7 Dok ciŋ lucaden aye bikwoŋo poto i kom dano meno me neke, ka lacen ciŋ lwak bipoto i kome. Kit meno miyo wubijwero gin marac woko ki i kinwu. Pido i nyim ajwagi ma Lulevi
Nwoyo Cik 17:8 “Ka ce pido mo onen i kinwu ma ŋolone oloyowu, macalo poko kin kit nek mapatpat, nyo lok kom twer ma dano mo-ni tye kwede i nyim cik, nyo lok kom ret ma dano mo oketo i kom lawote, kit pido mo ma twero nen i gaŋiwu ma ŋolone tek loyowu, ci wubia wucito i kabedo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu oyero-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 17:9 Wubicito bot ajwagi ma Lulevi, ki bot laŋolkop ma tye ka tic i kare meno, wubipenyogi ci gibititowu kit ŋolle.
Nwoyo Cik 17:10 Wubilubo kit ma gitito botwu i kabedo ma Rwot biyero; wubigwokke wek wuti kit gin ducu ma gicikowu kwede.
Nwoyo Cik 17:11 Wubitiyo kun wulubo kit pwony ducu ma gipwonyowu kwede, muporo kit ŋol ma gin guŋolo. Pe wubikwero lubo lok ma gin guŋolo, ento wubilubo kun pe wuŋak woko yo tuŋ acuc nyo tuŋ acam.
Nwoyo Cik 17:12 Dano ma lanywar ma okwero woro dog ajwaka ma ocuŋ ka tic i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu, nyo dog laŋolkop, dano meno bito; kit meno miyo wubijwero gin marac woko ki i kinwu.
Nwoyo Cik 17:13 Lwak ducu gibiwinyo pire, ci miyogi lworo, miyo ŋat mo pe dok bitimo tim anywar macalo meno.
Nwoyo Cik 17:14 “I kare ma doŋ wuo i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu, ma doŋ wucamo wubedo iye, gwok nyo wubiwacci, ‘Waket kabaka me loyowa, kit ma rok ducu ma gurumowa tye kwedeni.’
Nwoyo Cik 17:15 Doŋ ka wuketo kabaka ma loyowu myero wunen ni obedo dano ma Rwot Lubaŋawu oyero. Myero obed ŋat mo i kin utmegiwu; pe wuket larok olowu ma pe rokwu kikome.
Nwoyo Cik 17:16 En pe obed ka coko lwak aguragura pire kene, pe omi lwak odok cen i Ejipt pi wilo aguragura, pien Rwot yam owaco botwu ni, ‘Pe wubidok cen kunnu matwal.’
Nwoyo Cik 17:17 Pe onyom mon mapol, miyo ŋako cwinye woko; pe bene ocok lonyo madwoŋ pire kene.
Nwoyo Cik 17:18 “Ka doŋ obedo i wi komkerre, ci bicoyo lok me cik man ducu i buk kun kwanyo lokke ki i buk ma ajwagi ma Lulevi gwoko-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 17:19 En bibedo kwede ci bedo ka kwanone pi kare me kwone ducu, wek opwony lworo Rwot Lubaŋane pi gwoko lok ducu ma tye i cik man ki lubo gin ducu ma Rwot ociko,
Nwoyo Cik 17:20 wek pe obed ka wakke i cwinye ni edit ekato omegine, dok pe oŋak owek cik woko, pe odok yo tuŋ acuc nyo yo tuŋ acam, wek omedde bedo i kerre nakanaka, en ki likwaye i Icrael.
Nwoyo Cik 18:1 “Ajwagi ma Lulevi, wa kaka pa jo Levi ducu, pe gibilimo dul lobo mo nyo ginaleya mo i kin jo Icrael. Gibicamo gityer ma giwaŋo ki mac bot Rwot ki gin ducu ma myero dano gumi bot Rwot.
Nwoyo Cik 18:2 Pe gibileyo dul lobo mo i kin utmegigi, pien Rwot aye ginaleyagi kit ma yam ocikogi kwede.
Nwoyo Cik 18:3 Man aye bibedo waŋ wat pa ajwagi ma lwak gibimiyo botgi: Jo ma gityero gitum, kadi bibedo twon nyo romo, gibimiyo riŋo bat bot ajwaka, ki cwake aryo ki apika.
Nwoyo Cik 18:4 Kal ki koŋo vino ki moo mewu me wi mwaka, ki yer romo ma gikwoŋo nyarone, wubimiyo bot ajwaka;
Nwoyo Cik 18:5 pien Rwot Lubaŋawu yam oyero jo Levi ki i kin kakawu ducu wek gucuŋ ka tic i nyim Rwot, gin ki likwayogi matwal.
Nwoyo Cik 18:6 “Ka ce Lalevi mo oa ki i gaŋwu mo ma i lobo Icrael ducu, ka ma yam en bedo iye, ci bino i kabedo ma Rwot biyero, en twero bino kit ma cwinye mito,
Nwoyo Cik 18:7 ci bitic i nyiŋ Rwot Lubaŋane macalo Lulevi luwote ducu ma gicuŋ ka tic kunnu i nyim Rwot.
Nwoyo Cik 18:8 Gibilimo waŋ wat me acamagi ducu marom, medo ki lim ma Lalevi mo-ni olimo ki i jami pa kwarone ma ocato. Pe gilub kit tim pa lurok
Nwoyo Cik 18:9 “Ka doŋ wuo i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu, pe wubipwonyo lubo kit tim me kwer pa lurok ma kunnu.
Nwoyo Cik 18:10 Pe ginoŋ ŋat mo i kinwu ma owaŋo wode nyo nyare me gityer, nyo dano mo ma odoko latyet, nyo latyet ki ajaa, laŋi i dyel, latal,
Nwoyo Cik 18:11 lakot piny, lakor tipo, min jok nyo lapeny dog tipo pa lato.
Nwoyo Cik 18:12 Ka dano mo timo gin ma kit meno ci en bedo me kwer bot Rwot; pien pi timo gin me kwer ma kit meno miyo Rwot Lubaŋawu biryemo rok meno ducu woko ki i nyimwu.
Nwoyo Cik 18:13 Wun myero wubed laboŋo bal mo i komwu i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu;
Nwoyo Cik 18:14 rok magi ducu ma wubicamo lobogi-ni giwinyo dog lutyet ki ajaa ki lutyet mukene ducu, ento wun aye Rwot Lubaŋawu pe ye ni wutim kumeno. Lubaŋa ociko pi cwalo lanebi macalo Moses
Nwoyo Cik 18:15 “Rwot Lubaŋawu bicwalo lanebi mo macalo an, ma a ki i kin utmegiwu; wubiwinyo en
Nwoyo Cik 18:16 I nino ma yam wucokke iye i Koreb wubako dogwu bot Rwot Lubaŋawu kun wuwacci, ‘Pe dok awiny dwan Rwot Lubaŋawa, nyo anen kom mac madit-ti, wek pe ato.’
Nwoyo Cik 18:17 Ci Rwot owaco bota ni, ‘Gutimo ber pi waco lok meno ducu ma guwaco-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 18:18 Abicwalo botgi lanebi mo macalo in ma oa ki i kin utmegigi. Abiketo lokka i doge, ci en biwaco bot lwak lok ducu ma abicike kwede.
Nwoyo Cik 18:19 Ka ce dano mo okwero winyo lokka ma en biwacone i nyiŋa, ci an aye abipenyo dog dano-nu wek aket can i kome.
Nwoyo Cik 18:20 Ento ka lanebi mo ocorre ki wiye ka waco lok mo i nyiŋa ma onoŋo pe an aye acike ni oloki, nyo ma loko i nyiŋ lubaŋa mukene, lanebi meno bito.’
Nwoyo Cik 18:21 Ka ce iloko ki i cwinyi ni, ‘Wabiŋeyo lok ma Rwot pe owaco niŋniŋ mo no?’
Nwoyo Cik 18:22 ci agamo kit man ni, ‘Ka ce lanebi mo oloko i nyiŋ Rwot ce lokke-nu pe otimme nyo pe obedo me ada, meno nyuto ni lokke pe Rwot aye owaco.’ Lanebi meno ocorre ki wiye kene ki lokke gire, pienno pe myero wubed ka lwore.
Nwoyo Cik 19:1 “I kare ma Rwot Lubaŋawu doŋ otyeko lurok woko ma en bimiyo lobogi botwu- ni, ma doŋ wucamo lobogi ci wubedo i gaŋigi ki i odigi ducu,
Nwoyo Cik 19:2 ci wubipoko gaŋi adek woko pat i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋa doŋ omiyowu me bedo mewu.
Nwoyo Cik 19:3 Wubiyubo yo gudo dok wubipoko dye lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu i dul adek wek okony ŋat ma oneko dano me riŋo iye wek olar iye kome.
Nwoyo Cik 19:4 “Man aye lok me konyo kom lanek dano. Ka dano mo pe oneko lawote akaka, ma yam mone mo pe i kingi, myero en oriŋ kunnu wek olar kome.
Nwoyo Cik 19:5 Labolle ka dano mo ocito i buŋa ki lawote mo ka toŋo yen, ce otiŋo latoŋ me toŋo ki yen me areta piny ci latoŋ oput woko ki i purre, ogoyo lawote oneko woko, en myero oriŋ olar kome i gaŋ mo acel ma i kin gaŋi meno.
Nwoyo Cik 19:6 Ka pe kumeno, miyo lacul kwor remo ka kinigane olyetti biryemo kor lanek, mako woko iyo, pien noŋo piny bor, ci cobo neko woko. Ento dano macalo meno pe romo aneka, pien pe onoŋo mone mo tye i kingi i kare macon,
Nwoyo Cik 19:7 en gin mumiyo acikowu pi poko gaŋi adek pat.
Nwoyo Cik 19:8 I kare ma Rwot Lubaŋawu oyabo waŋ lobowu omedo malac kit ma yam okwoŋo kwede bot kwarowu, ma doŋ ominiwu lobo ducu ma yam ociko ni ebimiyo bot kwarowu,
Nwoyo Cik 19:9 dok ka ce wubigwoko cik man ducu ma acikowu kwede tin-ni, ni wumar Rwot Lubaŋawu, wulub yone ducu i kare ducu, ci dok wubimedo gaŋi mukene adek i kom maca.
Nwoyo Cik 19:10 Kit meno pe gibionyo remo pa dano mo ma pe ki bal i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu me aleyawu, ci miyo alii me to pe bedo i wiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 19:11 “Ento ka dano mo iye dag lawote, ce obuto okure i yo, ci olwenyo i kome, ocobo omedo ki neko woko, ka laco meno oriŋo olaro i gaŋ mo i kin gaŋ adek-ki,
Nwoyo Cik 19:12 ci ludoŋo me tuŋ pa lanek-ki gibicwalo dano giome ki kunnu, gimiye i ciŋ lacul kwor remo, wek gineke woko.
Nwoyo Cik 19:13 Kica pe bimakowu i kome, ento myero wulwok alii me to pa dano ma pe ki bal woko ki i Icrael kit meno, wek ariya mo obed pe i nyimwu. Waŋ lobo ma ludoŋo gupoko
Nwoyo Cik 19:14 “Pe ibikobo got ma poko waŋ lobo pa lawoti ma yam ludoŋo gutyeko pokone ki i lobo ma ibileyo bot kwarowu i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu me bedo mewu. Cik ma mako lucaden
Nwoyo Cik 19:15 “Lacaden acel pe miyo pido loyo dano mo pi kit bal mo nyo kit tim marac mo ma onoŋo otimo; ento kop biloyo dano pi lok pa lucaden aryo nyo adek.
Nwoyo Cik 19:16 Ka ce lacaden ma lagoba odoto dano mo ni otimo bal,
Nwoyo Cik 19:17 ci gin lupido aryo ducu gibicito i nyim Rwot, ki i nyim ajwagi pa Lubaŋa ki luŋolkop ma gitye i dog tic i kare meno.
Nwoyo Cik 19:18 Luŋolkop gibipenyo lokke mot. Ka ce lacaden ma lagoba odoto ominne ki adot me atoŋa
Nwoyo Cik 19:19 ci gibiketo can i kome ma rom ki can ma nene en mito ni giket i kom ominne-ni: kit meno miyo wubijwero tim marac woko ki i kinwu.
Nwoyo Cik 19:20 Jo mukene gibiwinyone, miyo gilworo, miyo ŋat mo pe dok bitimo tim marac macalo meno.
Nwoyo Cik 19:21 Kica pe bimakowu i kome; kwo gibiculo ki kwo, waŋ ki waŋ, lak ki lak, bad ki bad, tyen ki tyen.
Nwoyo Cik 20:1 “I kare ma wubicito ka monyo lumerokwu, ka ce wuneno gin tye ki lwak aguragura ki gadigadi lweny, dok monygi bene dit makato mewu, pe wubed ki lworo i komgi, pien Rwot Lubaŋawu bibedo kwedwu, en ma yam okwanyowu woko ki i lobo Ejipt.
Nwoyo Cik 20:2 Ka doŋ wurwayo cok ka lweny, ci ajwaka pa Lubaŋa bikato anyim ka lok ki lwak.
Nwoyo Cik 20:3 Biwaco botgi ni, ‘Wun jo Icrael wuwiny, tin doŋ wurwayo cok ka lweny i kom lumerokwu: cwinywu pe oryaŋŋe, pe wulwor, komwu pe omyel, atiba pe omakwu i komgi;
Nwoyo Cik 20:4 pien Rwot Lubaŋawu aye bicito kwedwu ka lweny piwu i kom lumerokwu ci bimiyo wuloyogi.’
Nwoyo Cik 20:5 “Lacen ludito mony gibilok ki dano kun giwacci, ‘Tye laco mo kany ma ogero ode ci peya okwero me donyo iye? Wek en odok cen paco, wek pe oto i lweny ci miyo dano mu kene aye dok bikwero ode.
Nwoyo Cik 20:6 Tye laco mo kany ma opito poto olokke ci peya ocamo nyige? Wek en odok paco, wek pe oto i lweny ci miyo ŋat mukene aye camo nyig olokke.
Nwoyo Cik 20:7 Tye laco mo kany ma otoŋo keny i kom dako ci peya obedo kwede.’ Wek en odok paco, wek pe oto i lweny ci miyo laco mukene aye bedo kwede.
Nwoyo Cik 20:8 Ludito mony dok gibimedde ki lokgi bot lwak kun giwacci, ‘Tye laco mo kany ma lalworo ma kome obaŋŋe woko? Wek en odok woko paco, pien bimiyo jo mukene cwinygi ryaŋŋe woko: macalo en-ni.’
Nwoyo Cik 20:9 Ka doŋ ludito gutyeko lokgi bot lwak, ci doŋ gibiyero lutel wi mony.
Nwoyo Cik 20:10 “I kare ma wurwayo cok ka lweny i kom gaŋ mo, koŋ wumi dwan me kuc i kome.
Nwoyo Cik 20:11 Ka jo me gaŋ meno gidok iye botwu ki dwan me kuc ce giyabo dog gaŋgi botwu, ci jo ducu ma binoŋŋe iye wubiketo tic muroni i wigi miyo gibedo macalo opiiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 20:12 Ento ka gukwero jolo lokwu me kuc, ce gucako lweny i komwu, ci monywu birumo gaŋ meno.
Nwoyo Cik 20:13 Ka Rwot Lubaŋawu omiyogi i ciŋwu, ci wubineko co ducu ki pala lucwan,
Nwoyo Cik 20:14 ento mon ki litino matino ducu ki limgi makwo, ki jami ma i gaŋ-gu ducu gibibedo me ayakawu, wubiyako wuterogi bedo mewu, ci wutwero tic ki jami ma wuyako ki bot lumerokwu, ma Rwot Lubaŋawu omiyo botwu.
Nwoyo Cik 20:15 Wubitimo gaŋi ducu ma tye ka mabor kwedwu kit meno, ma pe gaŋi pa lurok ma gibedo kanynyi.
Nwoyo Cik 20:16 “Ento gaŋi pa rok magi ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyo lobogi botwu obed mewu-ni pe wubiweko gin mo doŋ iye makwo;
Nwoyo Cik 20:17 wubijwerogi woko ducu liweŋ, gin aye jo Kit, jo Amor, jo Kanaan, jo Periji, jo Kiv ki jo Jebuc, macalo Rwot Lubaŋawu yam ocikowu kwede;
Nwoyo Cik 20:18 wek gin pe gubed ka pwonyowu ki timo gin me kwer ma gubedo ka timo me woro lwak lubaŋagi, ma bimiyowupoto i bal i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 20:19 “Ka ce wurumo gaŋ mo pi kare malac, kun wulwenyo i kome me makone, pe wubitoŋo yadi ma i ŋete woko ducu ki latoŋwu, Wutwero camo nyiggi ento pe wutoŋ yadi wuret woko piny, Yadi bene ma gitye i lum gudoko dano bo wek monywu orumgi olweny i komgi?
Nwoyo Cik 20:20 Ento yadi ma wuŋeyo ni pe gicamo nyiggi aye wubityekogi woko kun wutoŋogi wureto woko piny wek wuger ki cel matek me lweny i kom gaŋ ma tye ka lweny i komwu-ni, nio ka opoto i ciŋwu.
Nwoyo Cik 21:1 “Ka ce ginoŋo dano mo gineko i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu me bedo mewu, kun kome obuto i tim ata, ci pe giŋeyo ŋat ma oneke,
Nwoyo Cik 21:2 ci ludoŋowu ki luŋolkopwu gibibino kunnu, gibiporo bor piny nio wa i gaŋi ma orumo kom dano ma gineko-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 21:3 Ludoŋo ma i gaŋi ma cok ki kom dano ma gineko-ni gibikelo roya ma peya otiyo tic mo, ma peya oywayo kweri dyaŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 21:4 Gibitero roya wa i nota kulu mo ma piine mol kare ducu, i kabedo mo ka ma yam peya gipuro, ma pe gicoyo iye kodi. Gibituro ŋut roya woko ki i nota kunnu;
Nwoyo Cik 21:5 ci ajwagi ma gin likwayo pa Levi gibinyiko cok, pien yam Rwot Lubaŋawu oyerogi pi tic bote ki me lamo gum i nyiŋ Rwot, gin bene myero gutyek lok ducu me pido ki me bwami.
Nwoyo Cik 21:6 Ludoŋo me gaŋ meno ma cok ki ka ma ginoŋo iye kom dano ma gineko-ni gibilwoko ciŋgi malo i wi kom roya ma gituro ŋute i ŋota-ni,
Nwoyo Cik 21:7 ci gilamo doggi kun giwacci, ‘Ciŋwa pe ooyo remo pa dano man, waŋwa bene pe oneno ka gineke.
Nwoyo Cik 21:8 Ai Rwot, tim kica ki jo Icrael ma gin aye joni ma yam ikokogi-ni, pe iket alii me remo pa dano man ma pe ki bal-li i dye lwakki Icrael, ento itimgi kica pi bal me to man.’
Nwoyo Cik 21:9 Wubilwoko alii me remo ma pe ki bal woko ki i kinwu kit meno, ka ce wutiyo gin ma nen atir i waŋ Rwot. Mon ma gimakogi i lweny
Nwoyo Cik 21:10 “Ka wucito ka lweny i kom lumerokwu, ce Rwot Lubaŋawu omiyogi i ciŋwu ci wuyakogi wutero obedo dano alimawu,
Nwoyo Cik 21:11 gwok nyo ibineno dako mo mamwonya i kin jo ma iyakoni ci cwinyi mare matek kun imito ni ikwany odok dakoni.
Nwoyo Cik 21:12 Ka tye kumeno ci ibitere paco wa i odi. En koŋ bilyelo wiye ki ŋolo Lwete,
Nwoyo Cik 21:13 ci lunyo boŋone woko ma imake kwede me bedo opii, ruko mukene; ci bibedo i odi kun koko wonne ki minnne dwe acel kulu, ka lacen itwero bedo kwede macalo cware, ci en doŋ bibedo dakoni.
Nwoyo Cik 21:14 Ka inen cwinyi pe mare twatwal ci ibiweko en cito gire mot ka ma en bimito; ento pe ibicato woko giwilo ki lim, pe ibitime macalo aŋeca, pien noŋo ityeko lanye woko. Lim aleya pa latin kayo
Nwoyo Cik 21:15 “Ka laco mo tye ki mon aryo, acel dako ma gimaro ki acel ma pe gimaro, ci gin mon aryo ducu ginywalo litino ka latin kayo obedo wod pa dako ma en pe maro- ni,
Nwoyo Cik 21:16 i kare ma laco-ni poko lim me aleya ki awobene, pe omi bot latin kayo pa dako ma gimaroni dullim muporo dit pa latin kayo ma ka miyo bot latin kayone kikome ma wod pa dako ma en pe maro-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 21:17 Ento en bituco ni latin kayo en aye pa dako ma pe gimaro-ni, ci bimiye lim ma dodo dul aryo ma i kom jamine ducu ma en tye kwede; en acakki kero kome, dit me bedo latin kayo aye mere gire. Awobi ma lajemo
Nwoyo Cik 21:18 “Ka dano mo tye ki wode ma ŋute nwaŋ dok lajemo, ma pe winyo dog wonne ki minne, kadi bed gijuye matek, pe winyogi,
Nwoyo Cik 21:19 ci wonne ki minne gibimake gitere wa i dog gaŋ bot Ludoŋo me gaŋ meno ma en bedo iye-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 21:20 Ci gibiwaco bot ludoŋo ma i gaŋgi-nu ni, ‘Latin awobiwa man ŋute nwaŋ dok lajemo, pe winyo dogwa, en lacarcar dok lamero koŋo matek.’
Nwoyo Cik 21:21 Ci dano ducu me gaŋ meno gibicele woko ki got nio ka oto. Kit meno miyo wubijwero gin marac woko ki i kinwu; jo Icrael ducu gibiwinyo ci miyo gilworo. Cik mogo mapatpat
Nwoyo Cik 21:22 “Ka dano mo otimo bal ma romme noŋo can me to ci gineke woko, ma giŋabe malo i wi yat,
Nwoyo Cik 21:23 ci pe gibiweko kome bedo i wi yat dyewor. Wubiyiko kome i nino meno kikome, pien dano ma giŋabo i wi yat bedo dano ma Lubaŋa ceno; pe wubinyobo lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu me aleyawu.
Nwoyo Cik 22:1 “Ka ineno dyaŋ nyo romo pa omeru ma orwenyo woko ata, ci pe ikwer miyo kony; dwokgi cen bot omeru.
Nwoyo Cik 22:2 Ka ce en pe bedo cok kwedi, nyo ka pe iŋeye, ibitero lee-nu paco ci bibedo boti nio ka wonne oyenyo, ka doŋ ibidwokone bote.
Nwoyo Cik 22:3 Kanane bene ibitimo kit meno, ki boŋone nyo kit jami mo keken pa omeru ma orwenyo ki bote ma in inoŋo; pe ikwer miyo kony.
Nwoyo Cik 22:4 “Ka inoŋo kana pa omeru nyo dyaŋŋe ma opoto piny i ŋet yo, pe inen anena; kony omeru ki tiŋone malo.
Nwoyo Cik 22:5 “Dako pe oruk ginaruka pa co, dok laco bene pe oruk ruk pa mon, pien dano ma otimo kumeno bedo me kwer bot Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 22:6 “Ka ce icob i kom ot winyo mo ma tye i wi yat nyo piny i nom, ma litino tye iye, nyo toŋe, ki minne bene oumo wi litinone nyo obuto i wi toŋe, pe ibimako minne kacel ki litinone.
Nwoyo Cik 22:7 Ibiweko minne tuk cito, ento ibicoko litino icito kwede, wek ariya mo pe onen i nyimi ento ibed kwo pi kare malac.
Nwoyo Cik 22:8 “Ka ce igero ot manyen, ibigoyo wi ot meri irumo woko, wek pe ikel bal me oyo remo lodi, ma noŋo ŋat mo obut opoto piny ki i wiye.
Nwoyo Cik 22:9 “Pe ibicoyo poto olokki ki kit kodi mapatpat aryo, miyo gin ducu ma ocek iye myero giter i ot pa Lubaŋa, gin ma icoyo iye wa ki nyig olok bene.
Nwoyo Cik 22:10 Pe ibitweyo dyaŋ ki kana kacel me ywayo kweri dyaŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 22:11 Pe ibiruko boŋo ma gicweyo ki uci yer romo kacel ki uci camanini.
Nwoyo Cik 22:12 “Ibikwoyo jira aŋwen i twok boŋo ma iume kwede-ni. Cik ma mako cot
Nwoyo Cik 22:13 “Ka laco mo onyomo nyako ce obedo kwede, ka iye okwere woko,
Nwoyo Cik 22:14 ci otoŋo doge ki lok me lewic ma obalo nyiŋ nyako woko marac kun waco ni, ‘Anyomo nyako man ci ka anyiko bote cok pe anoŋo gin ma nyuto atir ni peya ocodo co,’
Nwoyo Cik 22:15 won latin dako-nu ki minne gibikelo boŋo ma nyuto atir ni latin dako-nu peya ocodo co bot ludoŋo ma i gaŋ meno ka ma gicokke iye i dog gaŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 22:16 Ci won latin dako-nu biwaco bot ludoŋo ni, ‘Amiyo nyara o ot laco man ci onyomo ka dok okwero en woko.
Nwoyo Cik 22:17 Ci, nen, okelo lok me lewic i kome kun waco ni pe enoŋo gin ma nyuto atir ni nyara peya ocodo co, Koŋ wunen, man en aye gin ma nyuto atir ni nyara peya ocodo co.’ Ci biyaro bone-nu i nyim ludoŋo ma i gaŋ meno.
Nwoyo Cik 22:18 Ludoŋo gibitero laco-nu gigoyo,
Nwoyo Cik 22:19 giŋolle cul me cekel me ryal miya acel. Gibimiyo limme bot won nyako, pien laco-nu obalo nyiŋ nya jo Icrael ma peya ocodo co. Ci bibedo dakone, pe biryeme woko matwal pi kare me kwone ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 22:20 Ento ka lokke ada ni, gin mo pe ginoŋo ma nyuto atir ni latin dako-nu peya ocodo co,
Nwoyo Cik 22:21 ci jo ma i gaŋ meno gibicele ki got gineko woko, pien otimo gin ma pe myero i Icrael pi codo co ki i ot pa wonne. Wubijwero tim marac woko ki i kinwu kit meno.
Nwoyo Cik 22:22 “Ka ginoŋo laco mo obuto ki dako pa laco mukene, gin aryo ducu gibito, laco ma obuto ki dako, ki dako bene. Kit meno miyo wubijwero gin marac woko ki i kinwu.
Nwoyo Cik 22:23 “Ka tye nyako mo ma peya oŋeyo laco, ma gitoŋo keny i kome ce laco mo oromo kwede i dye gaŋ ka obuto kwede,
Nwoyo Cik 22:24 ci wubitero gin aryo ducu woko i dog gaŋ, wucelogi ki got wunekogi woko, latin dako-nu pien pe ogoyo oduru kadi onoŋo tye i dye gaŋ, dok laco bene pi mako dako pa lawote ki tek. Kit meno miyo wubijwero tim marac woko ki i kinwu.
Nwoyo Cik 22:25 “Ento ka laco mo orwatte ki nyako mo ma gitoŋo keny i kome i dye tim ce omake tektek obuto kwede, ci laco ma obuto kwede-ni aye bito.
Nwoyo Cik 22:26 Pe wubitimo gin mo i kom nyako, pien en pe ki bal mo ma romo keto can me to i kome. Lok man rom ki pa laco mo ma olwenyo i kom lawote ci oneke woko.
Nwoyo Cik 22:27 Laco-nu obino i kom nyako-nu i dye tim ci kadi bed en ogoyo oduru noŋo ŋat mo pe kunnu ma lare.
Nwoyo Cik 22:28 “Ka laco mo orwatte ki nyako mo ma peya gitoŋo keny i kome ce omake tektek obuto kwede, ka gimakogi,
Nwoyo Cik 22:29 ci laco ma obuto kwede-ni bimiyo lim me luk bot won nyako ma romo cekel pyerabic, ci nyako-nu bidoko dakone, pien omake ki tek; pe biryeme woko matwal pi kare me kwone ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 22:30 “Laco mo pe obed ki ci-wonne, pe oket lewic i kom wonne kumeno.
Nwoyo Cik 23:1 “Dano ma gidino mane nyo ma giŋolo kome me co woko pe bidonyo i cokke pa Rwot.
Nwoyo Cik 23:2 “Latin luk pe bidonyo i cokke pa Rwot; kadi wa likwaye me aparre acel mo pe bidonyo i cokke pa Rwot.
Nwoyo Cik 23:3 “Dano mo pa jo Ammon nyo pa jo Moab pe bidonyo i cokke pa Rwot; kadi wa likwayogi me aparre ŋat acel mo ki i komgi pe bidonyo i cokke pa Rwot matwal,
Nwoyo Cik 23:4 pien gin yam gukwero jolowu ki kwon ki pii i kare ma wua woko ki i Ejipt, dok bene yam gukelo Balaam wod pa Beor ki i Petor ma i Mecopotamia ci guwilo ki lim wek ocenwu.
Nwoyo Cik 23:5 Ento Rwot Lubaŋawu pe owinyo dog Balaam; oloko lok me cenowu odoko me kelo gum i komwu, pien Rwot Labaŋawu onoŋo marowu.
Nwoyo Cik 23:6 Pe wutim gin mo ma kelligi kuc ki berbedo matwal, pi kare me kwo mewu ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 23:7 “Pe ii okwer Laedom mo, pien en omeru. Pe ii okwer Laejipt mo, pien yam in labedo i lobone.
Nwoyo Cik 23:8 Litinogi ma giliywalo ma likwayogi me adekke gitwero donyo i cokke pa Rwot.
Nwoyo Cik 23:9 “Ka wucito ka lweny ki lumerokwu, ma pud wutye i gony, myero wugwokke i kom gin maraco ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 23:10 “Ka tye laco mo i kinwu ma odoko keni pi gin ma otimme bote dyewor, ci en bicito woko i ne gony, bedo kunnu.
Nwoyo Cik 23:11 Ento ka piny oyuto bilwoko kome ki pii, ci ka ceŋ opoto en twero dwogo i gony.
Nwoyo Cik 23:12 “Wubiyubo kabedo mo woko i ŋe gony ka ma wubicito ka konnye iye.
Nwoyo Cik 23:13 Wubed ki tir i kin jami lwenywu; ci ka inyoŋo ka konnye ibikwinyo bur ki tir-ru, ka ilokke iumo wi coronni woko.
Nwoyo Cik 23:14 Pien Rwot Lubaŋawu woto limo dye gonywu pi larowu ki pi ryemo lumerokwu woko ki i nyimwu, mumiyo dye gonywu myero obed maleŋ wek en pe onen gin mo ma keni ci miyo en lokke wekowu woko. Cik mapatpat
Nwoyo Cik 23:15 “Pe ibidwoko opii mo bot rwode ka ce en oriŋo rwode olaro boti.
Nwoyo Cik 23:16 En bibedo i kinwu i kabedo mo ma en oyero ki i kin gaŋiwu, ka ma iye mito; pe wubiune.
Nwoyo Cik 23:17 “Kit me timo kwele me woro jogi obed peke i kin anyira Icrael, dok kit me timo kwele ki awobe mukene pi woro jogi obed peke ki i kin awobe Icrael.
Nwoyo Cik 23:18 Pe wubikelo lim ma ginoŋo pi tim kwele nyo pi tim caro macalo gwok i ot pa Rwot Lubaŋawu macalo cul me cobo kwoŋwu mo; pien gin ducu jami me kipyeda i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 23:19 “Pe ibimiyo omeru ma dano me Icrael mako banya boti me ciliŋ nyo me cam pi limo magoba, kadi banya me gin mo ma kelo magoba.
Nwoyo Cik 23:20 Itwero mako magoba i kom banya ma imiyo bot dano me rok mukene, ento pe i kom banya ma imiyo bot omeru ma Laicrael. Ka ilubo cik man ci miyo Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyi gum i kom gin ducu ma ibitiyo i lobo ma doŋ wucok donyo iye me camone-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 23:21 “Ka ikwoŋo kwoŋ mo bot Rwot Lubaŋani, pe ibed ka galle ki cobone; pien Rwot Lubaŋawu bipenyi pire ada, ci bibedo bal boti ka pe iculo.
Nwoyo Cik 23:22 Ka pe ikwoŋo kwoŋ, bal mo pe boti.
Nwoyo Cik 23:23 Ento tekke imine ka kwoŋo kwoŋ mo bot Rwot Lubaŋawu, myero igwokke mada ka cobo lok ma okatti ki i dogi.
Nwoyo Cik 23:24 “Ka iwok ki i dye poto olok pa lawoti, itwero camo nyige mabup macalo imito, ento pe ibipiko mogo i kicaani.
Nwoyo Cik 23:25 Dok ka iwok ki i poto pa lawoti ma kal Ocuŋ iye, itwero jako wite ki ciŋi, ento pe ibiketo pala kac i ŋut kal mucuŋ i poto pa lawoti.
Nwoyo Cik 24:1 “Ka laco mo onoŋo dako ce onyomo, ka dakone pe yomo cwinye pien onoŋo roc mo i kome, laco twero coyo waraga me keto nyom, miyo i ciŋe, ryeme kwede woko ki i ode, ci dako-ni a woko ki i ode.
Nwoyo Cik 24:2 Ento ka laco mukene onyome,
Nwoyo Cik 24:3 ce cware ma lacen-ni bene pe mite ci coyo waraga me keto nyom, miyo i ciŋe ci ryeme kwede woko ki i ode, nyo ka cware me aryone oto woko,
Nwoyo Cik 24:4 ci cware mukwoŋo ma yam oryeme woko pe dok owar en me bedo dakone ma onoŋo en doŋ oballe pi doko dako pa ŋat mukene, pien kit tim macalo meno bedo me kwer i nyim Rwot, wun pe wubikelo bal i kom lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyo botwu me aleyawu.
Nwoyo Cik 24:5 “Ka laco mo pud onyomo nyen, pe bicito woko kacel ki mony, dok pe gibicwale i dog tic mo; en bibedo paco mot pi mwaka acel, wek obed ki yomcwiny gin ki dakone ma onyomo-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 24:6 “Dano mo pe omi gijeŋ bote min kidi rego nyo nya kidi rego; meno rom ki kwanyo kwo pa dano me ajeŋa.
Nwoyo Cik 24:7 “Ka ŋatti mo ginoŋo okwalo dano mo ki i kin omege jo Icrael, ce otimo en kit ma gitimo ki opii, nyo ocate woko, ci lakwo meno gibinekone woko; kit meno miyo wubijwero tim marac woko ki i kinwu.
Nwoyo Cik 24:8 “I kom two dobo wubed ka gwokke matek kun wutimo gin ducu kit ma ajwaka ma Lalevi bititowu; kit ma yam acikogi kwede, wubigwokke ka tiyo kit meno.
Nwoyo Cik 24:9 Wupo gin ma yam Rwot Lubaŋawu otiyo i kom Miriam ki i yo ma onoŋo wua ki i Ejipt.
Nwoyo Cik 24:10 “Ka lawoti mo omako banya mo boti, pe ibicito i ode ka omo gin ma en jeŋo boti.
Nwoyo Cik 24:11 In ibicuŋ ki woko, ci dano ma omako banya boti-ni bikelo gin ma ojeŋo boti ki woko.
Nwoyo Cik 24:12 Ka en dano ma lacan, pe ibibuto ki gin ma en ojeŋo boti.
Nwoyo Cik 24:13 Ka ceŋ mito poto, in ibidwoko bote gin ma ojeŋo-ni wek en obut ki boŋone kun lammi gum; ci bimiyo Rwot Lubaŋawu bineni macalo dano ma kite atir.
Nwoyo Cik 24:14 “Pe ibiburo lapakacani mo ma lacan ma piny oloyo, kadi en bed omeru ma Laicrael nyo dano mo ma i kin lubedo ma gibedo i lobowu, i gaŋiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 24:15 Ibimiye mucarane i nino ma otiyo iye-ni ma onoŋo ceŋ peya opoto, pien en lacan, en bedo ka paro pire; wek en pe okok i komi bot Rwot ci bedo bal i komi.
Nwoyo Cik 24:16 “Won latin pe gibineko pi bal pa wode, nyo latin bene pe gibineko pi bal pa wonne; dano acel acel gibineko pi balle kikome.
Nwoyo Cik 24:17 “Pe ibal te pido pa labedo mo nyo pa latin kic wek lok oloye, pe iter boŋo pa daa-to me ajeŋa boti.
Nwoyo Cik 24:18 Ento ibipo ni yam ibedo opii i lobo Ejipt ci Rwot Lubaŋawu okoki woko ki i kunnu, en gin mumiyo aciko ni itim kit meno.
Nwoyo Cik 24:19 “Ka ikayo cam i potoni, ce wii owil ki larita bel mo iweko odoŋ i poto, pe idok cen ka omone; doŋ bibedo pi labedo ki latin kic ki daa-to; wek Rwot Lubaŋawu omii gum i kom tic ducu ma ibitiyo.
Nwoyo Cik 24:20 Ka ce igoyo yat jeitunini pi coko nyige, pe idok ibek obote; doŋ bibedo pa labedo ki latin kic ki daa-to.
Nwoyo Cik 24:21 Ka icoko nyig olok ki i potoni, pe idok cen ka beko obote; doŋ bibedo pa labedo ki latin kic ki daa-to.
Nwoyo Cik 24:22 Ibipo ni yam ibedo opii i lobo Ejipt, engin mumiyo aciko ni itim kumeno.
Nwoyo Cik 25:1 “Ka laro kop mo tye ikin dano, ka gubino ka ma gipido iye, ce luŋolkop guŋolo kop i kingi kun gituco dano ma pe ki bal, ka giŋolo kop loyo latim bal,
Nwoyo Cik 25:2 ka dano ma labalo romo agoya, ci laŋolkop miyo en buto piny ci gigoye ki i nyime ki wel odoo muporo kit balle.
Nwoyo Cik 25:3 Wel odoo twero bedo pyeraŋwen, ento pe okat kenyo, wek pe gigoye ki lwak goco makato meno miyo wucayo ominwu.
Nwoyo Cik 25:4 “Pe itwe dog twon ka tye ka nyono bel me dinone.
Nwoyo Cik 25:5 “Ka ce omego aryo gibedo kacel ce ŋat acel i kingi oto woko ma pe ki wode mo, pe wubiye dano ma welo ma pe ladoggolagi oter dako pa lato. Omin cware aye bilako dako-nu,
Nwoyo Cik 25:6 ci bedo kwede doko dakone wek onywal kwede litino ka wi ominne, wek nyiŋ ominne pe orweny woko ki i Icrael.
Nwoyo Cik 25:7 Ento ka laco pe mito lako ci-ominne, ci ci-ominne bicito ka ma ludoŋo me, gaŋ gucokke iye ci wacci, ‘Ywera okwero nywalo wi ominne wek nyiŋe pe orweny woko ki i kin jo Icrael; en pe oye cobo tic pa ywero i koma.’
Nwoyo Cik 25:8 Ka ludoŋo ma i gaŋgi gibilwoŋo laco-nu ci giloko kwede. Ka ce en pud medde ki lokke kun wacci, ‘An pe amito lake,’
Nwoyo Cik 25:9 ci-ominne bicito cok bote i nyim ludoŋo ci lunyo war woko ki i tyene, ka ŋulo laa i wane kun wacci, ‘Laco ma okwero nywalo litino ka wi ominne gibitimo kit meno.’
Nwoyo Cik 25:10 Ki nyiŋ doggolane gibilwoŋo i Icrael ni, ‘Doggola pa dano ma gilunyo war woko ki i tyene.’
Nwoyo Cik 25:11 “Ka ce co gitye ka lweny kekengi, ka dako pa ŋat acel onyiko cok ka laro cware ki i ciŋ dano ma tye ka goye-ni, ce ocwalo ciŋe omako kom me co pa laco-ni,
Nwoyo Cik 25:12 ci ibitoŋo ciŋ dako iŋolo woko, ma kica pe maki i kome.
Nwoyo Cik 25:13 “Pe ibed ki kidi aryo me pimo jami i kicaani, mapekke ki mayotte.
Nwoyo Cik 25:14 Pe ibed ki lapor jami aryo i odi, maditte ki matidine.
Nwoyo Cik 25:15 Ibibedo ki kidi lapim pek pa jami maberre ma romo kakare, ki agwata lapor jami maberre ma romo kakare, wek iri pi kare malac i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu.
Nwoyo Cik 25:16 Jo ducu ma gitimo gin macalo meno, ki jo ducu ma pe gitiyo gin ma tye atir, gibedo me kwer bot Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 25:17 “Wupo gin ma yam jo Amalek gutimo i komwu i yo i kare ma wua woko ki i Ejipt,
Nwoyo Cik 25:18 kit ma yam gulwenyo kwede i komwu i yo ca, i kare ma onoŋo wuder, ma komwu ducu oloc woko, kit ma gin guŋolo kwede wi jo ma gudoŋ i ŋewu ma gi goro; gin yam pe gulworo Lubaŋa wacel.
Nwoyo Cik 25:19 Ka ce Rwot Lubaŋawu doŋ omiyo wuywe ki lweny ki merokwu ducu ma orumowu dyere-ni, ki i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyo wucamo me aleyawu, ci wubijwayo jo Amalek woko ki i tam pa dano ducu ma gitye piny i te polo. Wukan lok man i cwinywu.
Nwoyo Cik 26:1 “I kare ma doŋ wuo i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu me aleyawu, ma doŋ wucamo lobo wubedo iye,
Nwoyo Cik 26:2 ibikwanyo dul mo i kom gin mukwoŋo cek i kom kit cam ducu ma ikayo ki i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu omii, ibiketo i aduku icito kwede i kabedo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu biyero ka ma biketo nyiŋe bedo iye.
Nwoyo Cik 26:3 Ibicito bot ajwaka pa Lubaŋa ma tye ka tic i kare meno, iwacce ni, ‘Tin atuco bot Rwot Lubaŋana ni atyeko o i lobo ma yam Rwot okwoŋo pire bot kwarowa ni ebimiyo botwa.’
Nwoyo Cik 26:4 Ci ajwaka bigamo aduku ki i ciŋ, ci keto piny i nyim keno tyer pa Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 26:5 “Ci ibidok iye ki i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu ni, ‘Kwarowa yam dano me lobo Aram, ma lamal gaŋ ata. Yam olak ocito wa i Ejipt obedo kunnu ma welgi nok mo; ki kunnu en odoko rok madit ki matek munya mapol.
Nwoyo Cik 26:6 Jo Ejipt gubedo ka timowa magwa marac twatwal, ma giunowa, giketowa i tic matego me opii.
Nwoyo Cik 26:7 Ka yam wakok bot Rwot Lubaŋa pa kwarowa, ci Rwot owinyo dogwa, oneno kit ma giunowa kwede, ki aroma ticwa, ki atwomwa.
Nwoyo Cik 26:8 Rwot okwanyowa woko ki i Ejipt pi twero me bade, ki ciŋe ma oryeyo, ki tim ma okelo lworo madwoŋ, ki lwak lanyut ki taŋo.
Nwoyo Cik 26:9 Okelowa wa i kabedo man, omiyowa lobo-ni, en lobo ma mol cak ki moo kic.
Nwoyo Cik 26:10 Ci doŋ inen ka tin akelo wi mwaka mua i poto ma imiyo bota; ai Rwot.’ Ka doŋ iketo aduku piny i nyim Rwot Lubaŋani, ci iryebbe piny iwore.
Nwoyo Cik 26:11 Cwinyi bibedo yom pi jami mabeco ducu ma Rwot Lubaŋani omiyo boti ki bot jo me odi; ci ibimiyo Lulevi ki lubedo ma gibedo i kinwu bene cwinygi obed yom kacel kwedwu.
Nwoyo Cik 26:12 “I mwaka me adekke, ma en aye mwakame miyo dul acel i kom apar, ibimiyo dul acel me apar me kit cam ducu ma ocek i potoni bot Lulevi, lubedo, litino kic ki mon-to wek gin bene gubed ki cam ma romogi i gaŋiwu ducu. Ka doŋ ityeko miyone botgi,
Nwoyo Cik 26:13 ci ibiwaco bot Rwot Lubaŋani ni meno, ‘Doŋ atyeko kobo jami maleŋ woko ki i oda, amiyo woko bot Lulevi, lubedo, litino kic ki mon-to kun alubo cikki ducu ma imiyo bota. Pe aturo cikki mo, pe bene wiya owil i komgi.
Nwoyo Cik 26:14 Pe acamo gin mo i kom dul acel me apar i kare ma atye ka kwero cola, pe akobo gin mo ki i oda ma onoŋo koma ki keni, pe atyero mogo bot tipo pa lato mo; doŋ aworo dogi, in Rwot Lubaŋana, atyeko tiyo gin ducu kit ma yam icika kwede.
Nwoyo Cik 26:15 Nen piny ki i kabedoni maleŋ-ŋi, nia ki i polo, ci imi gum i kom joni Icrael ki i kom lobo ma imiyowa kit ma yam ikwoŋo kwede bot kwarowa, en lobo ma mol cak ki moo kic.’
Nwoyo Cik 26:16 “Tin Rwot Lubaŋawu ociko ni wulub cik magi ki gin ma en oŋolo ducu, mumiyo wubigwokke mada ka lubogi ki cwinywu ducu ki tipowu ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 26:17 Tin doŋ wutuco lok i kom Rwot ni en aye Lubaŋawu, dok ni wubilubo yone ducu kun wugwoko cikke ki gin ma en ociko ducu, dok wubiworo doge.
Nwoyo Cik 26:18 Dok tin Rwot otuco lok i komwu ni wun aye wu jone kikome,
Nwoyo Cik 26:19 dok en bipilo wiwu makato rok ducu ma yam en oketo; gibipake piwu, nyiŋe biywek piwu, en bilimo deyo i komwu, dok otuco ni wun wubibedo rok maleŋ pi Rwot Lubaŋawu, kit ma yam owaco ni.”
Nwoyo Cik 27:1 Moses ki ludoŋo pa jo Icrael guciko lwak kun giwacci, “Wu mak cik ducu ma wacikowu kwede tin.
Nwoyo Cik 27:2 Dok i kom nino ma wuŋolo iye kulu Jordan pi donyo i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu, wubicibo iye kidi madito ci wupuyo komgi ki opuyu.
Nwoyo Cik 27:3 Wubicoyo lok me cik magi ducu i kare ma wukato wudonyo i lobo ma Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu, en aye lobo ma mol cak ki moo kic, kit ma Rwot, Lubaŋa pa kwarowu, yam ocikowu kwede-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 27:4 Ka wuŋolo loka Jordan, wubicibo kidi-nu gicuŋ i kom got Ebal, kit ma tin acikowu kwede, dok wubipuyo komgi woko ki opuyu.
Nwoyo Cik 27:5 Wubicano keno tyer kunnu pi Rwot Lubaŋawu, keno tyer ma gicano ki got; pe gitiŋ nyonyo mo me payo komgi.
Nwoyo Cik 27:6 Wubitumo gitum awaŋa i wi keno-nu bot Rwot Lubaŋawu,
Nwoyo Cik 27:7 ka dok wubityero iye gityer lakwecwiny ma wubicamone ki kunnu, ci cwinywu bibedo yom i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 27:8 Wubicoyo lok me cik man ducu i kom kidi ma wubicibogi kunnu maber ma kwanone yot.”
Nwoyo Cik 27:9 Moses ki ajwagi ma Lulevi guwaco ki jo Icrael ducu ni, “Wuliŋ mot, wuwiny, wun jo Icrael. I nino ma tin aye wudoko iye lwak pa Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 27:10 Mumiyo doŋ wuwor dog Rwot Lubaŋawu kun wumako cik mere ki gin ma en ociko ducu ma acikowu kwede tin-ni.” Ceno dano i kom got Ebal
Nwoyo Cik 27:11 Moses ociko lwak i nino meno kikome kun wacci,
Nwoyo Cik 27:12 “Ka doŋ wutyeko kato loka Jordan, jo magi gibicuŋ i wi got Gerijim ka gilamo gum i kom lwak: jo Cimeon, Levi, Juda, Icakar, Yucepu ki Benjamin;
Nwoyo Cik 27:13 ki jo magi gibicuŋ i wi got Ebal i kare ma giceno dano: jo Reuben, Gad, Acer, Jabulon, Dan ki Naputali.
Nwoyo Cik 27:14 Ci Lulevi gibiwaco lok man bot jo Icrael ducu ki dwan maloŋo ni.
Nwoyo Cik 27:15 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma otiyo cal Jok apaya mo nyo cal jok nyonyo ma giliyo aliya ma gin me kwer bot Rwot, ma ladiro otiyo ki ciŋe ci ocibo me awora i muŋ.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:16 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma pe woro wonne ki minne.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:17 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma okobo got ma poko waŋ lobo pa lawote woko.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:18 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma opaŋo wi lawaŋeoto oweko yo.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:19 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma obalo te pido pa labedo, nyo pa latin kic, nyo pa daa- to oweko lok oloye.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:20 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma obuto ki ci-wonne, pien oketo lewic i kom wonne.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:21 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma obuto ki lee mo.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:22 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma obuto ki laminne, kadi nya pa wonne, kadi nya pa minne.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:23 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma obuto ki marone.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:24 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma oneko lawote i muŋ ali.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:25 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma giwilo ki lim me Labal te pido pa dano ma pe obalo, miyo gineke nono.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 27:26 “ ‘Cen opot i kom dano ma pe moko lok ducu me cik man kun lubogi.’ Lwak ducu gibigamo ni, ‘Amen.’
Nwoyo Cik 28:1 “Ka wubiworo dog Rwot Lubaŋawu, ma wugwokke ka lubo cikke ducu ma acikowu kwede tin-ni, ci Rwot Lubaŋawu bipilo wiwu makato rok ducu ma wi lobo-ni,
Nwoyo Cik 28:2 ci miyo gum man ducu bipoto i komwu ci moko i komwu ka ce wuworo dog Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:3 Wubibedo ki gum i gaŋiwu dok wubibedo ki gum ipottiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:4 Gum bibedo i kom litino ma wubinywalogi, ki i kom cam ma bicek i pottiwu; i kom litino dyaŋiwu ki i kom litino romiwu ki dyegiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:5 Gum bibedo i kom adukuwu ma wuyeyo ki cam i kare me kac, gum bibedo i kom otakowu me myeno kwon.
Nwoyo Cik 28:6 Gum bipoto i komwu ka wudonyo i ot, ci gum bipoto i komwu ka wukato woko.
Nwoyo Cik 28:7 “Rwot biloyo lumerokwu ducu ma bibino ka lweny i komwu, miyo wubinekogi woko ki i nyimwu. Gibimol ka lweny i komwu ki i yo acel, giriŋo giket woko i yo abiro.
Nwoyo Cik 28:8 “Rwot Lubaŋawu biciko gum poto i kom derowu ducu, ki i kom gin ducu ma wubitiyo; bimiyowu gum i lobo ma en bimiyo botwu-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 28:9 “Rwot bimokowu me bedo lwakke maleŋ kit ma yam okwoŋo kwede botwu, ka ce wumako cik pa Rwot Lubaŋawu, kun wulubo yone ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:10 “Jo ma i wi lobo ducu gibineno ka gilwoŋowu ki nyiŋ Rwot, ci gibilworowu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:11 Rwot bimiyo wulony ki lwak jami mapol; bimiyo wunywalo litino mapol bimiyo limwu makwo nya madwoŋ ma pottiwu bene ceko cam mabup.
Nwoyo Cik 28:12 Rwot biyabo polo piwu, ma en ot kano limme maber, ci miyo kot cwer i lobowu i karene, ci miyo gum i kom tic ducu ma wutiyo. Jo me rok mapol gibimako banya botwu ento wun pe wubimako banya mo.
Nwoyo Cik 28:13 Rwot bimiyo wubedo jo ma telo nyim, pe jo ma coko ter; wubibedo ka cito anyim ma pe doŋ wudok cen, tekke wubedo ka lubo cik pa Rwot Lubaŋawu ma acikowu kwede tin-ni kun wugwokke ka cobogi maber,
Nwoyo Cik 28:14 ma pe wulokke wukwero lubo lok ducu ma acikowu kwede tin ci wuŋak wudok yo tuŋ acuc nyo tuŋ acam pi lubo kor lubaŋa mukene ki pi worogi. Can ma bino pi balo cik (Levi 26.14-46)
Nwoyo Cik 28:15 “Ka ce pe wuworo dog Rwot Lubaŋawu nyo pe wugwokke ka lubo lok ma en ociko ducu ki cikke ma acikowu kwede tin-ni, ci lwak cen magi ducu bipoto i komwu ci moko i komwu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:16 Cen bibedo i komwu i gaŋiwu dok cen bibedo i komwu i pottiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:17 Cen bibedo i kom adukuwu ma wuyeyo ki cam i kare me kac, cen bibedo i kom otakowu me myeno kwon.
Nwoyo Cik 28:18 Cen bibedo i kom litino ma wubinywalogi, ki i kom cam ma bicek i pottiwu, i kom litino dyaŋiwu ki i kom litino romiwu ki dyegiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:19 Cen bibedo i komwu ka wudonyo i ot, ci cen bibedo i komwu ka wukato woko.
Nwoyo Cik 28:20 “Ka ce wubwoto Rwot, ma wubedo ka tiyo gin marac, ci Rwot bicwalo cen i komwu bibaŋowu woko ci bijukowu i gin ducu ma wutemo tiyone nio ka wuto wutum woko oyotoyot.
Nwoyo Cik 28:21 Rwot bimiyo two gemo marac poto i komwu nio ka bityekowu woko ki i lobo ma wubicito iye ka camone.
Nwoyo Cik 28:22 Rwot bipwodowu ki two aona opiyo, ki aburu ki two akwota, ki lyeto madwoŋ; bicwalo oro malyet mada, ci miyowu kal mubwarre ki mupur woko.
Nwoyo Cik 28:23 Polo ma tye ka wiwu bibedo macalo mola, ki piny ma ka tyenwu bibedo tek macalo nyonyo.
Nwoyo Cik 28:24 Rwot bimiyo apulu ki apwa aye cwer ma ka kot i lobowu kun a ki malo duny i komwu nio ka otyekowu woko.
Nwoyo Cik 28:25 “Rwot bimiyo lumerokwu giloyowu woko. Wubilubo yo acel ka wucito ka lweny i komgi, ka wuriŋo wuket i yo abiro ki i nyimgi. Lworo bimako ker ducu ma wi lobo pi gin ma bitimme i komwu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:26 Komwu muto-ni bibedo cam pa winyo ducu me polo, ki pa lee timgu; pe bibedo dano mo ma ryemogi.
Nwoyo Cik 28:27 Rwot bipwodowu ki odeke kit ma yam otimo i kom jo Ejipt, ki bur adola ki nyac ki gwenyo, ma caŋone biloyowu:
Nwoyo Cik 28:28 Rwot bipwodowu ki two apoya ki to-waŋ-gu, dok bibaŋo tamwu woko.
Nwoyo Cik 28:29 Wubipanne apaŋa i dyeceŋ macalo lawaŋoto paŋŋe i colpiny, pe wubilimo gum mo i wot mewu ducu; gibibedo ka unowu ki yako jamiwu jwijwi, dano ma bikonyowu bibedo pe.
Nwoyo Cik 28:30 “Ibitoŋo keny i kom nyako, ci ŋat mukene aye bibuto kwede; ibigero ot ci pe ibibedo iye; ibipito poto olok ci pe ibicamo nyige.
Nwoyo Cik 28:31 Gibineko twonni i nyimi ma ineno ci pe ibibilo riŋone; gibimayo kanani ki i nyimi gitero woko ki tek, pe gibidwokone boti, gibimiyo romini bot lumerokki, ŋat mo ma konyi bibedo pe.
Nwoyo Cik 28:32 Awobeni ki anyirani gibimiyogi bot jo me rok mukene ma kun waŋi nenogi ci piny loyi i komgi matal, pe ibibedo ki twero me geŋogi wot.
Nwoyo Cik 28:33 Rok mo ma yam pe iŋeyo aye bicamo gin ma ocek i potoni pi tic matek ducu ma iyelle iye. Gibiuni auna keken, gibidiyi piny jwijwi,
Nwoyo Cik 28:34 miyo ibibaŋŋe woko pi gin ma ineno ki waŋi.
Nwoyo Cik 28:35 Rwot bipwodi ki odeke mudet i coŋi ki i tyeni ma caŋone biloyo dano; odeke bimwono komi woko liweŋ cakke i tyeni o kwede wa i wii.
Nwoyo Cik 28:36 “Rwot biterowu kacel ki kabakawu ma wuketo me loyowu i rok mukene ma yam peya wuŋeyo kadi wa kwarowu bene pe guŋeyo; wubiworo lwak lubaŋa mukene kunnu ma gipayo calgi ki bao nyo ki got.
Nwoyo Cik 28:37 Wubidoko gin ma kelo lworo i kin rok ducu ka ma Rwot biterowu iye, ci gibitiyo ki nyiŋwu macalo carolok ki lok aboka:
Nwoyo Cik 28:38 “Ibitiŋo lwak kodi madwoŋ itero i poto, ento ibicoko iye cam matidi mo, pien bonyo bicamo, tyeko woko.
Nwoyo Cik 28:39 Ibipito potti olok, iyubo maber, ento pe ibimato kono vinone, dok pe ibicoko nyige, pien kwidi bicamogi woko ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:40 Ibibedo ki yadi jeituni i dye loboni ducu, ento pe ibiwirre ki moone, pien nyige bio woko piny.
Nwoyo Cik 28:41 Ibinywalo awobe ki anyira, ento pe gibibedo joni, pien gibiterogi woko i opii.
Nwoyo Cik 28:42 Yadini ducu ki gin ma ocek i potoni bonyo aye bicamone woko.
Nwoyo Cik 28:43 Lubedo ma gibedo i kinwu gibidoko dito giloyowu, dok wigi bibedo doŋo i komwu, ento wun wubimedde ki doko jo matitino mogo.
Nwoyo Cik 28:44 Gin aye dok bimiyo wumako banya botgi, wun pe wubimiyo gimako banya ki botwu. Gin aye gibibedo jo ma telo nyim, wun wubicoko ter.
Nwoyo Cik 28:45 “Lwak cen man ducu bipoto i komwu kun lubo korwu, makowu, nio ka bityekowu woko, pien onoŋo wukwero winyo dog Rwot Lubaŋawu, pe wulubo cikke ki gin ma yam ocikowu kwede ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:46 Can magi gibibedo lanyut ki taŋo botwu ki bot likwayowu matwal,
Nwoyo Cik 28:47 pien yam pe wutiyo bot Rwot Lubaŋawu ki yomcwiny pi lwak jami ma en omiyowu-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 28:48 Pienno wubitic ki lumerokwu ma Rwot bicwalo ka lweny i komwu. Kec ki orwo pii binekowu, wubibedo munero ma can jami ducu omakowu, ci Rwot biriyo okol nyonyo i ŋutwu nio ka otyekowu woko ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:49 Rwot bikelo rok mo i komwu mua ki ka mabor, nia wa ki i agikki lobo, ma gidwir macalo ocur ma tuk, en aye rok mo ma pe wuŋeyo lebgi.
Nwoyo Cik 28:50 Gin rok ma waŋgi tek ma pe biparo pi woro jo, muti, kadi wa timo kica i kom jo matino.
Nwoyo Cik 28:51 Gibicamo litino dyaŋiwu woko, ki cam mucek i potowu nio ka gityekowu woko; pe kalwu mo doŋ, nyo koŋo vino nyo moo, gibiweko kadi wa litino dyaŋiwu ki litino romi ki dyegiwu, miyo wubito woko liweŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 28:52 Gibirumowu woko i gaŋiwu ducu nio ka cel maboco ki gogo ma wugenoni gupoto woko piny ki i lobowu ducu; monygi birumowu woko i gaŋiwu ducu ma oromo dye lobowu ducu ma yam Rwot Lubaŋawu omiyowu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:53 “Wubicamo riŋo kom litinowu, en aye riŋo kom awobewu ki anyirawu ma Rwot Lubaŋawu omiyo botwu, i kare ma girumo gaŋwu woko, i kare me can madwoŋ ma lumerokwu gibiketo i komwu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:54 Laco ma yam kome okwe mot ki kuc waŋe bicido woko i kom camme miyo twono ominne woko, ki dakone ma en maro, ki litinone mogo ma pud gudoŋ;
Nwoyo Cik 28:55 pe biye ni ŋat mo i kingi onywak camo kwede riŋo kom litinone ma en tye ka camone, pien pe tye gin mo mudoŋ bote, i kare me rumo gaŋ ki i kare me can madwoŋ ma lumerokwu gibiketo i komwu i gaŋiwu ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:56 Dako bene ma yam kome okwe mot ki kuc, ma yam lworo keto tyene piny i ŋom pien yam gigwoke mada, waŋe bicido woko i kom cware ma en maro, ki i kom wode ki nyare,
Nwoyo Cik 28:57 bitwonogi byero ma okatti ki i kin tyene ki riŋo kom litino ma en onywalo, pien bicamogi ki i muŋ pi can jami ducu, i kare me rumo gaŋ ki i kare me can madwoŋ ma lumerokwu gibiketo i komwu i gaŋ mewu ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:58 “Ka pe wugwokke ka lubo lok ducu ma i cik man ma gicoyo i buk man wek wubed ka lworo nyiŋ me deyo ki mapek pa Rwot, Lubaŋawu,
Nwoyo Cik 28:59 ci Rwot dok bikelo atwom madit i komwu ki i kom likwayowu, en atwom malik ma bedo nakanaka, ki two magwa ma ri nakanaka.
Nwoyo Cik 28:60 En bikelo i komwu kit two ducu pa jo Ejipt ma yam wubedo ka lworogi; twone biniaŋ i komwu matek.
Nwoyo Cik 28:61 Dok kit two ducu ki kit atwom ducu ma pe gicoyogi i buk man me cik Rwot aye bikelogi i komwu, nio ka otyekowu woko liweŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 28:62 Kadi onoŋo yam wunya mapol macalo lwak lakalatwe me polo, gibiweko welwu doŋ manok mo, pien pe wubedo ka woro dog Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:63 Kit ma yam cwiny Rwot obedo yom i komwu omiyo otimowu maber-ri dok omiyo wunya mapol, kit meno bene cwiny Rwot dok bibedo yom pi kelowu topiny ma bityekowu woko liweŋ; ci bikwanyowu woko ki i lobo ma doŋ wucok donyo iye ka camone.
Nwoyo Cik 28:64 “Rwot bikeyowu woko ata i kin rok ducu, cakke i agikki lobo tuŋ cel o kwede i agikkine mukene tuŋ cel. Wubiworo lwak lubaŋa mukene kunnu ma gipayo calgi ki bao nyo ki got, ma yam pe wuŋeyo kadi wa kwarowu bene pe guŋeyo.
Nwoyo Cik 28:65 I kin lurok magi pe wubinoŋo iye kuc mo, dok pe wubinoŋo iye ka yweyo tyenwu, ento Rwot bimiyo cwinywu myel kunnu, waŋwu bimyeno, tipo komwu bito woko lirut.
Nwoyo Cik 28:66 Cwinywu biŋabbe aŋaba pi kwowu me anyim; wubibedo ki lworo madwoŋ dyewor ki dyeceŋ, ma pe wutye ki gen mo i kwowu.
Nwoyo Cik 28:67 Odiko wubiwacci, ‘Kono nene obedo otyeno!’ dok otyeno wubiwacci, ‘Kono nene obedo odiko!’ pi lworo madwoŋ i cwinywu pi gin ma tye anyim ma waŋwu bineno.
Nwoyo Cik 28:68 Dok Rwot bidwokowu cen i Ejipt kun giterowu i mel, wubidok i wot ma yam aciko ni pe dok wubinwoyone-ni. Wubimine kekenwu kunnu bot lumerokwu kun wucatte ni giwilwu wubed opiigi ki aŋecagi, ento dano mo pe ma biwilowu.”
Nwoyo Cik 29:1 Man aye lok me gicikke ma yam Rwot ociko ki Moses ma oketo i kingi ki jo Icrael i lobo Moab, ma omedo i kom gicikke ma yam oketo i kingi i wi got Koreb.
Nwoyo Cik 29:2 Moses olwoŋo jo Icrael ducu ci owaco botgi ni, “Doŋ wutyeko neno gin ducu ma yam Rwot otiyo i lobo Ejipt ma wuneno ki waŋwu, gin ma en otimo i kom Parao ki i kom luticce ki i kom lobone ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 29:3 Wun yam wuneno ki waŋwu kit ma Rwot otemo kwede cwinye ki lwak, lanyut ki taŋo madito.
Nwoyo Cik 29:4 Ento Rwot peya omiyowu cwiny me niaŋ, nyo waŋ me neno, nyo it me winyo nio wa onyoo.
Nwoyo Cik 29:5 Doŋ atelo wiwu i dye tim mwaka pyeraŋwen ma boŋowu pe guti ki i komwu, ki war tyenwu bene pe guti woko ki i tyenwu.
Nwoyo Cik 29:6 I kare meno onoŋo pe wutye ki kwon me acama, pe wumato koŋo vino nyo kono makecce; meno aye oweko wuŋeyo ni an aye a Rwot Lubaŋawu.
Nwoyo Cik 29:7 Ka doŋ wuo i kabedo-ni, ci Cikon kabaka me Kecbon ki Og kabaka me Bacan gubino ka romo kwedwa i lweny, ento waloyogi woko,
Nwoyo Cik 29:8 ci wamayo lobogi woko wamiyo obedo ginaleya pa jo pa Reuben, ki pa jo pa Gad, ki pa nucu kaka pa Manace.
Nwoyo Cik 29:9 Pi meno myero wugwokke ka lubo lok ducu me gicikke man, wek gumkom omakwu i kom gin ducu ma wutiyo.
Nwoyo Cik 29:10 “Tin wun ducu wucuŋ i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawu: ludito wi kakawu, ludoŋowu, ludito ticwu ki co ducu pa jo Icrael,
Nwoyo Cik 29:11 litinowu ki mon mewu ki lubedo ma gibedo i gonywu ma gin aye lubar yenwu ki lutwom piiwu.
Nwoyo Cik 29:12 Wucuŋ kany wek wun ducu wukwoŋŋe pi donyo i gicikke man ma Rwot Lubaŋawu oketo i kinwu ki en tin,
Nwoyo Cik 29:13 wek en omi wubed jone tin, wek en obed Lubaŋawu, kit ma yam ocikke kwede botwu-ni, ki kit ma yam olwoŋo kwede bot kwarowu Abraim, Icaka ki Yakobo.
Nwoyo Cik 29:14 Pe aketo kwoŋ man ki gicikke man kwedwu keken,
Nwoyo Cik 29:15 ento okwako wa dano ma pe gitye kany kwedwa tin ma rom ki wan ducu ma wacuŋ kany i nyim Rwot Lubaŋawa tin.
Nwoyo Cik 29:16 “Wun wuŋeyo kit ma yam wabedo kwede i lobo Ejipt, kit ma wawoto wabino kwede kun wawok ki i dye rok mapol;
Nwoyo Cik 29:17 dok wuneno gin me kwer ma gitye kwede ducu, cal lubaŋagi me bao ki me got, me ryal ki me jabu;
Nwoyo Cik 29:18 Wugwokke wek laco mo nyo dako mo, nyo doggolawu mo, nyo kakawu mo pe onen i kinwu ma cwinye olokke oa woko i kom Rwot Lubaŋawa, ci okobo ocito ka woro lubaŋa mogo pa rok meno ducu, wek i kinwu pe onen iye dano mo ma rom ki lwit yat ma nyako kwir ki nyige makec.
Nwoyo Cik 29:19 Gwok nyo dano macalo meno ka owinyo kwoŋ man ki gicikke man ci lamo gum i kome kene i cwinye kun wacci, ‘An gira abibedo ki kuc, kadi bed cwinya nwaŋ
