Nwoyo Cik 29:20 Rwot pe bitimo dano macalo meno kica, ento kiniga pa Rwot ki nyekone aye bidunyo yito i kome, ki lok me ceno dano ma gicoyo i buk man bimoko i kome matwal, Rwot bijwayo nyiŋe woko ki i te polo.
Nwoyo Cik 29:21 Rwot bipoko en woko kene ki i kin kaka pa jo Icrael ducu, ci bolo can mapek i kome ma rwatte ki lok ducu me ceno dano ma i gicikke ma gicoyo i buk man me cik.
Nwoyo Cik 29:22 “Dok likwayowu ma gibilubowu, litinowu ma gibileyo ka tyenwu, ki lurok ma gua ki i lobo mabor, ka gibineno lwak aroma ducu ma opoto i lobowu ki lwak two ma Rwot omiyo omako dano,
Nwoyo Cik 29:23 dok ka gibineno lobowu ducu mac obalo, kun odoŋ gweŋ calfa ma mac olenyo, ki kado keken, ma pe gicoyo iye kodi mo, ma gin mo pe doŋo iye, ma lum pe lot iye, lobo muballe woko ma rom ki Codom ki Gomora ki Adma ki Jeboim, ma yam Rwot obalo woko ki kiniga ki akecane,
Nwoyo Cik 29:24 ada, ka guneno man ducu gibiwacci, ‘Piŋo Rwot otimo lobo-ni kit man? Lyeto me kiniga madwoŋ ma rom manni te lokke aŋo?’
Nwoyo Cik 29:25 Ci dano gibigamo ni, ‘Gin mumiyo otimo kit meno pien guweko lubo gicikke pa Rwot Lubaŋa pa kwarogi woko, ma ocikke iye kwedgi i kare ma okwanyogi woko ki i Ejipt,
Nwoyo Cik 29:26 ci guyeŋ gucito ka woro lwak lubaŋa mukene ki ryebbe piny i nyimgi, lwak lubaŋa ma onoŋo yam pe giŋeyo, ma yam pe gimiyo botgi me awora;
Nwoyo Cik 29:27 mumiyo kiniga omako Rwot i kom lobo man, ma okelo iye lwak lok ducu me ceno dano ma gicoyo i buk man.
Nwoyo Cik 29:28 Rwot oputo lwitgi woko ki i lobogi pi kinigane ki akecane ki akemone madwoŋ, ka obayogi woko wa i lobo mukene, macalo tye kwede wa onyooni.’
Nwoyo Cik 29:29 “Rwot Lubaŋawu tye ki muŋŋe; ento gin ma doŋ oyabo omiyo botwa doŋ bedo mewa ki pa likwayowa matwal, wek walub lok ducu ma i cik man.
Nwoyo Cik 30:1 “Ka gin man ducu doŋ opoto i komwu, gum ki lok me ceno dano ma atyeko ketone i nyimwu-ni, ka wupo pire ki i kin rok ducu ka ma Rwot Lubaŋawu yam ocwalowu iye-ni
Nwoyo Cik 30:2 ce wudwogo cen bot Rwot Lubaŋawu, wun ki likwayowu, ci wucako woro doge i lok ducu ma acikowu kwede tin-ni ki cwinywu ducu ki tipowu ducu,
Nwoyo Cik 30:3 ci Rwot Lubaŋawu bidwoko gum mewu botwu; en dok bicokowu woko ki i kin rok ducu ka ma yam okeyowu iye-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 30:4 Kadi wa jowu ma obayogi ka mabor wa i agikki te polo, Rwot Lubaŋawu bicokogi woko ki kunnu; en biomowu woko ki kunnu.
Nwoyo Cik 30:5 Rwot Lubaŋawu bikelowu i lobo ma yam kwarowu gucamo-ni wek wun bene wucam obed mewu. Lubaŋa-bimiyo wubedo ki lwak lonyo mabeco, kun wunya mapol makato kwarowu.
Nwoyo Cik 30:6 Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyo wubedo jo mulirre i cwinywu, wun ki likwayowu bene, wek wumar Rwot Lubaŋawu ki cwinywu ducu ki tipowu ducu wek wubed makwo.
Nwoyo Cik 30:7 Rwot Lubaŋawu biketo lok magi me ceno dano I kom lumonewu ki lumerokwu ma guunowu, tin-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 30:8 ci wun dok wubiworo dog Rwot kun wugwoko cikke ducu ma acikowu kwede
Nwoyo Cik 30:9 Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyo wubedo ki jami mabeco madwoŋ mada ma wubinoŋo pi ticwu; wubibedo ki litino mapol, limwu makwo binya mapol bene, potowu biceko cam mabup, pien cwiny Rwot dok bibedo yom pi miyowu lonyo ki jami mabeco, kit ma yam cwinye obedo yom i kom kwarowu-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 30:10 Ka ce wubiworo dog Rwot Lubaŋawu, ma wugwoko cikke ki gin ma ociko ducu ma gicoyo i buk man me cik, ka ce wudwogo cen bot Rwot Lubaŋawu ki cwinywu ducu ki tipowu ducu, ci Lubaŋa bimiyowu gum man.
Nwoyo Cik 30:11 “Pien cik ma acikowu kwede tin-ni pe tek twatwal ma cobone loyowu, dok pe tye ka mabor kwedwu.
Nwoyo Cik 30:12 Pe tye wa i polo, ma kono omiyo wuwacci, ‘Aŋa ma bicito ka omone botwa ki malo i polo kuca, wek okel botwa ka wek wawiny lokke walubi?’
Nwoyo Cik 30:13 Dok pe tye wa loka nam, ma kono omiyo wuwacci, ‘Aŋa ma bicito piwa wa loka nam kuca, wek okel botwa ka wek wawiny lokke walubi?’
Nwoyo Cik 30:14 Ento lokke tye cok kwedwu; wumako doŋ i cwinywu, ci wubedo ka tucone ki dogwu, miyo wutwero lubone.
Nwoyo Cik 30:15 “Nen maber ni, tin atyeko keto i nyimwu kwo ki lonyo ki to ki keckom.
Nwoyo Cik 30:16 Ka ce wuworo cik pa Rwot Lubaŋawu ma ocikowu kwede tin-ni, wek wumar Rwot Lubaŋawu, ma wulubo yone kun wugwoko cikke ki gin ma en ociko nyo oŋolo ducu, ci wubikwo dok wubinya mapol, dok Rwot Lubaŋawu bimiyowu gum i lobo ma wubidonyo iye ka camone-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 30:17 Ento ka ce cwinywu odok cen ka ryebbe i nyim lubaŋa mukene ki tiyo botgi ma wukwero winyo dog Rwot,
Nwoyo Cik 30:18 atuco atir botwu tin ni wubito wutum woko; pe wubiri pi kare malac i lobo ma wubecito iye loka Jordan ka camone-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 30:19 Alwoŋo polo ki lobo me bedo lucaden i komwu tin, ni, atyeko keto i nyimwu kwo ki to, gum ki lok me ceno dano; mumiyo wuyer kwo wek wun ki likwayowu wubed makwo,
Nwoyo Cik 30:20 ma kun wumaro Rwot Lubaŋawu, wuworo doge ci wumoko i kome matek; en aye kelo kwo botwu, ci miyo wuri pi kare malac, wek wubed i lobo ma yam Rwot okwoŋo pire bot kwarowu Abraim, Icaka ki Yakobo ni ebimiyogi.”
Nwoyo Cik 31:1 Moses dok omedde ki waco lok magi bot jo Icrael ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 31:2 Owaco botgi ni, “An mwaka me ditta doŋ romo miya ki pyeraboro tin, ci pe doŋ aromo wot ki dwogo kit ma iya mito. Rwot otyeko waco bota ni pe abikato loka Jordan.
Nwoyo Cik 31:3 Rwot Lubaŋawu kikome aye doŋ bitelo nyimwu wa loka ca. En bityeko rok magi woko ducu ki i nyimwu, ci wubicamo lobogi; ki Yocwa aye doŋ bikato loka ca ka telo wiwu kit ma doŋ Rwot owaco-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 31:4 Rwot bitimogi kit ma yam otimo i kom Cikon ki Og ma luker pa jo Amor ki i kom lobogi i kare ma otyekogi kwede woko-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 31:5 Rwot bimiyo gipoto i ciŋwu, wun wubitimogi ma lubo cik ducu ma atyeko cikowu kwede-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 31:6 Wubed oteka ma cwinywu nwaŋ; pe wulwor, pe atiba opot i komwu pigi, pien Rwot Lubaŋawu aye biwot kwedwu, pe bibwotowu ata, pe biwekowu wudoŋ kenwu.”
Nwoyo Cik 31:7 Lacen Moses olwoŋo Yocwa ci owaco bote ki i nyim jo Icrael ducu ni, “Bed oteka ma cwinyi nwaŋ, pien ibicito ki lwak man wa ilobo ma yam Rwot okwoŋo pire bot kwarogi ni ebimiyogi-ni; in aye ibimiyo gicamo doko megi.
Nwoyo Cik 31:8 Rwot aye bi telo nyimi, en bibedo kwedi, pe bibwoti ata, pe biweki keni. Pe ilwor, cwinyi pe opoti.” Cik myero gikwan i ge mwaka abiro abiro
Nwoyo Cik 31:9 Moses ocoyo cik man ducu ci omiyo bot ajwagi ma gin likwayo pa Levi, ma yam gitiŋo canduk me gicikke pa Rwot, ki bot ludoŋo ducu pa jo Icrael.
Nwoyo Cik 31:10 Ocikogi ni, “I ŋe mwaka abiro abiro, i kare ma giciko pire ni obed mwaka me weko banya, i nino me Bolo,
Nwoyo Cik 31:11 ma noŋo jo Icrael ducu gubino i nyim Rwot Lubaŋagi i kabedo ma en biyerone, wubikwano iye cik man i nyim jo Icrael ducu wek guwiny.
Nwoyo Cik 31:12 Wugur lwak kacel, co wa ki mon ki litino, ki lubedo ma gibedo i gaŋiwu, wek guwiny ci gupwony lworo Rwot Lubaŋawu, gugwokke ka lubo lok ducu me cik man,
Nwoyo Cik 31:13 ka wek litinogi ma peya guŋeyo lokke guwiny ci gupwony lworo Rwot Lubaŋawu, i kare ducu ma wubedo i lobo ma wucito iye loka Jordan ka camone- ni.” Pwony pa Rwot me agikkine bot Moses
Nwoyo Cik 31:14 Dok Rwot owaco ki Moses ni, “Nen, nino ma ibito iye doŋ onyiko cok. Lwoŋ Yocwa ci wucuŋ kwede i kema me rwatte wek acike.” Ci Moses ki Yocwa gucito gucuŋ i kema me rwatte.
Nwoyo Cik 31:15 Rwot ocako nen i kema ki wir me pol; ci wir me pol ocuŋ okemo doggola me kema.
Nwoyo Cik 31:16 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni, “Nen, in doŋ icok cito ka yweyo bot kwarowu; ci lwak man gibitwaro gicito ka woro lubaŋa mogo ma welo ki tim kwele kwele, i lobo ma gicito ka bedo iye i kingi-ni. Gibibwota woko dok gibituro gicikkena ma atyeko ketone i kinwa wan kwedgi.
Nwoyo Cik 31:17 Dok kiniga bi maka i komgi i kare meno, ci abitenyogi woko ma akano waŋa woko pe anenogi, miyo gibityekogi woko liweŋ, Gin maraco-gu ki lwak ayela mapol bipoto i komgi, mumiyo i kare meno gibiwacci, ‘Gin mumiyo can man opoto i komwa, pien Lubaŋawa doŋ pe tye i kinwa.’
Nwoyo Cik 31:18 Abikano waŋa woko i kare meno adada pi lwak balgi ducu ma gubedo ka timo, pien gudok woko cen bot lwak lubaŋa mukene.
Nwoyo Cik 31:19 Kombeddi doŋ ico wer man wek ipwony ki jo Icrael. Ket wer man i doggi, wek obed cadenna i kom jo Icrael.
Nwoyo Cik 31:20 Pien ka akelogi i lobo ma mol cak ki moo kic ma yam akwoŋo pire ni abimiyo bot kwarogi, ka gucamo ci guyeŋ gucwe kwede, ci gibidok cen bot lubaŋa mogo mukene. Gibiworogi ma kun gicaya woko, gituro gicikkena.
Nwoyo Cik 31:21 Dok ka gin maraco mapol ki lwak ayela mapol opoto i komgi, ci wer man bicuŋ i nyimgi me bedo caden botgi, pien likwayogi pud gibiwero, wigi pe biwil iye. Pien aŋeyo tam ma gutyeko yubone ma onoŋo peya aterogi i lobo ma yam akwoŋo pire ni abimiyogi.”
Nwoyo Cik 31:22 Moses ocoyo wer meno i nino meno kikome, ocako pwonyo ki jo Icrael.
Nwoyo Cik 31:23 Ka Rwot ociko Yocwa wod pa Nun kun waco bote ni, “Bed oteka ma cwinyi nwaŋ, pien in aye ibitero likwayo pa Icrael i lobo ma yam akwoŋo pire ni abimiyogi-ni, ci an abibedo kwedi.”
Nwoyo Cik 31:24 Ka yam Moses otyeko coyo lok me cik man ducu i buk nio ka otum woko ducu,
Nwoyo Cik 31:25 ci ociko Lulevi ma gitiŋo canduk me gicikke pa Rwot,
Nwoyo Cik 31:26 owacci, “Wugam buk man me cik, wuket i ŋet canduk me gicikke pa Rwot Lubaŋawu, wek obed kunnu me bedo caden i komwu.
Nwoyo Cik 31:27 Pien aŋeyo kit jemowu ki kit ma ŋutwu nwaŋ kwede ducu, Nen, ka tin dok wujemo i kom Rwot ma an pud atye kwedwu ma akwo, ci jemowu bibedo dwoŋ ma rom mene ka doŋ ato woko?
Nwoyo Cik 31:28 Wumi ludoŋo ma i kakawu ducu ki ludito ticwu gugurre kacel ka doŋ awac lok magi guwiny, ka doŋ alwoŋ polo ki lobo wek obed caden i komgi.
Nwoyo Cik 31:29 Pien aŋeyo adada ni, Ka doŋ ato, wubitimo tim aranyi; ci wubilokke, wubibarre woko ki i yo ma acikowu kwede. Gum marac bipoto i komwu i kare me anyim, pien wubitimo gin ma nen marac i waŋ Rwot kun wumiyo kiniga make ki gin ma wutiyo.” Wer pa Moses
Nwoyo Cik 31:30 Moses okwano lok ma i wer man nio ka otyeko ducu, kun lwak jo Icrael ducu ma gugurre kacel gubedo ka winyone:
Nwoyo Cik 32:1 “Wucik itwu, wun polo ducu, an doŋ abiloko; wek lobo bene owiny lok ducu ma i doga.
Nwoyo Cik 32:2 Lubaŋa omi pwonnya ocwer macalo kot, omi lokka oton macalo toyo, macalo kot ma ŋido i kom lum alita macalo kot ma wo i kom doo.
Nwoyo Cik 32:3 Pien abituco nyiŋ Rwot. Wutit dit pa Lubaŋawa!
Nwoyo Cik 32:4 “En aye Got, ma ticce ducu cobbe kakare; gin ducu ma en tiyo tye atir. En Lubaŋa ma lagen, ma pe ki bal mo; kite atir, gin ma en timo ducu tye maber.
Nwoyo Cik 32:5 Gutimo tim aranyi i kome; pe doŋ gin litinone, pien komgi ki mwonyo; gin aye yalwak muŋak mugom woko.
Nwoyo Cik 32:6 Wun mono dok wuculo Rwot kit meno, wun jo mamiŋ ki rok ma pe ki ryeko? Pe en aye wonwu ma oketowu? Pe en aye lacwec ma omiyo wutye makwo?
Nwoyo Cik 32:7 Po i kom kare ma yam con ca, tam pi lwak mwaka pa yalwak macon. Peny woru, ci binyutti maber, ki ludoŋowu bene gibititti.
Nwoyo Cik 32:8 I kare ma En Mamalo Twal yam omiyo ki rok ducu ginaleyagi, i kare ma opoko kin litino pa dano, yam opoko waŋ lobo pa rok acel acel kun lubo wei awobe pa Lubaŋa.
Nwoyo Cik 32:9 Pien lwak pa Rwot gin aye dulle, jo pa Yakobo aye gipiny ma gipoko bote.
Nwoyo Cik 32:10 “Yam onoŋo Yakobo i dye tim aroo, i lobo kweyo marac ma dano pe iye; okwake ki bade kun gwoke maber ogwoke macalo toŋ waŋe kikome.
Nwoyo Cik 32:11 Macalo ocur ma pwonyo litinone ki tuk kun teŋo bwome ma oyaro ka wigi, yaro bwome, jologi kwede, ci tiŋogi ki kono lacar madito.
Nwoyo Cik 32:12 Rwot kene aye yam telo wi jone, kun onoŋo lubaŋa pa lurok mo pe ka ŋete.
Nwoyo Cik 32:13 “Omiyo guriŋo i wi cere mutiŋŋe malo i lobo, opitogi ki cam mucek i poto; omiyogi doto moo kic ma noŋŋe i wi got, ki noto moo yaa mucek i dye pata got matek.
Nwoyo Cik 32:14 Omiyogi boto cak lukulu pa dyaŋi, ki mato cak ma libo bene pa dyegigi; gucamo moo litino romi ki nyogi romi, ki riŋo dyaŋi me Bacan ki riŋo dyegi, kacel ki moko ŋano mabecone twatwal, gumato kono vino makwar me pig olok.
Nwoyo Cik 32:15 “Ento Jecurun ocwe matek, ma loyone tek; jo pa Rwot gucwe ma komgi pek, muliŋŋe. Gubwoto Lubaŋa ma Lacwecgi woko, gucayo Got mularogi-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 32:16 Guworo lubaŋa ma welo-gu mumiyo nyeko omake, guŋeto cwinye ki tim marac me kwer omiyo kiniga omake.
Nwoyo Cik 32:17 Gutumo tum bot jogi ma pe gin lubaŋa, bot lubaŋa mogo ma yam pe giŋeyo, bot lubaŋa mogo manyen ma obino lacen ma yam kwarogi pe gulworo.
Nwoyo Cik 32:18 Gin pe guparo Got ma onywalogi-ni, wigi owil woko i kom Lubaŋa ma Wongi-ni.
Nwoyo Cik 32:19 “Rwot oneno ci ocayogi woko, pien awobene ki anyirane guŋeto cwinye.
Nwoyo Cik 32:20 Owacci, ‘Abikano waŋa woko ki botgi, wek dok anen kit ma gibitum kwede; pien gin yalwak muŋak woko ata, gin litino ma pe lugen.
Nwoyo Cik 32:21 Gumiyo nyeko omaka i kom gin ata ma pe lubaŋa; guŋeto cwinya ki cal jogi acweyagu. An bene abimiyo nyeko makogi i komji ata; abimiyo rok mo mamiŋ ŋeto cwinygi.
Nwoyo Cik 32:22 Pien kinigana doŋ omoko mac woko, doŋ tye ka waŋ wa i te bur matut me lyel, kun waŋo lobo ki gin ma ocek iye ducu, ka dok cwinyo mac waŋ wa te guti me godi.
Nwoyo Cik 32:23 “ ‘Abicoko can aguro i wigi; abityeko aterona woko i komgi.
Nwoyo Cik 32:24 Kec aye bimiyo gijony liŋok, dok awaŋogi ki lyeto ki two gemo maraco atyekogi woko liweŋ; abicwalo lak ŋuu i komgi ki kwir pa gin ma lak alaka i ŋom.
Nwoyo Cik 32:25 Pala lucwan bityekogi woko i tim, lworo bibedo wa i kicika ot; pala bityeko litino co ki anyira, litino ma dot wa ki jo ma wigi ki lwar.
Nwoyo Cik 32:26 Kono awacci, “Abikeyowu woko ka ma boco, abimiyo nyiŋgi pe doŋ gipo iye i kin dano,”
Nwoyo Cik 32:27 ento alworo lumerok wek pe guŋet cwinya, wek lumonegi pe guter marac, pe guwacci, “Waloyogi giwa, ciŋ Rwot pe otimo gin mo.” ’
Nwoyo Cik 32:28 “Pien gin aye rok ma gikwiya yubo lok, niaŋ lok bene loyogi woko.
Nwoyo Cik 32:29 Ka nene giryek, kono giniaŋ lok man, kono giŋeyo agikki me kwogi.
Nwoyo Cik 32:30 Dano acel ryemo jo alip kulu, jo aryo twaro jo alip apar, ka Gotgi aye pe omiyogi woko bot lukworgi, ka Rwot pe otenyogi woko?
Nwoyo Cik 32:31 Pien gotgi pe rom ki Gotwa, lubaŋagi pe tek ma rom ki mewa; wa merokwa bene giye lok man.
Nwoyo Cik 32:32 Lukworwa girom ki jo Codom ki Gomora, gical ki olok marac ma nyige kec; girom ki koŋo vino ma girubo ki kwir twol,
Nwoyo Cik 32:33 ki kwir twol golla mager-ri.
Nwoyo Cik 32:34 “Man aye gin ma akano, ma agwoko i ot kano limma.
Nwoyo Cik 32:35 An aye abiculo kwor, abiculo waŋe lacen. Akuro kare ma tyengi bicer; pien nino me to-pinygi doŋ cok, bipoto i komgi atura.
Nwoyo Cik 32:36 Pien Rwot bimiyo jone loyo kop, kica bimake i kom luticce ka oneno tekgi doŋ otum woko, ma dano mo pe odoŋ kadi opii nyo ŋat ma lone kene.
Nwoyo Cik 32:37 Ci bipenyogi ni, ‘Lwak lubaŋawu doŋ gitye kwene kaa, ki got ma yam wuriŋo wularo iyeni?
Nwoyo Cik 32:38 Jogi ma yam camo moo me gitumwu doŋ tye kwene, ki lumat koŋo vino me gityer amatawu? Wek doŋ gua malo ka konyowu, wek gin aye gubed jo ma gwokowu!
Nwoyo Cik 32:39 “ ‘Tin doŋ wunen ni, an aye a ene, an kena, lubaŋa mukene pe ka ŋeta. An aye aneko dok an aye amiyo kwo; an aye aketo ret dok acaŋo burre, dok pe tye ŋat mo ma laro dano ki i ciŋa.
Nwoyo Cik 32:40 Atiŋo ciŋa malo acimo polo ci akwoŋo kwon man ni, Macalo an Lubaŋa ma abedo kwo matwal-li,
Nwoyo Cik 32:41 ka ce apako pala lucwanna ma mil amila, ce aryeyo ciŋa pi ŋolo kop ci abiculo kwor i kom lumonena, abiketo can i kom jo ma gidaga.
Nwoyo Cik 32:42 Abimiyo aterona mer ki remo, pala lucwanna bicamo riŋo mabup, biyeŋ ki remo jo ma ginekogi ki ma gimakogi, bitoŋo wi lutel pa lumerok.’
Nwoyo Cik 32:43 “Wupake wun rok ducu kacel ki lwakke, pien en culokwor remo pa luticce; en culo kwor i kom lumonene pi kwanyo bal woko ki i lobo pa jone.”
Nwoyo Cik 32:44 Moses okwano wer man ducu wek lwak guwiny, en kacel ki Yocwa wod pa Nun. Moses ociko jo Icrael tyen me agikkine
Nwoyo Cik 32:45 Ka Moses otyeko waco lok magi ducu bot jo Icrael ducu ci owaco botgi ni,
Nwoyo Cik 32:46 “Wuket i cwinywu lok ducu ma awaco botwu tin-ni, wek wuketgi gubed cik ma mako litinowu bene, wek gugwokke ka lubo lok ducu me cik man.
Nwoyo Cik 32:47 Lok magi pe lok ma tere pe; gin aye kwowu kikome. Pi gwoko cik magi miyo wubiri pi kare malac i lobo ma wucito iye loka Jordan ka camone-ni.” Lubaŋa onyuto lobo Kanaan bot Moses
Nwoyo Cik 32:48 I nino meno kikome Rwot owaco bot Moses ni,
Nwoyo Cik 32:49 “It malo i wi got man me Abarim, got Nebo, ma tye i lobo Moab mukemo Jeriko, wek inen lobo Kanaan ma abimiyo bot jo Icrael obed megi.
Nwoyo Cik 32:50 Ibito i wi got ka ma iito iye-ni wek idok bot lutuwu, macalo omeru Aron yam oto i wi got Kor ci odok bot lutugi;
Nwoyo Cik 32:51 pien yam wuŋayo waŋa woko ki i dye jo Icrael, i dog pii me Meribakadec i tim me Jin; yam pe wuwora i nyim jo Icrael macalo an Lubaŋa maleŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 32:52 Pienno ibineno lobo-nu ki cen i nyimi kuca, ento pe ibicito kunnu, i lobo ma abimiyo ki jo Icrael.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:1 Man aye lamo gum pa Moses ma dano pa Lubaŋa-ni, ma yam olamo i kom likwayo pa Icrael ma onoŋo peya oto.
Nwoyo Cik 33:2 Moses olamo ni, “Rwot yam obino oa ki i wi got Cinai, ci otuc ki i Ceir wa i komwa cut, kun ryeny ki i wi got Paran. Obino ma oa ki i kin jo maleŋ alip ki alip, ki leb mac ma lyel tuŋ ciŋe malacuc.
Nwoyo Cik 33:3 Ada, en maro jone, gwoko jone maleŋ ducu i ciŋe. Pi meno waryebbe ka tyene kun en bedo ka pwonyowa,
Nwoyo Cik 33:4 ki cik ma yam Moses oketo i komwa me bedo me aleya pa lwak pa Yakobo.
Nwoyo Cik 33:5 Kit meno Rwot odoko kabaka i Jecurun i kare ma ludito ma gitelo wi lwak gucokke, ma kaka pa jo Icrael ducu gugurre kacel.
Nwoyo Cik 33:6 I kom kaka pa Reuben Moses olamo gum kit man. “Wek Reuben obed makwo, pe oto, kadi bed jone nok.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:7 Olamo gum i kom kaka pa Juda kit man, “Ai Rwot, winy dwan Juda, kele wa paco bot jone. In aye ilweny pire ki ciŋi, ikonye ka lwenyo i kom lumonene.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:8 I kom kaka pa Levi olamo ni, “Mi ki Levi Tumim meri, miye Urim meri pien en lwori. En aye dano ma yam iomo iye i Maca, en aye ŋat ma yam itemo i ŋet pii me Meriba.
Nwoyo Cik 33:9 Yam owaco i kom wonne ki minne ni, ‘Pe aparo pigi’; opokke woko ki omegine, dok pe oŋeyo wa litinone. Pien jo pa Levi gumako lokki, gulubo gicikkeni bene.
Nwoyo Cik 33:10 Gibipwonyo jo pa Yako bo ki lok ma iŋolo, gibipwonyo cikki bot jo Icrael; gibiwaŋo odok eceta i nyimi, gibityero gitum ma giwaŋo woko ducu ki berre i wi keno tyerri.
Nwoyo Cik 33:11 Ai Rwot, mi gum i kom gipinygi, dok igam tic ma gitiyo ki ciŋgi. Nyon pyer lumonegi piny, ma gin aye jo ma daggi, wek pe dok gutub i komgi.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:12 I kom kaka pa Benjamin olamo ni, “Dano ma Rwot maro-ni bedo ki kuc, Rwot Mamalo Twal gwoke kare ducu, tino en malo i wi gwoke.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:13 I kom kaka pa Yucepu olamo ni, “Rwot omi gum opot i kom lobone, ki mot mabeco ma a malo ki i polo, ki mua ki i kut matut ma oyarre i te lobo.
Nwoyo Cik 33:14 Omine nyig yadi mabeco ma nyak ki cen, ki lonyo me cam ma cek ki dwene;
Nwoyo Cik 33:15 Omine cam ma cek mabeco i kom godi muri mada, ki mubakke i wi cere ma bedo matwal;
Nwoyo Cik 33:16 omine mot mabeco me nom ki lonyone, ki gum pa Labedo i caka mulyel mac. Wek gum magi ducu gupot i kom Yucepu, i wi dano mubedo laker i kin omegine.
Nwoyo Cik 33:17 Ditte ki deyone bibedo rom ki pa wod twon me kayo, tuŋe aryo ducu tye macalo tuŋ twon ma i tim. En aye bitwomo kwede rok mapol, bicobogi ducu nio wa i agikki lobo; tuŋe aye jo Epraim ma gikato alip apar, ki jo Manace ma giromo alip mapol-li.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:18 I kom kaka pa Jabulon olamo ni, “Cwinyi obed yom, in Jabulon, ka ikato woko; ki in Icakar ka ibedo i kemani.
Nwoyo Cik 33:19 Gibilwoŋo rok ducu wek gucit i wi gotgi, gibityero gitum muporre kunnu, pien lim ma tye i nam obedo megi, kacel ki lonyo ma gikano i kweyo.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:20 I kom kaka pa Gad olamo ni, “Gum opot i kom dano ma oyabo i lobo pa Gadmalac! Gad obuto piny macalo min labwor, en yeco bat lee, dano wiye.
Nwoyo Cik 33:21 Oyero lobo maberre ni obed mere, pien onoŋo gikano lobo pa lawimony kunnu. Obino bot ludito wi lwak, otimo gin ma tye atir i nyiŋ Rwot, ocobo gin ma Rwot ociko kacel ki jo Icrael.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:22 I kom kaka pa Dan olamo ni, “Dan aye latin labwor ma kirre nia ki i Bacan.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:23 I kom kaka pa Naputali olamo ni, “Bed ki lonyo ma rommi, in Naputali, gum pa Rwot obed kwedi madwoŋ, nam ki lobo ma tun acuc obed meri.”
Nwoyo Cik 33:24 I kom kaka pa Acer olamo ni, “Acer olim gum madit makato litino ducu; wek cwiny omegine ducu omare; wek olwa tyene ki moo.
Nwoyo Cik 33:25 Laceg dog gaŋŋi obed nyonyo ki mola; bed ki tekkomi nio wa ka toni.
Nwoyo Cik 33:26 “Pe tye ŋat mo macalo Lubaŋawu, wun jo Jecurun, ma ito pol bino kwede ka konyowu, kun baro dye polo ki doyone.
Nwoyo Cik 33:27 Lubaŋa ma bedo nakanaka-ni en aye kabedowu, ciŋe tye ki tuŋ piny ma tiŋowu kwede malo. Oryemo lumerok woko ki i nyimwu kun wacci, ‘Tyekgi woko liweŋ.’
Nwoyo Cik 33:28 Icrael yam obedo ki kuc kit meno, waŋ it pa Yakobo obedo kene i lobo me kai ki koŋo vino; iyo, polo miyo toyo ton piny kunnu.
Nwoyo Cik 33:29 Cwinyi yom kuman, Icrael! Aŋa mono ma calo in kaa? In i rok ma yam Rwot olaro. Rwot aye kwot ma gwokowu, ki pala lucwan ma kelowu wayu! Lumerokwu gibibino botwu kun gimwolle amwola; ento wun wubinyonogi woko piny.”
Nwoyo Cik 34:1 Moses oa ki i lobo aroo me Moab, ocito i wi got Nebo, oito wa i wi lacol me got Piciga ma okemo Jeriko, ci Rwot onyutte lobo ducu. Onyutte lobo Gilead ducu nio kwede wa i Dan,
Nwoyo Cik 34:2 ki lobo Naputali ducu, ki lobo pa jo Epraim ki Manace, ki lobo Juda ducu nio kwede wa yo tuŋ potoceŋ,
Nwoyo Cik 34:3 ki Negeb kacel ki lobo bar-gu, ma en ayenota me Jeriko, ma gaŋ me yadi otit, ki nio kwede wa i Joar.
Nwoyo Cik 34:4 Rwot owaco bot Moses ni, “Man aye lobo ma yam akwoŋo pire bot Abraim ki Icaka ki Yakobo, ni abimiyone bot likwayogi. Doŋ aweki ineno lobone ki waŋi, ento pe ibikato loka ca.”
Nwoyo Cik 34:5 Moses latic pa Rwot oto kit meno ki i lobo Moab, kit ma yam Rwot owaco-ni,
Nwoyo Cik 34:6 ci Rwot oyike ki kunnu i nota ma i lobo Moab ma okemo Bet-peor; ento pe tye dano, mo ma oŋeyo kabedo ma oyike iye nio wa onyoo.
Nwoyo Cik 34:7 Moses onoŋo mwaka me ditte romo miya acel ki pyeraryo ka oto. Onoŋo waŋe peya ocor, ki kome bene onoŋo pud tek.
Nwoyo Cik 34:8 Jo Icrael gukoko Moses ki i lobo aroo me Moab pi nino pyeradek, ci doŋ kare me koko ki kumo pi Moses otum woko.
Nwoyo Cik 34:9 Yocwawod pa Nun yam opoŋ ki cwiny me ryeko, pien onoŋo yam Moses oketo ciŋe i kome; mumiyo jo Icrael gubedo ka woro doge, kun gilubo kit ma yam Rwot ociko ki Moses.
Nwoyo Cik 34:10 Lanebi mo mukene pe dok onen macalo Moses, ma yam Rwot nene kwede waŋ ki waŋ.
Nwoyo Cik 34:11 Pe tye ŋat mo ma rom kwede ma obedo ka tiyo lwak lanyut ki taŋo ducu ma Rwot ocwale kwede i lobo Ejipt, ma otiyo i kom Parao ki luticce ducu ki lobone ducu.
Nwoyo Cik 34:12 Pe tye lanebi mo mukene ma obedo ki twer madwoŋ ma rom ki mere pi tiyo kit tic madito ki ma kelo lworo madwoŋ kit ma yam Moses obedo ka tiyone ki i nyim jo Icrael ducu-ni.
